Chapter 1481: Please All Great Dao Scatter

One Dao, One Step

"To grasp the Three Thousand Great Daos with the power of a single individual. The Grand Magister's ambitions surprisingly align somewhat with my own." Li Biren cast his gaze around, a mixture of surprise and bewilderment flickering in his eyes.

Within the Grand Magister's inner world manifested the myriad aspects of all living beings, and also the myriad Great Daos appearing between heaven and earth. The countless beings copied by the Grand Magister had become vessels for the manifestation of these Great Daos. As Li Biren observed the countless faces arranged before him, he almost felt as if he were within the Dao Net itself. Conceptually speaking, the Grand Magister alone was indeed comparable to a "Dao Net." However, in terms of the meticulousness with which beings comprehended the Dao, and the sheer number of Dao principles, there remained a vast chasm compared to the Dao Net Li Fan had witnessed in the Shining Star Sea.

"These myriad Dao paths are all manifested through different living beings. But..." Li Biren shifted his gaze from Lan Yu to another mortal from Origin Dao Province. Upon this mortal coalesced the aura of a Great Dao related to 'painting.' The intensity of its fluctuations was such that it was utterly impossible for a mere mortal to possess! "The shadows copied by the Grand Magister possess a far deeper comprehension of the Dao than their original forms..."

Li Biren's gaze shifted to where the projections of all beings focused, in the depths of the cosmos, within the Shadow of Illusionary Life. Li Biren suddenly understood: "So that's how it is. The Shadow of Illusionary Life represents the ultimate transformation. It not only adapts to the times but can also produce various different reactions based on the different living beings it encounters."

When the disciples of the Ten Great Immortal Sects of the Immortal Realm entered Tiandu and saw the Shadow of Illusionary Life, each person's vision and hearing was filled with different cultivation techniques. But without exception, they were all profoundly related to what they had previously learned, as if tailor-made for them. The disciples of the Ten Great Immortal Sects thus concluded that the Grand Magister must have originated from the Immortal Realm, and that the teachings they received were Immortal Realm heritage techniques. "The Immortal Realm... what mortal methods could there be? Compared to Immortal techniques, the true inheritances of the Ten Great Immortal Sects are still far too lacking!" "They would never have imagined that the so-called heritage was merely a different evolution naturally produced by the [Shadow of Illusionary Life] after coming into contact with them, like a mirror!" "The Grand Magister placing them inside to behold the [Shadow of Illusionary Life], and later periodically freezing the living beings of Origin Dao Province, was likely for the sake of the Dao manifestations reflecting in this mirror."

Thinking of this, Li Biren couldn't help but look at this Grand Magister Tiandu with renewed respect. He possessed a supreme treasure that directly led to the Nameless realm, yet unlike the Starving Immortal who directly comprehended the Dao of the treasure, he instead used it as a tool, attempting to put all the Great Daos in the world into his grasp... And the Grand Magister was actually just a mere Half-Immortal. Such actions could only be described as arrogant and overconfident. But Li Biren knew very well that the Grand Magister, facing a supreme treasure of the Nameless realm, still managed to suppress his inner greed and remained steadfast for ten thousand years, never changing his original intention. He was by no means a fool. "He must have his reasons for doing this."

Li Biren did not press the interrogation for the moment. Instead, he looked at the Grand Magister, who had accumulated knowledge for ten thousand years, and the different Dao paths that had manifested through the Shadow of Illusionary Life in various living beings, and actually gave a rare smile. "His strength is insufficient. He is merely doing the work for others. Such a generous gift, I shall accept it."

With this thought, torrents of ink erupted from Li Biren. Like tentacles, they successively dyed all the myriad Dao manifestations within the Grand Magister. As Li Biren had deduced, within each figure was a comprehension of a different Dao path. They were like fruits condensed over tens of thousands of years, extremely enticing and fragrant to cultivators! Li Biren unceremoniously took them all for himself.

As the ten thousand Dao manifestations were swallowed by Li Biren, within Li Fan's main body, within the boundless ink ocean of the Slaughter Immortal Soul, different water droplets gradually began to appear. This was exactly the same as what happened when Mo Sha infiltrated the Xuanhuang Realm previously. The Grand Magister's comprehension of the Dao over ten thousand years, combined with Li Fan's own comprehension gained through countless reincarnations. Countless ink droplets representing different Dao paths differentiated themselves from the Slaughter Immortal Soul. While bringing vitality to the Slaughter Immortal Soul, they also provided a path for it to transform into different Great Daos.

Feeling the drastic changes occurring within his body, Li Fan's heart stirred, and a flickering flame, red with black edges, appeared in his palm. "Ink Slaughter as the core, Scarlet Flame as the manifestation." "This flame..." Li Fan flicked his finger, and the black flame instantly turned into a thread, flying out of the Xuanhuang Realm and colliding thunderously with the Heavenly Pillar formed by the Starving Immortal in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. Without even a ripple, the Heavenly Pillar stood unmoving. After all, it was formed by a Nameless True Immortal capable of resisting the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. Li Fan's main body was still only at the Half-Immortal realm. Although Mo Sha was peculiar, it was utterly insufficient to harm the Starving Immortal Heavenly Pillar. Li Fan was not surprised, raising his eyebrows slightly, and sensing a subtle, unremarkable black scorch mark on the Heavenly Pillar. "To merge with a Dao using a Nameless Immortal body, the strong repulsion towards other Dao paths, and yet it couldn’t completely eliminate Mo Sha." "Furthermore, along that black trace, Mo Sha’s erosion continues. Although slow, it is persistent." "If time is infinitely extended, even a towering Heavenly Pillar might eventually be breached." "And this is only the beginning..." Li Fan had a premonition that as he continued to infiltrate more Dao paths, Mo Sha's erosion ability would only grow stronger. "It's as if, though these different Dao paths are distinct, they still have certain commonalities. The more Dao paths infiltrated, the more commonalities are grasped." "Using these as keys, one can eventually overcome all obstacles." The thought of Li Fan infiltrating the Three Thousand Great Daos with Mo Sha had only just been conceived, yet it had already taken root and sprouted. Besides his own accumulations, a greater part of it was thanks to the Grand Magister's tens of thousands of years of accumulation.

As the torrents of ink completely submerged the Grand Magister's inner world. Li Fan also detected some characteristics of the Grand Magister's comprehension of the Dao. Unlike the Dao Net's nested structure with countless nodes, the Grand Magister ultimately centered around himself. Myriad Dao manifestations encircled him in the center. As if he were an emperor being worshipped by all Great Daos in the heavens! However, now, with Li Fan's intervention, this majestic emperor had become a solitary figure.

Li Biren confronted the true Grand Magister. Surrounded by countless original copies of himself, the Grand Magister Tiandu, trapped in a desperate situation, unexpectedly showed no signs of dejection, fear, or anger. His exterior, like a naive and innocent young disciple, remained calm. He was merely constantly calculating something with his fingers. Finally, seeming to achieve no results, he shook his head and chose to give up. He then asked in a faint voice, “Where does Fellow Daoist come from?” “Naturally, I come from where I came from,” Li Biren replied coldly.

Seeing that Li Biren was unwilling to reveal his origins, the Grand Magister asked no further questions. Instead, he began to negotiate: “I will cede the [Shadow of Extreme Simplicity] and allow me to leave. Is that acceptable?” “Extreme Simplicity?” Li Biren pondered for a moment. Then he coldly stated, “If I kill you, this Shadow of Illusionary Life will also be mine.”

Upon hearing this, the Grand Magister looked somewhat disheartened, but not out of fear of Li Biren’s killing intent. Rather, it was due to the different appellation Li Biren used for the illusory shadow: “So you see it as Illusionary Life.” “There is no difference,” The Grand Magister shook his head. “Before the birth of heaven and earth, there was chaos and boundlessness, and then Extreme Simplicity initially emerged. Afterward, all things began to arise and multiply. Extreme Simplicity is the ultimate power of change in the world. If Extreme Simplicity were still Extreme Simplicity, the world would not have become what it is today. The Great Dao itself is in decline. Extreme Simplicity transforming into Illusionary Life… Heh, I was deceived in the past.”

Li Biren narrowed his eyes, listening to these somewhat cryptic remarks. “Even if the Great Dao were not in decline, if the true Dao of [Extreme Simplicity] were placed before you, with your mere Half-Immortal cultivation, what could you possibly do?” Seeing that Li Biren did not act rashly, the Grand Magister was happy to live a little longer. “The Dao of Extreme Simplicity already has its master. That is precisely my Master.” “Although Master has departed, leaving only a residual shadow in the world, it is not something I can covet. I merely used Master’s divine might to comprehend the Dao paths of the world,” the Grand Magister spoke leisurely, not appearing like someone facing imminent death.

“You think that by fabricating a fictitious master, I would not dare to refine you?” Li Biren snorted coldly. The Grand Magister chuckled dismissively and pointed to his Daoist robe: “I have worn this disciple’s attire for countless years, just as I did when I served Master. I have not changed it for a long time, so how could it be fabricated?” “Whether you believe it or not. You need not worry. Even if you kill me, Master will not exact revenge for me. In the past, Master left behind a residual shadow, intending to prop up the collapsing heavens of the Immortal Realm. Unfortunately, before I could deliver the residual shadow, entire Immortal Regions were already engulfed by Dao Annihilation. Watching Master’s residual shadow, I then became greedy…”

“How could someone who can transcend be unable to control even their own residual shadow? Your lie is too crude,” Li Biren commented. The Grand Magister glanced at Li Biren, his tone inexplicably strange: “When I say Master departed, I mean ‘passed away,’ not ‘transcended.’ Master, although possessing heaven-defying divine abilities, since he chose to die, naturally no spiritual consciousness would remain.”

Li Biren was stunned upon hearing this. The Grand Magister's words were indeed somewhat beyond his expectations. “To merge with [Extreme Simplicity] and die so easily?” His tone was filled with disbelief. “Easily… Hehehehe.” The Grand Magister chuckled without answering, instead changing the topic: “Indeed, if Master had wished to continue living, there would likely have been methods to extend his life. But Master simply did not wish to!” “Who in this world wishes their Master to pass away more than I? After all, as long as he was alive, even the ruling Immortal Emperor of the Immortal Realm would have to treat me with utmost respect and courtesy. And once he died… Hehehe.” The smile on the Grand Magister’s face appeared somewhat sinister and twisted.

“So you say your Master was an unparalleled expert in the Immortal Realm. How does he compare to Shouqiu Gong?” Li Biren ignored the other party’s strange expression and directly asked. “Shouqiu Gong.” The name pulled the Grand Magister out of his resentment. For a moment, he seemed lost in thought. Then, he slowly said, “Master and Shouqiu Gong never met.” “Master was an acknowledged expert in the Immortal Realm, while Shouqiu Gong lived in solitude in the wilderness, suddenly rising to fame.” “I also asked Master about Shouqiu Gong, and he said…” The Grand Magister suddenly paused, intending to create suspense. Li Biren, surprisingly, resisted the urge to ask and simply stared coldly at the Grand Magister, waiting for his next words. After a period of stalemate, the Grand Magister felt it was uninteresting and said, “Master simply said five words: ‘Responsibility-free is naturally strong.’” “I don’t know what it means specifically.” “Anyway, until he passed away, he never mentioned that Shouqiu Gong again.”

Li Biren carefully savored these five words: “Responsibility-free is naturally strong.” After a long while, he suddenly asked again, “How many powerful beings like your Master were there in the Immortal Realm back then?” The Grand Magister’s expression became contemplative. “There were only three in the entire Immortal Realm who could sit and discuss the Dao with Master.” “Of course, this does not include Shouqiu Gong.” “Master would sometimes take me along when he traveled, and sometimes he would roam alone.” “I remember on one occasion, I asked Master who among the Four Sacred Monarchs was the strongest. Master did not answer, but merely smiled and tapped my forehead. He said…” “‘Who is the strongest, I do not know. But if you ask who is diligent, it must be the two Sacred Monarchs, [Lianshan] and [Guihai].’” “After Master finished speaking, as if recalling something joyous, he burst into laughter.”

The moment Li Biren heard the words [Lianshan] and [Guihai], his mind instinctively thought of the mountain and sea that Shouqiu Gong had witnessed. He couldn’t help but ask, “This Lianshan and Guihai…” The Grand Magister returned from his memories and stared at Li Biren. Unsure of what he was thinking, he remained silent for a long time before finally answering Li Biren’s question. “Lianshan, the first immortal in the world.” “Guihai, who opened the Infinite Spring.” “It can be said that these two Sacred Monarchs created the eternal prosperity of the Immortal Realm from nothing,” the Grand Magister said solemnly, word by word. From his demeanor, his reverence for these two Sacred Monarchs was evident.

These few words, to Li Biren, were like thunder. The Grand Magister’s words were not difficult to understand. Lianshan was the first immortal in the world. Guihai was the True Immortal who found a way to connect to the Infinite Sea, thus making immortal power endless. Someone who had personally witnessed the vastness of the Infinite Sea and could harness its power was definitely at an unimaginable level of strength. And the name “Lianshan,” when associated with the mountains that opposed the Infinite Sea, was rather thought-provoking. “Perhaps the mountain was the initial foundation of a True Immortal’s power.” Li Biren’s mind raced. The Grand Magister’s background was far greater than he had imagined.

“Besides the three Sacred Monarchs, [Extreme Simplicity], [Lianshan], and [Guihai], what about the remaining one?” Li Biren continued to extract information about the past Immortal Realm from the Grand Magister, who answered all his questions. “The remaining one…” the Grand Magister pondered for a long time, showing rare hesitation. “Cannot be spoken of.” After a long while, he shook his head. “Master, Lianshan, and Guihai have all passed away. Only this Sacred Monarch still exists in the world.” “If I mention his name, he will definitely be perceived.”

Chapter 1482: The Real Purpose

The True Purpose of the Return

The Grand Magister Tian Du spoke with noticeably more reverence when mentioning the remaining Sage Lord, the "unspeakable" one, compared to his master or the other two Sage Lords, Lian Shan and Gui Hai. This clearly indicated the significance of this final Sage Lord in his heart.

"The destruction of the Immortal Realm rendered the Sages no longer Sages," Li Biren stated coldly, his ignorance of such matters a stark contrast to the Grand Magister's awe.

The Grand Magister shook his head, "They are not Sages because they bear responsibility, but they become Sages because they are inherently Sages. Whether the Immortal Realm perishes or not has little to do with the Sages. If my master had understood this earlier, perhaps he could have lived longer."

"If your master knew you would say such a thing, he should have taken you with him when he perished."

Li Biren's sharp words left the Grand Magister speechless.

Yet, as if triggered by these words, he seemed to fall into distant memories.

"You, the Grand Magister of Tian Du, served the Four Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm for tens of thousands of years, yet you are still only a Half-Immortal. How is this possible?"

...

Li Biren continued to engage the Grand Magister in conversation, interspersing his questions with probes into the Xuanhuang Realm and the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. While gathering information, he was also subtly using the Mo Sha's dark energy to infiltrate the Grand Magister's true physical body.

The myriad Dao manifestations previously absorbed by Li Biren held no memories; they were merely records of the Great Dao reflected by the Illusory Life projection. However, through the infiltration of the Mo Sha's dark energy during this casual conversation, Li Biren discovered that the Grand Magister's body and soul were perfectly integrated, like a creation that should not exist in this world. He could find no weaknesses.

It would be easy to kill him. But to possess him and glimpse his past... that was beyond Li Biren's current capabilities.

...

The Grand Magister seemed completely unaware of Li Biren's hidden actions.

"Lian Shan will eventually return to the sea."

"My master and the other two Sage Lords have proven this. Why should I repeat their mistake?"

"Moreover, if not for my 'Half-Immortal' body, how could I have escaped the great calamity of the Immortal Realm's destruction? This is what is called retribution; everything is predetermined," the Grand Magister said dismissively, unfazed by Li Biren's mockery.

"If not for the appearance of someone like you, who should not have existed, I would have taken that crucial step as planned." The Grand Magister's tone held a hint of regret.

Just as Li Biren was about to retort, intending to shake the Grand Magister's resolve to facilitate the Mo Sha's infiltration, the Grand Magister, who had been incessantly questioned, suddenly took the initiative. "Fellow Daoist, could it be that you have obtained that treasure?"

"Treasure? I don't know what you're talking about," Li Fan's main body felt a tremor in his heart. However, Li Biren, being merely a tool executing Li Fan's commands, responded naturally.

"Stop making excuses for your failure. Wasn't the Heavenly King of Profound Heaven from ten thousand years ago almost captured by you? How could a mere Half-Immortal need an anomaly outside of fate to deal with you?" Li Biren responded with disdain.

The Grand Magister stared intently at Li Biren for a long time, finding no flaws.

He then turned his gaze towards the Origin Dao Province and the Xuanhuang Realm outside.

Looking at the Xuanhuang Realm, which had long since changed, he spoke with a drawn-out tone after a long silence, "It seems that after closing my eyes for just a moment, the outside world has turned upside down. However, what's strange is that all these changes do not encompass the area of my enlightenment."

"You have long been wary of me. But this is our first encounter..." The Grand Magister slowly closed his eyes, perhaps contemplating something internally.

"Your reputation as the Grand Magister of Tian Du is already renowned enough in the Xuanhuang Realm," Li Biren replied casually, offering no further explanation.

"You are definitely not from the Xuanhuang. The Xuanhuang Realm, or even this star sea, has all its past, present, and future predetermined. Like chess pieces on a board, taking turns. Even with the Immortal Realm's destruction, causing some variables, the pieces remain pieces. They cannot become jade..." The Grand Magister spoke slowly, seemingly suppressing some emotion within him.

Li Biren narrowed his eyes.

Meanwhile, the Mo Sha's dark energy, like dark clouds, enveloped the Grand Magister's head. And the myriad Dao manifestations that had been devoured earlier all cast indifferent gazes towards the Grand Magister.

Regardless of what the Grand Magister had guessed, Li Biren would not allow him to live any longer.

"My master's plan from back then was actually feasible."

"It's just a pity, it's too late."

The Grand Magister Tian Du, unfazed by the numerous cold gazes surrounding him, suddenly opened his eyes and looked back at Li Biren.

As if he had seen a rare treasure.

"No!"

"It's not too late yet!"

"If I could..."

The Grand Magister, who had appeared resigned moments before, suddenly became incredibly excited.

An immense force surged forth, expelling the Mo Sha's dark energy that Li Biren had infiltrated into him. The Grand Magister's Daoist robe billowed as if in a strong wind, rustling loudly.

"Everything. Can still be salvaged." The Grand Magister spoke heavily, staring at Li Biren.

Although surrounded by the myriad Dao manifestations controlled by Li Biren, the Grand Magister seemed to command them, as if they were bowing towards him.

Like an emperor or a sage, immensely noble!

Even Li Biren felt the influence. His Dao Net body, constructed from the Great Dao, inexplicably bent as if the weight of the Grand Magister alone surpassed that of all the other Great Daos combined!

Knowing that he could no longer wait, Li Biren immediately manipulated the myriad ink tendrils, erupting from the Dao manifestations and surging towards the Grand Magister in the center.

The Mo Sha dark energy, imbued with different Great Daos, transformed into various distorted humanoid figures. All sorts of Dao manifestations erupted like fireworks around the Grand Magister.

"Before Tai Yi, there was Xian."

"Wuji still existed before Tai Yi."

Two faint words, like pearls of calm in a stormy sea, instantly stilled the fluctuations of the myriad Great Daos.

The Grand Magister's figure emerged step by step from the mottled Dao shadows.

"Since you have seen Wuji..."

"Why not disperse?"

He asked again, and the surrounding Great Dao fluctuations, ignoring the pressure, scattered like a gentle breeze.

Even though the Mo Sha dark energy had already gained the upper hand, it could not prevent this process.

In the blink of an eye, Li Biren's "attackers" were gone.

Only the power of the Mo Sha Immortal Soul remained.

Moreover, Li Biren sensed that the two pillars of Mo Sha's existence, [Illusory Life] and [Eternity], were beginning to show signs of resistance.

Suppressing the commotion, Li Biren had to re-evaluate the Grand Magister Tian Du before him.

"Wuji still existed before Tai Yi?"

"What arrogance."

Although the Grand Magister still looked like an innocent child, his aura had undergone a complete transformation from before.

He stood aloof, looking down upon all beings, as if the Sage Lord of Tai Yi himself had descended, making it impossible to look directly at him.

"Sage Lord Tai Yi is indeed my master."

"But he accepted me as his disciple primarily because of my own unique nature."

"Does anyone truly deserve to remain by the Sage Lord's side for tens of thousands of years?" the Grand Magister said proudly.

"Master, please disperse."

The Grand Magister pointed towards the swirling black energy.

Then he bowed slightly.

Li Biren felt the two pillars of his Mo Sha dark energy instantly shake, losing nearly half of their power. The Dao of Illusory Life, due to its many years of evolution, was not entirely equivalent to Tai Yi, thus retaining a small amount of power.

"Master Uncle, please disperse."

The Grand Magister bowed again.

With these simple words, the other pillar of Mo Sha dark energy, the Dao of [Eternity], trembled and suddenly vanished.

With just two sentences, the fundamental basis of the Mo Sha Immortal Soul's existence was directly severed!

The black energy still remained, but it had completely lost its controllability, becoming like the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation – indifferent to all.

While the Mo Sha Immortal Soul had subtly usurped countless Dao manifestations, the Grand Magister Tian Du had also seen through its true nature!

The rampaging black energy made the Grand Magister's face appear terrifying.

Although stripped of the Mo Sha Immortal Soul's assistance, Li Biren did not panic.

He was contemplating the reason for this sudden turn of events.

Everything in the world had its logic.

Why could the Grand Magister, with just two sentences, cause the Great Daos of [Eternity] and [Illusory Life] to dissipate into thin air?

Recalling the scene he had witnessed earlier, where the Grand Magister was revered by countless Dao manifestations, Li Biren suddenly had an idea.

"The Grand Magister's goal was not to comprehend all these different Great Daos simultaneously."

"He was still using them as tools, like the Shadow of Illusory Life."

"Tools to aid his cultivation."

Li Biren's emotions stirred. "Not cultivating myriad Great Daos, but cultivating the Dao that makes myriad Great Daos bow down to him!"

"Is this superiority? Or reverence?"

For ordinary beings in the mortal world, achieving such an incredible Great Dao would be unimaginable.

But if the Grand Magister's claim was true, that he had a special identity possibly related to [Wuji] before [Tai Yi], then perhaps he could indeed achieve it!

"Cultivating this Dao path means that no divine ability or spell in the world can inflict harm upon him."

Li Biren tried it himself. As expected, all divine abilities and spells that approached the Grand Magister disappeared into nothingness within a dozen feet of him.

While Li Biren was contemplating countermeasures, the Grand Magister, moving freely through the chaotic Mo Sha dark energy, approached Li Biren.

"The one you mentioned, who nearly captured me, the Heavenly King of Profound Heaven..."

"He was born at the critical juncture of the Immortal Realm's destruction, making him truly special. Thus, he had the possibility of stepping outside the chessboard, with an immeasurable future. I didn't want to conflict with him, but he kept bothering me. So, I could only use a Dao body to mislead him."

"I never expected that his luck was so great. He disappeared from this star sea due to a chance encounter." The Grand Magister spoke as he moved beside Li Biren.

Wherever he went, all Great Daos yielded.

Li Biren, whose Dao Net body was constructed from the Great Dao, felt an unprecedented weakness, as if he might dissipate at any moment.

"But judging solely by this Heavenly King of Profound Heaven, it's perhaps unfair to judge my strength," the Grand Magister finally stood before Li Biren, face to face.

"Hand over the treasure, and I will let you leave," the Grand Magister promised solemnly.

Li Biren frowned.

Not because of his request.

But because the Grand Magister appeared so... childish.

"I don't know what you're talking about," Li Biren repeated his previous statement.

The Grand Magister, however, was extremely confident in his guess.

Seeing Li Biren's refusal to admit it, he shook his head with a hint of regret.

"Then I shall have to take it myself."

"Wuji..."

"Disperse all Daos."

The Grand Magister bowed slightly towards Li Biren.

Li Biren felt that all the remaining Great Daos within him were about to scatter in response to this command.

After all the Great Daos dispersed, only the treasure from beyond the Great Dao would remain.

"Are you that confident?"

Just as the Grand Magister was brimming with confidence, Li Biren suddenly said this.

A powerful hand suddenly gripped the Grand Magister's throat tightly.

They were so close that the Grand Magister had no time to react to this explosive surge of power.

"How is this possible?"

The Grand Magister looked at Li Biren, who had suddenly become full of power, his face filled with disbelief.

"Perhaps all the Great Daos in this world are bound by you."

"But what about the mountains and seas?"

Li Biren's figure was indistinct, as if standing on the peak of mountains and the edge of the sea.

The Grand Magister was stunned for a moment, then seemed to awaken from a dream. "Shouqiu Gong?"

Li Biren slightly shook his head: "It seems you have truly never met Shouqiu Gong."

"You are also unaware of Shouqiu Gong's arrangements here."

"This is understandable. After all, you are only a Half-Immortal. What you said earlier was correct: everything is predetermined. Everything happens for a reason." Li Biren returned his own words to the Grand Magister.

After this incident, Li Biren's killing intent towards the Grand Magister became unstoppable.

However, he was momentarily hesitant about how to deal with the Grand Magister.

Although he could suppress him for the time being with Shouqiu Gong's power, ordinary methods would find it extremely difficult to kill the Grand Magister. Furthermore, he might be related to the so-called [Wuji].

Even when held tightly by Li Biren, the Grand Magister remained unfazed.

"Shouqiu Gong's matter did exceed my expectations."

"But my origin lies beyond heaven and earth, at the beginning of the Great Dao. Therefore, the concepts of life and death are irrelevant to me."

"You cannot truly kill me."

As if Li Biren were the one being captured, the Grand Magister was still trying to persuade Li Biren to hand over the treasure.

Li Biren found it somewhat amusing: "You don't even know what this treasure is or what its specific effects are. Why are you so insistent?"

The Grand Magister replied very earnestly: "If you possess the treasure, at most you can reverse the heavens and save the world from peril."

"But if I possess it, I can correct all the things that should not have happened."

"My master, and the other three Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm. Their fates might also be rewritten."

Li Biren shook his head: "That's not possible. The so-called treasure cannot achieve all of that."

"It can."

The Grand Magister affirmed again.

Chapter 1483: Enlightenment of the Limitless Principle

Understanding the Principle of Wuji

After the "Return to Truth," a profound silence descended.

The Grand Magister seemed frozen in time, his expression solidified. In the end, he couldn't utter the word "save me" before his body, as if covered in a layer of gray, became dim.

Li Biren did not let down his guard, as the Grand Magister's life force had not yet vanished. However, after observing for a while, he finally confirmed that the Grand Magister should no longer be able to move.

The Grand Magister, whose sentience was stripped to its bare minimum, had not died but had transformed into something akin to a stone statue.

Around the stone statue, the forbidden zone of all Great Daos remained.

The effect of "Great Daos Retreating" was not significantly weaker than when the Grand Magister was still active. It was merely that, instead of deliberately targeting someone, it naturally radiated its characteristics outwards. Thus, Li Biren could barely maintain his form.

He stared at the stone statue, observing it closely. After a long while, he finally discerned something.

"It seems the Grand Magister did not lie."

"He is indeed deeply connected to Wuji before the primordial era. Perhaps he is even a direct manifestation of the Great Dao, like the [Primordial Dao Form] of the beast race."

"No..."

Recalling the Grand Magister's previous words, and the fact that despite living for tens of thousands of years, he remained so "childish," Li Biren suspected that the Grand Magister might not have achieved this manifestation solely through his own efforts.

Instead, he was guided by someone else.

"After Wuji came the creation of heaven and earth. The Grand Magister's [Wuji] is indeed genuine. Who else would be qualified to guide such an innate being other than the Four Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm?"

"Lian Shan, Gui Hai..."

"The Four Sage Lords can be traced back to the very beginning of the Immortal Realm's creation. In fact, the entire cultivation system of Immortals was created by them. The Grand Magister, as a remnant of the Great Dao of Wuji after the creation of heaven and earth, was discovered and then enlightened by them."

Li Biren pondered, gradually reconstructing the Grand Magister's past.

"Wuji." He contemplated the peculiar power emanating from the stone statue before him.

If the Immortal Realm Sage Lords had bestowed life upon the Grand Magister, then Li Biren had, with every strike, severed the Grand Magister's "life."

He had then returned the Grand Magister to his original state.

Without personal desires or thoughts, he was purely [Wuji].

Wuji and the world manifested by the Great Dao were inherently incompatible. While the Grand Magister could suppress his power in life, after his demise, the power of Wuji lost its restraint and began to spread outwards.

This was a natural trend.

Like the birth and death of the Great Dao, the rise and fall of Dao, this was the "destiny" of the Great Dao of heaven and earth, unstoppable.

"If allowed to spread, the [Primordial] possibility would, with the Xuanhuang Realm as the center, recreate heaven, earth, fire, and wind."

"However, this destruction is different from the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. This is a unique cycle of creation and destruction inherent to the heavens and earth. Even if it returns to Wuji, the world will eventually be recreated after countless years. But if it is swallowed by the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation..."

"...Then it will be eternal oblivion."

Li Biren was not repelled by the power of Wuji. Instead, he drew upon more of Shouqiu Gong's projection power, doing his best to inhibit the spread of Wuji.

Although dealing with the Grand Magister was troublesome, since he had already surmised that Li Fan might possess the "[Return to Truth]" ability, there was no reason to let him continue living.

Moreover, in the final moments, the Grand Magister had indeed called out for help.

If he had managed to call out for the last surviving Sage Lord, his Imperial Uncle, Li Fan would have been forced into a hasty "Return to Truth," even with Shouqiu Gong's projection protecting him.

"This change occurred entirely because I underestimated the Grand Magister's origin. But it's not that I was careless. Who could have imagined that the Grand Magister of Tian Du, who could contend with the Heavenly King of Profound Heaven, had such a profound background? Not only was he connected to the Immortal Realm, but he was also an innate being..." Li Fan's main body ordered Li Biren to guard the Grand Magister's stone statue temporarily. Meanwhile, Li Fan, through Li Biren's perspective, synchronized his observations and comprehension of [Wuji]. He couldn't help but feel a sense of emotion.

Even after capturing such a 'treasure' whose origin and background surpassed all else in the [Primordial] possibility, Li Fan felt no guilt.

Having truly understood the power of "[Return to Truth]" and knowing that it would likely intervene in critical moments, he was no longer as fearful of the Four Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm.

"The state of Wuji before the creation of heaven and earth still falls within the scope of possibility. [Return to Truth], with a single thought, can construct possibilities from nothingness, even return to the temporal node before the beginning of creation..."

"This means that [Wuji] is also encompassed within the power of 'Transformation between True and False'."

[Wuji] repelled all Great Daos in the world, but for beings transcending the mortal world, this repulsive characteristic was greatly diminished.

Li Biren could barely stand his ground and contain it with Shouqiu Gong's projection.

But Li Fan, relying on the power of [Return to Truth], could perceive it, and even transform it for his own use!

This was Li Fan's conclusion after observing the Grand Magister's stone statue for a long time.

"Simulating [Wuji] through the transformation between True and False."

Perhaps due to being immersed in the storm of thoughts from "[Return to Truth]" and influenced by countless past memories of the mortal world. Li Fan felt his comprehension ability had improved significantly.

Even with [Wuji], he vaguely felt a sense of familiarity. This familiarity was not with the Grand Magister, but rather an almost innate sense, as if Li Fan himself were an innate being who had observed [Wuji] from an outsider's perspective before the creation of heaven and earth.

This natural advantage allowed him to master, or rather "simulate," the use of Wuji at an incomprehensible speed.

A faint gray light appeared at Li Fan's fingertip.

The originally stable Great Daos of heaven and earth immediately became chaotic. Where the gray light appeared, the Great Daos retreated, creating an absolute void filled only with gray light.

It lasted for only three breaths, and Li Fan had consumed the power of a Xuanhuang Realm phantom within his body. The rapid depletion of energy made it difficult to circulate. Moreover, Li Fan did not possess the characteristic of "infinity."

Therefore, it was merely a brief taste, and the gray light at his fingertip quickly dissipated.

Accompanying the massive energy consumption was immense mental fatigue.

It was far more exhausting than when he had transformed the Dao Stone Mother into "True if False." Li Fan felt as if he had experienced multiple reincarnations in those brief moments.

"It seems I cannot forcefully simulate and utilize it too much with my current strength."

"But it's perfect for saving my life in critical moments."

"As long as I haven't transcended beyond the mountains and seas, and remain within the framework of the Great Dao system, I can largely disregard it..."

"Even if his cultivation is higher, the outcome remains the same. This is the suppression of the innate over the acquired."

The feeling from an observer's perspective was completely different from the actual experience of control.

Although Li Fan had easily stripped the Grand Magister of his sentience, making him appear weak, Li Fan now truly understood the power of [Wuji] after gaining a degree of control over it.

"A strike that bypasses cultivation levels."

"No wonder the Grand Magister always seemed so indifferent. Even after living for tens of thousands of years, he lacked much cunning. Protected by the power of Wuji, most things in the world couldn't affect him. Naturally, he didn't need to scheme with others or overthink. Innate power... can also be a hindrance."

"Perhaps it would have been more suitable for him to simply be a boy servant to some powerful figure."

With this thought, Li Fan's eyes narrowed, a plan forming in his mind.

However, it was merely a preliminary idea.

Its implementation would require further stages in subsequent 'lives.'

With the main body's assistance, Li Biren finally managed to contain the spreading power of Wuji, albeit with difficulty.

The price was that he had to divert a small portion of his power.

The surplus power gained from suppressing the Hungry Immortal was thus reduced by nearly half.

However, Li Fan believed this transaction was absolutely worthwhile.

Putting aside the knowledge of Wuji he had gained, the information revealed in the Grand Magister's words alone held immense value for Li Fan.

The Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm were a given.

What Li Fan was most concerned about was the possibility that the treasure "[Return to Truth]" had already existed since the Immortal Realm's inception.

"The older the existence, the more likely they are to know the truth about '[Return to Truth].' My various lies to conceal its existence might be meaningless to these powerful beings. They could see through them at a glance..."

Li Fan hadn't thought of a way to deal with this yet. However, knowing this, he would no longer be in a completely passive position.

After leaving the Grand Magister's body, the myriad Dao manifestations, upon reconnecting with heaven and earth, were partially replenished.

Countless distorted figures of Dao Annihilation, like myriad sentient beings, hid within the vast blackness of the Mo Sha Immortal Soul.

In the Suo Xing Sea, Li Fan had obtained a body-refining technique called the [Great Dao Descending Body Art].

Theoretically, reaching the pinnacle of this technique meant becoming one with the mortal world.

But for a mortal body to bear the Great Dao required unimaginable refinement.

"Compared to that, Mo Sha Immortal Soul's ability to absorb and contain different Great Daos is far simpler."

"Perhaps I can first allow my physical body to adapt to Mo Sha's characteristics."

Li Fan sensed a hint of "vitality" within the Mo Sha within his body and couldn't help but have numerous thoughts.

Of course, he wouldn't rashly test it himself.

Instead, he sent Li Biren to do it.

Li Biren's physical body had been destroyed, leaving only his Dao Net projection. It was perfect for testing the transformed Mo Sha Immortal Soul.

A drop of essence blood was flicked by Li Fan towards Li Biren.

After absorbing the essence blood, flesh and blood began to writhe within the silvery Dao Net.

Li Biren's "physical body" was thus crudely created.

Without any rare heavenly materials or earthly treasures added, this flesh and blood body was extremely weak.

But with the integration of a wisp of Mo Sha dark energy, the body immediately became extraordinary.

If it were purely the power of Mo Sha Immortal Soul, even if Li Fan merged with the Great Dao using Mo Sha, he wouldn't be able to integrate such destructive power with a flesh and blood body.

But now, Mo Sha was not just pure destruction; it had integrated with various Great Daos of heaven and earth.

The first experiment involved the most basic Great Dao of the Five Elements.

Five black energies, similar yet distinct, rotated and fused continuously.

Li Fan was extremely familiar with the process of the Five Elements flowing into himself, and thus smoothly transferred this black vortex into Li Biren's body.

The weak physical body, due to Mo Sha's destructive characteristic, slowly dissipated, quickly becoming riddled with holes and dilapidated.

It looked quite terrifying.

However, a small portion, relying on the Five Elements characteristic within Mo Sha, persisted. Using this as a foundation, it slowly began to replenish the physical body.

Li Biren moved his limbs slightly, conducting various tests.

After about half a day, he reached a conclusion.

This newly created physical body not only had an extremely strong capacity to bear Great Dao laws but also possessed considerable resistance to Dao Annihilation.

When Li Fan forcibly mobilized all of Shouqiu Gong's projection power, leaving only the primal bones and the Hungry Immortal Heavenly Pillar to stubbornly endure.

Facing the impending monstrous Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, the instinctive fear Li Biren felt was far less intense than before.

"Although the floodwaters are overwhelming, at least I can now swim. While I may still be ultimately devoured, I can at least endure for a while." Li Fan felt a sense of joy.

After all, surviving the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation was something only transcendent experts could achieve.

And Li Fan, through the "Mo Sha Immortal Soul," had achieved a similar effect through an indirect method.

More importantly, Li Biren's body could now only accommodate the Mo Sha power infused with the Five Elements characteristic.

As he gradually integrated all the Great Daos in the world in the future.

Perhaps he could face the tide of Dao Annihilation without flinching.

Of course, this was a long and arduous process.

Li Fan temporarily handed this arduous task to Li Biren.

He intended to resolve all the hidden dangers within the Xuanhuang Realm in one go.

Silver light emanated like a drizzle, covering Li Fan's entire body, forming what looked like protective armor.

This silver light was the power of Wuji.

Li Fan's destination this time was the dark sea deep within the Xuanhuang Realm.

The darkness that could devour everything retreated in deference to the silver light representing Wuji.

Like a massive ball of light illuminating this eternally dark area.

Li Fan walked calmly through the region.

The fear he had felt during his reincarnation was completely gone.

He traversed the shallow layers of the dark sea, finding nothing unusual.

Li Fan moved towards the depths of the dark sea, where the True Immortal's will to survive resided.

The formations left behind by the Heavenly King of Profound Heaven and the Law Transmitters were no longer obstacles. Li Fan didn't need to break them himself.

Under the radiance of the silver light, they all dissipated, rendering no resistance.

He saw again the vast accumulation of "momentum" that had been gathering in the depths of the dark sea for tens of thousands of years.

Before him, energy condensed in myriad forms, resembling clouds in the sky. Li Fan paused slightly.

He was now a Half-Immortal, looking down upon this scene.

"The reason Immortals were initially Immortals was because of [Lian Shan]."

"With mountains, the birth of Immortals was possible."

"The 'momentum' of Immortals..."

Li Fan looked at the mountains before him, seemingly seeing the Immortals of the past Immortal Realm.

"Immortal returns!"

He extended his right hand and gently grasped.

The dark sea instantly became turbulent.

The vast dark energy accumulated over tens of thousands of years surged towards Li Fan's palm.

Chapter 1484: The Way of the External Dao

The Dao Comes from Beyond

Before proving his Half-Immortal status, Li Fan had on several occasions utilized the Faceless Stone Statue to draw upon this dark power. He was, in essence, quite familiar with it. Now, having ascended to the Half-Immortal realm, capturing the accumulated energy within this Dark Sea was a simple matter.

Li Fan was not the master of the Dark Power. Therefore, as it was captured, it exhibited great resistance. But Li Fan was no longer the person he once was; with overwhelming power, all resistance from the Dark Power was futile. All of it obediently came into Li Fan's palm. Because it was "near-immortal power" nurtured from the remains of a True Immortal, it surprisingly possessed a property similar to the "infinite" nature of immortal power. Converging in Li Fan’s palm, it seemed to compress endlessly without limit.

When the entire Dark Sea was absorbed by Li Fan, ceasing to be dark, Li Fan’s palm held little more than a small, black, but slightly shimmering bead. As the long-settled darkness finally dissipated, Li Fan could clearly see the remains of the True Immortal in this place. Or rather, the residual traces. The True Immortal's corpse had been completely drained by the Spirit Gathering Ascension Formation, serving as nourishment. Only a few wisps of remnants, thinner than shadows, remained. Had Li Fan not observed with the discerning eye of a True Immortal from a superior position, he might not have even seen the last vestiges left by this fallen True Immortal.

"Immortal, depart~" Li Fan gazed calmly at the residual silhouette of the remains for a long time. The traces were too fragile; no effective information could be gleaned. With a gentle breath, he sent them completely scattering. It wasn't that Li Fan was suddenly becoming benevolent, intending to help this deceased True Immortal achieve transcendence. Rather, he wished to use the clearing of these traces as an opportunity to observe whether there were any other True Immortal remnants within this Dark Sea. The outcome was as expected. Besides the faint, almost inaudible roars emanating from the True Immortal’s will to survive below, there were no other resonant fluctuations in the vast Dark Sea, nor throughout the entire Xuanhuang Realm or the experimental field’s countless starscapes. "It seems this True Immortal is likely truly dead."

The Spirit Gathering Ascension Formation within the Dark Sea was initially built to serve as the power source for the Xuanhuang Realm’s escape from the Immortal Ruins. Now, Li Fan could, through his own strength, forcefully pull the Xuanhuang Realm away from the Immortal Ruins' attraction. Although he benefited from Shouqiu's ethereal projection, the strength he displayed far surpassed that of the entire Dark Sea. The process of subduing it was without incident, and as part of the cleanup, Li Fan turned his attention to the final participant present. The True Immortal's will to survive. It resembled the shadow of withered branches, or a hunched figure. Sensing Li Fan’s presence, it displayed a mixture of fear and yearning, like a wild beast in the forest encountering a hunter. It observed secretly, wavering between the desire to flee and the temptation of greed.

Li Fan, as if feeding a pet, divided a wisp of his own energy and offered it to the True Immortal’s will to survive. After circling a few times, the will to survive, as if fearing the food would escape, enveloped it, gnawing and swallowing. Li Fan’s lips curved into a faint smile. "Indeed, it’s just a foolish thing that’s nothing more than an instinctual will to survive." "The Slaughter Immortal Soul, especially a version fused with the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth, is not something you can easily digest." The True Immortal’s will to survive tried to consume the food, yet it could not diminish it in the slightest. Furthermore, this food within its belly was, in turn, beginning to devour it from the inside! The True Immortal’s will to survive let out a terrifying roar, like an ancient fierce beast. However, no matter how it struggled, it could not contend with the power of the Slaughter Immortal Soul. Helplessly, it rolled and thrashed in the deepest part of the Dark Sea. When the dust settled, the True Immortal's will to survive had transformed into one of the myriad aspects of the Slaughter Immortal Soul.

Li Fan had hoped to find some past memories within this wisp of the True Immortal’s residual consciousness. But after careful searching, he found only instinctive thoughts of consumption and rebirth. "A pity." "I couldn't figure out the true identity of this True Immortal buried at the bottom of the Dark Sea." "However, at most, it was just an ordinary True Immortal. Such matters are now insignificant." Being able to suppress a Nameless realm with a wave of his hand, Li Fan now had the qualifications to say such things. He surveyed the now empty Dark Sea, contemplating how to utilize such a large empty space in the future. Suddenly, he sensed the generation of some inexplicable energy from this place. "Hmm?" The energy source here had all been collected by him, so where did this newly generated energy come from? Li Fan was somewhat surprised but not panicked. After a divine sense sweep, he discovered that these tiny energy points, like countless faint light spots, were originating from various locations within the Xuanhuang Realm. These light spots were even more minuscule than the remnants of the True Immortal’s remains. Had it not been for their sudden appearance in the completely drained Dark Sea, Li Fan would have subconsciously ignored them. Li Fan summoned a light spot, and upon touching it, the light spot exploded and vanished like a bubble. It did not seem to exist within Li Fan’s body, its destination unknown. After a moment of contemplation, Li Fan gathered all the light spots into his hand, condensing them into a ball of light for careful observation. As the magnitude rose to a certain level, Li Fan began to feel a strange sense of familiarity. "This is..." "Spirituality?" "No. It doesn't involve the level of [Return to Truth]; it's much more basic." "However, it is still, to a certain extent, a convergence of cultivation talent."

He placed the ball of light together with the black orb formed from the Dark Sea. Li Fan seemed to understand what was happening. "The beings of Xuanhuang, in their original design, were merely pieces on a chessboard. From their creation, their attributes were predetermined: height, appearance, talent, temperament." "These light spots are the power of innate talent bestowed upon the beings by the natural workings of the Xuanhuang Realm. Now, they are being absorbed by the Dark Sea because the True Immortal's will to survive sensed this power and instinctively desired to seize it..." Li Fan frowned. "Although the beings of Xuanhuang are pawns, they are pawns of the higher-ups in the Immortal Realm. A mere wisp of survival intent..." He looked up at the beings within the Xuanhuang Realm. He wished to imitate them, to plunder the talents of all living beings. But clearly, it was impossible. "The True Immortal's will to survive has been destroyed by me, yet this extraction of talent still persists." Li Fan suddenly recalled a topic he had discussed with Bai Hua and Qiao Gong previously. During the tribulation of destruction, many cultivators had personally witnessed their homeland falling into the Immortal Ruins, with all things disintegrating and forming a fantastical scene of a strangely distorted light ring. As the cultivation world completely vanished into the Immortal Ruins, a massive amount of material seemed to erupt from the opposite direction. This was imperceptible to the naked eye or divine sense, yet it undeniably existed. The Immortal Puppet Ancestor of the Heavenly Mystery Realm had also become decadent solely because they approached the Immortal Ruins, leading to the continuous loss of something. Qiao Gong, at the time, had even used his "growing stupidity" as an excuse. "The Starving Immortal has been suppressed by me. The Immortal Ruins are no more..." Li Fan shifted his form and appeared in the starry sky outside the Xuanhuang Realm. He took out half of the light spots. Here, they did not exhibit a flowing trend but simply floated quietly in the void. They seemed unable to persist for long, quickly becoming dim. Before they completely dissipated, Li Fan recollected them. Regardless of how small this group of light orbs appeared, if all of it were bestowed upon a single individual, the resulting cultivator's talent would likely be no weaker than Zhang Haobo or Xiao Fan. "It seems that the Xuanhuang Realm has been by the side of the Immortal Ruins for too long; the world itself has developed this characteristic." "The talents and spirits of all beings are being extracted towards the opposite direction of the Immortal Ruins' suction. Even though the Immortal Ruins are gone, this trend cannot be completely reversed in a short time." After conducting comparative experiments at multiple locations in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, Li Fan tentatively drew a conclusion. "At least there isn't some scoundrel causing trouble," he said with relief. However, Li Fan naturally became curious about the reason behind this phenomenon. He, who had such profound comprehension of the Starvation Arts, was the top person in the [Primordial] possibility besides the Starving Immortal. He naturally knew that when comprehending the Starvation Arts, a suction force that devoured everything would surround him. He had never noticed anything that was not attracted by this suction force but was instead actively repelled. To verify this was not difficult. In the center of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, Li Fan unleashed a Starvation Art towards a spot not far away. Although not as powerful as the Immortal Ruins' renewed suction, it manifested like a massive vortex, suddenly appearing. The star sea became turbulent again. Li Fan, unmoved amidst the waves, threw a group of You Clan people into the vortex, whom he had initially noticed and then dismissed as the Dark Sea disappeared, causing them to howl in despair. Although the You Clan people were robust and could fight evenly with cultivators, how could they withstand the power of the Starvation Arts? Without even a sliver of struggle, they all turned to dust within the magnificent vortex. Without any emotional fluctuation, Li Fan threw them in one by one, observing closely. He had never paid special attention to this before, and it was normal to have overlooked this spiritual substance. In this detailed observation, Li Fan truly discovered this intangible substance. Furthermore, because all the You Clan people were descendants of the Xuanhuang’s original Great Heavenly Venerates, the spiritual substance extracted from the vortex was not insignificant. Li Fan, like a gold prospector, collected all the spiritual substance. "Interesting. Why does the enlightenment of the Starvation Arts produce such an anomaly?" "Perhaps it is related to the Dao path of [Hunger] itself." Li Fan recalled the scene when he had suppressed the Starving Immortal not long ago. In front of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection, the Starving Immortal, despite being outmatched, did not resign himself to fate but fought back desperately. Although the Starving Immortal's struggle was futile, what caught Li Fan’s attention was the profound, ghost-like voice that sounded like "Hunger, I am so hungry…" It seemed not to emanate from the Starving Immortal, but rather from a mysterious existence beyond the Great Dao itself. As if it wished to devour mountains and drink seas, turning everything in the world into its own sustenance. Li Fan suddenly looked again at the Starving Immortal Heavenly Pillar. "There seems to be something wrong with this Dao of Hunger." "It isn’t a Dao innate to the [Primordial] possibility? But rather, after devouring, it’s a case of usurping the nest?" Li Fan dared not be one hundred percent certain. But based on the current signs, it was already highly probable. "Spiritual substance is closely related to the creation of living beings, faintly involving the foundation of possibility evolution. Though the Dao of Hunger, an outsider, has outwardly occupied the Dao path, it has not yet fundamentally integrated." "Therefore, when devouring all things, such an anomalous extraction phenomenon occurs." The proof of Li Fan's conjecture lay within the Starving Immortal’s memories. The Starving Immortal had become a Heavenly Pillar, and its life experiences were open for Li Fan to browse. It was unlikely that the final truth would remain hidden for long. "Since the exotic beasts could flee from other possibilities, it's not surprising that there are other outsiders." "However, from the perspective of a later arrival, it’s quite comical." "These outsiders, much like those so-called transcended True Immortals who fled from the [Primordial] possibility, went through immense hardship believing they had found a safe haven. They never expected to meet their end there." "Or perhaps..." Li Fan narrowed his eyes, images of countless possibilities flashing within his sea of consciousness. With his current deductive abilities, even without knowing the specific names of those involved, he could, to some extent, infer past events based on their outcomes. "These outsiders who fled never intended for this place to be their final refuge. It was merely a temporary stopping point. Since they could escape once, they could escape a second, a third time..." "At the very least, they must have believed so. If the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation were to arrive again, they would simply flee once more." "To resist disaster, besides timing, the most important thing is unity. But if, among the masses, there are such born fugitives..." Li Fan, having served as a Grand Tutor for decades, naturally understood the harm caused by such troublemakers. If they merely passively fled, it would be one thing. What was most terrifying was their ability to invisibly infect, change, and destabilize the thoughts of those around them. Spreading like a plague, the consequences would be unimaginable. "This is not my speculation." "At that time, in the Immortal Realm, there were indeed such people." An image suddenly appeared in Li Fan's mind. "Sun Pianmiao." "And those who crafted the Immortal Realm’s chess pieces." "As well as Qing Yin and the True Immortal surnamed Ling, who presided over this Immortal Realm experiment field and then resolutely departed." "This is only the tip of the iceberg. One can imagine how many similar figures existed among the immortals of the Immortal Realm back then." "Working alongside such individuals, even Ten Thousand Heavenly King Tian Du, with all his grand ambitions, was destined for failure. If it were me, I would first use a fishing method to gather all these fugitives in one place. Then, I would eliminate them all!" "This would not only affirm loyalty but also yield a batch of consumables to resist Dao Annihilation..." Li Fan mused in this manner, a fierce glint flashing in his eyes. It wasn't that Li Fan genuinely harbored ambitions of being a savior Heavenly Emperor. It was merely a fleeting thought during his deduction of the past. The past is now but dust. The current [Primordial] possibility was merely a ruin struggling to hold on. All Li Fan could do, like those who fled, was to migrate to a new era.

Chapter 1485: Fishing for Xing Wuque

The Revelation of Wuji

Before reaching the Half-Immortal realm, Li Fan had utilized the Faceless Stone Statue multiple times to summon this dark energy, so he was quite familiar with it.

Now, having ascended to the Half-Immortal realm, he could easily capture the energy accumulated in the dark sea for countless years.

Li Fan was not the master of this dark energy. Therefore, during the capture process, it showed considerable resistance. However, Li Fan was no longer the same. With absolute power, all resistance from the dark energy was futile.

It all obediently gathered in Li Fan's palm.

Because it was born from the remains of a True Immortal, it possessed a quality similar to the "infinity" of immortal power. Converging in Li Fan's palm, it seemed to compress endlessly.

By the time the entire dark sea was absorbed by Li Fan, and darkness no longer lingered, Li Fan's palm held only a small, dark yet slightly shimmering, round bead.

When the long-accumulated darkness finally dispersed, Li Fan could finally see the remains of the True Immortal in this place.

Or rather, the remnants of the remains.

The True Immortal's body had been completely drained by the Spirit Gathering and Immortal Ascension formation, serving as nourishment. Only a few traces, thinner than shadows, remained.

If Li Fan had not used his True Immortal's aura to observe with meticulous detail from a superior vantage point, he might not have even noticed the last remaining trace left by this fallen True Immortal.

"Immortal departs~"

Li Fan gazed at the remnant's shadow for a long time. The trace was too fragile to leave any useful information.

He blew lightly, sending it to complete dissipation.

This was not out of sudden benevolence, wanting to help the deceased True Immortal transcend.

It was to use the act of clearing away this trace as an opportunity to observe whether any other True Immortal remnants remained in this dark sea.

The result was as expected.

Besides a few faint roars from the True Immortal's will to survive deep below, the vast dark sea, and even the entire Xuanhuang Realm and the countless starscapes within the experimental field, showed no other sympathetic fluctuations.

"It seems this True Immortal is truly dead."

The Spirit Gathering and Immortal Ascension formation within the dark sea was initially created to serve as the power source for the Xuanhuang Realm's escape from the Immortal Ruins.

Now, Li Fan could, with his own strength, forcibly pull the Xuanhuang Realm out of the Immortal Ruins' attraction.

The power he could display, even if partially borrowed from Shouqiu Gong's projection, was still far superior to the entire dark sea.

The process of suppression was smooth and without complications, and during the cleanup, Li Fan turned his attention to the last remaining participant.

The True Immortal's will to survive.

Resembling withered branches, or a hunched figure, it showed both fear and desire upon sensing Li Fan's presence.

Like a wild beast in the forest observing a hunter, it watched from the shadows, torn between fleeing and greed.

Li Fan, as if feeding a pet, divided a wisp of his energy and tossed it towards the True Immortal's will to survive.

After circling a few times, the True Immortal's will to survive, fearing the food would escape, enveloped and began to chew it.

Li Fan smiled faintly as he witnessed this.

"Indeed, it is merely a foolish entity, left with only its primal instinct for survival."

"The Mo Sha Immortal Soul, especially after integrating with the Great Daos of heaven and earth, is not something you can easily digest."

The True Immortal's will to survive tried to consume the food but found it impossible to diminish it in any way.

Moreover, the food in its "stomach" was beginning to devour it from within!

The True Immortal's will to survive let out horrifying roars, like an ancient ferocious beast.

However, no matter how it struggled, it could not contend with the power of the Mo Sha Immortal Soul.

Helplessly, it rolled and thrashed in the deepest part of the dark sea.

By the time the dust settled, the True Immortal's will to survive had been transformed into one of the myriad Dao manifestations of the Mo Sha Immortal Soul.

Li Fan had hoped to find some past memories within this remnant of True Immortal intent, but after a thorough search, he found only primal instincts related to consumption and resurrection.

"What a pity."

"I couldn't figure out the true identity of this True Immortal buried beneath the dark sea."

"However, he was likely just an ordinary True Immortal. It's insignificant now."

With the ability to suppress Nameless beings with a mere wave of his hand, the current Li Fan was qualified to say such things.

He surveyed the now empty dark sea, contemplating how to utilize the vast empty space.

Suddenly, he sensed the generation of some inexplicable energy.

"Hmm?"

Although the source of the energy had been entirely collected by him, where did this new energy originate?

Li Fan was slightly surprised but not panicked.

After a sweep of his divine sense, he discovered that these tiny energy points, like countless faint specks of light, were coming from various parts of the Xuanhuang Realm.

These specks of light were even more minuscule than the remnants of the True Immortal's remains.

If not for the sudden appearance in the completely drained dark sea, Li Fan would have instinctively ignored them.

Li Fan gathered the specks of light, and upon contact, they exploded like bubbles and vanished.

They also seemed to not exist within Li Fan's body, disappearing to an unknown destination.

After pondering for a while, Li Fan gathered all the specks of light into a ball of light for closer examination.

Upon reaching a certain level of magnitude, Li Fan felt a sense of uncanny familiarity.

"This is..."

"Spirituality?"

"No. It doesn't involve the level of '[Return to Truth]' yet, much lower."

"But it is still a convergence of cultivation talent to some extent."

Gathering the ball of light with the black orb formed from the dark sea, Li Fan seemed to understand what was happening.

"In the original design, all sentient beings in the Xuanhuang Realm were mere chess pieces on the board. From their creation, they were imbued with various attributes: height, appearance, talent, temperament."

"These light spheres represent the power of talent bestowed upon sentient beings through the natural operation of the Xuanhuang Realm. And now they are being drawn into the dark sea because the True Immortal's will to survive sensed their presence and instinctively desired to steal them..."

Li Fan frowned.

"Although the sentient beings of the Xuanhuang Realm are chess pieces, they are chess pieces of the higher echelons of the Immortal Realm. How could a mere will to survive..."

He looked up at the beings within the Xuanhuang Realm.

He wanted to emulate them, to plunder the talents of sentient beings.

But clearly, it was not possible.

"The True Immortal's will to survive has been eradicated by me, yet this extraction of talent still persists."

Li Fan suddenly remembered a topic he had discussed with Bai Hua and Qiao Gong in the past.

During the great tribulation of destruction, many cultivators had witnessed their homeland fall into the Immortal Ruins, everything disintegrating and forming a bizarre, distorted halo of light. As the cultivation world completely vanished into the Immortal Ruins, a large amount of matter seemed to erupt from the opposite direction. This substance could not be detected by the naked eye or divine sense, yet it truly existed.

The Celestial Mechanism Realm's former Immortal Puppet Ancestor had also suffered from the constant loss of something due to being close to the Immortal Ruins, eventually becoming corrupted. At that time, Qiao Gong had even used his "stupidity" as an excuse.

"The Hungry Immortal has been suppressed by me, and the Immortal Ruins no longer exist..."

Li Fan flickered his figure and arrived in the outer space of the Xuanhuang Realm.

He took out half of the light spheres.

Here, they did not exhibit a flowing trend but simply floated quietly in the void. They seemed unable to persist for long and quickly dimmed.

Before they completely dissipated, Li Fan collected them again.

Although this ball of light was small, if all of it were bestowed upon a single person, the cultivator shaped would likely have a talent no less than Zhang Haobo or Xiao Fan.

"It seems that the Xuanhuang Realm, having stayed near the Immortal Ruins for too long, has itself been shaped by this influence."

"The extraction of spirituality from its sentient beings, even after the Immortal Ruins are gone, this trend cannot be completely reversed immediately."

After conducting comparative experiments in multiple locations within the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, Li Fan initially reached a conclusion.

"It's not that some monstrous entity is causing trouble." He first breathed a sigh of relief.

However, naturally, Li Fan became curious about the reason behind this phenomenon.

His comprehension of the Hungry Immortal's Dao was arguably the highest in the [Primordial] possibility, second only to the Hungry Immortal herself.

He naturally knew that practicing the Hungry Immortal's Dao would generate a suction force that devoured everything.

He had not noticed anything that was not attracted by this suction force but actively repelled it.

To verify this, it was not difficult.

In the center of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, Li Fan unleashed the Hungry Immortal's Dao towards a nearby location.

Although not as powerful as the Immortal Ruins' resurgence, it still manifested like a colossal vortex.

The Utmost Darkness Star Sea was once again thrown into turmoil. Li Fan, unmoved amidst the waves, threw a group of You Clan people he had noticed earlier into the vortex. They were from the Xuanhuang Realm's original bloodline and had emerged after the dark sea had been drained.

The You Clan people, although physically robust and capable of fighting cultivators, were no match for the power of the Hungry Immortal's Dao.

Without uttering a sound, they all turned to dust within the magnificent vortex.

Li Fan observed them one by one, showing no emotional fluctuation.

Previously, he had not paid much attention to this spiritual essence, considering it normal to overlook it. However, upon closer observation this time, he indeed discovered this intangible substance.

Moreover, because the You Clan people were all descendants of the Xuanhuang Realm's first Heavenly Venerate, the amount of spiritual essence extracted from the vortex was not insignificant.

Li Fan, like a prospector, collected all the spiritual essence.

"Interesting. Why does the enlightenment of the Hungry Immortal's Dao produce such a phenomenon?"

"Perhaps it is related to the Great Dao of [Hunger] itself."

Li Fan recalled the scene when he suppressed the Hungry Immortal not long ago.

In front of Shouqiu Gong's projection, the Hungry Immortal, though outmatched, did not simply surrender. Instead, she fought back fiercely.

Although the Hungry Immortal's struggle was futile, Li Fan was intrigued by her chilling voice, like a ghost's whisper, "Hungry, I am so hungry..."

It seemed not to have come from the Hungry Immortal herself, but rather from a mysterious existence beyond the Great Dao.

As if wanting to devour mountains and drink seas, turning everything in the world into sustenance!

Li Fan suddenly looked towards the Hungry Immortal Heavenly Pillar again.

"This Great Dao of Hunger seems to have a problem."

"It's not originally from the [Primordial] possibility? But rather, it occupied the position after devouring something else?"

Li Fan was not 100% certain.

However, judging from the current signs, it was highly probable.

"Spiritual essence is closely related to the creation of sentient beings. It subtly involves the foundation of possibility evolution. The Great Dao of Hunger, this outsider, although it appears to have occupied the Dao path on the surface, has not fundamentally integrated with it."

"Therefore, when it devours all things, such phenomena of extraction occur."

The method to prove Li Fan's hypothesis lay within the Hungry Immortal's memories.

The Hungry Immortal had already transformed into a Heavenly Pillar, and her past life was open for Li Fan to browse. It wouldn't be long before the final mystery was unraveled.

"Since migratory beasts can escape from other possibilities, it's not surprising that there are other outsiders."

"But from the perspective of later generations, it's somewhat laughable."

"These escaping outsiders never intended for this place to be their final refuge. It was merely a temporary stop. Since they could escape once, they could escape a second, a third time..."

"At the very least, they must have thought so. If the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation were to return, they would simply escape again."

"To resist a calamity, besides favorable timing, unity is most crucial. But if there are such innate 'escapists' among the people..."

Li Fan, having served as a Grand Tutor for decades, understood the devastating consequences of such detrimental elements.

If they merely passively fled, it would be one thing. But the most terrifying aspect was their insidious influence, capable of infecting, changing, and deterring the thoughts of those around them.

Spreading like a plague, the consequences would be unimaginable.

"This is not my baseless speculation."

"At that time, there were indeed such individuals among the Immortals of the Immortal Realm."

A figure suddenly appeared before Li Fan's eyes.

"Sun Piaomiao."

"And those who forged the Immortal Realm Chess Pieces."

"As well as Qing Yin and the True Immortal surnamed Ling, who presided over this Immortal Realm experimental field and then resolutely departed."

"This is just the tip of the iceberg. One can imagine how many similar individuals existed among the Immortals of the Immortal Realm back then."

"Working alongside such people, even Emperor Tian Luo, with all his ambitions, was destined to fail. If it were me, I would first use the method of 'fishing' to gather all these escapees in one place. Then, I would eliminate them all!"

"This would serve to test the hearts of men, and also provide consumable materials to resist the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation..."

Li Fan mused, a fierce glint flashing in his eyes.

This was not to say that Li Fan truly harbored the ambition of being a world-saving Celestial Emperor. It was merely a momentary thought arising from his deduction of past events, imagining himself in their shoes.

All that was in the past has turned to nothing.

The current Primordial possibility was merely a broken remnant struggling to survive.

Li Fan could only do as those escapees had done: change his dwelling and move on.

Chapter 1486: The King of Heaven's Past Affairs

The King of Heavenly Kings' Past Affairs

The opportunity to reverse their predicament was right before him. After observing for a while, there seemed to be no anomalies around the Nameless Shadow. That Nameless True Immortal, who had just attained enlightenment, should have left.

He could no longer suppress the restless stirring in his heart and mobilized his remaining strength, charging towards that figure.

He had originally thought that from this point onwards, all would be well, but he never expected that...

Time rewound to the present. He looked at the two solitary Heavenly Pillars before him. After observing them repeatedly, he confirmed he was not mistaken. His heart trembled involuntarily.

“One of them should be the Southern Immortal Heavenly Pillar.”

“And the other one…”

“The one suppressed within is actually that Nameless True Immortal who just attained enlightenment not long ago! This!”

“Who in the world is it!”

Something isolated.

Recalling the words he had heard earlier, countless thoughts flashed through his mind in an instant.

Although his body was merely a Nameless Dao Shadow, freshly resurrected, he was still confident in his own strength. Being able to capture and suppress him so easily…

The other party’s strength was unfathomable!

“In the ten thousand years I was heavily injured and trapped, what happened in the outside world? Could it be that the Immortal Realm has been rebuilt?”

Even with a hundred or a thousand thoughts, all could only be deeply hidden in his heart at this moment.

A terrifying immense force, dense all around him, completely suppressed him. Even speaking or transmitting a message was a luxury.

Just as he was filled with anxiety, a majestic figure suddenly appeared in the field.

Being suppressed, he could not see the other party’s appearance clearly. However, the aura emanating from the other party, vast as mountains and seas, reminded him of the two Immortal Emperors he had seen before.

The figure spoke no nonsense and grabbed him again.

He only felt that his Nameless Dao Shadow body instantly became chaotic.

Although the Dao Shadow was constructed from the power fluctuations of that Nameless True Immortal who attained the Dao of ‘Hunger,’ it was merely borrowing its impact. In essence, it was still the power contained within the massive ‘Form of Living Beings’ he had personally crafted!

The impact of attaining the Nameless Realm was like a hammer striking down, forging an imprint.

However, at this moment, the Life Dao Principles condensed within this imprint were uncontrollably flowing towards the figure before him, then returning after a circuitous tour. While becoming calm again, it was as if it had been tidied and organized by someone, becoming even more ‘focused.’

He also sensed that numerous Life Dao Principles were fiercely surging towards him from the outside.
