“Barely adequate.” The figure in front shook his head, seemingly somewhat dissatisfied. But he still manipulated the myriad Life Dao Principles, constantly filling and stuffing.

“This is… trying to make me into a Heavenly Pillar?” He was, after all, knowledgeable and quickly discerned the other party’s intentions.

And the subsequent encounter seemed to verify his guess.

The vast Life Dao Principles gathered from nowhere continued to flow endlessly, and the pressure from the outside did not lessen for a moment, even gradually increasing.

He did not doubt that under such pressure, even a True Immortal would turn to dust in an instant.

Thinking of being eternally sealed within a Heavenly Pillar, never to transcend, the misery would likely surpass that of the past ten thousand years. His heart was filled with despair and fear.

A True Immortal is outside of all worldly matters. He should no longer have such mortal emotions. And he had once been Nameless, so he should have been even less susceptible. But when the great tribulation of the past arrived, the ‘Nameless True Immortal’ he once was had actually died.

What remained was merely an ordinary cultivator who only wanted to struggle for survival.

After thinking this through, he knew he could not continue like this.

Once the Heavenly Pillar was completely formed, even if he possessed heaven-defying divine abilities, it would likely be futile.

Gritting his teeth, he made a resolute decision. The mask on his face shattered with a boom.

The surrounding binding forces instantly vanished.

He hurriedly cried out, “Senior, please wait!”

“In the Azure Gloom Starfield, the Administrative Immortal Minister, Situ Xing, pays his respects!”

…

“Administrative Immortal Minister.”

Hearing Xing Wuque’s words, Li Fan’s suppressing power loosened.

However, he did not release him but quietly observed him carefully.

The sudden shattering of the bronze mask earlier had almost caught him off guard. He hadn’t expected that something seemingly within his grasp could suddenly erupt with such resistance.

Fortunately, he had urgently summoned Shouqiu Gong’s projection and continued to increase the pressure. Only then did he avoid revealing any flaws.

“What times are these, still using Tian Luo Emperor’s methods.”

“What, you administrative immortal minister, still intend to rule over me?”

After pondering for a moment, Li Fan ridiculed him with a mocking tone.

Since his understanding of the past Immortal Realm was not particularly clear yet, Li Fan decided to directly lead the other party into the trap he had fabricated, rather than getting too entangled in that aspect: “The Immortal Realm is now destroyed, and all the Immortals have either died or fled.”

“You, the former Immortal Minister, cannot rule over a mountain king like me. Hmph!”

These few sentences were enough to allow the other party to roughly guess his origins.

While he could use the identity of the ‘Hidden Emperor’ with those people from Suo Xing Sea, to pry information from this Administrative Immortal Minister, he had to adopt a different persona.

As expected, after hearing Li Fan’s words, Situ Xing began to speculate in the direction he was guided.

“Occupying a mountain as king. The Great Tribulation of Dao Annihilation descends, and even the lower realms cannot survive. Only isolated islands remain. This person suppressing a Nameless Immortal to become a Heavenly Pillar is to strengthen their ability to resist the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation…” Situ Xing’s thoughts raced, but his heart gradually cooled.

He had originally thought that his former title as Administrative Immortal Minister would at least make the other party hesitant. But now…

“Don’t call me ‘Senior’.”

“In my cultivation so far, I’ve only cultivated for about six thousand years at most, and I’ve never been to any Immortal Realm. Heh heh, speaking of which, you, the Administrative Immortal Minister, have lived for quite some time, haven’t you? I should be the one calling you ‘Senior’!”

Li Fan sneered and suddenly increased the suppressing force.

“Just stay here in this pillar and serve as my gatekeeper!”

“Six thousand years to reach such strength? How is that possible?”

“But it does seem somewhat unusual. That person is indeed not a True Immortal. Could it be that in the years I was trapped, a new cultivation system has developed in the world?”

Situ Xing heard this and instinctively felt shocked and disbelieving.

But he felt the sealing force around him, which had been static, tightening again. He had no time to think carefully.

In his panic, he frantically searched his mind for possible ways to escape.

“Not from the Immortal Realm, so all my past experiences are useless to him…”

The surroundings began to blur.

That fierce and brutal figure was gradually obscured by the gathered Life Dao Principles.

Situ Xing knew that this was a sign that the Heavenly Pillar was about to be completely sealed.

“A person from the lower realm…”

In this moment of extreme danger, a figure suddenly flashed in Situ Xing’s mind. After hesitating for a moment, he decided to try anything as a last resort. Using his remaining strength, he shouted, “Senior, please wait! I am also one of the Twelve Heavenly Kings of the Profound Heaven Sect in the past, Xing Wuque!”

It was a desperate long shot, and he did not believe the title of ‘Twelve Heavenly Kings’ would be of any use at all. But what Situ Xing didn’t expect was that upon hearing his words, the restraining force actually lessened slightly!

“Xing Wuque, one of the Twelve Heavenly Kings?”

“Those twelve people around Xuanyuan Hong?” Li Fan asked suspiciously, scrutinizing him.

The words ‘Xuanyuan Hong’ seemed to have evoked some ancient memories in Situ Xing, causing him to momentarily daze.

But at this moment of life and death, he could not afford to think further and hurriedly said, “Exactly, exactly.”

“Back then, what Xuanyuan Hong liked, was it Luo Yichen, or Ji Yuzhen, or perhaps Granny Nie?” Li Fan suddenly asked with an inscrutable tone and playful expression.

Situ Xing, or rather Xing Wuque, was stunned on the spot.

“Hmm?”

“…Uh, none of them! Although they all had feelings for him, according to my observation, Xuanyuan Hong had long harbored feelings for someone else. So he always kept his distance from them,” the other party seemed about to suppress him again in the Heavenly Pillar at any moment. Situ Xing’s heart leaped, and he hastily replied.

“Hahaha, you observed quite carefully. Xuanyuan Hong indeed had a childhood sweetheart, and she was also an extraordinary person…” Li Fan spoke halfway, leaving endless room for speculation for Situ Xing. Then he slightly loosened his grip on Situ Xing.

The towering mountain hanging overhead was temporarily moved away. Situ Xing couldn't help but breathe a sigh of relief.

He tried to probe for more information: “Senior, do you know Xuanyuan Hong?”

“Indeed. Back then, he saved my life during the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. However, later, he disappeared without a trace. I had always wanted to find an opportunity to repay him, but I never saw him again,” Li Fan replied.

“This truly sounds like something Xuanyuan Hong would do.” Situ Xing nodded secretly in his heart.

“By the way, you were someone close to Xuanyuan Hong, how did you end up like this?”

Hearing the other party’s question, Situ Xing gave a wry smile: “This matter… is hard to explain in a few words.”

“Then tell me slowly. I haven’t had a good chat with anyone in a long time. With the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation descending, living beings are scarce. There isn’t even a fellow cultivator to communicate with!” Li Fan said in a deep voice, patting Situ Xing on the shoulder and completely removing the suppressing force.

Although temporarily freed, Situ Xing couldn’t help but cast a glance at the two Heavenly Pillars beside him without daring to act rashly.

He sized up Li Fan, weaving words in his mind to explain everything.

“Judging from the meaning of the other party’s words, Xuanyuan Hong now seems to have attained an extremely high cultivation level. At the very least, he is definitely not below this person. But this is also as it should be.”

After a long while, Situ Xing finally spoke: “To let Senior know, I was not speaking in vain just now. My true self is indeed the Administrative Immortal Minister of the Azure Gloom Starfield, Situ Xing. To suppress a star domain of the Immortal Realm at the Nameless realm. However…”

Li Fan waved his hand, interrupting his words: “I know this. You people went down to the lower realm, searching for opportunities for some supreme treasure, didn’t you? This is unimportant, get to the point!”

Situ Xing was astonished, he opened his mouth, but his mind suddenly went blank.

“What? You allow yourselves to go to the lower realm, can’t Xuanyuan Hong do the same? Facing the great tribulation, everyone uses their own abilities! Don’t you think someone that could make all of you follow him willingly and be utterly devoted couldn’t be ordinary?” Li Fan scoffed with a smile.

Situ Xing’s expression changed several times.

“Indeed. Indeed.” He suddenly seemed lost in thought, muttering repeatedly.

“Back then, most of us had our spiritual senses obscured. However, during the tens of thousands of years I was trapped in the ‘Form of Living Beings,’ as I gradually regained my true consciousness, I vaguely guessed Xuanyuan Hong’s abnormality.”

“But he acted too much like a mortal…”

“How could a mere mortal make all of us True Immortals who descended to the lower realm willingly follow him back then?” Situ Xing’s words were filled with confusion.

“Right. That’s what I thought too.”

“I even pressed him back then, and he stubbornly refused to admit it,” Li Fan said with a smile.

“Uh… is that your guess too?” Situ Xing was surprised and looked up sharply at Li Fan.

“What? My guess is wrong?” Li Fan’s eyes turned cold, and after a brief stare, Situ Xing was startled by the chilling indifference in his eyes and quickly looked away.

“Makes sense. Very sensible.”

“Because that supreme treasure must have sentience. Waiting with a purpose is very likely to be in vain. Therefore, we all chose to seal our spiritual senses and rely purely on personal luck. As the saying goes, survival of the fittest. This also avoids disputes from the Immortal Realm above.” Situ Xing continued.

“Those who can become True Immortals all possess extraordinary talent and disposition. Even if they walked the mortal world again, they would undoubtedly be outstanding individuals. However, it seems that all of our luck was not enough. Firstly, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation came too quickly. The speed at which the Immortal Realm collapsed was completely beyond our imagination. As a result, before we could return to the Immortal Realm…”

“We were in different locations in the upper realm. When the ascension channel of the Xuanhuang Realm was destroyed, some were still safe. Some had their true bodies suffer great calamity. Some had their true consciousness begin to awaken, but we all maintained a tacit and delicate balance among ourselves.”

“It was all because of Xuanyuan Hong’s uniqueness,” Situ Xing said slowly.

“You suspect that the supreme treasure fell into Xuanyuan Hong’s hands?” Li Fan suddenly interjected with a smile.

Situ Xing was silent for a moment, then nodded slightly.

“Otherwise, it is truly difficult to explain his rapid rise, and how he overshadowed all his peers in the lower realm.”

“After all, Xuanyuan Hong’s aptitude was really not that high, yet he always took that one step ahead of everyone else,” Situ Xing said with a hint of confusion in his tone.

“But before confirming it, no one could act directly. Moreover, Xuanyuan Hong’s true identity was unknown, so we could only wait patiently for the opportunity. Unexpectedly…”

“One day, he suddenly disappeared and never reappeared again,” Li Fan finished for Situ Xing.

Situ Xing nodded continuously.

“He disappeared too quickly, too suddenly. And at the last moment, he even warned us…”

“It’s really hard to tell whether he used it as an opportunity to escape, or if he truly met with misfortune.”

“There were disagreements among us after that. Some chose to follow his tracks and continue to pursue. Others felt their luck was insufficient and gave up…”

Li Fan shook his head slightly: “No wonder the Profound Heaven Sect, which was so grand back then, vanished instantly after the Profound Heaven King disappeared.”

Chapter 1487: Ascension to the Immortal Realm Again

Re-Ascension of the Immortal Realm

Situ Xing gave a wry smile: “A mountain cannot tolerate two tigers. It is already incredible for so many Nameless beings to gather in one realm. For us to have been around Xuanyuan Hong for tens of thousands of years, calling each other brothers, and still maintaining stable relationships, is even more unbelievable…”

“Especially Luo Yichen and Ji Yuzhen, those two women. They were already mortal enemies in the upper realm.”

Seeing Li Fan’s interested expression, Situ Xing continued: “Luo Yichen was known as the ‘Clear Stream Divine Mother’ in the Immortal Realm. Her style of conduct, just like when she encountered Xuanyuan Hong in the Xuanhuang Realm before, was to keep many male consorts, regardless of gender. Vast star domains were all her subjects.”

“As for Ji Yuzhen, her name in the upper realm was also Ji Yuzhen. It is said that Ji Yuzhen was originally a native of the Clear Stream Starfield, influenced by the unique culture of service there since childhood, and was deeply devoted. However, by chance, she one day managed to leave the Clear Stream Starfield and arrived in a starfield governed by a normal Immortal Minister. The huge contrast twisted her mentality, and she turned from reverence to hatred…”

Situ Xing paused, hesitated for a moment, then added: “My true self’s memories from the upper realm are somewhat incomplete. Hearing all this, it may not be entirely true. However, the fact that those two had an untold entanglement is absolutely true. At that time, we were all wondering why these two seemed to have an ancient enmity.”

“Later, Ji Yuzhen awakened her true self first and directly attacked, intending to kill Luo Yichen. Fortunately, Xuanyuan Hong intervened in time and stopped her.”

“I still remember Ji Yuzhen’s eyes at that time. Hehe…” Situ Xing clicked his tongue.

“I must say, Xuanyuan Hong truly had some skills. Not only could he maintain balance between the two women when he was around, but even after he disappeared, Ji Yuzhen and Luo Yichen actually coexisted peacefully for a while. It was only when they had different opinions on how to deal with Xuanyuan Hong that their relationship gradually deteriorated.”

“Luo Yichen believed that she and that treasure were ultimately fated to be apart, and the Clear Stream Starfield, though not yet affected by Dao Annihilation, was already on the brink of peril. Therefore, she chose to return to the Immortal Realm and escape.”

“As for Ji Yuzhen, she chose to follow the clues left by Xuanyuan Hong. She firmly believed that Xuanyuan Hong would not abandon her like this.”

Situ Xing gave a wry smile: “Ji Yuzhen’s stubborn nature was quite famous in the upper realm.”

Li Fan thought of the billions of Ji Yuzhen souls wandering in the ring mountains of the Eastern Eternal Continent. He raised his eyebrows slightly: “Didn’t Ji Yuzhen die?”

As he spoke, he waved his hand, displaying the current scene of the Eastern Eternal Continent in the Xuanhuang Realm to Situ Xing.

Upon hearing this, Situ Xing was initially shocked. However, after observing for a while, he shook his head slightly: “The cultivation method Ji Yuzhen practiced ensured she wouldn’t perish so easily. These billions of soul fragments, including the primal soul hidden in the center, are almost all related to Xuanyuan Hong’s memories. She likely discarded them intentionally.”

“That Eastern Eternal Continent is precisely the place where Xuanyuan Hong returned after ascending and met her. She probably intended to sever all her infatuation with Xuanyuan Hong.”

As expected of a former Nameless True Immortal, Li Fan, through the indirectly displayed images, could discern the truth of those billions of soul fragments.

“No wonder, in the memories of these soul fragments, there is no scene without Xuanyuan Hong.”

Li Fan’s judgment of Situ Xing had become somewhat convinced.

“Back then, how many of you Twelve Heavenly Kings truly died? And how many intentionally disappeared?”

Situ Xing felt that the senior before him seemed excessively interested in the matters of the Profound Heaven Sect in the past.

“Could it be that he later encountered one of us Twelve?”

Thinking this, but constrained by the deterrence of the two Heavenly Pillars beside him, Situ Xing still answered honestly: “Uh, Sikong Lin is probably truly dead. Affected by the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation in the Immortal Realm, his true body was annihilated, and his clone suffered severe injuries. It’s unlikely he can recover. Zhou Yangli and Cui Zhiyuan's true bodies were definitely affected, but it’s uncertain if they escaped.”

“As for the others…”

“It’s not something I can speculate on.”

Li Fan pointed in the direction of the underground dark river in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea: “What about you? How did you end up in this state?”

Situ Xing heard this and felt somewhat embarrassed: “My true self’s consciousness awakened the latest. Until Xuanyuan Hong disappeared, I had not regained my original consciousness. At that time, I couldn’t understand some of the events happening among us. I continued to follow Xuanyuan Hong’s orders, carving the ‘Form of Living Beings’ beneath the star sea. And I rarely communicated with others. Even if they awakened their true consciousness, they weren't sure of my true identity. They weren’t even sure if I was a True Immortal from the lower realm…”

“I hadn't been working in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea for long before my true self tragically perished, and I was also affected. Being able to barely preserve my divine sense from dissipating was already fortunate,” Situ Xing sighed.

“So, your clone is quite loyal.” Li Fan observed and said.

“Well, it’s not entirely as Senior thinks. In fact, I was willing to stay in the underground Life Dark River because I sensed the benefits of carving the ‘Form of Living Beings’.” Situ Xing smiled and did not hide anything.

“Benefits?”

“After the Immortal Realm was destroyed, the infinite nature of our True Immortal immortal power was affected to varying degrees. Some with good luck might still possess infinite immortal power. But some lost their connection to the Infinite Sea. And I belong to the latter category.”

Situ Xing sighed and continued: “And by carving the ‘Form of Living Beings’ and shaping this star sea, and helping it recover, I could use the lower realm’s star sea as a temporary channel to reconnect with the Infinite Sea. At that time, even though the Immortal Realm was destroyed, I would still be a True Immortal. Even if my true self met misfortune, I would not be greatly affected.”

“It’s just a pity that things didn’t go as planned.”

“The Infinite Sea is the main culprit that attracted the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. Even after the Immortal Realm was destroyed, you are still obsessed with it!” Li Fan interrupted Situ Xing’s words, his expression gradually turning cold.

Situ Xing was somewhat stunned, finally seeming to understand why Li Fan lacked immortal power.

He pondered, then carefully explained: “It wasn’t the Infinite Sea that caused the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, but rather the failure to withstand the Infinite Sea that led to the occurrence of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. We True Immortals connect to the Infinite Sea through the power of ‘Lian Shan.’ As the saying goes, mountains and seas are connected.”

“And whether we use infinite immortal power or not, it will not affect the trend of the great tide of Dao Annihilation.”

“I suspect that the destruction of the Immortal Realm and the‘Tian Luo Immortal Emperor’s’ headstrong actions are absolutely responsible for the majority of it.”

Situ Xing’s words were within Li Fan’s blind spot.

Since he could not verify the truthfulness of it, he did not directly refute. Instead, he retorted: “I have also heard that the ‘Heavenly Emperor Tian Luo’ before the destruction of the Immortal Realm seemed to have taken some extreme actions. What exactly was he trying to do?”

Mentioning the Heavenly Emperor Tian Luo, Situ Xing’s expression became somewhat strange, very much like when he recalled Xuanyuan Hong.

“The Heavenly Emperor Tian Luo wanted to completely resolve the threat of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. And the method…”

“Was the plan for the entire Immortal Realm to ascend again. If successful, they would transcend above mountains and seas. No matter how the tides rose and fell, they could no longer affect us.”

“Hmm?” Li Fan’s expression also became subtle.

“Either that Heavenly Emperor Tian Luo was an absolute madman, or he must have had some reliance. I heard that back then, Emperor Tian Luo was not lacking in followers…” He stared at Situ Xing, wanting to get the answer from his mouth.

“Theoretically, Emperor Tian Luo’s plan did have a certain feasibility. Otherwise, I wouldn’t have chosen to follow him back then. It’s just that, in terms of results, he ultimately failed.”

“But the specific reason for its feasibility involves the Immortal Realm’s ascension plan, which is top secret. I did not receive synchronized information. And that secret, perhaps, was completely buried along with the destruction of the Immortal Realm,” Situ Xing’s eyes flashed with a hint of regret.

The Heavenly Pillar space fell into a strange silence for a moment.

“Immortal Realm’s Ascension…”

Li Fan savored these four words in his heart.

It was indeed too crazy.

No wonder Qing Yin and the True Immortal surnamed Ling, who were stationed in the experimental field space, thought Emperor Tian Luo was insane after learning of this plan, and ultimately decided to flee far away.

The power of Immortals came from mountains and seas, and Emperor Tian Luo actually wanted to transcend mountains and seas with the power of an entire realm.

Even if he had some reliance, it seemed too fanciful.

But to be able to occupy the position of the ruling Immortal Emperor of the Immortal Realm, Tian Luo was definitely not an ordinary person. He must have weighed his options when making this decision. At the very least, in his view, there was a high probability of success.

“Even ‘Returning to Truth’ might not be able to transcend mountains and seas. Back then, the Immortal Realm was still trembling under the ravages of the Dao Annihilation tide, yet Emperor Tian Luo, what basis did he have?” Li Fan’s heart was filled with infinite curiosity.

However, this question was destined to have no answer in the short term.

“You said that the Infinite Immortal power was not the culprit that attracted the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. Then, do you think all the Immortals are blameless for the occurrence of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation?” After pondering for a while, Li Fan redirected the conversation.

Li Fan’s stance was already very clear.

He glanced at the Heavenly Pillar beside him again. Situ Xing hesitated several times, unable to answer this question.

After a long while, he finally said hesitantly: “Not just me. Most True Immortals probably think so. And the fact is also the same. Whether we use infinite immortal power or not, the Infinite Sea is always there.”

“And the fusion of mountains and seas is the general trend. If we were to say who was truly at fault…”

“Perhaps, from the very beginning, the birth of Immortals was a mistake.”

“Since the birth of Immortals with the power of ‘Lian Shan,’ the approach of the Infinite Sea was inevitable.”

Situ Xing also had some principles.

Facing Li Fan’s menacing gaze, he did not change his statement. He said frankly.

“Does the birth of Immortals, and the fusion of mountains and seas, have nothing to do with you Nameless True Immortals who attained enlightenment and departed?” Li Fan suddenly asked sternly.

He waved his hand, and five Shouqiu Gong projections appeared around them, presenting themselves before Situ Xing.

“Not to mention becoming a pillar yourself. Even Shouqiu Gong, who left behind a Dao-carrying projection, couldn’t do that, could he?”

The name ‘Shouqiu Gong’ was indeed extraordinary.

Looking at the projections that suddenly appeared around him, Situ Xing trembled uncontrollably.

After calming down, he bowed to the projections.

Then he pondered again and said: “This question was already discussed in the Immortal Realm back then.”

“The general trend of mountain and sea fusion cannot be reversed by the persistence of one or two Dao paths. In fact, whether there are more or fewer Dao paths supporting it, from a macroscopic temporal perspective, it does not have much impact. Just like the sanctuary you built here with two Heavenly Pillars, though seemingly safe for now…”

“Ultimately, destruction is inevitable.”

“Perhaps it can be delayed for some time, but ultimately it is futile.”

“We cannot completely deny the path of True Immortal advancement just because of this. Moreover, for us who attained the Nameless realm, a minor transcendence, or even true transcendence, leaping above mountains and seas, might allow us to truly find a way to stop the fusion of mountains and seas.”

Situ Xing spoke righteously, his words becoming faster and faster.

His eyes were firm, as if this was what he truly believed in.

“Hmph. Placing hope on the illusory future.”

“The Immortal Realm has now been destroyed, and countless Nameless True Immortals have perished. Have you found a method to save the world?” Li Fan retorted.

This question left Situ Xing with only silence.

After a long while, he finally said: “Perhaps, on the other side of the Infinite Sea, there is a world that has found the solution.”

“Transcendent True Immortals continuously stream in from worlds of all origins, gathering in that magnificent world. With their combined efforts, they should be able to find a method to save the world. This was the tacit understanding of countless Nameless True Immortals at that time.”

“Dwelling on one world, the final outcome, Emperor Tian Luo has already provided a demonstration.”

“Senior, you have not walked the path of becoming an Immortal, so you naturally don’t understand this aspect.” Situ Xing spoke eloquently, but could not shake Li Fan’s heart at all.

No, that was not the case.

Because the cold countdown timer of ‘Returning to Truth’ was steadily decreasing, telling the ultimate fate of the mortal world.

“Perhaps he is right.”

“The fusion of mountains and seas is the true general trend of the mortal world.”

“In front of mountains and seas, the impact of one possibility is insignificant. Let alone Nameless True Immortals who only attained one Dao.”

“No matter what they do, whether they leave behind methods to carry the Dao. At most, it will only delay the arrival of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation for a short time.”

“It cannot change the final outcome of destruction.”

Li Fan suddenly thought of Xie Subai, Hei Tianyi, and Shouqiu Gong, who had clearly possessed the ability to easily resist the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation yet had left leisurely.

“A tacit understanding among Nameless True Immortals…”

“Are they just pursuing their own power, or do they still have this so-called tacit understanding in their hearts?”

“Does that grand gathering of Transcendent beings on the ‘Other Shore’ truly exist?”

Countless thoughts flashed through Li Fan’s mind.

However, no matter what he thought now, he could not show any sign of being convinced by Situ Xing’s words on the surface.

“The lives that all living beings in the world should have had, have disappeared prematurely because of your excuses.”

“How should this debt be settled?”

“Should they all die?”

Li Fan waved his hand, and scenes of countless beings howling in the doomsday instantly appeared before Situ Xing.

Chapter 1488: When Proving the Dao is Nameless

The Moment of Attaining the Nameless Realm

Not only were the scenes Li Fan had personally experienced during his reincarnations, but also those he had glimpsed from Xie Subai, ‘Returning to Truth,’ and the Infinite Sea.

Countless tragic and horrifying scenes of the apocalypse, a billion times more terrifying than hell, replayed before Situ Xing’s eyes.

Even though he had once been a Nameless True Immortal, after witnessing scenes a billion times more terrifying than hell, his expression still changed slightly.

Situ Xing did not evade, taking in all these scenes with his eyes. After a period of silence, he finally spoke with some difficulty.

He had not changed his initial belief: “All living beings perish in the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation; this is the destiny of living beings under the unchanging general trend. As the saying goes, born with the Dao, perish with the Dao. No one in this world is inherently responsible for the lives and deaths of others. Moreover, in the eyes of us True Immortals, these…”

“Most of them are not even considered ‘living beings.’”

Situ Xing’s initial voice was somewhat weak, but as he continued, it became firmer.

Li Fan scoffed: “You’ve spouted all this righteous talk, but it boils down to ‘the weak have no right to survive.’ Today, you are the fish, and I am the blade. You are sealed to become a Heavenly Pillar, what excuses do you have?”

Situ Xing opened his mouth but did not utter any self-contradictory remarks: “The strong prey on the weak; I have nothing to say. Being sealed into a Heavenly Pillar is due to my inferiority in skill, it is my own tribulation.”

“However, I advise Senior that using two or three Heavenly Pillars can only ensure temporary safety in one place. If you truly seek a method to save the world, you need to go to the ‘Grand World of the Other Shore.’ With Senior’s strength, you should have no problem…”

Situ Xing still wanted to speak, but suddenly felt the surrounding Great Daos tightening powerfully again.

This time, Li Fan gave him no more chances to quibble.

The Great Dao merged with his body, his vision, his thoughts, all frozen and sealed.

Besides the Primordial Bone and the Hungry Immortal, another Heavenly Pillar appeared in this space.

But after all, its foundation was merely a Nameless Immortal’s shadow. Compared to the other two, this third Heavenly Pillar was clearly ‘thinner.’

Moreover, since it was not formed by true Great Dao, this ‘Heavenly Pillar’ could not help bear too much pressure from the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

And Li Fan still intended to seal Situ Xing.

It was not that he feared this ancient Heavenly King or Nameless being from the lower realm. The main purpose was still to slowly extract memories from their minds while suppressing them, just as he did with the Hungry Immortal.

In Li Fan’s opinion, Situ Xing’s value was even greater than the Hungry Immortal’s. The Hungry Immortal’s life in the Immortal Realm, for the first half, was merely the identity of an ‘immortal servant’ of ‘Non-Action.’

But Situ Xing was the Administrative Immortal Minister of the Azure Gloom Starfield. From the snippets he revealed earlier, he must have known countless secrets of the Immortal Realm.

“Immortal Minister, judging by the name, he should be a ruler of an Immortal Domain. At the Nameless realm, he indeed has the qualification to lead a star domain. Although Situ Xing himself said that due to the impact of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, his true self’s memories were incomplete…”

“But the truth of the matter is something I must see for myself.”

If the Hungry Immortal’s inner world was just a loose ball of light, then Situ Xing’s consciousness was like a brilliant pearl. Countless thoughts and memories were compressed into the smallest point, making it incredibly solid. For an outsider to pry, they would first need to crack open a fissure in this hard, unified entity.

Li Fan, worthy of being a master manipulator, observed for a while and discovered a flaw in Situ Xing’s heart.

He couldn't help but let out a cold laugh: “He spoke so grandly. His true self perished in the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, but it still brought him immense psychological trauma. As long as we approach from this angle…”

Li Fan formed hand seals with his hands.

The clone, Li Biren, cooperated simultaneously.

In the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, the Shouqiu projection, the Primordial, and the Hungry Immortal, who were serving as Dao Annihilation pillars, began to retract their powers.

As if intending to shift all the pressure entirely onto Situ Xing alone, who had just arrived.

When the great edifice is about to collapse, it cannot be supported by a single beam. Let alone the world-ending Tribulation of Dao Annihilation?

A sound, like a vast surging tide rolling in from beyond the heavens, could be faintly heard. In the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, which had just received relatively complete Dao nourishment from the outer star domain, wisps of black Qi of Dao Annihilation suddenly emerged.

Gloomy and terrifying, like ghosts.

The revived Great Dao was thrown into turmoil again.

The beings within the star sea all inexplicably felt a sense of impending doom. Although most were slumbering peacefully in the Xuanhuang Realm’s ‘Land of Utmost Bliss,’ they still furrowed their brows instinctively, their expressions uneasy.

The world was already in such a state, let alone Situ Xing, who was ‘holding up’ the world from ‘above.’

Precisely because he had truly experienced the horror of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, when facing it again, this formerly eloquent Nameless from the lower realm had his mental defenses broken within moments.

Facing imminent disaster, he was no longer as calm as he had appeared.

Crying out in terror, he let out a primal scream.

There was no difference between him and the beings in the apocalypse Li Fan had shown in the illusion.

“Nameless True Immortal. It’s nothing more.”

Li Fan looked at Situ Xing, who was like a clown, and couldn’t help but mock him.

Situ Xing alone, forming a Heavenly Pillar, could not hold on for too long. Li Fan did not want Dao Annihilation to truly descend.

Seizing the opportunity of his broken defenses, Li Fan sent a wisp of his divine sense along the crack in his mental defenses, entering within.

Although it was not comparable to the thoughts of ‘Returning to Truth,’ the overwhelming past that rushed forward all at once instantly plunged Li Fan into a stormy sea.

But fortunately, having survived greater storms before, Li Fan adapted for a while and could barely move freely.

“It seems Situ Xing did not lie.”

“This sea of thoughts is indeed incomplete.”

Li Fan looked around, finding that Situ Xing’s thoughts were not presented continuously like a normal person’s. Instead, at intervals, there were patches of pitch-black emptiness stretching across.

From these hollows, Li Fan sensed the aura of Dao Annihilation.

And at this moment, these hollows within his thoughts were resonating with the true Dao Annihilation outside, slowly expanding outwards.

It was imaginable that one day, they would completely swallow Situ Xing’s mind.

“Even if the clone escaped the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, the mind is still being eroded by it. Not only is it a physical blow, but also a mental one.”

Li Fan cautiously avoided these Dao Annihilation hollows, first looking at the memory closest to him and most conspicuous.

It was the most glorious moment of Situ Xing’s life.

Even though his true self had perished, his clone still held it firmly in his heart.

It was precisely the moment Situ Xing attained the Nameless realm!

Unlike the solitary scene Li Fan had witnessed when the Hungry Immortal attained enlightenment, in Situ Xing’s memory, countless True Immortal figures stood around, observing and congratulating him.

And in the distant sky, numerous Immortals were escorting a tall figure.

“Congratulations to Situ!”

Amidst the congratulations of the crowd, Situ Xing bowed deeply towards the tall figure in the distance.

“Given the Azure Gloom Starfield.”

“Bestowed with an Innate Spiritual Treasure.”

“Bestowed with tens of thousands of immortal servants.”

…

Voices echoed.

Under the gaze of the crowd, Situ Xing’s emotions surged, his heart filled with excitement.

Chapter 1489: The Grand Supreme's Taoist Scripture

The Heavenly King's Past Affairs

The Dao that Situ Xing attained was ‘Carving.’

Using himself as a blade, he could carve anything tangible or intangible in heaven and earth.

Initially, he was inspired by the carving method of that ‘Immortal Who铭s the Dao with Supreme Virtue,’ and combined with Situ Xing’s greatest skill, he thus created this unique Dao technique in the world.

The reason for Situ Xing’s grand ceremony of attaining the Dao was that his carving and creation could serve as a lower-tier substitute for Dao铭ing.

The Four Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm were lofty and revered.

They never opened the path of Immortality or unblocked the Infinite Spring. Although they benefited all Immortals and made great contributions for eternity, for the vast majority of True Immortals in the Immortal Realm, they had never experienced the ancient era when ‘there were no Immortals in the world.’ Whether it was the existence of the Immortal Path or the infinite nature of immortal power, it was all taken for granted.

The Four Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm were merely symbols like gods in their minds.

But the Immortal Who铭ed the Dao was the one most admired by the True Immortals of the Immortal Realm. Why? Because the Immortal Who铭ed the Dao possessed peerless talent, comprehended all three thousand Great Daos, and then inscribed and transformed the formless Great Daos he had observed and comprehended, bestowing them upon the world.

A sprawling article, the ‘Supreme Dao Book,’ detailed the ultimate principles of heaven and earth.

It was said that almost half of the Nameless True Immortals in the Immortal Realm were born after observing the ‘Supreme Dao Book.’

Unfortunately, the Supreme Dao Book, which originally floated in the ‘Boundless Star Domain’ for all Immortals to observe, unfortunately encountered the first large-scale Tribulation of Dao Annihilation that erupted in the Immortal Realm.

It was said that at the moment the Dao Annihilation tide descended, every character of the Supreme Dao Book burst forth with infinite light, transforming into a heavenly band of light that temporarily resisted the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

It bought a brief moment of escape time for the True Immortals observing and comprehending below.

But ultimately, it was just a Dao Book and could not withstand this terrifying tribulation. In the end, it was swallowed by Dao Annihilation along with the entire star domain.

Only a few Dao symbols survived.

Situ Xing was fortunate enough to be born before the disappearance of the ‘Supreme Dao Book’ and, through observation, precisely determined his Dao path.

That was to become the second Immortal Who铭ed the Dao!

It should be noted that although the Supreme Dao Book spanned the Boundless Star Domain and was accessible to all Immortals, the Immortal Realm stood tall above the ‘Upper Mountain,’ boundless and limitless.

The ‘Boundless’ domain alone was beyond the reach of immortal power. There were very few who had the ability, determination, and luck to truly reach the Boundless Star Domain to view the Dao Book.

The Supreme Dao Book was like a sculpture built against a mountain, immovable.

But if someone could engrave and transfer the Dao Book, making it so that True Immortals in the world need not travel far to see its true appearance, that would also be a great merit!

Situ Xing resolved to do just that.

Although the Dao Book’s guidance was gone, the path to becoming the second Immortal Who铭ed the Dao was fraught with peril. But Situ Xing's talent and luck were both extraordinary. After much struggle and spending half a lifetime, he finally achieved the Nameless realm as he wished.

Having attained the Dao of ‘Carving,’ it meant that there was a successor to the Immortal Who铭ed the Dao, and the Immortal Realm was naturally greatly shaken.

Numerous Nameless beings came to visit; it was the most glorious period of Situ Xing’s life.

Unfortunately…

The act of Dao铭ing was far more complicated than he had imagined.

Initially, he could still carve various Dao paths into tangible forms based on his past memories of observing the ‘Supreme Dao Book.’

But as time went by, Situ Xing gradually discovered that his success rate in Dao铭ing was getting lower and lower. Because after attaining the Nameless realm, his body and the Dao of Carving merged, naturally distancing him from other Daos.

To try carving again…

Attempt, failure, attempt again, fail again.

Only after finally giving up did Situ Xing truly recognize the power of the Immortal Who铭ed the Dao in the face of this cruel reality.

The act of Dao铭ing was beyond the capabilities of ordinary people.

Unfortunately, after leaving behind a ‘Supreme Dao Book,’ the Immortal Who铭ed the Dao disappeared without a trace, leaving Situ Xing unable to ask for guidance on how to harmonize various Daos, turning it into an impossibility.

Situ Xing was not the type to be defeated by setbacks.

Although he could not directly carve Dao paths, he could still engrave his insights and the insights of the Immortals, which could still benefit the world. In a sense, Situ Xing’s ambition to become the second Immortal Who铭ed the Dao had been realized.

…

“‘Upper Mountain’?”

“‘Supreme Dao Book’?”

Li Fan emerged from Situ Xing’s glorious remnant memory.

Even though it was a remnant, the memories were incredibly real. Especially with the assistance of the Supreme Dao Book in the memory, Li Fan’s divine sense was absolutely immersed, almost losing himself.

Thankfully, due to the imminent Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, Situ Xing’s thoughts churned, allowing Li Fan to regain his senses in time.

He recalled the power of the Shouqiu projection and the other Heavenly Pillars, and the combined support slowly transformed the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation into an intangible form.

But Li Fan keenly sensed that compared to before, the pressure on each Heavenly Pillar seemed to have increased slightly.

“It seems that this method of scaring them with the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation cannot be used too often. Every time it is used, it creates a loophole and brings the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation closer.”

However, this was not within Li Fan’s considerations. At least in this lifetime, before he truly ‘Returned to Truth,’ he could repeat this four or five times, which should be enough.

Moreover, after experiencing the ‘Dao Annihilation scare’ once, Situ Xing’s sea of thoughts had been breached. It was no longer as condensed and flawless as before. Li Fan could take some effort to examine it himself, just as he had spied on the Hungry Immortal.

From the memories of Situ Xing, a Nameless True Immortal who had attained enlightenment long ago, Li Fan indeed gained much valuable information.

“‘Man ascends the mountain to become an Immortal.’”

“Sage Lord Lian Shan was the first sage who ascended the ‘Upper Mountain’ and found a path of ascension for all living beings.”

“The Upper Mountain and the Infinite Sea. They should be existences of the same scale in the mortal world.”

“The Immortal Realm, built upon the ‘Upper Mountain,’ is also infinite in a sense.”

Compared to the mountains and seas, True Immortals were no different from ants. But when ants ascended, they crushed mountains and seas under their feet, creating a glorious era.

It almost gave Li Fan a stirring feeling of ‘man conquering nature.’

Besides the Four Sage Lords, Lian Shan, Gui Hai, and others, the Immortal Who铭ed the Dao also belonged to the ranks of those who could seemingly defy mountains and seas.

In Situ Xing’s memory, the Supreme Dao Book floating above the Boundless Star Domain was awe-inspiring and venerable. It seemed to exhaust the principles of mountains and seas.

“The True Immortal篆 inscriptions I glimpsed before, including ‘Creation,’ seem to have originated from this Dao Book.”

“Even just one or two characters are already so profound and boundless. It is truly hard to imagine how shocking the complete Dao Book would be.”

Even in the lower realm, there were legends about the Immortal Who铭ed the Dao. Li Fan initially learned of his existence from Bai Hua’s words. The fame of the Immortal Who铭ed the Dao and his profound influence on the Immortal Realm were evident.

As for the Four Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm, and even Shouqiu Gong, their strength might have been greater, but in terms of widespread influence, they were far inferior.

This was determined by the nature of different Daos.

“The Immortal Who铭ed the Dao disappeared long ago and is no longer active in the world. Perhaps he has already left the ‘Primordial’ possibility.”

“His method of铭ing Three Thousand Daos to achieve transcendence was indeed understandable.”

…

Thinking of this, a doubt arose in Li Fan’s heart.

Through his interactions with True Immortals, and even Nameless True Immortals, during this period, he had managed to barely understand the origin of the Immortal Realm and the reason for the descent of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

But now, an unavoidable question arose in Li Fan’s mind.

“The formation of the Immortal Realm originated from mountains and seas.”

“But what is the connection between different possibilities and the ‘Upper Mountain’ and ‘Infinite Sea’?”

“Based on my previous deduction of the ‘All My Avatars Unite’ theory, mountains and seas are clearly powerful beings of the same level. Conversely, backtracking, this implies that even in the infinite possibilities, there is only one Infinite Sea and one Upper Mountain.”

“Perhaps, by coexisting between the same mountains and seas, this is the theoretical basis for jumping between different possibilities.”

…

After pondering for a long time, Li Fan finally shook his head slightly.

Without reaching that realm, no matter how much he fantasized, he would not be able to understand the underlying principles. However, with the mountains and seas now present, it pointedLi Fan towards a direction for his Dao path, which had been shrouded in mist and stalled at the Half-Immortal stage.

“Let’s not talk about transcending mountains and seas for now.”

“Existing between mountains and seas, to gain powerful strength, one inevitably has to borrow the power of mountains and seas.”

“Lian Shan, Gui Hai. These are the titles of two Sage Lords, and they also expound the true meaning of the power of ‘Immortal.’”

“Everything was fine initially. True Immortals stepped on mountains and seas, creating a glorious era. But the current problem is…”

“The ‘Fusion of Mountains and Seas.’”

Based on Situ Xing’s understanding, the Immortal Realm seemed to be built upon the ‘Upper Mountain.’

When mountains and seas merged, the mountains would cease to be mountains, and the seas, seas.

The Immortal Realm would naturally disappear along with everything.

Recalling the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation he had personally witnessed, Li Fan’s heart suddenly stirred: “The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation is not as simple as the Immortal Realm being swallowed by the Infinite Sea.”

“Rather, when mountains and seas merge, mountains cease to be mountains, and seas cease to be seas.”

“Perhaps, it is returning to a state before mountains and seas existed…”

The prophecy left by Sun Piaomiao at that time resurfaced in Li Fan’s mind.

Mountain and sea arguing, the sea retorted to the mountain: “What does ‘belonging’ mean? Is our infinite lifespan inherent?”

Countless scenes involuntarily appeared in Li Fan’s mind.

“Situ Xing said that the fusion of mountains and seas is the general trend. But the key to solving all problems lies in why mountains and seas actually fused.”

Li Fan looked towards the horizon. In the direction where Hei Tianyi had traversed possibilities and charged forward violently.

“Perhaps, the true answer to this question lies in the ‘Grand World of the Other Shore’ where the ‘Transcendent True Immortals’ gathered.”

“Heavenly Physician, Su Bai, Dao铭, Shouqiu…”

“Whether it is someone I have personally encountered, or only heard about in historical legends. They might all be gathered there.”

Faces flashed one by one in Li Fan’s mind, and he couldn’t help but take a deep breath to calm his racing heart.

Objectively speaking, Li Fan’s strength was still far from theirs.

But possessing the supreme treasure ‘Returning to Truth,’ it was an ironclad certainty that he would reach their level one day.

“The key is, how to get there.”

“Currently, the idea of me using Ink Slaughter to devour and evolve Three Thousand Great Daos, merging Dao into my body, is still the most suitable for me.”

“Especially after learning of the existence of the ‘Supreme Dao Book.’”

“Unfortunately, the Supreme Dao Book was swallowed by Dao Annihilation long ago. Only a few characters remain occasionally. Otherwise, if I could have swallowed the Dao Book, I might have instantly leaped to the Transcendent realm.” Thinking of this, Li Fan couldn’t help but feel a sense of regret. A perfect shortcut was lost.

But then he thought, although the true Dao Book had disappeared, there might still be some True Immortals in the history of the Immortal Realm who had seen it and were still alive.

“Those who survived the great tribulation of the Immortal Realm back then must have been powerful. It is highly likely they had visited the Boundless Star Domain and seen the Dao Book. Such True Immortals, like Situ Xing, are great supplements to me!”

“At the very least, it can save me thousands of years of hard thinking!”

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan’s eyes.

This was not to say that Li Fan truly harbored the ambition of being a world-saving Celestial Emperor. It was merely a momentary thought arising from his deduction of past events, imagining himself in their shoes.

All that has passed has turned to nothing.

The current Primordial possibility was merely a broken remnant struggling to survive.

Li Fan could only do as those escapees had done: change his dwelling and move on.

Chapter 1490: The Myriad Manifestations Dao Net is Formed

The Myriad Manifestations Dao Net is Formed (6k)

“Without the Xuanhuang Realm, there is no ‘Ancient Primordial Essence.’”

“Without the Ancient Primordial Essence, our clan cannot traverse possibilities. We can only await death in despair where the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation approaches,” Situ Xing’s tone was calm, but his ancient and infinitely wise eyes were fixed on Li Fan.

“That may not necessarily be the case. I recall you mentioning that your clan possesses the ‘Furnace Unification’ method. Since you were able to traverse possibilities, the fused entity after the unification of myriad beasts should also be able to do so. Why then must you seek help from others?” Li Fan said casually, his right index finger slowly rising, blocking Situ Xing’s view.

A small ball of ancient bronze energy suddenly appeared at his fingertip. It was the Ancient Primordial Essence that Situ Xing had been desperately seeking!

Situ Xing’s pupils contracted. But before he could speak, the ancient bronze ball shattered like bubbles and disappeared.

Knowing that this was Li Fan’s deliberate act, Situ Xing took a deep breath and revealed the truth: “It is not that we do not want to, but that we cannot.”

“The method used by Ku Ying and me to traverse possibilities has severe limitations…”

“It can only transport a single consciousness at a time, not to mention the risk of being lost in the spacetime turbulence.”

Li Fan did not reply, still looking quietly at Situ Xing.

Situ Xing’s face was filled with helplessness: “After Wan Shi Yong died, Ku Ying acted in his stead and went outside the High Wall. After experiencing various events over the years, he joined the ‘Immortal Hunt.’”

“This is the most powerful force in the star sea outside the High Wall. The cultivators within possess a treasure called the ‘World-Crossing Mysterious Coffin.’ The people of the Immortal Hunt do not seem to know its origin and only recognize it as a replica. However, Ku Ying can sense fluctuations from our clan from another possibility within this Mysterious Coffin.”

“Perhaps it is because our clan has traversed so many possibilities that we are more sensitive than ordinary people…”

As Situ Xing was speaking, Li Fan suddenly waved his hand gently: “Is it this item?”

A Mysterious Coffin appeared before Situ Xing.

Situ Xing was stunned at first, and when he saw it clearly, his expression changed drastically.

This Mysterious Coffin was the one that Li Biren had previously taken from Wu Xian and Qian Ruo Chang, who were residing within it.

And the Star Sea side seemed to have always concealed the existence of Li Fan, the ‘Hidden Emperor,’ from Li Fan. Although Situ Xing had ‘Wan Shi Yong’ as an insider, he was unaware of the drastic changes that had occurred in the Star Sea over the past hundred years and his ‘senior’ before him was actually deeply involved.

“This World-Crossing Mysterious Coffin was crafted from the remains of a human Transcendent expert, hence it can traverse to the other shore. However, it requires a specific method to cooperate. You certainly do not know this method, yet you can utilize the item to its fullest and complete the traversal… You do have some skill,” Li Fan commented indifferently. He then put away the World-Crossing Mysterious Coffin again, preventing Situ Xing from examining it closely.

Although this Mysterious Coffin was genuine, Li Fan had severed its spiritual connection, rendering it incapable of traversing possibilities. It might fool Situ Xing at first glance. But if left out for too long, it might reveal its flaws.

The appearance of the Mysterious Coffin further proved Li Fan’s unfathomable strength.

Situ Xing’s resolve became even firmer: “Senior displayed immense divine power when saving me before. With Senior’s ability…”

“Indeed. I can help your clan traverse. But on what grounds? As the saying goes, ‘Those of different species, their hearts must be different.’ The thirteen Ancient Dao Forms all exist in fullness… If I help you traverse, wouldn’t I be inviting trouble?” Li Fan interrupted Situ Xing’s words.

Situ Xing, having come to persuade Li Fan, had prepared his arguments in advance: “Senior’s concerns were anticipated. However, please rest assured. In the possibility we are currently in, there is an artifact called the ‘Myriad Beasts Reincarnation’!”

“This Reincarnation is actually the Myriad Beasts Furnace from the past. It has witnessed the entire process of the clan’s life from myriad to one, and then from one back to myriad. Therefore, it possesses a certain authority that transcends our clan’s life form…”

As he spoke, Situ Xing’s long eyebrows and hair suddenly fluttered without wind, flying wildly.

Hair and beard connected, forming a circle. A phantom image of a reincarnation wheel appeared from the circle. Li Fan seemed to see countless different exotic beasts roaring fiercely within the phantom image.

“The clan is entirely under the control of this Reincarnation, even those thirteen Ancient Dao Forms…”

“Except for the five Dao Forms that were originally buried by the Nameless True Immortal of Humanity, the remaining eight are also subject to the control of this Reincarnation. ‘Que Chen Xi’ and ‘Ji Liang Shou,’ among other Ancient Dao Forms, gathered a portion of themselves into the furnace when they helped the clan traverse possibilities and were on the verge of extinction. Although it wasn’t the Ancient Dao Forms of that glorious world who did all this, strictly speaking, there is no difference between THEM.”

“With this Reincarnation, Senior’s worries can be resolved,” Situ Xing explained with a nonchalant expression.

The phantom image of the reincarnation wheel gradually solidified, transforming into a tangible entity, and Situ Xing presented it to Li Fan.

Li Fan looked at the patterns on the Reincarnation wheel and seemed to genuinely feel the majestic aura of myriad beasts charging forward. In his previous reincarnations, he had also seen the Myriad Beasts Reincarnation, but it was merely the one passed down by the Beast Taming Sect. Compared to the one Situ Xing personally offered, it was clearly inferior.

After examining it thoroughly, Li Fan found that Situ Xing had not lied. Holding the Reincarnation, scenes of the birth of beast-clan life forms from nothing to something seemed to appear before his eyes. Even Situ Xing and Di Yi were among them.

The secrets of beast-clan life were no longer a mystery to Li Fan; he could understand and control them with ease.

“Hehehe. Di San, do your clan’s people know about your act of offering the Myriad Beasts Reincarnation?” Li Fan looked at the intelligent beast with a playful expression.

Situ Xing lowered his head and replied calmly: “Naturally, they do not know. Moreover, they do not even know that the ‘Myriad Beasts Reincarnation’ exists in the world.”

“Then aren’t you going to bear the eternal infamy of ‘Beast Traitor’?”

“Heh heh, I’ve been wearing this title for tens of thousands of years. What’s one more?” Situ Xing seemed completely unconcerned.

He looked at Li Fan sincerely: “Compared to the continuation of the clan, everything else is insignificant.”

Li Fan pondered, finding it difficult to ascertain the true intentions of this intelligent beast.

But no matter what, he would never give up on the ‘feast’ of the thirteen Ancient Dao Forms.

“With Li Biren’s current strength as a clone, he can probably only contend with one of the Ancient Dao Forms individually. But this is only under normal circumstances. If I were to unleash the full power of the Shouqiu Gong projection…”

“Even though it would further exacerbate the crisis of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea’s Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, if it could be exchanged for the opportunity to feast on thirteen Great Daos, it would be worth it.”

“Regardless of whether the Myriad Beasts Reincarnation is useful or not, I can thoroughly ‘process’ these Dao Forms…” Li Fan’s thoughts raced.

Then, he burst into laughter: “Very good. As the saying goes, ‘The wise submit to circumstances; Di San, you are truly the embodiment of your clan’s wisdom.”

Li Fan’s expression suddenly changed: “I will not hide anything from you. Your clan’s thirteen Dao Forms are of great use to me…”

As he spoke, Li Fan deliberately put on a greedy and desirous expression.

“I must eventually return to my homeland.”

“Moreover, I must personally kill the two sc*m who almost destroyed my homeland. They wronged me.” Li Fan lightly tapped, and images of Hei Tianyi and Xie Subai appeared in the air before him.

Li Fan stared at the two figures, paused for a moment, and said: “But I must admit, my current strength is still somewhat lacking compared to them. But I have inherited an supreme Dao lineage. As long as you give me some time and resources…”

He ended with a cold laugh, leaving Situ Xing with endless speculation.

“Supreme Dao lineage.” Situ Xing truly sensed the key point in Li Fan’s words.

In the fabricated past of Li Fan, his homeland, although destroyed, had left behind many Dao lineages in the lower realm, which could even resist the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation for a time.

And Li Fan’s ability to create ‘Ancient Primordial Essence’ out of thin air was the best proof of his inheritance of an supreme Dao lineage, making it impossible for Situ Xing not to believe him.

“Does Senior mean that the Ancient Dao Forms are the resources you need?” The intelligent beast then quietly asked.

Li Fan nodded proudly in acknowledgment.

“You don’t need to worry, I will not harm your ordinary clansmen. Only the Dao Forms naturally derived from Great Daos are my sustenance.”

“Will you choose to betray the Ancient Dao Forms, thus preserving the lives of the majority of your clan? Or watch them all perish in the great tide of Dao Annihilation…”

“You make your choice.”

Situ Xing’s reply was swift: “My answer will not change. I have already thought through the pros and cons on the way here.”

“The only thing I didn’t expect was that Senior could manipulate the Great Dao forms into use…” Li Fan smiled sinisterly.

He moved like a ghost and appeared beside Situ Xing, placing his hand on his head.

Situ Xing felt as if a mountain had descended upon him, instantly rendered immobile.

It was as if a carving knife was constantly chiseling and slicing through his mind. Even with his experience, he could not endure such torment.

The physical abnormality came suddenly and disappeared quickly. A moment later, he recovered completely.

The previous pain felt like an illusion, but a faint shadow resembling Li Fan remained in his mind, forever present.

No matter how he tried to calm his heart, it steadfastly loomed over his consciousness.

“It’s just a small restrictive technique; you don’t need to be nervous. As long as you follow the plan, everything will be fine.”

“Conversely…”

Li Fan let out an inexplicable laugh: “I don’t mind you testing your entire clan’s lives.”

Situ Xing’s expression turned solemn, and he bowed his head, murmuring, “I dare not.”

Next, Li Fan and Situ Xing discussed the general details of the reception plan, and Li Fan asked the crucial question: “How much Ancient Primordial Essence is needed to traverse possibilities?”

Situ Xing took out a strange mask: “Based on our past experience, we only need to fill this divine mask.”

Li Fan took the mask and sensed it. After a brief induction, he said: “It can be done. Three days later, I will deliver the filled mask of Ancient Primordial Essence to you.”

“Also…”

“When you traverse possibilities this time, please wear this item.”

Situ Xing looked closely. Floating quietly before him was a sculpture made of an unknown material.

Mountains and seas embraced each other, and above them, a figure stood with its hands behind its back, as if standing tall.

The moment he touched the sculpture, the image of mountains and seas merged into his body, making it impossible to sense its location.

“You may go now.”

After being asked to leave, Situ Xing’s vision blurred, and he returned to the Xuanhuang Realm.

He did not leave but waited quietly.

While standing, he observed his surroundings. Compared to a hundred years ago, the world had been completely transformed.

Not only was the sky and earth higher, but the most prominent change was the pervasive vitality.

Situ Xing felt a sense of illusory familiarity, as if he had returned to the ancient times before the tribulation descended.

“If we could reproduce and thrive here, it would indeed be a blessing.”

“Although it cannot last forever, it is a temporary paradise.”

“Moreover, as long as there is enough Ancient Primordial Essence, even if this place becomes uninhabitable one day, we can find another place.” Situ Xing thought silently.

…

Within the Heavenly Pillar space.

Li Biren stood with a solemn expression, his eyes closed, acting as the bridge connecting the main body and the Shouqiu Gong projection’s power.

As an energy form capable of supporting the traversal of possibilities, the quality of Ancient Primordial Essence must be extremely high. To create enough to fill an entire mask was no easy task.

Even Li Fan at this moment found it somewhat strenuous.

Therefore, he needed to borrow power.

Of course, Li Fan would not directly use the power of Shouqiu Gong projection or other Heavenly Pillars. Instead, he transferred it through the connection between his clone and main body via the Dao Net.

After quietly comprehending the Dao for a hundred years, the gradually expanding Myriad Manifestations Dao Net, formed by Ink Slaughter, allowed Li Fan’s main body to withstand the power of the Shouqiu Gong projection.

The boundless power of mountains and seas, using Li Biren as a link, was transferred into the great net woven by Ink Slaughter. As expected.

Ink Slaughter, with its nature similar to Dao Annihilation, belonged to the transformation of the fusion of mountains and seas.

As if sharing the same origin, the power of the Shouqiu Gong projection was completely converted without any blockage. In the net Li Fan had woven, stars rushed and rivers flowed, endless and inexhaustible.

It was like applying ‘False becomes True’ to himself, resulting in a severalfold increase in strength.

The power surged out of nowhere, inexhaustible and inexhaustible.

“False becomes True…”

The memory and sensation of creating Ancient Primordial Essence out of thin air reappeared in his mind.

Through a hundred years of enlightenment, the proportion of residual energy had significantly increased, from one in ten thousand to one in five thousand.

And now, with the amplification of external forces and a leap in strength to the Nameless realm. This residual proportion had jumped again to five in a thousand!

Although there was still a loss of nine hundred and ninety-five in a thousand.

However, in the face of the nature of ‘Infinity,’ these losses could all be ignored.

Operating the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net of Ink Slaughter to its maximum capacity, Li Fan indulged in the experience of creation.

With each drop of light born, his comprehension of the true and false transformation deepened.

…

Three days later.

Di San Mo was summoned again.

A mask was hurled towards him, and he instinctively caught it.

The surging, familiar aura from the mask caused the ancient wise beast’s body to tremble uncontrollably.

In his eyes, this mask contained not only energy but also the hope of his entire clan’s survival.

“I will not fail Senior’s trust.”

Di San Mo said solemnly.

If before this moment, he had harbored even a sliver of hesitation, then now, after seeing the entire mask filled with Ancient Primordial Essence, there was not a trace of doubt left.

“As long as there is enough of this energy, we can continuously search for new safe havens until the entire mortal world is destroyed. At the very least, before that, the clan can guarantee its safety. We don’t have to gamble anymore.”

“Compared to that…”

“The sacrifice of a few Ancient Dao Forms is insignificant.”

Di San Mo’s resolve was hidden beneath his cloudy eyes. He once again headed towards the border of the Star Sea.

…

Li Fan watched Di San Mo’s disappearing figure, sensing his location in his mind, and nodded slightly.

The imprint he had left in Di San Mo’s mind was the culmination of his hundred years of enlightenment in the Dao of ‘Carving.’

He did not expect it to be useful after Di San Mo traversed possibilities, but as long as he could track what happened within the World-Crossing Mysterious Coffin, then Li Fan could also personally find the possibility where the thirteen Great Daos existed.

In an enemy territory, if his strength was insufficient, Li Fan could still find a way to deal with them later.

Moreover, in Li Fan’s view, the possibility of Di San Mo betraying the plan was extremely small.

“It’s time to make arrangements.” A sense of excitement arose in his heart.

Only after truly digesting the Great Daos contained within a Nameless True Immortal did Li Fan realize how much he had gained.

From a realm perspective, Li Fan’s main body was still at the ‘Half-Immortal’ stage.

But as long as the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net of Ink Slaughter was deployed, he could easily capture opponents whose ‘weight’ was below his.

The so-called ‘weight’ was Li Fan’s description of the position occupied by the Dao paths he cultivated within the Great Dao of heaven and earth.

There were no quantitative data, only sensory anchoring.

Just like the Dao of ‘Carving,’ which he glimpsed from Situ Xing’s memories, although it was incomplete, it originated from a Nameless True Immortal who had merged with the Dao. The weight of its Dao was almost equivalent to half a Nameless True Immortal.

Far beyond what ordinary True Immortals could compare to.

And this was merely one of the types of Dao within Li Fan’s Myriad Manifestations Dao Net.

Formless, Hunger, Creation, Primordial…

And so on, each distributed in different parts of the Dao Net.

With these comprehended Dao Principles as leverage, Li Fan was qualified to contend with true Nameless True Immortals without being at a disadvantage.

This had been verified through Li Fan’s occasional sparring with his clone over the past hundred years.

Strictly speaking, this was not Li Fan’s own power. It was ‘adapting to the local conditions and fighting with power.’

Without the leverage available within the Dao Net of this possibility, it might instantly become empty.

But at the very least, within the ‘Primordial’ possibility, with this move, Li Fan was almost in a state of semi-invincibility.

Except for some old monsters who survived the great tribulation of the Immortal Realm, Li Fan feared none of them.

“Shouqiu Gong’s projection. My own Dao Net.”

“Every time a Nameless True Immortal is suppressed and devoured, both of these can be greatly strengthened.”

“Shouqiu Gong’s projection power has an upper limit, but my Ink Slaughter Myriad Manifestations Dao Net has no limits. Perhaps, the limit is my ideal state: ‘All Three Thousand Great Daos, returned to me.’”

Li Fan was very satisfied with the gains from his hundred years of seclusion.

As the saying goes, ‘familiarity breeds contempt,’ so he couldn’t help but cast his gaze towards the nearby Star Sea.

Because of the time difference caused by traversing different possibilities, it might be another hundred years before Di San Mo sent news.

Li Fan could not possibly just wait like this during this period.

He had reached a preliminary cooperation agreement with the remaining True Immortal factions. The Star Sea, which was filled with True Immortals, was naturally his ideal hunting ground.

Through the hundred years, Wu Xian had been reporting news of the progress between both sides.

Although it was slow, with the joint efforts of certain forces, the Immortal Hunt and the True Immortals had gradually let go of their past grievances and agreed to jointly bear the responsibility of resisting Dao Annihilation.

After all, the condition promised by the Immortal Hunt, to release all the True Immortals imprisoned deep within the Dao Net, was truly sincere.

The condition was that before leaving the Dao Net, they would have to leave behind a ‘Dao-Carrying Projection’ using the ‘Projection Carries Dao’ method.

The only flaw of the Dao-Carrying Projection was that when one truly transcended, they would have to recall the projection.

Even Shouqiu Gong had not been able to achieve this, let alone these prisoners.

Therefore, they all agreed.

“They didn’t reveal the list of True Immortals who were released.”

Li Fan, hidden behind the High Wall, gazed at the nearby Star Sea.

Over the past hundred years, Xuanhuang Realm had been continuously drawing upon the Dao principles of the Star Sea to nourish the weakened and depleted Utmost Darkness Star Sea. Although the impact was minimal, the unusual fluctuations had still attracted the attention of the Star Sea side. They had sent people to investigate several times.

But they were all repelled by Li Fan’s attack.

“They endured for a few times, but they can’t endure forever.”

“Let me add more fuel to the fire for you.”

For Li Fan, fighting near the High Wall gave him an absolute advantage in terrain. Therefore, any plan was best executed with the battlefield drawn to this location.

With his mind made up, the Dao path formed by Li Biren opened its monstrous mouth once again.

Like a bottomless sea abyss, it greedily devoured the Dao principles of the Star Sea.

This time, Li Fan showed no restraint. The magnitude of the phenomenon was so great that it formed a distorted halo near the High Wall.

The Star Sea was instantly alarmed.

After a moment of silence, two figures arrived together.

One of them was Wu Xian.

The other figure, Li Fan had not seen before.

However, this person emanated no True Immortal aura. Instead, wherever he passed, the surrounding Dao principles rippled as if a giant beast was swimming underwater.

“This is a show of force,” Li Fan thought with amusement.

This person clearly belonged to the Immortal Hunt.

Given the control over the Dao Network that this person displayed, it was impossible for them to cause such a commotion while traveling.

Li Fan quietly observed the aftermath of the Dao Network.

“A Dao Net woven over tens of thousands of years, with Nameless True Immortals as pillars. It is indeed imposing, far surpassing my Myriad Manifestations Dao Net.”

“However…”

“Such commotion is still too excessive!”

Li Fan moved his mind, and the boundless power of Wuji erupted.

Transforming into a giant hand, it reached out towards the Immortal Hunt member whom Li Fan was observing.

Chapter 1491: Bestowing Divine Skills

Li Fan's strike was sudden, like a black shadow appearing abruptly beneath the water's surface.

The Immortal Hunt cultivator from the Star Sea noticed the incoming attack and was initially slightly startled. But he quickly calmed down.

A hint of anger hid in his expression.

He was about to suppress the intruder with the immense power of his Dao Net, but little did he expect…

The magnificent Great Dao, inexplicably, melted away like ice and snow the moment it neared the shadow. He threw a punch with the force of a thousand pounds, but it felt listless, unable to even stir a leaf.

Not only that, but the very foundation of his power, his Dao Net, was itself dissolving!

It was as if the shadow had corroded a vast hole within the Dao Net, and he was now falling into this profound black abyss.

The anger in the Star Sea Immortal Hunt cultivator’s eyes instantly turned to terror.

Wu Xian, who had been watching with the intention of being entertained, also sensed something was amiss. Just as he was about to move to rescue him, he felt a hand gently press down on his shoulder. The weight of mountains descended upon him, rendering him immobile!

He could only watch as the Immortal Hunt cultivator was swallowed by the black shadow.

"What is the meaning of this?"

After everything settled, Li Fan's voice rang out lazily. He made no mention of the suppressed Immortal Hunt cultivator, as if he had casually swatted a fly, deeming it unworthy of notice.

Knowing that his previous rude actions must have angered this capricious "Hidden Emperor," Wu Xian understood why Li Fan had acted.

Thinking that the Elder Wei, who ranked among the top three in strength within the Star Sea’s Administrative Council, had been so easily captured, Wu Xian's heart chilled.

Over the years, the Administrative Council had tried various means to analyze this Hidden Emperor's strength. However, the realm the other party had inadvertently displayed at this moment was absolutely far beyond the scope of their analysis.

"Even that esteemed Lord probably couldn't achieve this."

"No wonder, despite knowing of this Hidden Emperor's existence all these years, no one came to pay their respects. They were afraid…"

Wu Xian's thoughts churned, but his actions remained unchanged. He bowed respectfully and said, "We detected anomalous Great Dao fluctuations at the star sea's frontier. Fearing it might be Senior's summons, we hurried here to investigate."

Wu Xian didn't mention the Immortal Hunt cultivator at all.

"Hmph."

"It shouldn't be a problem for me to draw a little bit of your fundamental Great Daos, right? Anyway, you have the Dao Net supporting you, and in the past hundred years, you've even gained the augmentation of some True Immortal Dao Manifestations." Li Fan asked coldly.

With the Elder Hunt cultivator who had backed him up now captured, Wu Xian dared not show the slightest dissent. He could only nod bitterly, "No problem, no problem."

"I have been awake for a long time, and now that the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation has subsided, and all is to be rebuilt. I wish to re-establish the Immortal Court…"

As Wu Xian was calculating how to report back to the Star Sea Administrative Council, Li Fan's words struck him like a thunderbolt, completely blanking his mind.

"Re-establish the Immortal Court?" Wu Xian stood dumbfounded.

Years ago, the grand scene of the boundless Immortal Realm couldn't help but surface in his mind.

"The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation has not yet receded, so re-establishing the Immortal Realm is impossible for now. However, restoring a region of immortal domain…"

"That can still be barely managed," Li Fan said proudly.

"It will be completed in the coming days. At that time, those of you who are interested can come and witness it. However, those who are extraneous, or disrespectful, need not bother coming."

Wu Xian was still immersed in the explosive news, his mind feeling hazy. Just as he was about to respond, he felt the gravity on his shoulders increase again. The scenery before his eyes flickered, and by the time he regained his senses, he had been thrown thousands of miles away.

And it seemed something had been thrown out along with him.

However, that object stopped its flight just three thousand miles outwards. It stood quietly in the void.

At first glance, it seemed to be a stone pillar.

A large character, '静' (Stillness), was inscribed on it.

However, after observing for a moment, Wu Xian felt a chill run down his spine, as if he had fallen into an ice cellar.

What stood before him was no stone pillar at all.

It was clearly the Immortal Hunt elder who had come with him!

"At the very beginning of the Dao Net's creation, Wei Dao Fu was already one of its pillars. Immersed in the Dao Net for many years, one with the myriad Daos. Even facing several Nameless beings, he handled them with ease."

"The power he displayed just now when he repelled three simultaneous attackers during the negotiation – how could he be in such a state now…"

Wu Xian's heart was filled with despair and fear.

"At that time, the 'Nameless True Immortal' he once was had indeed died. What remained was merely an ordinary cultivator who only wanted to struggle for survival."

After thinking this through, he knew he could not continue like this.

Once the Heavenly Pillar was completely formed, even if he possessed heaven-defying divine abilities, it would likely be futile.

Gritting his teeth, he made a resolute decision. The mask on his face shattered with a boom.

The surrounding binding forces instantly vanished.

He hurriedly cried out, "Senior, please wait!"

"In the Azure Gloom Starfield, the Administrative Immortal Minister, Situ Xing, pays his respects!"

…

"Administrative Immortal Minister."

Hearing Situ Xing's words, Li Fan's suppressing power loosened slightly.

However, he did not release him but quietly observed him carefully.

The sudden shattering of the bronze mask earlier had almost caught him off guard. He hadn't expected that something seemingly within his grasp could suddenly erupt with such resistance.

Fortunately, he had urgently summoned Shouqiu Gong's projection and continued to increase the pressure. Only then did he avoid revealing any flaws.

"What times are these, still using Emperor Tian Luo's methods."
