"What, you administrative immortal minister, still intend to rule over me?"

After pondering for a moment, Li Fan ridiculed him with a mocking tone.

Since his understanding of the past Immortal Realm was not particularly clear yet, Li Fan decided to directly lead the other party into the trap he had fabricated, rather than getting too entangled in that aspect: "The Immortal Realm is now destroyed, and all the Immortals have either died or fled."

"You, the former Immortal Minister, cannot rule over a mountain king like me. Hmph!"

These few sentences were enough to allow the other party to roughly guess his origins.

While he could use the identity of the ‘Hidden Emperor’ with those people from Suo Xing Sea, to pry information from this Administrative Immortal Minister, he had to adopt a different persona.

As expected, after hearing Li Fan’s words, Situ Xing began to speculate in the direction he was guided.

"Occupying a mountain as king. The Great Tribulation of Dao Annihilation descends, and even the lower realms cannot survive. Only isolated islands remain. This person suppressing a Nameless Immortal to become a Heavenly Pillar is to strengthen their ability to resist the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation…" Situ Xing’s thoughts raced, but his heart gradually cooled.

He had originally thought that his former title as Administrative Immortal Minister would at least make the other party hesitant. But now…

"Don’t call me 'Senior'."

"In my cultivation so far, I’ve only cultivated for about six thousand years at most, and I’ve never been to any Immortal Realm. Heh heh, speaking of which, you, the Administrative Immortal Minister, have lived for quite some time, haven’t you? I should be the one calling you 'Senior'!"

Li Fan sneered and suddenly increased the suppressing force.

"Just stay here in this pillar and serve as my gatekeeper!"

"Six thousand years to reach such strength? How is that possible?"

"But it does seem somewhat unusual. That person is indeed not a True Immortal. Could it be that in the years I was trapped, a new cultivation system has developed in the world?"

Situ Xing heard this and instinctively felt shocked and disbelieving.

But he felt the sealing force around him, which had been static, tightening again. He had no time to think carefully.

In his panic, he frantically searched his mind for possible ways to escape.

"Not from the Immortal Realm, so all my past experiences are useless to him…"

The surroundings began to blur.

That fierce and brutal figure was gradually obscured by the gathered Life Dao Principles.

Situ Xing knew that this was a sign that the Heavenly Pillar was about to be completely sealed.

"A person from the lower realm…"

In this moment of extreme danger, a figure suddenly flashed in Situ Xing’s mind. After hesitating for a moment, he decided to try anything as a last resort. Using his remaining strength, he shouted, "Senior, please wait! I am also one of the Twelve Heavenly Kings of the Profound Heaven Sect in the past, Xing Wuque!"

It was a desperate long shot, and he did not believe the title of ‘Twelve Heavenly Kings’ would be of any use at all. But what Situ Xing didn’t expect was that upon hearing his words, the restraining force actually lessened slightly!

"Xing Wuque, one of the Twelve Heavenly Kings?"

"Those twelve people around Xuanyuan Hong?" Li Fan asked suspiciously, scrutinizing him.

The words ‘Xuanyuan Hong’ seemed to have evoked some ancient memories in Situ Xing, causing him to momentarily daze.

But at this moment of life and death, he could not afford to think further and hurriedly said, "Exactly, exactly."

"Back then, what Xuanyuan Hong liked, was it Luo Yichen, or Ji Yuzhen, or perhaps Granny Nie?" Li Fan suddenly asked with an inscrutable tone and playful expression.

Situ Xing, or rather Xing Wuque, was stunned on the spot.

"Hmm?"

"...Uh, none of them! Although they all had feelings for him, according to my observation, Xuanyuan Hong had long harbored feelings for someone else. So he always kept his distance from them," the other party seemed about to suppress him again in the Heavenly Pillar at any moment. Situ Xing’s heart leaped, and he hastily replied.

"Hahaha, you observed quite carefully. Xuanyuan Hong indeed had a childhood sweetheart, and she was also an extraordinary person…" Li Fan spoke halfway, leaving endless room for speculation for Situ Xing. Then he slightly loosened his grip on Situ Xing.

The towering mountain hanging overhead was temporarily moved away. Situ Xing couldn't help but breathe a sigh of relief.

He tried to probe for more information: "Senior, do you know Xuanyuan Hong?"

"Indeed. Back then, he saved my life during the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. However, later, he disappeared without a trace. I had always wanted to find an opportunity to repay him, but I never saw him again," Li Fan replied.

"This truly sounds like something Xuanyuan Hong would do." Situ Xing nodded secretly in his heart.

"By the way, you were someone close to Xuanyuan Hong, how did you end up like this?"

Hearing the other party’s question, Situ Xing gave a wry smile: "This matter… is hard to explain in a few words."

"Then tell me slowly. I haven’t had a good chat with anyone in a long time. With the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation descending, living beings are scarce. There isn’t even a fellow cultivator to communicate with!" Li Fan said in a deep voice, patting Situ Xing on the shoulder and completely removing the suppressing force.

Although temporarily freed, Situ Xing couldn’t help but cast a glance at the two Heavenly Pillars beside him without daring to act rashly.

He sized up Li Fan, weaving words in his mind to explain everything.

"Judging from the meaning of the other party’s words, Xuanyuan Hong now seems to have attained an extremely high cultivation level. At the very least, he is definitely not below this person. But this is also as it should be."

After a long while, Situ Xing finally spoke: "To let Senior know, I was not speaking in vain just now. My true self is indeed the Administrative Immortal Minister of the Azure Gloom Starfield, Situ Xing. To suppress a star domain of the Immortal Realm at the Nameless realm. However…"

Li Fan waved his hand, interrupting his words: "I know this. You people went down to the lower realm, searching for opportunities for some supreme treasure, didn’t you? This is unimportant, get to the point!"

Situ Xing was astonished; he opened his mouth, but his mind suddenly went blank.

"What? You allow yourselves to go to the lower realm, can’t Xuanyuan Hong do the same? Facing the great tribulation, everyone uses their own abilities! Don’t you think someone that could make all of you follow him willingly and be utterly devoted couldn’t be ordinary?" Li Fan scoffed with a smile.

Situ Xing’s expression changed several times.

"Indeed. Indeed." He suddenly seemed lost in thought, muttering repeatedly.

"Back then, most of us had our spiritual senses obscured. However, during the tens of thousands of years I was trapped in the ‘Form of Living Beings,’ as I gradually regained my true consciousness, I vaguely guessed Xuanyuan Hong’s abnormality."

"But he acted too much like a mortal…"

"How could a mere mortal make all of us True Immortals who descended to the lower realm willingly follow him back then?" Situ Xing’s words were filled with confusion.

"Right. That’s what I thought too."

"I even pressed him back then, and he stubbornly refused to admit it," Li Fan said with a smile.

"Uh… is that your guess too?" Situ Xing was surprised and looked up sharply at Li Fan.

"What? My guess is wrong?" Li Fan’s eyes turned cold, and after a brief stare, Situ Xing was startled by the chilling indifference in his eyes and quickly looked away.

"Makes sense. Very sensible."

"Because that supreme treasure must have sentience. Waiting with a purpose is very likely to be in vain. Therefore, we all chose to seal our spiritual senses and rely purely on personal luck. As the saying goes, survival of the fittest. This also avoids disputes from the Immortal Realm above," Situ Xing continued.

"Those who can become True Immortals all possess extraordinary talent and disposition. Even if they walked the mortal world again, they would undoubtedly be outstanding individuals. However, it seems that all of our luck was not enough. Firstly, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation came too quickly. The speed at which the Immortal Realm collapsed was completely beyond our imagination. As a result, before we could return to the Immortal Realm…"

"We were in different locations in the upper realm. When the ascension channel of the Xuanhuang Realm was destroyed, some were still safe. Some had their true bodies suffer great calamity. Some had their true consciousness begin to awaken, but we all maintained a tacit and delicate balance among ourselves."

"It was all because of Xuanyuan Hong’s uniqueness," Situ Xing said slowly.

"You suspect that the supreme treasure fell into Xuanyuan Hong’s hands?" Li Fan suddenly interjected with a smile.

Situ Xing was silent for a moment, then nodded slightly.

"Otherwise, it is truly difficult to explain his rapid rise, and how he overshadowed all his peers in the lower realm."

"After all, Xuanyuan Hong’s aptitude was really not that high, yet he always took that one step ahead of everyone else," Situ Xing said with a hint of confusion in his tone.

"But before confirming it, no one could act directly. Moreover, Xuanyuan Hong’s true identity was unknown, so we could only wait patiently for the opportunity. Unexpectedly…"

"One day, he suddenly disappeared and never reappeared again," Li Fan finished for Situ Xing.

Situ Xing nodded continuously.

"He disappeared too quickly, too suddenly. And at the last moment, he even warned us…"

"It’s really hard to tell whether he used it as an opportunity to escape, or if he truly met with misfortune."

"There were disagreements among us after that. Some chose to follow his tracks and continue to pursue. Others felt their luck was insufficient and gave up…"

Li Fan shook his head slightly: "No wonder the Profound Heaven Sect, which was so grand back then, vanished instantly after the Profound Heaven King disappeared."

Chapter 1492: Creating the Primordial Immortal Realm

Creating the Primordial Immortal Realm

"Divine Blessing..."

Just three simple words, with no further explanation, but they ignited endless contemplation within Li Fan.

"Illusion is Truth," these words were self-evident, referring to the Great Dao of "When illusion is true, truth also becomes illusion."

The key lay in the preceding words, "Divine Blessing."

"Divine... Blessing..." Li Fan carefully savored this phrase on the "Return to Truth" panel.

The core revolved around "Divine."

"Illusion is Truth" was a divine ability bestowed upon Li Fan by "Return to Truth." It could certainly be considered a form of protection.

So, who did the preceding "Divine" refer to?

Was it "Return to Truth" itself?

Did it imply that in "Return to Truth's" own perception, it belonged to the ranks of the divine?

"What is a god?"

Li Fan couldn't help but recall the allegory left by Sun Piaomiao and the legends of the Creator God, the Mountains, and the Seas.

"I've searched almost the entire Xuanhuang Realm over these years. Yet, I still haven't found the book that Liu Ruchen mentioned. It left no trace, as if it evaporated into thin air."

"The probability of it being naturally annihilated in the long river of history is low. Either it was taken away individually, or it was swept away along with the escape of the Ten Immortal Sects and other supplies..."

"The remnants of the Ten Sects are almost all in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea."

Li Fan's gaze once again turned towards his neighbors beyond the High Wall.

The acquisition of "Illusion is Truth: Divine Blessing" was no less than gaining a combat power equivalent to a Nameless True Immortal, ready to assist at any time.

Perhaps even far more than that.

Suppressing his surging excitement, after approximately twenty-four hours passed, Li Fan sensed that "Illusion is Truth" could be used again.

He immediately calmed himself and reactivated it, returning to the Infinite Sea.

Instead of being surprised by the incredulity of "Return to Truth's Divine Blessing," he immediately began searching for the true method of using "Illusion is Truth."

"Although it is merely an inferior mortal thing, it can deceive the heavens and cross the seas. During the period of divine protection, it aligns with the Infinite Sea..."

Li Biren's consciousness roamed within this vast ocean, attempting to guide the Infinite Power within into reality.

Because of the alignment, this "guidance" did not require acknowledging any pressure. It was as if it were the ocean's own actions.

The main body in the current world initiated the guidance.

He scattered the remaining Immortal Realm fragments around the Primordial Celestial Pillar.

It was as if heaven and earth were being reopened, recreating fire, earth, water, and wind. The Immortal Realm fragments returned to the Great Dao, arrayed around the Celestial Pillar.

Looking at this incomplete heaven and earth, Li Fan connected his Ink Slaughter Myriad Manifestations Dao Net to it.

What was insufficient would be supplemented.

What overlapped, he attempted to tame.

At the center of the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net was the power of Wuji.

If any being was unwilling to submit to the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net, they were directly dispersed. Then, Li Fan would re-evolve them using his own comprehended Dao.

Amidst a misty haze, heaven and earth were born.

There were no living beings within, only the Primordial, the Hungry Immortal, and Wuji, among other Celestial Pillars, standing tall.

And Li Fan's indistinct figure remained above these Celestial Pillars.

"When the universe is set, all manifestations shall arise."

The Dao Net, hidden outside of heaven and earth, emitted countless different shimmering lights. All sorts of Great Daos began to manifest within this nascent world.

It was not an independent deduction; Li Fan directly copied it from the "[Primordial]" possibility, thus evolving without any deviation.

With flashes of light and shadow, in a short time, a Primordial world appeared.

The five Shouqiu projections, along with the Celestial Pillars, supported the Primordial heavens.

As the world took form, the Infinite Immortal Power guided by Li Biren surged downwards along the path of the Dao Net.

Rumble! Rumble! Rumble!

A terrifying commotion, akin to the descent of Dao Annihilation, unfolded within the Primordial world.

The newly formed firmament was completely engulfed by dark clouds. Due to immense pressure, fissures even appeared. The world itself trembled violently, heaven and earth shaking, as if on the verge of collapse.

But the irrigation of Infinite Immortal Power brought clear benefits.

The newly born, desolate world, like a long-parched land, greedily absorbed the power of the Infinite Sea.

The distance between heaven and earth grew more immense with each passing second.

On the ground, mountains rose, rivers and seas, lakes and forests, and various terrains emerged. It was no longer a barren, desolate, and bare continent.

In the sky, the fissures caused by exceeding their limits were being repaired by the power brought by the Infinite Sea.

Li Fan, guided by inspiration, did not eliminate these "Heavenly Scars" entirely. Instead, he preserved thirteen tangible scars and additionally infused them with much Infinite Power.

Due to Li Fan's special attention, as the heavens rose and the earth widened, each of the thirteen Heavenly Scars accumulated nearly as much colossal energy as the entire Primordial world.

Li Fan sensed that these Heavenly Scars, due to the accumulation of so much energy, seemed to be developing a faint spirituality.

After pondering for a long time, Li Fan still chose not to inject a wisp of his divine sense into them, thereby gaining control over these Heavenly Scars.

The Infinite Immortal Power accumulated within the Heavenly Scars had already surpassed the scope of his control. Attempting to forcefully dominate it might instead lead to a backlash.

Li Fan merely refined and separated the connection channels between each Heavenly Scar and the Infinite Sea. As long as he held the connection channels, it was equivalent to having reins on them. No matter how they evolved in the future, as long as he held the reins, he wouldn't fear them spiraling out of control.

Inspired by this, when Li Fan sensed that this Primordial world was also gradually developing consciousness, he intentionally divided this Primordial world into five regions: East, West, North, South, and Center.

Each was connected to a different channel of the Infinite Sea.

Like a great river branching, the consciousness of the Primordial world was also split into pieces.

The uneasy premonition that had been vaguely rising in Li Fan's heart also disappeared.

"It seems that if the Primordial consciousness were to be born, it would be too strong. There would be a risk of losing control," Li Fan mused.

Standing outside of heaven, Li Fan quietly watched this Primordial world continue to evolve.

Endless Immortal Power flowed abundantly from the Infinite Sea.

Under unimaginable pressure, the Primordial world, while continuously growing, was also being compressed to be incredibly solid.

"Externally built by the pressure of the Infinite Sea, and internally possessing the Ink Slaughter Dao Net, which has infinite adaptability and can devour all Three Thousand Great Daos..."

"Even if I unleashed my full power, I probably couldn't cause much damage to this continent."

"Moreover, it is still in a visible growth phase and seems nowhere near its limit. As long as the irrigation from the Infinite Sea continues, it can keep growing forever..."

Li Fan watched the changes within, secretly amazed.

He also felt that with the birth of this continent within the High Wall, it was as if a solid pillar had been added.

Even the entire experimental field space felt "more stable."

...

In the Infinite Sea.

Li Biren was amidst an extremely turbulent vortex, yet he was completely unaffected.

After attempting to guide the power of the Infinite Sea into the real world, he discovered that no matter how much he increased the guidance, the Infinite Sea would always adapt in corresponding ways.

And it did not attract the attention of the Infinite Sea itself.

Li Biren gradually let go, continuously increasing the intensity. The current vortex he was in covered all the observable areas of the Infinite Sea!

Although he could command the Infinite Sea with the characteristics of "Illusion is Truth," the Primordial continent in the real world had limited carrying capacity.

The outflow channel had limited output, and channeling power to gather here formed a vortex that could be called a supreme miracle.

"The time has come."

While within the thunderous vortex, yet unaffected, standing outside of it, Li Biren silently observed and suddenly felt something.

"The duration is much shorter than last time."

"It seems that causing such a huge stir, 'Return to Truth' still had to expend considerable effort to conceal it."

Li Biren mused and, following the vortex channel, skillfully returned.

Without the guide, the nourishment for the Primordial continent was cut off.

The flourishing world instantly fell into stillness.

Then, the thirteen Heavenly Scars and the five world consciousnesses all simultaneously emitted dissatisfied roars.

Li Fan's indistinct figure stood amidst the heaven and earth. He let out a cold snort, suppressing all their anomalies.

In the ensuing silence, these nascent beings finally understood the source of their sustenance.

They all fawned over Li Fan, begging him.

Li Fan remained silent.

He was merely waiting for the next use of "Illusion is Truth."

While waiting silently, Li Fan also used his hand as a knife, carving magnificent and imposing buildings on the earth and in the sky. Their templates were sourced from the Immortal Realm that Li Fan had glimpsed before.

Benefiting from the cultivation of the wooden cat treasure before, Li Fan had also flawlessly recreated these Immortal Realm buildings.

Days passed. When the cooldown for "Illusion is Truth" ended, Li Fan did not rush to activate it again.

Instead, he observed and summarized the attitudes displayed by the thirteen Heavenly Scars and the five world consciousnesses during this period.

Among the Heavenly Scars and world consciousnesses, the one that roared the loudest, Li Fan did not connect it to Infinite Immortal Power.

When the vast Infinite Immortal Power again descended, they could only watch with envy as their "brothers" enjoyed the feast, while they themselves received nothing.

These nascent beings did not possess complex consciousness.

"Others have it, but I don't." Driven by instinct, they felt immense anger.

Their roars echoed throughout the land, even surpassing the commotion of the Infinite Immortal Power's infusion.

Li Fan, however, let out a cold laugh and severed all connections to the Infinite Sea once more.

The Heavenly Scars and world consciousnesses that were greedily absorbing were stunned.

After much effort, they finally understood why Li Fan had stopped the Infinite Immortal Power.

For the sake of their own rations, they united and ganged up to teach those two troublemakers a severe lesson.

It must be said that these beings born from the natural evolution of heaven and earth were indeed powerful.

The Primordial continent was scarred in this great battle.

Fortunately, the outcome was positive.

The troublemakers, outnumbered, no longer dared to make a sound, only able to watch enviously as their brothers contentedly fed.

When the duration of "Illusion is Truth" ended again, facing Li Fan's cessation of feeding, although these Primordial consciousnesses still complained, the commotion was much smaller than before.

Especially the ones who did not receive food this time were completely silent.

The next time, Li Fan switched the target for deprivation.

The two who had learned their lesson and behaved well were given the chance to connect and draw from the Infinite Sea. The severed Heavenly Scar, however, was both terrified and enraged, not knowing what it had done wrong.

Little did it know that Li Fan had merely chosen it randomly.

Once again, everyone was happy, and everyone received food. The Heavenly Scars and world consciousnesses rejoiced.

And then, after waiting for a long time, they never received the Infinite Immortal Power. The Primordial consciousnesses gathered outside the towering building where Li Fan stood in the sky, but dared not act rashly, only watching silently.

Then, Infinite Immortal Power was reconnected to all of them.

Thus, day after day, year after year, Li Fan used this method of constant "dog training" to discipline these Primordial consciousnesses.

Fifteen years passed in the blink of an eye.

Li Fan sensed that this Primordial continent had reached its limit of growth.

Although it could still absorb Infinite Immortal Power, it could no longer be strengthened.

Li Fan sat high in the clouds, looking at the vast continent beneath him.

As he slowly raised his hand, two giant palms descended and enveloped the Primordial world.

With strokes like dragons and snakes, forms of living beings were carved upon the land.

After a burst of dazzling light, the complex characters disintegrated into countless fragments.

And on the Primordial continent, countless beings, transformed from stones, plants, mountains, and lakes, emerged like bamboo shoots after rain.

Though their consciousness was dim, they knew the one who had bestowed life upon them.

They knelt on the ground, all shouting in unison, "Thank you, Great Master, for bestowing life!"

Li Fan waved his hand again, distributing the access rights to the Infinite Sea to every living being.

Of course, the scale of Infinite Immortal Power that these post-natal beings could wield was far inferior to the thirteen Heavenly Scars and the five world consciousnesses.

Collectively, perhaps their combined power was merely equivalent to one of them.

"This is 'Authority'."

Li Fan sensed that within this Primordial world, all access rights to the Infinite Sea were under his management.

With a thought, he could bestow it; with a thought, he could revoke it.

"Perhaps the former ruling Immortal Emperors were like this, wielding absolute power over life and death?" Li Fan suddenly seemed to gain some insight.

The Primordial continent became lively. Li Fan silently recited "Illusion is Truth" again in his heart.

The target of the divine ability was no longer the Infinite Sea.

Instead, it was this Primordial world before him.

After activating "Divine Blessing," Li Fan seemed to have become a part of the Primordial world.

Not only could he clearly sense everything happening within the world, but he could also clearly perceive the subtle communication between the world consciousnesses.

It was as if he had become one of them, while they were completely unaware of this "brother" who had inexplicably appeared among them.

After listening for a while and finding no treasonous remarks from these world consciousnesses, Li Fan nodded with satisfaction.

"This 'Illusion is Truth' divine ability is truly useful."

"Moreover..."

Li Fan silently sensed the duration of the divine protection.

"As expected. The duration varies depending on the target of use."

"When applied to this Primordial continent, it can last almost indefinitely. Even if this world perishes with the passage of time, the effect of 'Illusion is Truth' will still exist."

"This Primordial Immortal Realm is already an extraordinary creation. Yet, the gap between it and the Infinite Sea remains so vast..."

Li Fan's arrogance as a "creator" vanished instantly.

The cold reality brought him back to his senses.

Chapter 1493: The Scroll Attracts All Immortals

Only three simple words, with no further explanation, sparked endless speculation in Li Fan.

Illusion is True clearly referred to the Dao of "When True becomes False, False also becomes True."

The key lay in the preceding two words, "Divine Blessing."

"Divine, Blessing..." Li Fan carefully savored the words on 'Return to Truth's' panel.

The core lay in "Divine."

Illusion is True was a divine ability bestowed upon Li Fan by 'Return to Truth,' so calling it a blessing was not unreasonable.

Then, who did the preceding "Divine" refer to?

'Return to Truth' itself?

Did it imply that, in 'Return to Truth's' own perception, It belonged to the category of gods?

"What is a god?"

Li Fan couldn't help but recall the parable left by Sun Piaomiao and the legends of the Creator God, the Mountains, and the Seas.

"Over the years, I've searched almost every corner of the Xuanhuang Realm, yet I still haven't found the book mentioned by Liu Ruchen. It vanished as if evaporating into thin air, leaving no trace."

"The probability of it being naturally annihilated in the river of history is low. Either it was taken away individually by someone, or it was swept away along with other materials when the Ten Immortal Dao Sects fled..."

"The remnants of the Ten Sects are almost all in the Star Sea Sea."

Li Fan's gaze shifted back to his neighbors outside the high wall.

The acquisition of the "Divine Blessing: Illusion is True" was equivalent to gaining a Nameless True Immortal-level combat force at his beck and call. It might even be far beyond that.

Suppressing his overwhelming excitement, Li Fan waited until approximately twenty-four hours had passed. When he sensed that "Illusion is True" could be used again, he calmed himself and re-entered the Infinite Sea.

Without being surprised by the incredulity of 'Return to Truth's' divine blessing, he immediately began to search for the true usage of Illusion is True.

"Although it is a lowly and common thing, it can deceive heaven and earth. During the duration of the divine blessing, it shares the same status as the Infinite Sea..."

Li Biren's consciousness roamed within the vast ocean, attempting to draw the infinite power within into reality.

Because they shared the same status, this "drawing" did not require acknowledgment of any pressure. It was as if the ocean itself was acting.

The main body drew upon it in the real world.

Li Biren scattered the remaining Immortal Realm fragments around the Yuan Shi Heavenly Pillar.

As if the heavens and earth were being recreated, creating fire, water, and wind. The Immortal Realm fragments returned to the Great Dao, arranging themselves around the Heavenly Pillar.

Looking at this incomplete world, Li Fan connected his Ink Slaughter Myriad Manifestations Dao Net to it.

What was lacking would be supplemented.

What was overlapping would be tamed.

At the center of the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net was the power of Wuji.

Anything that was unwilling to submit to the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net was directly shattered and re-evolved according to Li Fan's own comprehension.

In a misty haze, heaven and earth began to take shape.

There were no living beings within it, only the Heavenly Pillars of Yuan Shi, Hungry Immortal, Wuji, etc., standing tall.

And Li Fan's vague figure hovered above these Heavenly Pillars.

"Heaven and Earth are established, and from them, myriad things arise."

The Dao Net, hidden outside the heavens and earth, emitted countless different rays of light. All sorts of Great Daos began to manifest in this nascent world.

This was not an independent deduction, but a direct replication from the [Primordial] possibility by Li Fan, hence the evolution proceeded without any deviation.

As light and shadow flashed, in a short while, a world resembling the primordial Great Desolation appeared.

The five Shouqiu Gong projections and the numerous Heavenly Pillars supported the grand sky of the Great Desolation.

With the world established, the Infinite Sea power drawn by Li Biren surged downwards through the Dao Net pathway.

Rumble!

A terrifying phenomenon resembling the descent of Dao Annihilation unfolded in the Great Desolation world.

The newly formed sky was completely engulfed by dark clouds. Due to the immense pressure, cracks even appeared. The world itself trembled violently, shaking and seemingly on the verge of collapse.

However, the benefits of the Infinite Sea's nourishment were also evident.

The nascent, wild world greedily absorbed the power of the Infinite Sea as if it had been parched for a long time.

The distance between heaven and earth grew farther apart with each passing moment.

On the earth, mountains rose, rivers, seas, lakes, forests, and plains—various terrains emerged. It was no longer a barren and desolate land.

In the sky, the cracks formed from the extreme pressure were being repaired by the power brought by the Infinite Sea.

With Li Fan's special attention, as the sky grew higher and the earth expanded, the thirteen Heavenly Scars, each accumulated an enormous amount of energy equivalent to the entire Great Desolation.

Li Fan sensed that due to the accumulation of so much energy, these Heavenly Scars seemed to be developing a form of sentience.

After pondering for a long time, Li Fan ultimately chose not to inject a wisp of his divine sense into them to gain control, fearing the unknown consequences.

The Infinite Immortal power accumulated within the Heavenly Scars exceeded his current control. If he forcibly tried to dominate them, he might even suffer a backlash.

Li Fan merely refined and separated the connection channels between each Heavenly Scar and the Infinite Sea. As long as he held the connection channels, he had effectively attached reins to them, ensuring they wouldn't spiral out of control, regardless of their future evolution.

Inspired by this, when Li Fan sensed that this Great Desolation world was also gradually giving birth to consciousness, he deliberately divided this Great Desolation world into five regions: East, West, South, North, and Center.

Each region was connected to a different channel of the Infinite Sea.

Like a great river branching into tributaries, the consciousness of the Great Desolation world was also fragmented.

Li Fan's faint premonition of unease vanished along with this fragmentation.

"It seems that if the Great Desolation's consciousness were to be born, it would be too powerful. There was a risk of losing control." Li Fan mused.

Standing outside the heavens, Li Fan watched this Great Desolation world continue to evolve.

Endless immortal power poured down from the Infinite Sea.

Under immense pressure, the Great Desolation world, while growing, was also being compressed into an incredibly solid form.

"Externally shaped by the pressure of the Infinite Sea, and internally possessing adaptable properties that can devour all three thousand Great Daos through the Ink Slaughter Dao Net..."

"Even if I were to attack with my full strength, I might not be able to cause much damage to this continent."

"Moreover, it is still in a visible growth phase and seems far from reaching its limit. As long as the Infinite Sea continues to nourish it, it can continue to grow indefinitely..."

Li Fan watched the changes within, inwardly astonished.

He also had a feeling that with the birth of this continent within the high wall, it was as if a sturdy pillar had been added, strengthening the entire experimental field, making it feel considerably more "stable."

Chapter 1494: The Fifth Saint Monarch Takes Shape

During the period when the clone simulated the Sage Emperor's era, the cat-like creature, whose true nature was not fully understood, displayed three heaven-defying abilities: item replication, life-form simulation, and marrow cleansing.

Even Li Fan, who had now become the creator of a true Immortal Domain, could not easily replicate these feats.

And the cat-like creature was merely a vanguard of the hunt. The power of the forces behind it could be imagined.

Most importantly, Li Fan had a comprehensive understanding of the Star Sea's forces by now, yet he found no trace of anything related to the cat-like creature.

Therefore, the forces behind the cat-like creature either came from star systems far beyond,

or...

Perhaps from other possibilities!

If it were merely the former, it would be manageable. But if it were the latter...

Then he might need to re-evaluate the "fishing pond" hidden within the Xuanhuang Realm.

Currently, only one location within the high wall remained beyond Li Fan's control: the fishing pond.

Within the fishing pond, myriad treasures twinkled like starlight, all captured by the fishing pond from various places. However, the starscape of the [Primordial] possibility, which was depleted of life, seemed unable to support such a profusion of treasures.

The treasures within the fishing pond often possessed very distinct characteristics, almost as if each originated from a unique civilization. In the [Primordial] possibility, where the world was on the brink of destruction and even the Immortal Realm had been annihilated, it could no longer give birth to so many diverse cultivation civilizations.

The fishing pond connected to the true myriad worlds.

This was the fundamental reason why Li Fan, despite possessing the strength to easily handle Nameless True Immortals, had not dared to interfere with the fishing pond.

As long as he did not provoke it, the fishing pond, like a tranquil pond, remained as it was. Li Fan was unwilling to risk interfering.

In the past, Li Fan needed the various treasures within the fishing pond to aid his cultivation. But now...

Having understood the "Transformation between True and False," aside from 'Return to Truth,' there were no longer any treasures Li Fan felt he could not afford to part with.

The fishing pond and the cat-like creature's various aspects aside for now.

As Li Fan's scroll unfurled, the True Immortals of the Star Sea were already on their way to offer their congratulations.

Not wanting these people to discover the existence of the high wall, Li Fan had Li Biren and the three Heavenly Scars wait outside the high wall.

Soon, led by [Chaos], the True Immortals of the Star Sea stepped beyond the coverage of the Dao Net and entered the annihilation zone.

Compared to the past, after Li Fan actively absorbed the abundant Great Daos of the Star Sea, the annihilation zone near the high wall showed a slight resurgence of vitality. However, the areas destroyed by Dao Annihilation could not be restored, and the terrain remained narrow and elongated.

The moment the True Immortals set foot on it, they sensed the Dao path manifested by Li Biren.

"Interesting."

"Isn't this a variation of the [Dao Net]?"

"It's a pity those Immortal Hunt cultivators couldn't make it. Otherwise, seeing this path, their expressions would be very amusing." A voice emanated from the formless void leading the group.

Other True Immortals walking on the [Path] had varied expressions.

Having fought for so long, they were quite familiar with the Star Sea's Dao Net. In their opinion, the path beneath their feet seemed to be no inferior to the [Dao Net].

But how was this possible?

The Star Sea's Dao Net was built upon the foundation of multiple Nameless experts, supported by numerous True Immortals, and even that one who manipulated the Dao Net with a single hand...

Only through their combined efforts did such a creation emerge, allowing mortals to contend with True Immortals in an instant.

And this path, what was it based on?

Was it solely the personal achievement of that Hidden Emperor?

If so, then this Hidden Emperor's strength was likely far greater than they had anticipated.

As the Immortals looked ahead, their eyes were drawn to a stone pillar standing in the void.

The large character [Stillness] carved upon the pillar sent a chill down their spines.

They had all heard about the Immortal Hunt Elder Wei being suppressed and transformed into a pillar, but seeing it with their own eyes still sent a shiver down their spines.

"There's a reason he's called the 'Hidden Emperor.'" They thought to themselves.

Although they sympathized with Elder Wei, none proposed to rescue him.

Passing the stone pillar, Li Biren and the eleven to thirteen Heavenly Scars had been waiting for a long time.

"Esteemed guests, we meet again." Thirteen grinned, his tone sinister.

Eleven and Twelve also eyed the True Immortals before them like hunters sizing up their prey.

Having witnessed the power of the Infinite Sea emanating from Thirteen before, and now seeing two entirely comparable beings beside him, the Immortals couldn't help but feel nervous and uneasy.

Among the Immortals, only [Chaos] focused its attention entirely on Li Biren.

Sensing the unique aura of the Infinite Sea that Li Biren exuded after his recent return, 'Chaos's' attitude subtly shifted.

Li Biren manifested a seven-colored path, guiding the Immortals.

Stepping onto the path, they were enveloped by myriad rays of auspicious light. Their vision and hearing were obscured.

It was as if they were rapidly advancing, crossing thousands of mountains and rivers in an instant.

When the seven-colored auspicious light dissipated, the magnificent and sacred Great Desolation Immortal Realm suddenly appeared before the Immortals' eyes.

Even 'Chaos,' a Nameless True Immortal, froze abruptly.

Seeing it through a mere painting and experiencing it firsthand were two entirely different concepts.

What they had perceived from the painting was less than a ten-thousandth of what they felt now.

The heavens were high and the earth was vast, boundless and expansive.

Like a mirror-like expanse of lakes, mountains hidden in clouds, and palaces standing tall in the sky...

Overflowing with life, nurturing infinite possibilities.

What truly made the Immortals' expressions dazed, as if they had returned to their homeland, was the immense Infinite Immortal power permeating this realm.

They hadn't enjoyed such comfort in who knows how long.

Although their power possessed the characteristic of infinity the moment they reached True Immortal status,

they still cherished the atmosphere of being surrounded by [Infinity].

In their lives in the lower realm, despite their strength preventing substantial harm, their existence felt awkward. It was like being stuck in a muddy swamp; although they could still walk, the splashing mud made them uncomfortable.

Stepping into this Great Desolation Immortal Realm now was truly like a fish returning to water or a bird soaring through the sky.

It felt like coming home.

Many True Immortals shed tears on the spot.

They had fought fiercely in the harsh environment of the lower realm for so many years, never expecting to see the Immortal Realm again.

Even if it was merely an Immortal Domain, it was enough.

...

While the Immortals were overwhelmed with emotion, the Great Desolation Immortal Realm suddenly fell silent.

All living beings unified, looking up at the sky, holding their breath.

Then, they slowly bowed down.

The Immortals followed the gaze of the world's inhabitants and looked up.

Thirteen Heavenly Scars were distributed across the sky.

And five palaces, shrouded in purple mist, flickered in and out of existence beyond the heavens.

"Are those..." The Immortals vaguely glimpsed gazes emanating from these structures, resembling those of deities.

Looking down from above, they surveyed the Immortals.

The Immortals instantly felt the illusion of facing the ruling Immortal Emperor of the Immortal Realm they had encountered before.

Infinite immortal power surged around the Immortals like fierce winds, creating pressure that made it difficult for some True Immortals to remain calm, nearly causing them to bow down to these five figures.

However, 'Chaos,' a Nameless True Immortal, stopped them.

"Planetary Consciousnesses."

"One evolved into five."

As expected of the Nameless realm, they understood the true nature of the five figures outside the heavens with a single glance.

As the five planetary consciousnesses naturally born within the Great Desolation Immortal Realm, their strength surpassed that of the thirteen Heavenly Scars.

'Chaos' assessed that facing the thirteen Heavenly Scars, he could remain composed.

But facing these five rulers of the Great Desolation Immortal Realm...

"Unless I resort to my final trump card, it might be somewhat difficult." 'Chaos' inwardly evaluated.

"I never expected this Immortal Domain to have gathered so many powerful innate beings?"

This completely exceeded 'Chaos's' expectations.

In the past Immortal Realm, though vast and boundless, innate beings were extremely rare. And those capable of connecting to the Infinite Sea were even rarer.

But now, this one Immortal Domain had gathered them all!

"That Hidden Emperor, what exactly is he..."

'Chaos's' heart sank. He searched continuously, trying to find the Hidden Emperor who created this Immortal Domain.

But after searching everywhere, he still found nothing.

From this point on, he didn't need to search.

In the absolute silence of the world, Li Fan finally spoke.

His voice did not come from the heavens above or the earth below.

It emanated spontaneously from every corner of the Great Desolation Immortal Realm, as if it were omnipresent.

"After countless years, the Immortal Realm has been rebuilt. Its achievements are immortal, and today it is complete."

"Today, the Immortal Realm is newly established, and the Immortal Court begins."

"Title: Emperor Jun of the Central Cyan Heaven, the Great Emperor of Wuji."

"Title: Emperor Ziwei of the Eastern Azure Heaven, the Great Emperor of Cang Tian."

"Title: Emperor Jade of the Western Azure Heaven, the Great Emperor of Hao Tian."

"Title: Emperor Underworld of the Southern Yellow Heaven, the Great Emperor of Huang Tian."

"Title: Emperor Longevity of the Northern Dark Heaven, the Great Emperor of Xuan Tian."

...

With each pronouncement, the figures sitting in the five palaces beyond the heavens changed in appearance, gaining form and attire.

If they were previously like flowers in a mist, indistinct, then now, adorned with crowns and imperial robes, they were exceptionally clear.

The moment the five Planetary Consciousnesses received their titles from Li Fan, the sky and the earth beneath it formed natural barriers and boundaries.

The Great Desolation Immortal Realm was divided into the Central Jun Tian, Eastern Cang Tian, Western Hao Tian, Southern Huang Tian, and Northern Xuan Tian by the words echoing through the heavens and earth.

And the five Heavenly Emperors each resided in their respective heavens, sitting majestically.

Within the five regions of heaven, different environments began to evolve.

For instance, in the Northern Xuan Tian, where all things lived forever, the vitality was clearly more abundant than in other heavenly regions.

The Eastern Cang Tian represented supreme nobility. Life forms within this heavenly region, simply by existing within its bounds, spontaneously began to ascend in their life forms. In practical terms, the upper limit of Infinite Immortal power they could draw from the Infinite Sea began to slowly increase.

As for the Central Jun Tian, it was characterized by impartiality and peace. It was like an uncrowned king; though it did not contend, it achieved eternal victory.

...

With the enfeoffment of the five Heavenly Emperors, they became like five great mountains, pressing down upon the Immortals.

This pressure, emanating from the entire Great Desolation Immortal Realm, was beyond the capacity of these Immortals to resist.

Therefore, even though they were reluctant, they were forced to lower their heads, unable to meet the gaze of the five Heavenly Emperors.

Even 'Chaos,' a Nameless True Immortal, was no exception.

"These five Planetary Consciousnesses have become even stronger." 'Chaos' felt a shock in his heart.

"The voice echoing through heaven and earth should be the Hidden Emperor."

"It is because of his bestowal that the Planetary Consciousnesses have truly gained recognition from this world and are able to control the various aspects of heaven and earth..." 'Chaos's' thoughts raced.

Compared to the ruling Immortal Emperor of the past, who held authority within the Immortal Realm, this Hidden Emperor now possessed an even greater power.

"Relatively speaking, the ruling Immortal Emperor and the five ennobled emperors today are of the same caliber."

"Could it be..."

'Chaos's' heart trembled violently, and a bold speculation instantly surged into his mind.

"Has that Hidden Emperor embarked on the path of becoming a Sage?"

"Otherwise, his actions are difficult to explain?" 'Chaos's' heart could no longer remain calm.

There had been successive Immortal Emperors in the Immortal Realm, but the Four Sage Lords remained unchanged.

For an unknown expanse of time, the fifth Sage Lord had yet to be born.

"Could it be that with the destruction of the Immortal Realm, the fifth Sage Lord is about to emerge?"

'Chaos' lowered his head, trying to find the trace of the Hidden Emperor.

However, this Hidden Emperor seemed to have forgotten about them, the observing True Immortals.

After enfeoffing the Heavenly Emperors, the next to be enfeoffed were the thirteen Heavenly Scars.

The status of the Heavenly Scars was slightly lower than that of the Planetary Consciousnesses.

They were granted the title of "Revered Ones."

The originally formless Heavenly Scars instantly solidified and took shape upon being enfeoffed.

Some resembled primordial beasts, others towering mountains, and still others resembled ordinary mortals.

Their forms were diverse.

After the enfeoffment of the thirteen Revered Ones, the grand voice slowly faded.

The five Heavenly Emperors and the thirteen Revered Ones each began to select generals and soldiers from the living beings within the Immortal Realm.

The scene was bustling.

In contrast, the observing True Immortals from the Star Sea were left waiting.

After all the commotion finally subsided, a hundred days had passed.

And Li Fan, from beginning to end, had not appeared to meet them.

On this day, Thirteen, clad in ornate robes, appeared before all beings.

"Greetings, Revered One."

Led by 'Chaos,' a Nameless True Immortal, the other Immortals could only follow suit.

After being granted the title of Revered One, Thirteen's demeanor was no longer as frivolous as before.

"The Great Master has decreed that the ceremony of observation is complete. It is time for you to depart."

The Immortals were momentarily stunned.

"But we haven't even seen..."

"Hmm?" Thirteen's expression turned stern, and the disdain in his tone was evident.

He almost blurted out the words, "You don't deserve it," but managed to restrain himself.

"This Thirteen Revered One is also much stronger than before." 'Chaos' pondered for a moment before cupping his hands in a salute.

Then, leading the observing Immortals, they departed the Great Desolation Immortal Realm along the seven-colored path that reappeared.

"Ugh..."

Perhaps because they had stayed for too long in an environment filled with Infinite Immortal power, upon returning to the Star Sea, the Immortals instinctively felt a sense of discomfort.

The drastic difference caused them to instinctively look back towards the direction of the Great Desolation Immortal Realm.

Unfortunately, with the closure of the seven-colored path, they could no longer return.

It took the Immortals quite some time to re-adapt to the harsh environment of the Star Sea. Their expressions were varied, each lost in their own thoughts.

'Chaos' had fulfilled his mission and safely returned the Immortals. Furthermore, the information they provided was extremely valuable, especially their estimations of the Hidden Emperor's strength, which forced the Star Sea faction to re-evaluate their strategy.

However, 'Chaos' himself remained distracted since his return.

Chapter 1495: Tomb Wind Blows Through the Immortal Realm

Besides lingering thoughts of the Great Desolation Immortal Realm, 'Chaos' Nameless was more concerned about the Hidden Emperor himself.

Because in the ancient legends of the Immortal Realm, Sage Lords possessed the supreme divine ability to "draw forth True Immortals and transcend."

"Since the destruction of the Immortal Realm, the Four Sage Lords have all vanished without a trace. If this individual has embarked on the path of [Becoming a Sage], then perhaps..." Whenever 'Chaos' thought of this, an irresistible urge to revisit the Hidden Emperor and seek an audience welled up in his heart.

However, having attained enlightenment long ago, 'Chaos' still possessed some composure.

"This matter cannot be rushed. It requires careful planning."

"It would be best to contact the others. After all, with just me alone, I might not be worthy of the Sage Lord's attention."

'Chaos' pondered the legends he knew about the Four Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm in the past.

[Tai Yi], [Lian Shan], [Gui Hai], [Jing Fen].

Sage Lord Tai Yi, rumored to be the first living being in the world. He witnessed the world's creation from nothingness, and his wisdom was unparalleled.

Sage Lord Lian Shan, who, within the [Upper Mountain], opened the path to immortality. He was the first immortal in the world, and his strength was truly immeasurable. If one were to determine the strength of True Immortals based on the Upper Mountain, then Sage Lord Lian Shan, standing at its pinnacle, would undoubtedly be the one.

Sage Lord Gui Hai, who opened the [Infinite Spring], causing a qualitative leap in the strength of Immortals. After countless years of excavation, the Infinite Spring transformed into the boundless Infinite Sea, granting every True Immortal in the Immortal Realm inexhaustible resources. Mastering the sea to control the mountain, his power was in no way inferior to Sage Lord Lian Shan.

Sage Lord Jing Fen...

The moment the name came to mind, 'Chaos' instinctively felt a chill run down his spine.

He instinctively recited an incantation, and only then did the intense fear slowly subside.

Sage Lord Jing Fen was born after the Immortal Realm reached its peak of prosperity, and he was also the last Sage Lord to attain enlightenment in the history of the Immortal Realm.

Although the Immortal Realm had pioneered the method of infinity, the cycle of Dao's birth and death, Dao's growth and decay, was still within the natural order. Even the Immortal Realm could not escape it.

However, the Immortal Realm was filled with vitality and lacked the decay of Dao everywhere, all thanks to Sage Lord Jing Fen, who used himself as a grave to bury the Great Daos of the heavens. This ensured that Dao's decay and annihilation would not affect the flourishing Immortal Realm. Only when the Great Dao cycled and Dao began to grow anew would Sage Lord Jing Fen release the Great Dao.

"Jing Fen devours Dao and opens cycles, upon the desolate mausoleum."

This was an ancient proverb passed down in the Immortal Realm.

It was precisely because the Four Sage Lords stood like pillars supporting the Immortal Realm's sky that it became a boundless, vast, and infinitely vibrant paradise for Immortals.

Yet, it was precisely because the Four Sage Lords were too burdened with responsibility and unable to manage the Immortals that the Immortal Realm had successive Immortal Emperors.

In the early days of the Immortal Realm, True Immortals still knew the names of the Four Sage Lords and often recited words of gratitude. But over time, as years passed and the Four Sage Lords did not appear for a long time, although the Immortals did not forget them, they gradually faded from memory, becoming mere symbols in their minds.

wWw OOC

If the Four Sage Lords had remained consistent, perhaps the subsequent events would not have unfolded. The turning point began when Sage Lord Jing Fen "went on strike."

Although it seemed disrespectful to say so, the reality was thus.

After burying and sorting the decaying Great Daos of the Immortal Realm for an unknown number of years, this Fourth Sage Lord of the Immortal Realm suddenly "went on strike" one day.

With three loud laughs, he exhaled all the decaying Great Daos that had not yet completed their cycle.

That corrosive wind, capable of annihilating all immortal Dao, instantly swept across the entire Immortal Realm. Countless immortal servants, immortal puppets, and immortal artifacts decayed upon contact with this "Grave Wind." Even True Immortals and Nameless True Immortals could not escape this Qi of Dao decay. The Immortal Realm suffered immeasurable losses.

However, in the face of the Infinite energy source of the Immortal Realm, this loss was insignificant. With some time, it could be repaired.

The key was that Sage Lord Jing Fen had stopped working.

Dao's decay and annihilation could no longer be dealt with. They could only be left unattended, or the Immortals could only avoid them.

Furthermore, because it became imbued with infinite properties, this Dao decay and annihilation became even more powerful. It not only transformed into a corrosive wind that attacked various parts of the Immortal Realm from time to time but also manifested numerous apocalyptic destructive phenomena that descended irregularly upon the Immortal Realm and even the lower star sea.

One of the four pillars suddenly vanished.

This was bound to bring immense chaos to the Immortal Realm.

It was said that Sage Lords Tai Yi, Lian Shan, and Gui Hai, unable to bear witness to the suffering of the Immortal Realm, had jointly persuaded the somewhat "capricious" Sage Lord Jing Fen.

The final outcome is unknown.

However, after a brief disappearance of three thousand years, the anomalies in the Immortal Realm began to gradually emerge in various places.

However, instead of a large-scale outbreak, it started from scratch, with increasing intensity and frequency. At least it gave the Immortals a considerable period to adapt.

Under the direction of the three Sage Lords, the ruling Immortal Emperor enfeoffed numerous Nameless experts to suppress the "Grave Wind" anomalies in various regions. With the combined efforts of the Immortals, the chaos in the Immortal Realm was finally brought under control.

'Chaos' was one of these many Nameless experts.

That was a long time ago. So long that when 'Chaos' Nameless recalled this event, he could no longer be certain how many Immortal Emperors had reigned in the Immortal Realm since then.

Later, the Immortals of the Immortal Realm gradually adapted to the various anomalies brought about by the Grave Wind and slowly forgot its origin. They simply accepted it as the natural state of the Immortal Realm.

In truth, what in the Immortal Realm was truly innate?

Although Sage Lord Jing Fen withdrew from worldly affairs, he did not disappear entirely. All those who criticized his actions, even in their hearts, were sensed by him.

These True Immortals, without exception, were captured by Sage Lord Jing Fen and thrown into his belly.

Keep in mind that Sage Lord Jing Fen could absorb and transform even decaying Great Daos. To him, Enlightened True Immortals of the Immortal Realm were almost indistinguishable from delicious food.

They were powerless to resist and were all transformed into corrosive Grave Wind.

At that time, countless True Immortals in the Immortal Realm verbally condemned Sage Lord Jing Fen, but none were spared. He treated them all equally.

After this cleansing, the Immortal Realm felt almost "emptied."

This was a great calamity in the early days of the Immortal Realm.

But it was only a calamity for the True Immortals at that time.

For the Immortal Realm as a whole, history later proved it to be a blessing.

After Sage Lord Jing Fen devoured numerous Immortals, after many more years, he gradually released the Daos comprehended by the True Immortals.

Some of these Daos replenished the Immortal Realm's heaven and earth, while others quickly found new masters.

The Immortal Realm once again flourished.

However, after this incident, very few people remembered Sage Lord Jing Fen.

Only the proverb "Jing Fen devours Immortals and initiates Dao, upon the desolate mausoleum" remained in the hearts of the few surviving True Immortals.

Due to Sage Lord Jing Fen's "resignation," the subsequent ability of the Sage Lords to "point and draw forth True Immortals to transcend" became known to the world.

Sage Lord Jing Fen's act of devouring numerous Immortals not only incited fear among them but also awe. Some True Immortals were so shocked by the power displayed by Sage Lord Jing Fen that they became even more devout, even fanatical.

Most of these "believers" were ignored by Sage Lord Jing Fen.

However, due to constant contemplation, Sage Lord Jing Fen saw through their inner thoughts.

Three of them received his favor.

They were then "pointed and drawn forth" and, before the eyes of all, transcended and departed.

This further fueled the madness of Sage Lord Jing Fen's believers.

Later, another wave of cleansing occurred, and the slanderers and fervent believers disappeared from the world.

Only a faint four-character title remained in the world.

As for where Sage Lord Jing Fen went after the destruction of the Immortal Realm,

'Chaos' Nameless did not know.

...

"The Hidden Emperor's strength is definitely inferior to the Four Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm."

"However, since he has embarked on the path of [Becoming a Sage], then perhaps 'pointing and drawing forth True Immortals to transcend' is not difficult for him."

"After all, the various Heavenly Emperors and Heavenly Scars in the Great Desolation Immortal Realm indicate his close connection with the Infinite Sea."

"And to achieve transcendence and cross the shore, this is the most crucial point."

...

'Chaos's' thoughts churned. After a long pause, instead of seeking out other Nameless experts,

he summoned 'Wu Xian.'

Among the Star Sea cultivators, this individual had the most contact with the Hidden Emperor.

Over the past hundred years, he had been responsible for running errands and delivering messages.

After thoroughly inquiring about every detail of Wu Xian's interactions with the Hidden Emperor, 'Chaos' attempted to gauge the Hidden Emperor's temperament.

"It seems he is not particularly difficult to approach."

"Relatively speaking."

In 'Chaos' Nameless's view, the method of transforming beings into stone pillars was hardly noteworthy.

After dismissing Wu Xian, 'Chaos' pondered and ultimately decided that a prompt decision was necessary.

Thus, the Nameless experts of the Star Sea gathered once more.

The first to speak was the black-robed figure with the white cat: "What we see is not necessarily the truth. The Hidden Emperor might not truly be a Hidden Emperor. Even if the Great Desolation Immortal Realm was indeed created by him, it doesn't necessarily indicate his true strength. After the destruction of the Immortal Realm, the Administrative Immortal Emperor's authority also disappeared. Perhaps this person was simply lucky and obtained the authority, masquerading now."

"If he were a true former Immortal Emperor, he would have approached us long ago upon descending to the lower realm."

"How could he have quietly lived beside us for so many years?" The black cat on the white-robed figure's shoulder spoke, its tone laced with sarcasm.

The pair of large blue hands also chimed in, "The region occupied by that Hidden Emperor... is somewhat peculiar."

"It is the territory of the Sage Merchant."

Upon hearing the name "Sage Merchant," the expressions of the True Immortals in the hall changed to varying degrees.

During their previous battles with the Immortal Hunt, the greatest losses they suffered were often inflicted by the Sage Merchant.

After a moment of silence, 'Chaos' spoke, "Brother Bo Yan, I believe you are overthinking. No matter how formidable the Sage Merchant was, they cannot compare to that Hidden Emperor."

"Indeed, they developed many powerful artifacts, some even capable of severely injuring us. However, none of them involved the Infinite Sea. This is the most crucial point."

The black cat immediately retorted: "'Chaos,' you may not be aware, but the Sage Merchant's predecessor was the Merchant Immortal Boat, which split from the Profound Merchant Immortal Boat. If there is a Sage Merchant, why wouldn't there be another Sage Profound in this world?"

"Furthermore, the Sage Merchant did not master the power related to the Infinite Sea? I doubt that. The Sage Merchant disappeared from the star sea in a single day. Wasn't that an escape to another possibility? Without the connection to infinite power, how could they achieve that?"

The black cat's words left 'Chaos' speechless.

However, due to his experiences in the Immortal Realm, 'Chaos' would not engage in verbal disputes and remained silent.

The white-robed figure stroked the black cat on its shoulder, and the black cat's voice abruptly ceased. It seemed to have regained control.

The white-robed figure said, "The black cat's reasoning is not without merit. Upon reflection, the Hidden Emperor's sudden appearance does have many illogical aspects."

"However..."

The white-robed figure smiled. "None of this matters."

"The key is, what is his true strength?"

"If we can defeat him, regardless of whether he is a Hidden Emperor or something else. Everything in the Great Desolation Immortal Realm will belong to us. Even the authority connecting to the Infinite Sea..."

His words left the Immortals' hearts stirred, their expressions uncontainable.

Only 'Chaos' was stunned.

He truly could not comprehend how his seemingly rational companions could make such a foolish judgment.

His gaze inadvertently flickered towards the black cat on the white-robed figure's shoulder. After a long pause, he spoke with difficulty.

"Esteemed Brothers, do you remember the Great Sage Jing Fen of the past?"

"Great Sage Jing Fen?"

This was an ancient name.

At least half of the attendees had never heard this title and looked bewildered.

The remaining ones who had heard it instinctively showed a trace of fear in their eyes.

But they quickly retorted: "Brother 'Chaos,' you are mistaken! That Hidden Emperor merely created a small Immortal Land. How can he be compared to Great Sage Jing Fen?"

"That Great Desolation Immortal Realm, however grand it sounds, is actually smaller in scale than my former cave dwelling. Hmph, if the Immortal Realm still existed..."

"Brother 'Chaos,' you are exaggerating. If the Hidden Emperor truly possessed the power of Great Sage Jing Fen, then we would simply be his food."

...

Listening to the varying refutations from his companions, 'Chaos' Nameless gradually understood.

The reason they arrived at completely different judgments from his own was primarily threefold.

Firstly, they had not personally visited the Great Desolation Immortal Realm. They had not experienced firsthand the Hidden Emperor's majesty when he established the Immortal Court and enfeoffed the Heavenly Emperors. Hearing only his descriptions, they easily made the wrong judgment.

Secondly, they had become greedy for the authority connecting to the Infinite Sea, which the Hidden Emperor had revealed.

Thirdly, and most crucially.

The black cat, representing an unknown force behind it, gave these True Immortals confidence.

"The Star Sea Sea, gathering Immortals, is indeed more diverse than a single corner like the Star Sea."

"But..."

Recalling the voice from beyond the heavens that echoed outside the Great Desolation Immortal Realm, 'Chaos' quickly made his decision.

"You all decide for yourselves."

"As for me, I am not going."

Chapter 1496: Truly the Limit

The resolution of Nameless Chaos caused the Immortals of the Azure Star Sea to burst into laughter. However, Chaos had always acted with caution, and the Immortals were used to it.

The man in white stroked the black cat on his shoulder and quipped, "Don't worry, Brother Chaos. Once we capture that imposter Hidden Emperor, there will definitely be a palace in the heavenly dome of the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm for you. After all, even if you didn't contribute, you certainly labored."

The other Immortals chimed in their agreement.

Chaos, however, did not seem angered.

Although Shan Hua's words were a bit harsh, since he had spoken publicly, he would never go back on his word. In this way, it was all the more beneficial to Chaos.

If it turned out that Chaos was mistaken and the Hidden Emperor was truly a paper tiger, then with his past achievements, he would still be able to secure a place in the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm.

And if they were all gravely mistaken…

Nameless Chaos secretly began to calculate his options.

"It's a pity that 'Ni' is not here now, otherwise, we wouldn't have to go through all this trouble," Nameless Chaos glanced at the black cat on Shan Hua's shoulder and let out a cold snort in his heart.

…

Li Fan was currently unaware of the events unfolding in the Azure Star Sea.

Since bestowing titles upon the five Heavenly Emperors of the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm that day, a completely new sensation, unprecedented in his heart, had surged within him.

Taking it as 'casting a long line to catch a big fish,' he directly put aside the matter of Nameless Chaos and the others, focusing solely on studying this change.

The origin of this sensation was precisely from the 'Sitting and Enjoying the Fruits of Labor' technique.

Li Fan had assumed that after reaching the Half-Immortal stage, this method of passively benefiting would become obsolete. And indeed, it seemed to be as he had thought; regardless of how many cultivators he had indirectly or directly assisted in their cultivation, he had received no feedback whatsoever.

Until this grand enfeoffment.

After the establishment of the Five Heavenly Emperors, the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm was finally stabilized, transitioning from its fabricated state to a true Immortal Domain.

It now stood upon the 'Upper Mountain.'

And Li Fan, who had facilitated this, felt as if a veil had been lifted the moment it was accomplished. It was as if a stepping stone had appeared beneath his feet, allowing him to ascend slightly higher. The scenery before his eyes instantly transformed, revealing myriad wonders.

"So, it's not that the 'Sitting and Enjoying the Fruits of Labor' technique has become ineffective. It's just that after attaining the Immortal path, ordinary feedback is no longer sufficient to propel my progress. Only the creation of an Immortal Domain from nothingness can barely suffice." Li Fan's heart became clear.

Although his strength had not changed in the slightest, precisely because of this minuscule 'elevation,' his perception of the Shouqiu projection within the high wall, the Hungry Immortal, the Wuji Heavenly Pillar, and others, felt entirely different compared to before.

"Looking down from a height, a sense of familiarity and mastery." The words 'looking down from a height, a sense of familiarity and mastery' spontaneously appeared in Li Fan's mind.

After a brief period of contemplation, Li Fan clearly understood the origin of this feeling.

Whether it was the Shouqiu projection or the various Heavenly Pillars, Li Fan had spent over a hundred years in seclusion comprehending them. If not intimately familiar, he was at least very acquainted with them.

And the feedback from the 'Sitting and Enjoying the Fruits of Labor' technique, based on this foundation of familiarity, had doubled this familiarity after the creation of the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm.

It had saved Li Fan a hundred years of effort.

Li Fan's eyes narrowed.

In an instant, he scanned himself and discovered that it wasn't just his comprehension of the Shouqiu projection and the Heavenly Pillars. Everything he had learned and known had nearly doubled with this slight upward 'ascension.'

Even his Ink Slaughter Myriad Manifestations Dao Net was included.

This terrifying rate of progress made Li Fan himself incredulous. After repeated confirmation, he had no choice but to accept this fact.

"An inch higher on the 'Upper Mountain' represents an earth-shattering and heaven-defying change!"

"The increase in strength is not a uniform progression as one ascends; rather, the higher one stands, the exponentially greater the increase in cultivation!"

"No wonder the gap between True Immortals and True Immortals, and between Nameless and Nameless, within the same major realm, can be so unimaginably vast."

"It's even greater than the gap between cultivators in the lower realms."

"Give me a billion cultivators who have merged with the Dao, and purely by numbers, I could surround and kill Supremacy experts like Changsheng and even Tianyi. But…"

"Similarly, a billion True Immortals might still not be a match for any single one of the Four Sage Lords."

Li Fan looked back at his past self before this comprehension.

Excluding any external forces, if he were to rely solely on his own strength, the current Li Fan could easily suppress his pre-creation self.

"The 'Upper Mountain' possesses such a unique nature, leading to unimaginable disparity even among those within the same realm of True Immortals and Nameless True Immortals."

"After all, theoretically speaking, so-called Transcendent experts are also considered to be within the ranks of Nameless True Immortals."

Only by personally ascending can one truly know the height of the mountain.

This was Li Fan's first personal advancement in strength since reaching Half-Immortal, and he could already glimpse a corner of the grand and unfathomable 'Upper Mountain.'

"It's truly difficult to imagine how powerful those Sage Lords standing at the apex of all Immortals truly are."

"And the 'Infinite Sea' and the 'Upper Mountain' themselves…" Li Fan's heart yearned for them profoundly.

After a period of deep contemplation, his thoughts returned to reality.

Li Fan looked at the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm he had personally crafted below. He could faintly sense that with his continuous irrigation of Infinite Immortal power day and night, it had already become a part of the 'Mountains and Seas.'

Even if he were to sever the connection between the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm and the Infinite Sea, he could not alter this fact.

"This is the 'price.'"

"Everything in the mortal world, compared to the 'Infinite Sea' and the 'Upper Mountain,' is not of the same caliber. Although one can ingenaturally borrow their strength, the result is being eroded by the power of Mountains and Seas and becoming a part of them."

"The Immortal Realm is like this. True Immortals are also like this."

"When the Mountains and Seas eventually merge, that will be the time when the debts of Dao Annihilation are repaid."

All the scenes he had witnessed in his past reincarnations now replayed before his eyes. The so-called Dao Annihilation, the so-called tribulations, could not escape this pattern.

"This is the realization that arose in my heart after I truly established an Immortal Domain."

"Although I consider myself to have decent comprehension, those former Immortal Emperors and even the Four Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm – their talents were undoubtedly no less than mine."

"How could they not understand these principles?"

"They stood higher, and thus saw further."

…

Li Fan couldn't help but look up towards the 'Upper' direction.

"Therefore, they knew this day would come, and thus sought to climb higher and higher before the merging of Mountains and Seas."

"The lifespan displayed on the 'True Revelation' panel represents the lifespan of the entire 'Mortal World.' However, it may not fully reflect the lifespans of the 'Infinite Sea' and the 'Upper Mountain.'"

"The merging of Mountains and Seas is a trend. However, trends always have an endpoint."

A flash of lightning split the fog in Li Fan's mind.

In an instant, it was as if he had leaped out of the mortal world and saw only the boundless Mountains and Seas before his eyes.

When the Mountains and Seas merged, the mortal world below would vanish with this fusion.

The great tide of Dao Annihilation would continue to press towards the mountains.

The powerful beings on the mountainside would all ascend upwards.

"If one climbs high enough, perhaps they can escape the calamity of the merging of Mountains and Seas!"

Li Fan felt as though he had reached the summit of the Upper Mountain, gazing down at the tumultuous waves below. His heart trembled, and this thought uncontrollably surfaced.

But then, he inevitably thought: "Just how high does one need to climb to avoid the fate of the merging of Mountains and Seas?"

"Shouqiu Gong, the Four Sage Lords?"

"Or…"

"'True Revelation'?!"

As inspiration struck, Li Fan's mind suddenly recalled this treasured item that had accompanied him for so long.

And this time, 'True Revelation' responded, though its response was peculiar.

It neither confirmed nor denied.

It merely conveyed a sense of low emotion.

And the mere negative emotion displayed by 'True Revelation' had an immense impact on Li Fan.

"Perhaps no matter how high one climbs, annihilation is inevitable."

"Ascending the Upper Mountain is incredibly difficult with each step. Missing the initial opportunity when the Upper Mountain was first opened, how can one catch up now…"

"In the past, when I cultivated in the Xuanhuang Realm, thanks to 'True Revelation,' I always had absolute confidence. As long as I was given enough reincarnation time, I could gradually strengthen myself step by step. From Qi Refining to Foundation Establishment, to Core Formation and Nascent Soul. Ultimately, I could even trample upon those in the Longevity Realm. But now…"

"The Upper Mountain has stood for millennia, and at this point, where do I begin?"

"The projection left by Shouqiu Gong is already so powerful. What would Shouqiu Gong's true strength be? And if Shouqiu Gong is already like this, what about the Four Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm?"

"Based on what grounds can I hope to surpass them?"

Li Fan's gaze became increasingly lost, gradually falling into a daze.

Just as Li Fan was about to be consumed by despair, 'True Revelation,' thankfully, sensed something was amiss. It completely retracted its emotional fluctuations.

Without the influence of 'True Revelation,' Li Fan gradually emerged from this 'inner demon.'

Even though he had experienced countless reincarnations, he couldn't help but break out in a cold sweat.

Li Fan was by no means a passive person.

He always believed that as long as he possessed 'True Revelation,' he would one day achieve complete transcendence and freedom.

But the emotional stirrings of 'True Revelation' were merely an incidental trigger. The fundamental issue was Li Fan's daze and slight despair after finally glimpsing the scenery atop the 'Upper Mountain.'

The gap between him and those powerful beings standing at the pinnacle of Mountains and Seas was simply too vast. So vast that even with his infinite reincarnation ability, he lacked the absolute confidence to bridge it.

Especially as Li Fan's strength grew and he drew closer to these powerful beings, the risks he would face would inevitably increase. And the external forces he could rely on would become increasingly scarce.

The experts among Mountains and Seas were limited. The surrounding cliffs were bare, leaving no room for leverage.

How could he cross that chasm, let alone surpass them?

If it were in the past, as long as the 'Transformation between True and False,' his ultimate trump card, was present, he would not have been affected by such negative emotions.

But the current situation was extremely peculiar.

Because even 'True Revelation' itself was affected by this pessimistic emotion, dragging Li Fan down with it.

After 'True Revelation' suppressed its emotions, it fell silent, and all previous events seemed like an illusion.

But Li Fan's trembling body indicated that the experience he had just gone through was not a figment of his imagination.

It took him a long time, relying on immense willpower, before Li Fan could temporarily break free from that emotional state. However, Li Fan himself knew that the shadow had not been completely erased.

It still existed in a corner of his heart, ready to erupt at any moment.

Li Fan closed his eyes, erased the gloom from within, and then reopened them.

What truly concerned him was not his momentary loss of focus. After all, this was not the first or second time.

It was precisely the emotional fluctuations of 'True Revelation' that were truly beyond his expectations.

"After witnessing all of Mountains and Seas, have I finally glimpsed the limit of 'True Revelation'?"

Li Fan was slightly lost in thought, filled with endless emotion.

Once upon a time, he had always believed 'True Revelation' was omnipotent. As long as he possessed the treasured item, he could forge ahead relentlessly.

Now, it seemed he was finally reaching the point where he had to rely on himself.

Li Fan's expression was as deep as dark water.

He knew that 'almost reaching' was still a long way off. However, it was now within his 'sight.'

It was no longer distant.

Facing Li Fan's myriad thoughts, 'True Revelation' seemed to have returned to the state it was in when Li Fan first began cultivating, without any emotional fluctuations.
