Li Fan stood erect like a statue, motionless.

Until faint fluctuations from outside the high wall disturbed him.

The commotion was so great that it almost made the path constructed by Li Biren unsustainable.

Li Fan looked coldly into the distance.

The ones arriving were the Immortals of the Azure Star Sea.

Led by Nameless Wu Xian, the True Immortals of the Azure Star Sea had arrived together at the high wall.

"We heard that Senior has recreated the Immortal Realm and the Immortal Court with great divine power. We are filled with admiration and have come uninvited, hoping to witness its wonders." The voice of the figure in white spoke loudly.

This voice seemed to possess infinite magic. Upon reaching Li Fan's ears, all the emotions that had arisen from the unexpected incident with 'True Revelation' instantly dissipated.

Li Fan even inexplicably felt a sense of joy for a moment.

It was as if an old friend he hadn't seen in years had come to visit.

Overjoyed, Li Fan was about to wave his hand to invite the Immortals of the Azure Star Sea in.

Suddenly, his heart trembled, and he detached himself from the illusion.

"Hmm?"

"What was that just now…"

"Shan Hua?"

Li Fan's eyes narrowed, a hint of danger flashing within them.

"It's worthy of being a Nameless True Immortal. Even I was almost misled by him."

"Fortunately, I possess [Wuji]. No matter what divine abilities any Great Dao possesses, all can be ignored."

Having regained his senses, Li Fan did not change his actions.

As if he had been mesmerized by the power of 'Shan Hua,' completely unperturbed by their uninvited arrival, he let out a hearty laugh and directly welcomed the Immortals of the Azure Star Sea inside.

Li Fan keenly sensed that among these visitors, there appeared to be some unfamiliar faces.

And that 'Nameless Chaos' was not among them.

Li Fan instantly understood their intentions.

"Since my Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm has just been established and is still rather empty."

Having encountered the 'True Revelation' incident, Li Fan's mood was less than pleasant.

And coincidentally, the Azure Star Sea cultivators had come knocking on his door.

In the grand scheme of things, their tragic fate was already sealed.

Of course, at this moment, these True Immortals were still unaware.

They were still immersed in the shock of arriving in the Immortal Domain for the first time.

Chapter 1497: Swallowing the Heretics Whole

After the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm was officially established and stood upon the Upper Mountain, with the blessing of the Five Heavenly Emperors and Thirteen Heavenly Scars, it underwent earth-shattering changes with every passing moment.

Now connected to the Infinite Sea, there were no longer any constraints on energy sources. The officially enfeoffed administrators of the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm could freely reshape the world according to their own desires.

Therefore, compared to the realm witnessed by Nameless Chaos not long ago, the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm had undergone significant transformations. The five Heavenly Domains each evolved into different landscapes.

As the saying goes, "When one person attains the Dao, even their chickens and dogs ascend to heaven." The strength of all living beings within each Heavenly Domain also increased with time.

This scene of vigorous vitality indeed far exceeded the expectations of the Immortals of the Azure Star Sea.

Although its scale could not compare to the former Immortal Realm, in terms of liveliness, it had long surpassed it.

"It doesn't matter, my Shan Hua ability is still effective. Even if they have numbers on their side, we only need to go for the 'yellow dragon'," the white-robed figure transmitted telepathically to stabilize the wavering morale of the Immortals.

The black cat on the white robe's shoulder also chimed in, "As long as we can successfully meet that Hidden Emperor this time, with the treasure's blessing, no matter what divine abilities he possesses, he will surely be defeated on the spot. Capture the leader and the followers will disperse. The beings within this Immortal Domain can be used by us instead."

The treasure mentioned by the black cat seemed highly convincing, and the Immortals' emotions quickly stabilized.

Looking at the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm, their greed reignited.

Led by the white-robed Shan Hua, the Immortals had a brief tour before bowing deeply towards the heavens, "Senior's recreation of the Immortal Realm is truly an unprecedented achievement. It can be compared to the Four Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm and Shouqiu Gong."

"We admire you immensely and truly hope to meet Senior's divine presence soon…"

As if highly satisfied with the white-robed figure's flattery, various auspicious phenomena occurred within the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm. Golden light rained down like blossoms. From the thirteen Heavenly Scars, various colorful halos erupted. It sounded like the roar of the sea wind, echoing throughout the Immortal Domain.

This was a sign of the Infinite Sea freely releasing its Infinite Immortal power.

"As expected, this Hidden Emperor controls the authority!" Among the Immortals, several Nameless beings, including Shan Hua, could not conceal their excitement.

"Ever since Emperor Tian Luo caused great disaster, the Immortal Realm was destroyed, and the Four Sage Lords vanished, it was thought that this authority had disappeared without a trace. Who knew it would reappear in this lower realm Hidden Emperor… Everyone, if we can seize the authority, we can truly rebuild the Immortal Realm upon the Dao Net!"

"Moreover, it will be a mobile Immortal Realm that floats above Dao Annihilation! We will never have to worry about Dao Annihilation again!" The black cat's words were extremely provocative, seemingly possessing a magical charm that solidified the determination of the Immortals who were hesitant.

Kill the Hidden Emperor, seize the authority!

"You, please come up!" A thunderous voice echoed from beyond the heavenly dome of the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm. Perhaps due to Shan Hua's earlier flattery, the voice held a hint of pride.

The moment the voice appeared, all sentient beings within the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm knelt down. Even the Five Heavenly Emperors in the heavenly palaces revealed themselves and bowed towards the true master of the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm.

The Azure Star Sea Immortals also confirmed the true identity of the owner of this voice. It was undoubtedly the Hidden Emperor.

A silver path descended from beyond the heavenly dome, like a flowing ribbon, reaching before the Immortals.

Sensing the envious emotions of all beings in the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm, the Immortals suppressed their inner excitement and stepped onto the path.

"Wait, Shan Hua, this path…"

"A Dao Net?"

"Hiss… Could it be that the Hidden Emperor has helpers?"

The reason why the Azure Star Sea Immortals asked such a question was because the Azure Star Sea's Dao Net was created by the combined efforts of the Immortals. Now, a similar creation appeared in the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm, so how could they not be astonished and uncertain?

"No need to worry, it's just a gathering of a few Dao paths. How can it be compared to the 'Sen Luo Dao Net'? If he didn't have such power, how could he have created an Immortal Domain?" Shan Hua tried to appease them.

After exchanging glances with the black cat on his shoulder, his expression became even more serious.

The Immortals followed the heavenly path, disappearing from the eyes of the beings of the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm.

The next moment, they found themselves in a realm of darkness.

This darkness, of unknown origin or birth, could actually block the Immortals' senses!

It caused them to suddenly lose their sight, unable to distinguish north from south, east from west.

"Where is Senior?" The Immortals, though surprised, did not panic and gathered around Shan Hua.

But there was no response.

What awaited them in the darkness was utter silence.

"Brother Shan Hua, something seems to be wrong." Someone among the Immortals reminded them.

The black cat suddenly let out a yelp, "It's Dao Annihilation!"

The Immortals were slightly stunned before looking at the surrounding darkness and suddenly realizing.

The dark aura around them felt identical to the desolate areas after being cleansed by Dao Annihilation, as if they shared the same origin. However, they were not exactly similar, which was why they had failed to distinguish it at first.

The Immortals began to realize that this place was a trap.

But after all, they were beings who had survived the ancient tribulations, and when they genuinely encountered a crisis, they did not descend into chaos for a moment.

"He dares not reveal his true self and only resorts to trickery, which only shows his inner weakness."

"Fellow Daoist, please take out your treasure!"

…

The Immortals had various expressions, but most looked towards the black cat on Shan Hua's shoulder.

Although Shan Hua Nameless maintained a calm expression, a surge of doubt couldn't help but rise in his heart.

His Shan Hua ability had clearly not failed. In fact, its effect on the surroundings had remained unchanged from beginning to end. So why did the Hidden Emperor's attitude change so drastically after entering this space?

"Could it be that, from the very beginning, he was not affected by me at all? And intended to lure us in?"

Once this thought arose, it could no longer be dispelled.

Shan Hua's heart gradually grew cold.

His Shan Hua Dao principle was indeed powerful. As long as one could not resist the influence of Shan Hua, they had no room for resistance before him and could only be slaughtered at his will.

But conversely, if the other party could ignore Shan Hua…

Then he, a Nameless True Immortal, was no different from a lamb waiting to be slaughtered.

Just as he was about to discuss countermeasures with the black cat on his shoulder, a cold voice suddenly sounded from the darkness.

"Since you all wish to meet me so badly…"

"Then I shall grant your wish."

The darkness gradually receded, and the Heavenly Pillars that had been hidden in the darkness also appeared in the Immortals' vision.

From heaven to earth, they stood in solitude, seemingly recounting tragic past events.

Looking at the Heavenly Pillars before them, waves of coldness rose from the Immortals' hearts.

They found it hard to believe: "That is… the Southern Immortal Heavenly Pillar?! How is that possible! Didn't it completely disappear into Dao Annihilation along with the Tai Li Star Domain and the Ancient Realm of Sentient Beings?"

"This one is the Heavenly Pillar of Hunger?"

"This one… I can't sense it at all!"

The Immortals gradually fell into panic.

Primordial, Hungry Immortal, Grand Master Tiandu, Situ Xing.

The four Heavenly Pillars struck their hearts like four heavy hammers.

And surrounded by the four pillars, a figure stood silently.

He looked at the Immortals, as if surveying livestock in a pen, awaiting slaughter.

Being scrutinized by such a gaze, the Immortals felt both anger and fear.

"There is no need for alarm, everyone. Watch as I capture them!"

The black cat's green eyes locked onto Li Fan from afar, revealing a hint of mockery.

Then, it leaped forward, instantly closing the distance to Li Fan.

Two resplendent green lights shot out.

Transforming into a saber and a sword, they instantly surrounded Li Fan.

The black cat's sudden pounce was within Li Fan's expectations, but the green saber and sword emanating from its eyes were somewhat out of his control.

Because Li Fan discovered that the protective [Wuji] power surrounding him was actually ineffective against this pair of green saber and sword!

Goosebumps instantly erupted on his skin, and his heart pounded with alarms.

"Not within the Dao principles of the [Primordial] possibility?"

In an instant, Li Fan understood.

He vaguely saw a world of only weapons within these green saber and sword, as if it had suffered a world-ending calamity, leaving life extinct and only countless blades of ice remaining.

He didn't know how many years had passed. These 'artifacts' settled in the desolate starry sky, and out of instinct, they imitated their former masters.

They gradually occupied the Heavenly Daos.

The Dao struggle between artifacts was even more brutal than that between humans.

Without any emotional factors, it was relentless and absolute.

As artifacts fought and merged,

In the end, only a saber and a sword remained in that cold starry sky!

[Dao Saber Dao Sword]!

Like the Dao Dissolving Mother Stone, what the black cat was using now was actually the manifestation of a complete Great Dao within a possibility!

Even though it was a desolate possibility after a calamity, it was still the fusion of a complete Great Dao.

As the green saber and sword approached, Li Fan found himself seemingly trapped in a desperate situation.

The two cold auras of killing intent had firmly locked onto him.

Even any formations, divine abilities, or Dao techniques seemed unable to block the attack of this saber and sword!

"No wonder these True Immortals, despite knowing everything about the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm, were still so confident and insisted on provoking me."

"With this [Dao Saber Dao Sword] in hand, even the strength of the Five Heavenly Emperors I enfeoffed would probably be instantly killed and become nourishment for the saber and sword."

Because they grew through mutual combat, this [Dao Saber Dao Sword] possessed an intrinsic interest in killing and devouring other Dao principles.

Li Fan could practically feel the greed and excitement emanating from this pair of green saber and sword.

In an instant, as the saber and sword closed in again.

With no more time to spare, at the last moment, Li Fan made the most suitable decision.

The green saber and sword pierced through his body with a whoosh.

A massive aura caused the Heavenly Pillar space to churn and boil.

Even the four Heavenly Pillars seemed to be affected, trembling incessantly.

However…

Under the watchful eyes of the Azure Star Sea Immortals, the Hidden Emperor's figure still stood upright.

He even reached out his hand and slowly caressed the pair of green saber and sword beside him.

"Peeking at Stars? What's going on?" Shan Hua's expression changed drastically, unable to contain himself any longer, he questioned the black cat on his shoulder.

The black cat also looked incredulous.

After unleashing the [Dao Saber Dao Sword], its spirit was already severely depleted. Seeing the enemy unharmed by its ultimate move, it felt unspeakable terror and confusion.

Unwilling to admit defeat, the black cat attempted to summon the [Dao Saber Dao Sword] again to injure the enemy.

But for some reason, that figure seemed to not exist in this world. No matter how powerful the [Dao Saber Dao Sword] was, it could not inflict the slightest damage!

This situation was completely beyond its comprehension!

…

Li Fan ignored the now utterly panicked Immortals. Under the protection of 'Illusion is True,' he continued to caress the pair of green saber and sword beside him.

Just now, in the nick of time, he had decisively activated this protective ability of 'True Revelation.'

He had transformed into the pair of saber and sword.

A moment later, the warnings in his heart completely vanished.

The killing intent of green light could no longer harm him in the slightest.

Just like when he merged with the Infinite Sea and could freely summon infinite power, he had now become a part of this saber and sword.

The saber and sword were sharp, but how could they cut their own being?

"As expected, Dao principles from another possibility."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, feeling a completely unfamiliar aura from this pair of green saber and sword.

Like the Primordial Essence he encountered after leaving the high wall and interacting with the Azure Star Sea, it seemed to be a completely unfamiliar system.

But ultimately, it was still the evolution of Great Dao under different circumstances.

"Today, my Ink Slaughter Myriad Manifestations Dao Net shall have a taste of this 'foreign flavor.'"

The power of the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul surged from Li Fan.

Under the illusion of 'Illusion is True,' he eagerly pounced towards the [Dao Saber Dao Sword].

Since it was a manifestation of Dao, it could not escape the erosion of Dao Annihilation.

Once its offensiveness could be ignored, this [Dao Saber Dao Sword] was merely a meal for the Ink Slaughter Myriad Manifestations Dao Net.

Just as Li Fan was devouring this collection of Dao principles from another possibility,

The Azure Star Sea Immortals belatedly came to their senses.

Especially the black cat, which repeatedly cried out, "Quick, stop him! He's devouring my treasure!"

Even in their desperate situation, the Immortals did not choose to passively wait for death.

They unleashed all their divine abilities and attacked Li Fan in unison.

But all their attacks vanished the moment they approached within three feet of Li Fan!

This anomaly also surpassed the Immortals' understanding.

However, one Nameless among the Immortals seemed to recognize something.

The black cat, named 'Peeking at Stars,' stopped screaming. Despite its unwillingness, it could only do so helplessly. The green aura completely receded, as if it had left the black cat.

"[Wuji]…"

"Great Venerable…" Shan Hua trembled, his eyes towards Li Fan now filled with despair.

Although there were three thousand Great Daos in the world, a Dao like the one before him, capable of ignoring all other Dao attacks…

Only the legendary [Wuji Great Dao], which predated all existence!

It was said to be personally selected and taken in by a Sage Lord.

Even the successive Ruling Immortal Emperors had to treat it with great respect. It was truly invaluable!

He never expected that the person they wanted to hunt today was actually Him!

At this moment, only endless regret filled Shan Hua's heart.

Indeed, the authority of the Ruling Immortal Emperor was originally granted by a Sage Lord. Now that the Immortal Realm was destroyed and the Immortal Emperors had perished, who else could wield this authority besides the disciples of the Sage Lords?

"Great Venerable, please calm your anger! Great Venerable, please calm your anger!"

Completely plunged into despair, Shan Hua suddenly seemed to recall a life-saving straw and repeatedly said.

Chapter 1498: The Shocking Discovery of the Cat Treasure's Strangeness

"In the past, Emperor Zhai Yang paid respects to Sage Lord Tai Yi. Although his fortune was poor and he never had the chance to meet the Sage, he was fortunate enough to be bestowed a scroll of scripture.

"Afterward, for my meritorious service in resisting Dao Annihilation, Emperor Zhai Yang rewarded me with this scroll.

"At that time, the Emperor said that this scripture was personally written by Sage Lord, and it was too profound. Sage Lord Tai Yi, pitying the common folk for their inability to understand, ordered the Great Venerable to annotate it…"

Shan Hua spoke rapidly, for he was sharp-eyed enough to notice that the Immortals from the Azure Star Sea accompanying him, as well as the reinforcements from the Guangwu Star Sea, were all gradually transforming into miniature Heavenly Pillars.

It seemed the strength of the Great Venerable Wuji was truly terrifying. Among the Immortals were those no weaker than him, yet they possessed no ability to resist and were nearly annihilated.

Shan Hua's fear was evident, and he quickly produced what he believed to be a life-saving scripture.

"The Chapter of Mountain and Sea First Creation!"

Li Fan looked at the scripture floating above Shan Hua's head and, with a wave of his hand, snatched it over.

Indeed, from the countless tiny characters on it, he could feel the aura of "Wuji."

"So, you and I have a connection?"

Li Fan examined the scripture as he spoke,

and then casually admitted his identity as the Great Venerable Wuji, saying calmly.

"Great Venerable indeed has eyes like a torch!" Shan Hua nodded repeatedly.

Meanwhile, his mind raced, trying to recall information about this Great Venerable under the Sage.

The Four Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm existed almost entirely in legends. Even successive Immortal Emperors found it incredibly difficult to meet them.

However, except for Sage Lord Jing Fen, the other three Sages had spokespersons.

Among them, this Great Venerable Wuji was the easiest to deal with.

As long as one went along with him and appeased him, and perhaps made some remarks about connections, the Esteemed Venerable would often be greatly pleased.

"This 'Chapter of Mountain and Sea First Creation' was inspired by Sage Lord Tai Yi observing Sage Lords Lian Shan and Gui Hai as they built the grand Immortal Realm from nothingness. The text within is mysterious and profound, almost transcending the Dao itself. I, Shan Hua, am dull-witted. Without your annotations, Great Venerable, even with this treasure scripture in hand, I would find it difficult to comprehend its marvels."

"Great Venerable, you are truly my master!"

"When Emperor Zhai Yang first entrusted this scripture to me, he also mentioned that your comprehension of the Dao far surpassed his. Truly worthy of being a disciple of the Sage Lord!" Shan Hua, at this point, cared little for the former Immortal Emperor who had long since passed away, and spoke whatever came to mind, fabricating freely.

Li Fan, amidst Shan Hua's flattering words, carefully examined the scripture in his hand.

In a sense, Shan Hua was not entirely lying.

Although this "Chapter of Mountain and Sea First Creation" depicted the creation of the Immortal Realm from the Infinite Sea and the Upper Mountain, it also contained many of Sage Lord Tai Yi's own insights from witnessing these great events.

It was quite similar to the "Reminiscences of Shouqiu" that Li Fan had obtained before.

However, compared to the straightforwardness and directness of Duke Shouqiu, Sage Lord Tai Yi appeared much more "literary." The entire scripture was almost devoid of direct descriptions, filled instead with countless seemingly meaningless words and phrases.

If not for being personally transmitted by Sage Lord Tai Yi, Li Fan would have almost mistaken it for the ramblings of a madman.

This astonishing scripture seemed not to be intended for mortal beings of the world. The Immortals of the Immortal Realm were also included in this category of mortals. Only the other Sages might be suitable readers for this scripture.

If there were no annotations from Wuji.

The Great Venerable Wuji, also known as Grand Master Tiandu, had served Sage Lord Tai Yi for countless years, receiving direct instruction. Compared to everyone else in the world, he was naturally better able to understand Sage Lord's thoughts.

His annotations, while not perfectly matching Sage Lord's original intent one hundred percent, were at least eighty to ninety percent accurate.

As for the scripture itself, Li Fan truly couldn't understand it.

But with the addition of Grand Master's annotations, he could at least catch a glimpse of Sage Lord Tai Yi's state of mind.

One passage,

at the moment Sage Lord Lian Shan became the first Immortal in the world, all living beings at that time benefited to varying degrees. All beings were filled with immense joy. Only Sage Lord Tai Yi, while feeling a faint joy, also experienced an equal measure of worry. At that time, Sage Lord Tai Yi could not understand the source of this worry.

Another passage, described Sage Lord Gui Hai opening the Infinite Spring and inviting Sage Lords Lian Shan, Tai Yi, and others to witness the ceremony. Gui Hai playfully said to Lian Shan, "Brother, do you know which is higher, mountains or seas? If you don't know, we can wait and see." Lian Shan smiled and replied, "Though mountains are high and seas are deep, Immortals can stand on the mountaintops and tread the Infinite Spring. Therefore, Immortals are the highest." Gui Hai clapped his hands and laughed. Sage Lord Tai Yi, in a daze, saw the looming presence of mountains and seas in the two Sage Lords before him. He felt a sudden, shared emotion.

…

With the help of this "Chapter of Mountain and Sea First Creation," Li Fan seemed to return to the beginning of the Immortal Realm's creation, experiencing ancient events through the perspective of Sage Lord Tai Yi.

Besides the matters concerning the various Sage Lords and the birth of the Immortal Realm, this scripture also spoke of some primordial beings and the Primordial Immortal Realm.

It was a vast and boundless continent. The continent was populated with many mysterious primordial beings. Some of these beings were embodiments of Great Daos, some were sentient formations from rare treasures, and others were "humans."

However, the "humans" in this Primordial Immortal Realm were far stronger than current mortals. Perhaps due to being nurtured by heaven and earth, these "humans" could hunt the Dao-nurturing primordial beings on the continent, digest and absorb them, and use them for their own purposes.

But as time passed, the "humans" realized that this simple and crude method of devouring could not truly grasp the Daos. Once they died, the Dao would return to heaven and earth. And they could not pass on the "Dao" through "reproduction." Thus, the "humans" began to ponder a method to truly control the Dao.

They began to learn from and emulate the primordial Dao-nurturing beings on the continent. Some even abandoned their human forms entirely to grasp the Dao. Over a long period, countless "races" began to appear and evolve. The primordial beings, due to the covetousness of the "humans," gradually went into seclusion.

The "Chapter of Mountain and Sea First Creation" did not explicitly describe Sage Lord Tai Yi's true identity. However, from various details, it might be inferred that Sage Lord Tai Yi was not originally "human" but a primordial being who transformed.

…

"However, at the level of strength like Sage Lord Tai Yi, the form of life is no longer important."

"As long as one is willing, myriad transformations can be achieved at any time."

The "Chapter of Mountain and Sea First Creation," like the "Reminiscences of Shouqiu," was profound and vast, requiring a great deal of time to read and comprehend fully.

Although Shan Hua had gifted such a valuable treasure, Li Fan had no intention of letting him go.

Shan Hua's Dao had a certain resemblance to "Illusion is True," making him very suitable for filling the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net.

And Shan Hua's intuition was indeed sharp.

He could sense Li Fan's "ill intentions" and, looking at the numerous Heavenly Pillars surrounding them, he broke out in a cold sweat, blurting out, "Does Great Venerable require True Immortals as Heavenly Pillars?"

"There are still many True Immortals surviving in the Azure Star Sea. Furthermore, the Guangwu Star Sea, which gathers even more True Immortals, I am willing to be your vanguard!"

Hearing this, Li Fan's eyes flickered, and he temporarily halted his downward-falling hand.

Although he had suppressed quite a few True Immortals this time, the quality was somewhat disappointing.

Most were ordinary True Immortals. Only two were at the Nameless realm.

One was the Dao of "Tong Sheng" (Mutual Prosperity). Its controller could enjoy all the benefits of the prosperity of the faction they belonged to, and provide a certain degree of amplification to their companions within the faction.

And he himself could avoid the negative effects brought about by the decline of the faction. Even if the faction he belonged to perished, he could retreat safely. His primary focus was on enjoying prosperity together and sharing hardships separately.

While this Dao ability seemed somewhat redundant, its amplification effect was truly terrifying. It grew with each passing day and could snowball. Tong Sheng Nameless had once been a favored guest of several ruling Immortal Emperors.

If it weren't for the irresistible factor of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, the Immortal Realm might have truly been able to prosper indefinitely.

The other Nameless True Immortal suppressed by Li Fan this time was "Shen Si" (Divine Thought). Even if the Star Seas were disconnected due to the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, with the Dao of Divine Thought, they could find surviving civilizations in various isolated corners.

The Guangwu Star Sea and the Nameless True Immortal called "Peeking at Stars" were contacted through Divine Thought.

…

"It's not that these Daos are useless, but..."

"The strength is truly somewhat disappointing. Perhaps the true powerhouses among Nameless True Immortals have already fled to other possibilities."

Thinking of this, Li Fan became even more interested in the remaining Nameless experts in the Azure Star Sea faction.

"Besides Shan Hua, there are also Hun Du and Ni."

"And the large blue hand that constructed the Dao Net."

Having begun to absorb memories from the suppressed True Immortals, Li Fan had gained a preliminary understanding of this mysterious powerhouse.

Unlike other Nameless who openly displayed their achieved Daos,

this one who single-handedly created the Azure Star Sea's Dao Net had never truly revealed his true identity. Whenever he appeared, he was replaced by a blue light manifestation. Yet, the Immortals could not discern which Dao he controlled.

It was likely that the True Immortals suppressed within the Azure Star Sea's Dao Net knew his true identity, but even after the True Immortals and Immortal Hunters united, they were not released. They remained firmly suppressed in the depths of the Dao Net.

…

Li Fan couldn't help but think of the City Lord of Extreme Bliss.

He had almost forgotten that he still had an appointment with this True Immortal.

"Soon. Wait a moment, and I will liberate you."

"Shan Hua is indeed somewhat useful for now; there is no need to seal him into a Heavenly Pillar. Anyway, it's still a long way until the Thirteen Ancient Dao Forms mentioned by Di San Mo return."

Thinking this, Li Fan let out a cold snort, "Seeing as you're acting sensibly, I'll spare you your great disrespect for now."

Nameless Shan Hua was greatly relieved and hurriedly thanked the Great Venerable for his kindness.

Just then, something else happened that made his blood run cold.

The black cat on his shoulder, which had temporarily fallen into a coma due to the Nameless Peeking at Stars borrowing its body, had now languidly woken up.

When it looked at the figure not far away and heard him spouting arrogance towards its master, its fur stood on end, and it fiercely snarled at Li Fan.

"Meow~ Meow~ Meow~ Meow!"

"Impudent little beast! May the Great Heavenly Venerate overlook this!" Shan Hua also disregarded his precious treasure and slapped the black cat on the head.

The black cat, in pain, not only did not cease but instead growled lowly at its owner.

"An ungrateful beast! May the Great Heavenly Venerate not take offense!"

Shan Hua smiled wryly, his expression tense, and apologized to Li Fan.

"Do you think I would quibble with an unintelligent beast?" Li Fan sneered, beckoned, and summoned the black cat into his hand in mid-air.

He carefully examined the little creature.

Indeed, the black cat bore some resemblance to Mao Bao in appearance. No wonder Li Fan almost mistook it at first glance.

Now that the black cat was in Li Fan's grasp, its life hanging in the balance, it remained oblivious.

It still fearlessly bared its fangs and claws at Li Fan, constantly growling.

"It's quite fierce." Li Fan clicked his tongue and said.

Shan Hua wiped the cold sweat from his forehead and said, "I have been nurturing this little beast with Infinite Immortal Power all along. Perhaps after consuming too much, it has become unruly. It is the same when it encounters other True Immortals."

"It's not targeting Great Venerable."

"Alas, it was quite cute when it was young."

Li Fan, hearing this, conjured streams of Infinite Immortal Power from his fingertip and offered it to the black cat's mouth.

As expected, the black cat immediately became docile and devoured the energy from the Infinite Sea with great gulps.

The little thing could really eat.

After a long while, it finally ate its fill.

However, what surprised Li Fan was that after he had fed the black cat, he thought it would become more obedient.

Unexpectedly, the beast instantly turned on him and growled lowly at Li Fan again.

Seeing Li Fan's expression slowly turn displeased, Shan Hua secretly lamented and nervously explained, "This beast has the temperament of cats everywhere. It only gets close to people it knows."

"Outsiders, even if they use some tricks, can never make it truly obedient."

…

Li Fan lost all interest and, feeling dejected, tossed the black cat back to Shan Hua.

However, at this moment, his movements paused slightly.

Shan Hua's heart tightened again, thinking Li Fan had changed his mind.

But he heard Li Fan ask leisurely, "What did you just say?"

Shan Hua was confused and could only repeat his words.

"...Has the temperament of cats everywhere. It only gets close to people it knows."

…

With these words, in Li Fan's mind, Mao Bao slowly appeared.

And the image of it lying quietly on the Sacred Emperor's shoulder.

One cat and one person, as if standing before him.

Crossing space and time, meeting Li Fan's true self in silent gaze.

A point that Li Fan had long overlooked surfaced in his mind.

How could a divine entity like Mao Bao be subdued by mere Primordial Essence?

Everything the Sacred Emperor wanted, Mao Bao would cooperate fully.

Even for tasks that consumed a lot of energy, the Sacred Emperor would appease it by feeding it some Primordial Essence.

Could others...

Could they achieve this?

Li Fan had never considered this question before.

But now...

Chapter 1499: Dharma Expansion and Dao Ascension

"It seems it wasn't simply that the Sage Emperor tamed Mao Bao with 'Primordial Essence'."

"Rather, Mao Bao instinctively felt a kinship with the Sage Emperor, which is why it willingly lay on the Sage Emperor's shoulder at all times and served him."

Li Fan looked at the black cat that had returned to Shan Hua Nameless's shoulder, his mind recalling the origin of the Sage Emperor's clone.

Sage Emperor Li Ping was created by Li Fan using the blood essence of Wang Xuanba and Sun Erlang.

However, in that life of the Sage Emperor, Mao Bao had direct contact with Wang Xuanba and Sun Erlang, yet did not show any particular affection towards them.

"So, the problem lies with the 'Li Fan' body?"

During the process of creating the clone, using their blood essence was only to strip them of their talents.

The reason why the clone became a clone was still dependent on Li Fan's own blood essence.

Li Fan's eyes flickered, and a storm surged in his heart. The 'Li Fan' he referred to was not himself, but the original owner of his body.

The frail scholar who existed before Li Fan transmigrated and possessed the 'True Revelation' treasure.

Even after a hundred reincarnations, Li Fan had completely merged with his body, with no lingering disharmony. However, it could not be denied that he had indeed 'stolen' someone else's body.

"If Mao Bao's original owner was the original Li Fan…"

Li Fan's eyes flickered, and he looked towards the high wall.

"The original body's cultivation aptitude was indeed quite poor, but not entirely unculturable."

"And this was when performing within the high wall, in the Xuanhuang Realm, where the Great Dao was desolate."

"In a normal environment, he would definitely be considered a talent with potential."

"'Infinite possibilities'…"

Li Fan's thoughts spun rapidly.

"Theoretically, it is indeed possible for a mortal to rise and achieve supreme power."

"In other words, theoretically, anyone in the high wall, or even in the [Primordial] possibility, might have another supreme expert identity in other possibilities. Just like Hei Tianyi and Xie Subai."

"But the current reality is not like this."

The high wall served as a shield, concealing from the attention of these supreme experts who sought to devour their other selves. However, ever since Li Fan entered the experimental field space within the high wall and obtained the power of the Shouqiu projection, completely controlling the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, he had also sent out the so-called prodigies from within the wall in batches.

None of them had attracted any anomalous fluctuations from beyond the possibility.

Not to mention crossing space like Hei Tianyi, not even telepathic sensing or control like Xie Subai had occurred.

Among these prodigies were even Di Jing Lun and Qiao Si Dao, whose talents Li Fan considered absolutely top-tier.

"If there were truly infinite possibilities, there would definitely exist supreme expert counterparts of them."

"But in reality, there are none."

"This also implies that 'infinite' is not truly infinite."

"Because of the rampant Dao Annihilation Tribulation, the vast majority of possibilities have long since been annihilated."

"The other supreme expert counterparts of most people in this world can probably only be found in the records of the Infinite Sea."

To survive to this day in the context of the mortal world having only seven million years of lifespan remaining, one either had good luck, or like Shouqiu Gong, possessed strength that could even resist the Dao Annihilation Tribulation to a certain extent.

Regardless of which it was, it was definitely not good news for Li Fan.

Based on what happened to Tian Yi and Su Bai before, if Li Fan's guess was correct, then the moment he stepped out of the high wall, he might be sensed by the 'Sage Emperor Li Fan' from another possibility.

Between the two, there should be a situation of either you die or I die.

"If the other party can truly cross possibilities to come here, even if I unleash all my cards, I might still not be their opponent. The only option would be to rely on 'True Revelation' and make a hasty escape."

To verify this conjecture was actually very simple. Li Fan only needed to take a step out of the high wall with his main body.

Taking a deep breath, Li Fan temporarily suppressed this eager impulse.

Even though he was impatient to verify it, the time was not yet right.

"Fortunately, I am cautious and have not easily stepped out of the high wall until now."

"Otherwise, I would have been greatly alarmed."

"The current priority is to steadily increase my strength. The remaining True Immortals in the Azure Star Sea, the so-called 'Guangwu Star Sea,' and the Thirteen Great Dao Forms – if their combined strength is still insufficient, then I will suppress and devour all the remaining True Immortals in the [Primordial] possibility."

"I refuse to believe that even then, I would still be a match for the 'Sage Emperor.'"

With this thought, Li Fan said coldly to the trembling Shan Hua in front of him, "I will give you thirty days to achieve this. If you cannot provide me with a satisfactory result within thirty days…"

Li Fan glanced at Nameless Shan Hua.

Shan Hua's heart skipped a beat, and he quickly re-assured him.

Without uttering any threatening words, Li Fan merely waved his large sleeve and dismissed Shan Hua.

His mood gradually calmed from its agitation, and he began to digest his gains from this occasion.

What surprised Li Fan the most, naturally, was the [Primordial Chapter of Mountains and Seas] written by Sage Lord Tai Yi that Shan Hua had presented. However, in terms of what could maximize Li Fan's current combat strength…

He extended his left hand, and a pair of saber and sword emitting a strange green light appeared in Li Fan's palm.

They were precisely the killer moves used by the Nameless expert named '[Peeking at Stars]' who had possessed the black cat.

Frankly speaking, the Immortals of the Azure Star Sea had the confidence to charge forward.

Even if all the beings in the Ancient Desolation Immortal Realm joined forces, along with Li Fan himself, they might not be able to survive the combined attack of this saber and sword.

"In the Azure Star Sea, there are the Saber Island and the Sword Domain, which are the manifestations of the remnants of saber and sword Dao in the [Primordial] possibility."

"And this pair of saber and sword, the saber and sword are merely the surface."

Li Fan gently caressed the green light in his palm, closed his eyes, as if he was in that desolate, deadly starry sky.

"Slaughter, Devour, until all Daos merge."

"This is the true essence of this treasure."

"It perfectly suits my Myriad Manifestations Dao Net!"

Li Fan rejoiced in his heart.

He slightly parted his lips and directly swallowed the pair of green saber and sword into his abdomen.

Countless streams of green light instantly erupted from the saber and sword, merging into Li Fan's Myriad Manifestations Dao Net.

On the originally grim Dao Net, a pair of transparent saber and sword were now faintly suspended. Among the numerous Dao manifestations that took human form, they looked extremely out of place. But precisely because of this, they added a unique charm to the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net.

"Saber and Sword, Slaughter, End."

Completely new experiences of Dao intent flowed into Li Fan's heart.

This was a Dao path entirely different from the Primordial possibility, not simply originating from other possibilities. It was a new possibility of Dao principles attached to and carried by 'non-living entities.'

In the Primordial possibility where Li Fan was located, although Dao manifestations as objects existed, these supreme treasures could not cultivate like humans.

Possessing a Dao was an inherent characteristic they were born with, but it was also their lifelong limit.

The Dao Saber Dao Sword from the Starry Sky of Ultimate End directly opened up a supreme Dao path for this kind of existence.

With a thought, a bloody red circular jade artifact appeared before Li Fan.

It was the complete body of the 'Law Derivation Jade' taken from the little girl Yan Fa Jue.

Without Infinite Immortal power, the shattered Law Derivation Jade was no longer an Immortal artifact. Its ability to deduce the laws of the mortal world was useless to Li Fan.

Li Fan's original idea was to repeat the process of Xuanhuang sublimation and transform the Immortal Realm again, promoting the shattered Law Derivation Jade, like himself, to become immortal again. But now, Li Fan had found a better method.

"Even capable of creating a perfect substitute for the Law Derivation Jade."

"'Dao Derivation Jade'!"

Li Fan had already carefully examined the Law Derivation Jade. Its ability to deduce all possibilities in the world likely stemmed from a certain form of [Exhaustive Enumeration]. However, its crude method of realizing countless possibilities was unexpectedly efficient. As if by instinct, it could inherently eliminate impossible scenarios.

"The Law Derivation Jade represents the Dao of 'Derivation'."

"Although it is only a projection of a part of the Dao, it may not be impossible to reverse the situation through the method of devouring and strengthening the Dao Saber Dao Sword."

"Transforming illusion into reality!"

Li Fan clenched the blood-red circle in his palm. The scenes and comprehensions of the ultimate blade and sword possibility, absorbed by the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net, were then infused into it.

The blood jade, which already appeared somewhat strange, became even more bizarre after absorbing wisps of eerie green light.

As the saying goes, "A single true teaching is worth a thousand gilded words."

With the extremely rich experience of mutual devouring from the Dao Saber Dao Sword, the damaged Law Derivation Jade had almost quickly learned this advanced experience. As if it had been starved for thousands of years, it instinctively wanted to launch attacks on its surroundings.

But it was reprimanded by Li Fan with a merciless slap. This was not an ordinary slap, but one containing wisps of [Wuji] power.

"Only what I feed you, can you eat."

"What I don't feed you, you can only watch."

After several attempts to feed and being severely disciplined, Li Fan successfully established rules for the Law Derivation Jade.

Looking at the ravenously hungry blood-colored circle, Li Fan looked at the few low Heavenly Pillars standing in this space.

Without reaching the Nameless realm, they had almost no capacity to bear the Dao. They merely resembled Heavenly Pillars in shape, but in reality, they could not be called true Heavenly Pillars. And their comprehension of the Dao, after being devoured by Li Fan's Myriad Manifestations Dao Net once, was now almost useless.

Standing here, they were merely an eyesore.

They were perfect for feeding the Law Derivation Jade.

As the low Heavenly Pillars disappeared one by one, the Law Derivation Jade gradually became crystal clear.

The blood color was no longer as dazzling, but contained within, warm and moist.

Li Fan played with the fully sated Law Derivation Jade again.

As expected, its 'Derivation' ability was more than ten times stronger than before.

And as Li Fan had expected, it had already begun to transcend the boundaries of 'Law Derivation.'

It was rapidly advancing towards the broader path of 'Derivation.'

"The Dao Saber Dao Sword represents the process of progressing from bottom to top, step by step, devouring one's true Dao path through projections. It can even ultimately accommodate the possibility of all Three Thousand Great Daos."

"In fact, it can be seen as an alternative Myriad Manifestations Dao Net."

"However, there are subtle differences between these two. The Myriad Manifestations Dao Net is the true fusion of myriad Daos. No matter how much is devoured, it only presents the complete appearance of all devoured Great Daos. But the devouring of the Dao Saber Dao Sword…"

"While devouring, it inevitably retains its original attributes. Just like them, even if they devoured the Dao paths of an entire possibility, in the end, they would still revert to their original form of 'Blade and Sword.'"

"The Law Derivation Jade is also like this. No matter how it devours and evolves, it will ultimately still resemble the 'Law Derivation Jade.'"

Li Fan felt no regret for them. Instead, this made them even more useful to him.

"By analogy, not only the Law Derivation Jade, but even any Dao projection can be like this."

With this thought, Li Fan had found a way to create trouble for Hei Tianyi and Xie Subai.

"I will need to experiment thoroughly."

Thirty days passed quickly.

And Shan Hua did not disappoint Li Fan.

On the twenty-fifth day, Shan Hua, along with Chaos, came to visit.

"Please forgive my previous hesitation. We deserve punishment for our indecision."

Before Shan Hua could speak, Nameless Chaos first apologized to Li Fan.

"I already knew they intended to harm Senior, yet I did not step forward to stop them…"

Although Chaos's expression was unreadable, his words were filled with regret.

Li Fan smiled and said, "You are a wise person, and I like wise people who obey. The more the better."

Chaos was overjoyed, and the anxiety in his heart disappeared. "I am willing to serve Senior wholeheartedly."

Li Fan glanced at Shan Hua, who had also come to pay his respects, and asked, "Shan Hua, have you seen the [Primordial Chapter of Mountains and Seas] that you collected?"

Chaos looked at Shan Hua beside him with surprise and shook his head. "I have not had the good fortune to feast my eyes upon it."

Li Fan waved his large hand, revealing the scripture written by Sage Lord Tai Yi to Chaos.

Chaos's reaction was the same as anyone else who saw this scripture for the first time; he was immediately engrossed.

However, before he could savor it in detail, Li Fan took it back.

Chaos looked regretful, but in front of Li Fan, he dared not be presumptuous. He could only forcefully suppress the instinctive urge in his heart.

"Merit will be rewarded, and mistakes will be punished."

"Do you two wish to earn merit, or to commit a transgression?"

This was when Shan Hua had the opportunity to state his intentions. "Shan Hua and I have investigated and found that there are still four Nameless beings suppressed within the Azure Star Sea's Dao Net. Including 'The Great Net' itself, we wish to offer them all to Great Venerable."

"'The Great Net'?"

"'The Great Net' is the title given to the creator of the Dao Net. To our shame, we have faced him for tens of thousands of years and cooperated for a hundred years, yet we still do not know his true identity or the Dao he comprehends." Chaos explained.

"However, this person must be at the Nameless realm. And his strength is no less than that of Chaos and me," Shan Hua asserted confidently.

"So how do you plan to offer these five to me?" Li Fan asked with interest.

Chaos and Shan Hua exchanged glances, and finally, Shan Hua whispered, "Our connection with the Guangwu Star Sea was entirely through [Divine Thoughts] and my black cat."

"Divine Thoughts has already been captured by you…"

Shan Hua looked towards the location where Divine Thoughts had transformed into a Heavenly Pillar, only to be surprised to find it empty. His words faltered.

"Are you looking for him?"

Li Fan slowly showed the blood-colored circle in his hand to the two Nameless True Immortals.

Even though the two Nameless beings had lived through countless calamities and were immortal, their expressions changed drastically at this moment.

Chapter 1500: The Twin Treasures Break the Dao Net

Among the Immortals of the Azure Star Sea, Divine Thoughts was known for his good temperament and popularity. His voice and appearance were still vivid in their minds, yet at this moment, Chaos and Shan Hua sensed the Dao aura belonging to Divine Thoughts from the blood-red circle in Li Fan's hand.

The implication was self-evident.

Their former companion had been transformed into food for an artifact.

These two Nameless realm powerhouses could not help but feel grief and fear.

But seeing Li Fan's cold and emotionless gaze, they quickly sobered up from their sorrow. The deceased were gone; survival was the most important thing now!

Shan Hua naturally continued, "Divine Thoughts is gone, so for the time being, contact with the Guangwu Star Sea can only rely on me. In the past, when I returned to the Azure Star Sea, I did not go deep into the Dao Net, but contacted Chaos from afar to plan."

"Therefore, 'The Great Net' is currently unaware of the complete annihilation of our expeditionary True Immortals."

"Although a considerable time has passed without any reply, it will surely arouse his suspicion. However, he will at most assume that we are locked in a fierce battle or a stalemate. He will never believe that we have been so easily and comprehensively defeated. Otherwise, why would he have agreed to the expedition in the first place…"

Shan Hua analyzed methodically: "Under such circumstances, Chaos and I can send a signal for support to 'The Great Net.' Considering it from the overall strategic situation and the initial investment cost, 'The Great Net' is highly likely to come to our aid. And once he arrives, with Senior's methods, he can surely capture him with ease…"

Chaos added, "Although the strategy sounds exceedingly simple, the key lies in how to gain the trust of 'The Great Net.' Over the past period, Shan Hua and I have made ample preparations, constantly transmitting false battle reports to 'The Great Net.' 'The Great Net' seems to have detected nothing unusual and even proactively inquired if we needed support."

"Although 'The Great Net' is powerful, nearly half of its strength is embodied in the Dao Net. If we can lure him out of the Dao Net, capturing him will be twice as effective with half the effort," Shan Hua also chimed in.

…

After the two Nameless True Immortals briefly explained their plan, Li Fan looked at Chaos and smiled, praising, "It seems you have long harbored intentions of submission. Very good, very good."

Li Fan's fingers caressed the blood-red circle as he paced and approached one of the Heavenly Pillars standing in this space.

"Your plan might barely work. Unfortunately, in my opinion, there is a fatal flaw."

His eyes shifted to the Heavenly Pillar, and his voice was ethereal.

Chaos and Shan Hua's expressions became solemn. "We hope Great Venerable will enlighten us."

"Just as you are full of confidence in capturing me, your plan seems to assume that as long as 'The Great Net' is lured out, you can definitely defeat and suppress him."

"You overestimate your own strength while underestimating the opponent."

"Since his origins, background, and Dao path are unknown, how can you be so sure that as long as I act, I can definitely subdue him?"

"What if I inadvertently bring a wolf into the house and, through carelessness and underestimation, fall victim to defeat?"

"Or is this what you truly hope for? To feign surrender, but actually to enact a plan within a plan, just to turn the tables in a desperate situation?"

Li Fan's voice grew colder.

Chaos and Shan Hua's expressions and bodies trembled violently.

"Great Venerable, please do not misunderstand! How could we dare harbor such disloyal intentions?" Shan Hua quickly clarified.

"Junior wholeheartedly considers your concerns, and the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth can bear witness to my sincerity." Chaos reiterated his loyalty.

In their hearts, however, they both lamented inwardly.

This legendary Great Venerable seemed to have undergone a drastic change in temperament after experiencing the destruction of the Immortal Realm. He was suspicious, capricious, and cruel.

Compared to the cruel Immortal Emperors of the past, he was even more so.

"Whether you truly intend to deceive me or not, and what your true thoughts are, I have no interest in knowing. It is not important."

"After all, whoever wins, you will follow. Whoever loses, you will follow."

"Since that is the case, I also have my own plans."

Li Fan reached out his hand, seemingly touching the Wuji Heavenly Pillar, but in reality, the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net had already activated, engulfing the Heavenly Pillar and the stone statue of Grand Master contained within it.

Although he had comprehended the Wuji Great Dao for a hundred years, he was certainly not as proficient as Grand Master Wuji himself.

"Since the enemy is there, let's just go and defeat them directly."

Amidst a thunderous roar, the Wuji Heavenly Pillar was taken by Li Fan. It continuously shrank, finally transforming into a gray-white stone rod.

A figure flickered in the space ahead.

It was Li Biren, summoned by Li Fan.

"Take this!"

Li Fan directly threw the Wuji Heavenly Rod towards his clone.

Considering the possibility of the existence of the 'Sage Emperor Li Fan' from other possibilities, this time, the clone had to act on his behalf again.

Both cultivating the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net, Li Biren held the Wuji Heavenly Rod without any difficulty.

Protected by the Wuji Great Dao, any Dao technique from the [Primordial] possibility could not approach Li Biren's body.

"Unless this 'Great Net' is also a visitor from another possibility, as long as this Wuji stone rod is in hand, the clone is in an invincible position."

"Protection is sufficient, but offense is still slightly lacking."

Li Fan pondered, then spat out a pair of water-green saber and sword from his mouth.

"Take this treasure as well."

"If you still cannot defeat him, then flee quickly. If you cannot even escape…"

"Then self-destruct immediately."

These instructions were conveyed only telepathically.

Shan Hua and Chaos, present at the scene, were unaware.

From their perspective, they only saw Li Fan generously distributing two supreme treasures without any reluctance.

After a brief induction, their hearts were filled with both joy and shock.

The joy stemmed from the fact that they had recognized the origins of these two supreme treasures. The pair of saber and sword originally belonged to Nameless Peeking at Stars. They had personally witnessed the power of this treasure before, otherwise, they would not have collaborated with him so easily and been persuaded by him. As for the gray stone rod, although its mysterious origins were unknown, its ability to ignore the senses of the two Immortals alone indicated that it was definitely an extraordinary treasure.

With the assistance of these two treasures, 'The Great Net' was bound to become a prisoner.

The shock stemmed from how extraordinary the Dao Saber Dao Sword was, yet Li Fan, this Great Venerable, could subdue it in such a short time. More importantly, such a treasure was handed over so readily, as if it were nothing. If they were in Li Fan's position, they would definitely find a secluded and safe place to go into seclusion and comprehend it.

Chaos secretly mused, "That ancient scripture passed down by Sage Lord Tai Yi, he also regards it with indifference. Truly worthy of being someone who served Sage Lord for a long time; his vision is naturally far superior to us crude beings."

"You two can follow along. Whether you contribute or not is entirely up to yourselves," Li Fan instructed indifferently.

Then, with a wave of his large sleeve, he sent Li Biren and the two Nameless beings out of the high wall.

"Although there is a ninety percent chance of success, we must also prepare for failure." Li Fan looked into the distance, thinking silently.

The protection of 'Illusion is True' had already been bestowed upon him.

As soon as there was any anomaly, he would immediately revert to 'True Revelation.'

If 'The Great Net' could truly win against the combined might of the Wuji stone rod and the Dao Saber Dao Sword, then this person would be someone Li Fan, in his current state, could not contend with. Direct reversion would be the only correct choice.

…

In the dim starry sky, Li Biren placed the Wuji stone rod on his shoulder, just like his main body, swallowing the green saber and sword into his abdomen. Then, using his body as a path, he stirred up Shan Hua and Chaos and charged directly towards the Azure Star Sea's Dao Net.

As if they had rehearsed the attack route countless times, they were incredibly proficient, aiming directly for the core area of the Azure Star Sea's Administration Council.

Using his body as a path, traversing the starry sky, covering millions of miles in an instant.

Before the two Nameless beings could react, Li Biren had already penetrated the Dao Net's coverage.

Under normal circumstances, if there was any foreign object invading the Dao Net, it would instantly trigger a response from the entire Dao Net.

Not only would they face the pressure of all the Daos within the Dao Net, but they would also be besieged by countless Immortal Hunters.

Even for a Nameless True Immortal, being trapped so deeply within the net would result in either death or severe injury.

In their years of interaction with the Azure Star Sea, Shan Hua and Chaos had already recognized this as a fundamental truth. Therefore, in their previous battles with the Azure Star Sea, the True Immortal side had always used tactics such as attempting infiltration and ambushing the Dao Net's periphery.

But now…

Li Biren's direct assault on the heart of the territory completely shattered their understanding.

Wherever he passed, the Dao Net failed to react.

The densely woven Dao strings seemed to crumble at the first blow, as if struck by a scorching flame, creating holes in the Dao Net!

The Dao strings snapped one after another. The Dao Net was no longer a net!

This bizarre situation made Chaos and Shan Hua, the two Nameless beings, stare dumbfounded.

Even in their wildest fantasies, they had never imagined such an easy dismantling of the Dao Net.

While they were still stunned, Li Biren had already reached the center of the Dao Net.

The Immortal Hunter headquarters and the Azure Star Sea Administration Council were all located here.

Looking at the Azure Star Sea personnel in utter chaos, as if waking from a dream, the two True Immortals looked at the gray stone rod in Li Biren's hand.

An unbelievable, yet the most fitting conclusion for the current situation, sprang into their minds.

They had personally witnessed this stone rod transform from a Heavenly Pillar.

They had been unable to ascertain the Dao path sealed within this Heavenly Pillar before, but now, as the stone rod displayed its might within the Dao Net, they could finally confirm it.

Thus, the two Nameless beings, who had lived for an unknown duration, trembled uncontrollably.

"Wuji…"

"Great Venerable?"

The reason they had mistaken Li Fan for the former Great Venerable Wuji, disciple of Sage Lord Tai Yi, was because Li Fan had previously displayed the Wuji power capable of nullifying all Daos.

And now, as the gray stone rod displayed the same ability, they finally understood.

The power of Wuji did not originate from the Hidden Emperor.

Rather, it came from Wuji himself, who was sealed and suppressed by the Hidden Emperor!

"That is a disciple of a Sage Lord, an innate being, incredibly noble!"

"Even though the Immortal Realm is destroyed, the Sage Lord may not have perished. If they angered the Sage Lord…"

"Even Wuji Venerable ended up in such a state…"

In an instant, countless thoughts surged into the minds of the two Nameless beings.

But ultimately, it transformed into a deep fear of Li Fan, the Hidden Emperor of unknown identity.

And Chaos, in particular, became certain of his judgment.

"It seems he has truly embarked on the path of becoming a Sage."

"Only by being a Sage can one disregard the face of other Sage Lords."

The hearts of the two Immortals trembled violently. Meanwhile, Li Biren was already wreaking havoc in the depths of the Dao Net.

After coldly stating, "Those who resist shall die," and the Azure Star Sea faction still continued to attack. Li Biren ruthlessly unleashed the Dao Saber Dao Sword.

Billions of green lights fluttered like willow branches in the wind.

Wherever they passed, no screams were heard. Beings vanished, leaving behind only emptiness.

Only the flying green lights became slightly denser.

With the Wuji Heavenly Rod clearing the path and the Dao Saber Dao Sword eliminating the enemies, Li Biren plowed straight through, breaking open the densely packed Dao Net layer by layer.

He did not search for the mysterious Nameless being 'The Great Net' within the Dao Net, but directly headed for the four pillars of the Dao Net.

The cages that imprisoned the Nameless True Immortals.

As the most stable structures within the entire Dao Net, these solemn cages were like paper in the face of Wuji's power.

They offered no defense whatsoever.

Soon, Li Biren locked onto the location of one of the imprisoned Nameless True Immortals.

The stone rod flickered, and with one blow, he shattered the cage.

The imprisoned Nameless being had various colored Dao strings inserted into their body.

They seemed to still be in a deep sleep.

Li Biren waved his hand and removed all the Dao strings from their body.

The imprisoned Nameless being then showed signs of slowly waking up.

"This one seems to be 'Lord of Wealth'?"

Chaos, following behind Li Biren, seemed to recognize the Immortal's identity and exclaimed in surprise.

Like Shouqiu Gong, they were both addressed as 'Gong.'

But clearly, their strengths were incomparable.

Perhaps it was merely because they were associated with the Dao of 'Wealth.'

Li Biren paid little attention and, before Lord of Wealth could fully awaken, the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net's power erupted, instantly enveloping him.

Then, he was directly sent to the inside of the high wall, to the main body's location.

Seeing Li Biren's actions, Chaos seemed to want to speak but stopped short.

However, Shan Hua shook his head slightly, causing him to suppress his words.

With the loss of one of the Four Pillars,

the already tattered Dao Net's suppression power was greatly reduced.

Both Chaos and Shan Hua felt the pressure around them lessen significantly.

"Strange, even at this point, why hasn't 'The Great Net' appeared?"

"Be careful. 'The Great Net' is not someone who gives up easily. Based on my understanding of him, he must be gathering strength for a killing blow."

Having completed the destruction of the Dao Net together with Li Biren, the two Nameless beings were now irrevocably tied to Li Fan, the Hidden Emperor.

Their relationship with the Azure Star Sea had become one of mutual destruction, with no possibility of reconciliation.

For the sake of their future, they had to remind him.

Li Biren seemed oblivious, continuing towards the next cage.

This time, it was the Nameless True Immortal whose Dao was '[Rock Solid].'

This Nameless being was in much better condition than Lord of Wealth.

Despite being imprisoned for an unknown number of years, he appeared to be in high spirits.

Seeing the sudden intruders, this 'Rock Solid' Nameless being was somewhat taken aback.

Just as he was about to say something, Li Biren's Myriad Manifestations Dao Net arrived.

Chapter 1501: Striking the Yellow Dragon

[Rock Solid], a Nameless expert, faced Li Biren's sudden, swift strike with a flash of earthy yellow light in his eyes. Though imprisoned beneath the Dao Net for tens of thousands of years, he remained unfazed.

He stomped his feet firmly, and in an instant, his form became like a majestic mountain, standing tall between heaven and earth. Li Biren’s Myriad Manifestations Dao Net, which had been used to ensnare him, suddenly felt as if it were being gripped by a powerful hand, creating a stalemate that rendered it momentarily immobile. The mountain formed by [Rock Solid] stretched out vast and immeasurable. Even with the Wuji power surging within the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net, it was difficult to completely dissolve the mountain of [Rock Solid] in a short time.

Slightly hindered, Li Biren showed no hesitation. With a direct strike, he swung his rod towards the ancient Nameless expert, [Rock Solid]. This situation was exactly as Li Fan had anticipated. Although he had attained enlightenment for a hundred years and integrated the power of Wuji into his use, he had not yet reached the stage of becoming Wuji itself. Facing true powerhouses among the Nameless True Immortals, instantaneous suppression might not be achievable. This was why Li Fan had brought the Wuji Heavenly Pillar.

Though the Nameless expert [Rock Solid] was old yet exceptionally firm, against the true Wuji Great Dao, he was still somewhat lacking. The Wuji Heavenly Pillar pierced directly into the heart of the mountain. The hardened rock on the majestic mountain range crumbled like tofu upon contact. The earthy yellow light in [Rock Solid]'s eyes, like a candle flame blown out, instantly vanished. Only confusion remained.

"This Nameless expert, [Rock Solid], his Dao path formed a mountain range, seemingly mimicking the [Upper Mountain]."

After suppressing this Nameless expert and sending him to the high wall, Li Biren, while savoring the Dao path gleaned from his recent opponent, moved on to the third Heavenly Pillar. With two supreme treasures in hand, Li Biren encountered no worthwhile resistance and successfully abducted the third Nameless True Immortal, [Speechless], who was sealed within the Dao Net.

Four pillars, three now lost. The Star Sea’s Dao Net had lost most of its supporting anchor points and its suppressing power was greatly reduced. Chaos and Harmonious Prosperity could now move freely within it, unaffected by significant influence. The decline of the Dao Net, along with the Star Sea’s starry sky, began to undergo subtle changes. Under the pressure of Dao Annihilation, the existence of the Dao Net was like integrated Heavenly Pillars, supporting the heavens that were on the verge of collapse. Now that Li Fan had abruptly removed three of its pillars, while the Star Sea within the high wall became more stable, the Star Sea here was undoubtedly becoming precarious.

Life within the Star Sea still existed for the moment, but beyond the Star Sea, it was as if a shadow had been cast, accompanied by intermittent muffled roars like mountains and oceans. Both Harmonious Prosperity and Chaos, two Nameless experts, were clearly not unfamiliar with these signs. Their memories were so profound that they instinctively felt extreme unease and fear.

Li Biren ignored their emotions, faithfully carrying out Li Fan's orders to proceed to the location of the last imprisoned Nameless expert. Harmonious Prosperity and Chaos could only follow behind, unable to refrain from reminding him, "Something seems amiss. This operation has been far too smooth."

"The Dao Net is about to collapse, yet [The Great Net] has not appeared. Where could he have gone?"

"It's impossible that he simply fled. The Dao Net is his life's work; he would never abandon it so easily. Unless, the target he is currently pursuing is even more important than the Dao Net!"

A thought surfaced in the minds of both Nameless experts. Li Biren seemed to have guessed their thoughts, only pausing briefly before continuing forward. At the location of the last Dao Net pillar, there were no longer any Immortal Hunt cultivators resisting. The area was quiet, with only the last Nameless pillar barely supporting the collapsing Dao strings around it.

Once this last pillar was taken, the Star Sea’s Dao Net would cease to exist from this day forward. Li Biren repeated his method, with the Wuji Heavenly Pillar clearing the path and dissolving the Dao Net's remaining defenses. A gaunt figure appeared in his sight. He seemed to have suffered unimaginable mistreatment, or perhaps had been imprisoned for the longest time. This last Nameless expert sat cross-legged, head lowered, his clothes in tatters. Compared to the previous three, he appeared extraordinarily miserable. Li Biren even sensed that the Great Dao drawn from this Nameless expert by the Star Sea’s Dao Net was even more than that drawn from the other three combined. He alone seemed to bear the pressure equivalent to the sum of all other Dao Net pillars! His body was covered in dense Dao strings, a horrifying sight!

"Do you recognize him?" Li Biren suddenly asked the two Nameless experts behind him. Chaos and Harmonious Prosperity inspected him closely, both shaking their heads slightly. "The Immortal Realm is boundless, and the number of those who have attained the Nameless realm is countless. It is normal that we do not know all of them," Harmonious Prosperity explained.

Li Biren nodded thoughtfully and observed the prisoner before him, not rushing to rescue him. With his current understanding of the Great Dao, he could discern the backgrounds of the previous three Nameless experts at a glance. Wealth, Rock Solid, Speechless… Although these Great Daos were embodied by Nameless experts, the experts themselves, not having transcended, naturally left some traces within the world. It was precisely through these traces that Li Fan could glimpse their Dao paths. But the one before him fell within Li Biren's blind spot. A completely unfamiliar, unknown Dao path.

"Could it be from another possibility? Or perhaps..." Despite his doubts, with two supreme treasures in hand, Li Biren felt no excessive fear. He cautiously proceeded, and the Wuji Heavenly Rod swung down again. The remaining Dao strings entangled around the last prisoner dissolved and vanished.

Just as the prisoner was freed and the Dao Net was about to completely collapse… a pale, emaciated hand suddenly grabbed the Wuji Heavenly Rod tightly. The Dao strings, which had already dissipated, suddenly surged out from the person before him again. Although Li Biren was mentally prepared, his heart suddenly skipped a beat. He tried to control the Wuji Heavenly Rod and retrieve it, but found that the gray stone rod seemed to be firmly stuck to the opponent’s palm. No matter how hard he tried to manipulate it, the Wuji Heavenly Pillar was immobile!

Li Biren also sensed that during the brief moment the prisoner grasped the Wuji Heavenly Rod, wisps of Wuji aura began to emanate from his body. A sense of foreboding washed over Li Biren. At this moment, the last Nameless True Immortal suddenly opened his eyes. "Little friend, why do you destroy my Dao Net?"

...

Not long ago, within the high wall.

Li Fan, who was observing Li Biren's actions, suddenly felt an inexplicable sense of vexation. Startled, he carefully investigated the origin of this strange emotion. Since he began his cycle of reincarnation and cultivation, his intuition had saved him countless times. Although he could not yet ascertain the exact origin of this incredibly accurate intuition, Li Fan had tentatively accepted it as a unique innate talent, similar to his own infinitely reducible spiritual essence. A warning from his intuition was surely due to a cause.

Li Fan's thoughts raced. Amidst myriad possibilities, he narrowed down the target. "[The Great Net]?" "The Dao Net is destroyed, yet he remains indifferent. Is he planning to confront me directly?" Li Fan couldn't help but find the situation absurd. Although the Wuji Heavenly Rod and the Dao Saber Dao Sword had been taken by Li Biren, within the high wall, he was practically invincible. Not only did he have the support of the five Shouqiu projections, but he also had the entire populace of the Primordial Immortal Realm as his soldiers. Unless it was a Transcendent expert among the Nameless, Li Fan feared no one. "This intuitive warning is different from previous ones. It is not a fatal crisis, but it definitely carries a potential threat." "This indicates that [The Great Net]'s strength should not be underestimated." After careful consideration, Li Fan did not directly escape. He intended to face this mysterious Nameless expert first.

While he was contemplating, Li Biren had already arrived at the location of the last prisoner. And when the gaunt old man uttered the words, "Little friend, why do you destroy my Dao Net?", a blue figure suddenly appeared in the Primordial Immortal Realm like a phantom, without warning. It directly locked onto Li Fan's true location. The distance between them was barely a thousand feet. The Primordial Immortal Realm was entirely under Li Fan's control. He was naturally aware of this uninvited intruder's presence immediately. This made him even more shocked. Undoubtedly, the blue figure was [The Great Net]. But Li Fan had no clue how he appeared inside the high wall. Logically, with the high wall providing concealment, any True Immortal attempting to cross would have attracted Li Fan's attention. After all, he was now a quasi-Shouqiu successor, possessing authority over the major portions of the experimental field. However, [The Great Net] completely disregarded this rule.

"How..." Li Fan stared intently at the mysterious figure before him. Without hesitation, he unleashed his full strength. Shouqiu projections, sealed Heavenly Pillars. Even his own woven Myriad Manifestations Dao Net. He intended to instantly suppress the Nameless [Great Net]. In the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, it was as if a stormy sea had erupted. In the Primordial Immortal Realm, winds and clouds changed, and the heavens tore apart. The Heavenly Emperors and Heavenly Scars, alerted by the phenomenon, finally noticed the two figures confronting each other in the Immortal Realm. Seeing someone dare to challenge the majesty of the Creator Father God, the beings of the Primordial Immortal Realm were collectively enraged. They descended like streams of light, standing behind Li Fan like dark clouds, glaring at the blue figure ahead. They awaited Li Fan's command to charge forward and tear the defiant intruder to shreds.

However, the grim-faced Li Fan's heart was already in turmoil. Because he discovered that the power of the Shouqiu projections... was actually ineffective! It wasn't that the five Shouqiu projections within the high wall had lost their power. It was that Li Fan could no longer borrow power from the projections! In an instant, Li Fan's greatest reliance was inexplicably nullified. "Could this so-called [Great Net] be Shouqiu Gong?" The thought struck him, and Li Fan's heart pounded uncontrollably. At this moment, he was completely incapable of confronting Shouqiu Gong. "No. [The Great Net]'s actual performance is far inferior to the legendary Shouqiu Gong." "He fought back and forth with a group of fallen Nameless experts for tens of thousands of years. He cannot possibly be Shouqiu Gong himself." Li Fan quickly calmed down, rapidly pondering the reason for this bizarre phenomenon. "He stole my control over the Shouqiu projections." "He can freely traverse in and out of the high wall." Li Fan's eyes narrowed, and he already had an answer in his heart. "[The Great Net] and I both originated from within the high wall? And he also entered the hidden space of the experimental field and obtained Shouqiu Gong's inheritance..." "But not from our Utmost Darkness Star Sea." "But from another segmented space within the experimental field."

...

The words spoken by the blue figure then seemed to confirm Li Fan's guess. "Obtained Shouqiu Gong's inheritance, yet engages in such actions?" He pointed to the sealed Heavenly Pillars here and said indifferently. Li Fan's thoughts raced. Since the other party did not attack directly, there was room for negotiation. Regardless, it was time to gather useful information. After all, protected by [Illusion is True], he was already in an invincible position. With a wave of his hand, he dismissed the surrounding Primordial Immortal Realm beings. Li Fan laughed heartily, "So it's a case of the Dragon King of the East Sea offending the Dragon King of the West Sea!" "Perhaps I can call you Senior Brother?" The blue figure calmly refused, "I dare not accept." Li Fan did not pursue the matter further, changing the subject, "What I did, and what you are doing, what is the difference? Both are transforming Immortals into pillars." "This has been the practice in the Immortal Realm since ancient times. Even successive Immortal Emperors could not fault me." Li Fan sneered coldly, "Using immortal bodies to support Dao Annihilation is a great merit. Others may do so, but you cannot, because you received Shouqiu's inheritance." The blue figure interrupted Li Fan, "I cannot. But can you?" "I naturally cannot defy it either." The blue figure interrupted Li Fan's words. "But the lower Star Sea is on the brink of annihilation. There is no time to reason with True Immortals anymore. So I took the initiative to enter the net myself." As the figure spoke, the blue light around him dissipated, revealing his true form. It was exactly the same as the gaunt old man sealed in the deepest part of the Dao Net! Or rather, the two were the same person! "Without setting an example, how can you expect other Nameless experts to willingly follow?" The old man said faintly. "You!" Only now did Li Fan understand. The mysterious Nameless expert who built the Dao Net was actually one of its four pillars! The owner of the Dao Net was also its prisoner! "Since you obtained Shouqiu's writings, why do you still need to be a pillar yourself?" "The Shouqiu projections should suffice!"
