After a moment of shock, Li Fan recovered and squinted, questioning, "Although projections are indeed true, they are still projections. How can they compare to the true Great Dao?" "Of course, the most crucial issue is that there was not enough time." "If I had been given twice the time, perhaps I could have cultivated enough Shouqiu projections." The old man said as he observed the Primordial Immortal Realm here. "Indeed, Harmonious Prosperity and the others did not exaggerate. This place does have the remnants of the Immortal Realm." He nodded in evaluation. "May I know your honorable name, Brother?" Li Fan cupped his hands respectfully. "Having learned my master's Dao, I embody it with my body and will. My Dao path is the word [Embody]." The old man said solemnly.

Chapter 1502: The Immortal Realm is Full of Teachers

"Embody." Li Fan savored the two words.

Then, he solemnly cupped his hands and said, "Setting an example by entering the net willingly. Brother Embody, I admire your actions. However..."

Li Fan let out a cold laugh, "You may call yourself a gentleman, but I am merely a small person who stumbled upon an opportunity and only wishes to survive."

Pointing to the Heavenly Pillars around him, Li Fan said with a calm expression, "Without my master's projections and these Nameless Heavenly Pillars for protection, this star sea would have likely collapsed long ago. To be frank, brother, I am naturally insecure. I fear that one day Dao Annihilation will strike, and my master's projections will be unable to protect me. It is only natural to take some precautions."

Li Fan spoke casually. No matter who heard it, they would find it hard to associate the "minor precautions" he mentioned with the Nameless True Immortals.

"Although I wish to emulate my master and embody the Dao with projections, my comprehension and talent are insufficient. It is truly beyond my ability, and I can only resort to shortcuts."

"Brother, you have woven such a magnificent Dao Net; your cultivation must be extraordinary. Could you teach me?" Li Fan smiled and waved his hand gently.

Before him, the figure of Shouqiu Gong sitting on the mountain and gazing at the sea suddenly appeared. Countless lights and shadows continuously shifted around Shouqiu Gong's figure. This was Li Fan's understanding of [Shouqiu's Jottings].

Seeing his master's image, the Nameless expert Embody immediately became serious. He first bowed, and then carefully observed.

Seeing this, Li Fan felt reassured, and his worries were largely dispelled. The Nameless expert Embody did not prevaricate. He meticulously studied the insights Li Fan presented and then began to explain them on the spot.

As expected of a Nameless expert who had attained [Embody], it felt almost identical to the sensation Li Fan experienced when receiving the inheritance from Shouqiu Gong. It was as if a sage was by his side, imparting wisdom.

Li Fan was so engrossed that he almost forgot his perilous situation. He frequently asked questions, clearing up all the doubts he had accumulated over the past hundred years of his Dao comprehension.

The Nameless expert Embody also answered everything he knew. Li Fan's confusion was completely resolved, and he was overjoyed.

The time spent discussing the Dao seemed to pass in an instant. After the Shouqiu Gong projection gradually disappeared, the Nameless expert Embody focused his gaze on Li Fan again.

"Your doubts have been resolved, but your crime cannot be erased."

"You rely on your master's inheritance and act recklessly; you deserve punishment."

"Death can be avoided, but you cannot escape punishment!"

"Your punishment is to reside with me in the depths of the Dao Net and reflect on your actions!"

As the Nameless expert Embody shouted, a brilliant azure light erupted and enveloped Li Fan. Li Fan clearly saw that the azure light before him was not just ordinary blue light. It was a superposition of countless dense Dao strings! Each one felt as heavy as a Heavenly Pillar. When the Nameless expert Embody made his move, it was as if he was casting the entire Dao Net upon Li Fan.

"That old fellow is so strong!" Li Fan silently marveled.

But he was not afraid; instead, he became interested. Since there was no threat to his life, he might as well indulge the opponent in a spar. After all, ever since Li Fan ascended to immortality, he had not had a sparring partner of comparable strength for a long time.

"Illusion is True!" Li Fan first chanted silently in his heart.

The rapidly approaching Dao Net instantly grasped at emptiness. Li Fan was clearly standing there, but like a fisherman's net unable to catch water, the rules protecting him now transcended the Great Dao, making it impossible for the Dao Net to capture him.

"Brother, watch my technique!" Facing the Nameless expert Embody's shock and uncertainty, Li Fan let out a cold laugh.

With a flick of his finger, myriad Dao threads intertwined with the azure Dao Net. The net formed by Li Fan's Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul began to erode the Nameless expert Embody's comprehension of the Great Dao simultaneously. In reality, this meant that the azure light within the Dao Net began to flicker unstantly. Dark shadows continuously spawned in various places. Ink Slaughter's innate restraint over the Great Dao caused the Dao Net to be unable to resist at all for a time, allowing Li Fan to devour it at will.

Countless insights into the Great Dao continuously poured into Li Fan's mind. The efficiency was even higher than when he had previously absorbed Grand Master Tiandu. Li Fan keenly sensed that this not only included the insights of the Nameless expert Embody but also the residual insights of the True Immortals who had been sealed within the Dao Net.

"Wicked path!" Just as Li Fan was gleefully stealing these insights, the Nameless expert Embody roared.

The azure Dao Net, which had been flickering under the invasion of shadows, instantly stabilized. It was as if it was no longer just a solitary net, but had a substantial support behind it.

Li Fan looked at the azure halo before him, and for a moment, he felt the illusion of facing the Mountains and Seas.

"Deep as the sea, stable as the mountain."

"The Great Dao is formless, its origin lies beyond."

Li Fan suddenly gained some insight. Although his Myriad Manifestations Dao Net had been deduced for a hundred years and had devoured many Great Daos, its foundation was still not entirely stable. It was manageable when dealing with opponents weaker than him. But if he encountered an opponent of equal or superior strength, a slight push might be enough to break free from the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net. Though the Dao Net had woven myriad manifestations, it couldn't tightly bind enemies.

However, the Dao Net woven by the Nameless expert Embody had no such flaw. Like the palm of a mountain and sea, it pressed down firmly, anchoring the swirling Dao Net. Just as Li Biren had previously used the Wuji Heavenly Pillar's power to rampage within the Dao Net and even dismantle three Heavenly Pillars, the true foundation of the Star Sea's Dao Net remained intact.

"The Heavenly Pillars were just pillars; the foundation of the anchor points remained."

"As long as he captured more True Immortals, the Dao Net could quickly recover."

Li Fan understood. The reason the Star Sea’s Dao Net hadn’t collapsed earlier, despite Li Biren's actions, was that its foundation, supported by the power of Mountains and Seas, remained. The Nameless expert Embody's Dao Net, bolstered by the power of Mountains and Seas, was naturally beyond the reach of Li Fan's techniques.

Like a delicious piece of meat suddenly turning into a notoriously difficult bone to chew, Li Fan had no choice but to temporarily give up and retract his Myriad Manifestations Dao Net.

"Brother Embody, you have marvelous skills!"

"Be careful!" The praise and the sneak attack came simultaneously.

"Since you borrow the power of Mountains and Seas, I shall sever your connection with them!" A cold light flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

Although this was ostensibly a spar, if he could truly capture this Nameless expert Embody, Li Fan would not hesitate. Mountains and Seas transcend the mortal world. Few people in the world could see the true form of Mountains and Seas. Li Fan was certain that this Nameless expert Embody had never personally witnessed Mountains and Seas. The reason he could borrow the power of Mountains and Seas was likely through the description in Shouqiu Gong's inheritance.

However, Li Fan happened to be one of the few people who had. In a trance, it was as if he had returned to the boundless Infinite Sea. In the distance stood the Upper Mountain, which had no peak. Amidst the fusion of Mountains and Seas, turbulent echoes reverberated. With the mystical power of [Illusion is True], Li Fan did not return to the Mountains and Seas, but it seemed as if he had personally experienced them again. Hence, he sensed the faint connection between the Nameless expert Embody and the Mountains and Seas.

Although he did not understand how this connection was formed, it did not prevent Li Fan from employing a trick of substitution. Replacing Mountains and Seas with himself! The Nameless expert Embody could not distinguish between Li Fan, empowered by [Illusion is True], and the true Mountains and Seas. Compared to the lofty and unattainable Infinite Sea and Upper Mountain, Li Fan, the imitator, would actively approach. Under these circumstances, it was only logical for the Nameless expert Embody to mistake Li Fan for the Mountains and Seas.

Thus, the connection between the Nameless expert Embody’s azure Dao Net and the Mountains and Seas gradually became chaotic and was eventually severed. Li Fan, who had briefly borrowed the name of Mountains and Seas, seized this fleeting opportunity and saw the reason for this connection.

"As expected." A faint figure stood with his hands behind his back amidst the Mountains and Seas. Shouqiu Gong, although existing in the mortal world, had left his mark within the Mountains and Seas. The Nameless expert Embody, a disciple of Shouqiu, was not an ordinary disciple. He had inherited Shouqiu's legacy and thus could sense the mark left by Shouqiu Gong within the Mountains and Seas, allowing him to borrow their power to suppress the Dao Net!

In a flash, Li Fan also locked onto the location of Shouqiu Gong's mark within the Mountains and Seas. However, he did not rashly attempt to interact with it. As long as he could master this mark, no matter where he was in the future, no longer confined within the high wall, he could borrow the power of Mountains and Seas like the Nameless expert Embody.

But the problem was... Shouqiu Gong himself still existed in the mortal world. The Nameless expert Embody was Shouqiu Gong's legitimate disciple. Embodying the Dao with his body and will, such a disciple, borrowing his master's name and power, was something Shouqiu Gong would certainly not blame. Perhaps if he sensed his disciple was in danger, he might even traverse space and time to offer assistance.

And what about him, Li Fan? He used Shouqiu's projection, and it was through his clone Li Biren. Moreover, he had used the projection meant to bear Dao Annihilation as a weapon to seal Nameless True Immortals, undoubtedly resorting to deception. It was fine within the high wall. But if he rashly approached Shouqiu Gong... Li Fan was certain that even if Shouqiu Gong was magnanimous and extraordinary, he might not particularly care. But a casual slap from him would be something the current Li Fan could not withstand. It might even expose his true existence.

"Perhaps, in a life-or-death situation, I can proactively trigger [True Revelation]. Shouqiu Gong's name should be terrifying enough. It could cause chaos as a cover, and I could then calmly revert to reality." Li Fan had used such a method numerous times since his mortal life, and it was now second nature.

"It's a pity, it seems I cannot easily deal with this Nameless expert Embody."

"As expected, students who perform well are their teachers' favorites," Li Fan thought regretfully.

Recognizing the reality, Li Fan quickly changed his strategy. Since the duration of [Illusion is True] impersonating Mountains and Seas had ended, Li Fan actively halted the struggle between them.

"Brother Embody's cultivation is indeed far superior to mine. I have learned a lot today." He changed his expression and said with seemingly sincere admiration.

Facing Li Fan's flattery, the Nameless expert Embody snorted coldly without responding. Li Fan's actions, which easily neutralized the Dao Saber Dao Sword, far exceeded his expectations. With such capabilities, he had to be treated with caution.

Li Fan did not care about Embody's cold demeanor and continued to say with a smile, "Actually, speaking of which, Brother and I have no irreconcilable conflict."

"I am merely seeking a place of peace."

"It is not impossible to release the True Immortals imprisoned in the Heavenly Pillars..."

Embody seemed surprised, looking at Li Fan, almost as if the words "I don't believe you" were written on his face.

"Does Brother Embody care about these imprisoned True Immortals in the Heavenly Pillars because they are like me?" Li Fan countered.

Embody pondered for a moment and then nodded calmly, "All Immortals in the Immortal Realm have received grace and learned the methods of our master. In a sense, all Immortals in the Immortal Realm are disciples of Shouqiu. How can fellow disciples harm each other?"

"Well said, 'How can fellow disciples harm each other!' Brother's words today truly enlightened me!" Li Fan exclaimed, clapping his hands in admiration after a moment of surprise. Naturally, he now referred to the Nameless expert as 'Brother.'

After a pause, seeing that Embody did not object, Li Fan continued with a smile, "Under Brother's guidance today, I have realized my past mistakes. As I said before, I am willing to release the True Immortals imprisoned in the Heavenly Pillars unconditionally. Furthermore, I can assist Brother in rebuilding the Dao Net..."

Embody asked, "What are the conditions?" Obviously, he had already understood Li Fan's character.

"My vision of creating a safe haven has always remained unchanged. Brother, you do not wish for the projections left by our master to turn to dust in the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, do you?" Li Fan continued, "Brother, you must know that I have a method that satisfies both of us, which will not harm our fellow Immortal brothers."

"Foreign races, Taigu Great Dao manifestations. Has Brother heard of them?" Li Fan asked with a smile.

Embody's expression shifted slightly, "Nameless foreign races? When did such monsters appear in this world?"

"No, no. It is not from this world, but from beyond the heavens!" Li Fan pointed into the distance. Beyond the high wall, beyond the possibilities.

At this point, Embody's expression completely changed. "How many?" He asked, his voice deepening, completely unlike his previous demeanor of discussing Immortal Realm matters.

"Thirteen." Li Fan uttered the word calmly.

"Hmm?" Even Embody was startled by this number. "Is this true?" His voice rose several octaves.

Li Fan said seriously, "How could I dare to deceive Brother? This is precisely why I have strived to increase my strength with all my might. Those thirteen Taigu Great Dao forms are simply too aggressive. I am unable to sleep or eat in peace." Li Fan sighed deeply.

Embody pondered for a moment and then made a decisive statement, "Junior Brother, do not worry. With me here, even if all thirteen Nameless foreign races attack together, they will not be able to harm you."

"You are right. With the addition of these thirteen Taigu Great Dao forms, the Star Sea's plan to lure is completely resolved!"

Chapter 1503: A Spirit Stone from the Mountains and Seas

"To be honest, brother, I have a divine treasure called [Myriad Beasts Wheel], which can restrain foreign Nameless experts. However, its power is limited, and it can only restrain about eight of them. As for the rest, it will have to trouble Brother." Li Fan said with surprising frankness.

At the same time, he displayed the treasure gifted by Di San Mo. Embody looked at the illusory images of strange life forms appearing within the wheel and nodded slightly, "Indeed, it carries the aura of Great Dao from beyond the heavens. Heh heh, Junior Brother, rest assured. With your elder brother here, these foreign races will not cause any significant trouble."

Embody's confidence did not seem feigned, which made Li Fan even more curious. "Brother is powerful, but with just you alone, you might not be able to defeat these foreign Nameless experts working together, right? Could it be..." Li Fan pointed to the sky, hinting at Shouqiu Gong.

Embody smiled nonchalantly, "This is a small matter. There's no need to trouble Master. While it might be appropriate to show some restraint when dealing with fellow disciples, when dealing with these foreign races..."

"One can resort to any means." Li Fan's eyes lit up, and he cupped his hands, "Please enlighten me, Brother."

Embody did not answer directly but first asked inexplicably, "The one beside my True Body, is that your clone?"

"Brother's perception is indeed extraordinary. My clone is not connected by blood essence, but only by a spiritual connection, which others can hardly detect."

"Then watch carefully."

The scene returned to the depths of the Star Sea's Dao Net. Li Biren and the original body of Embody were locked in a stalemate. Chaos and Harmonious Prosperity wanted to assist, but were blocked by the surging myriad Dao strings, as if the gaunt figure concealed another Dao Net within him! Even with the power of Wuji, it would take some time to dissolve these Dao strings. Chaos and Harmonious Prosperity could only defend.

"Who is this person? Strange!"

"These Dao strings seem to be projections of the Great Daos of heaven and earth, but in reality, they are mostly his own insights. I can even see my Dao of Harmonious Prosperity within them! How is this possible?"

The two Nameless experts instantly recognized the peculiarity of Embody's power, and their hearts filled with dread. However, they were completely unaware that Li Biren and Embody, who had been mortal enemies moments ago, had now become allies. Moreover, Embody had begun to actively explain and demonstrate for Li Biren.

"Junior Brother, watch carefully." Embody's hand, holding the Wuji Heavenly Rod, did not loosen but gripped it tighter. Li Biren sensed that the Wuji aura churning within the opponent's body was becoming increasingly intense.

Suddenly, a hundred Dao strings moved as if they had spiritual sentience, all attacking Li Biren.

"This is..."

"Wuji?!"

These hundred Dao strings could ignore the defense of the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net, and even the Wuji Heavenly Rod was no exception. If Li Biren had not immediately used the Dao Saber Dao Sword to block these Dao strings, he would have likely been impaled by them by now.

"The name Embody is not just empty words. It is practiced with body and will." Billions of Dao strings heavily surrounded Li Biren, isolating them from the probing senses of Harmonious Prosperity and Chaos outside.

"While constructing the Star Sea Dao Net externally, I embody the Dao Net internally. Even if the Great Dao is annihilated and the Dao Net ceases to exist one day, I can still become the Dao Net, become the Great Dao!" Embody's voice thundered.

In Li Biren's eyes, this gaunt old man seemed to truly be the embodiment of the Star Sea's Dao Net, sitting majestically, bearing the weight of heaven and earth!

"Brother Embody's actions are indeed admirable. But if it's just this, it's probably not enough. After all, the Immortals have departed, and this world's Great Dao is already incomplete. Brother's Dao will be further diminished... And those thirteen Primordial Dao forms of the foreign races, each one is a complete Great Dao. A fully formed infant might not be as strong as a single powerful limb," Li Biren shook his head.

Embody did not directly refute Li Biren's words but smiled and asked, "What if I embody a complete Great Dao?"

"Observe!" The Dao strings erupting from Embody seemed endless, completely obscuring the surrounding sky. The original Star Sea Dao Net was merely an insignificant part of it.

Embody's body completely disappeared, and Li Biren seemed to have fallen into an infinite starry sky, with radiant Great Daos everywhere! Although much more blurry than directly observing the true Great Dao itself, one could still benefit greatly from careful observation.

Li Biren looked at the true Dao Net hidden within Embody's body and suddenly thought of two words. Ming Dao Immortal, [Supreme Dao Scripture].

"What he is doing, embodying the Dao, is essentially no different from Ming Dao, and the Dao Scripture."

"Ming Dao Immortal manifests the formless Dao and then translates the Great Dao, making it visible, understandable, and usable by the world."

"Perhaps Embody realizes his own limitations and cannot emulate Ming Dao Immortal's feat. He is simply willing to become a 'mirror' that reflects all the Great Daos of the heavens."

"However, being a 'Dao Mirror' is also an extraordinary feat. In addition to his own understanding of the Great Daos of the heavens, the most crucial factor is..."

"The timing. Not to mention the Immortal Realm suffering calamity and the Great Dao being submerged by Dao Annihilation, even in the past, when the Immortal Realm was intact, many Nameless True Immortals transcended and departed, leaving the Great Daos of heaven and earth incomplete. Where did the Great Daos he reflects come from?"

Li Biren's thoughts raced. As if sensing Li Biren's doubts, Embody's faint voice echoed from all directions, "I was originally a spirit stone by the side of the Mountains and Seas. Having been nurtured in the Immortal Realm for hundreds of millions of years, I still could not gestate. Even when Master was about to transcend and depart, I had not yet gained sentience."

"Later, Master discovered a star sea in the lower realm experimental field that might help me. Thus, he left me here."

Li Biren saw a dark, chaotic star sea before his eyes. It was one of the countless block spaces within the Immortal Realm's experimental field. Li Fan had observed this area before and found nothing special.

The scene reversed, and myriad blue lights emerged from the darkness. This was the original appearance of this star sea from countless years ago. It was a vast, boundless ocean. Water overflowed, filling the entire star sea. The source was actually a small mountain peak, no larger than a palm. Streams flowed endlessly from the mountain. This stream seemed to exist outside the cycle of the mortal world; once born, it did not participate in the cycle of heaven and earth and did not disappear. Over time, it accumulated more and more, gradually occupying the entire star sea. Only the small mountain peak in the center of the Star Sea remained unaffected. Shouqiu Gong placed the spirit stone there, at the peak, by the spring's source. Washed by the stream day and night, it eventually took human form!

...

Li Biren sighed, "So, Brother has such an extraordinary background!"

"When I was a spirit stone, I reflected all the scenes of the world. Those who have passed away and disappeared are all within my past. Except for those who have truly transcended, I can reflect them all with my mind." Embody's Dao Net, which had filled the surroundings, vanished, and he returned to his appearance as a gaunt old man.

"It only takes time."

"Unfortunately, time is of the essence," Embody sighed. "As you have seen, it took me tens of thousands of years to construct the Star Sea Dao Net. If I were to re-establish the myriad Daos of the heavens, it would likely take millions of years..."

Li Biren pondered for a moment and somewhat understood, "If not for the pressure of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, Brother, you would not have needed so much time, right?"

"Precisely. Ultimately, I am merely embodying its Dao image, not the true Great Dao itself. If there are no True Immortals to embody the Dao as pillars, even if I could recreate the complete Great Dao, it would be like a castle in the air, fragile and easily scattered!"

"Brother, you need not be so modest. Manifesting the complete Great Dao, such a feat and realm, is by no means comparable to ordinary Nameless experts. I just don't know what Brother meant by resorting to 'any means' earlier..." Li Biren was very curious.

"Replacing the Dao with the image, and transforming the image into Dao." The gaunt old man, still seated, slowly uttered the eight characters.

Li Biren carefully pondered these words. "The Dao paths among different possibilities may have slight differences, but they ultimately remain within the mortal world and cannot escape the Mountains and Seas. I, a spirit stone born by the Mountains and Seas, can likely devour and absorb them. And then transform them into Dao images within my memory."

"Furthermore, perhaps influenced by the Mountains and Seas, my absorption is not particularly difficult, and to a certain extent, I can even ignore the opponent's will."

As if to verify his words, Embody tightened his grip on the Wuji Heavenly Rod. Instantly, the Wuji aura surging from his body intensified fivefold. Li Biren sensed that the Wuji Heavenly Rod itself had been weakened. Although [Wuji] remained [Wuji], its upper limit had weakened.

"These are likely disciples of the Sage Lords sealed within. Venerable Wuji..." Embody shook his head and reinjected the Wuji power he had seized back into the Wuji Heavenly Rod. The Wuji Heavenly Rod, having regained its lost portion, returned to its original state.

"Having my Dao stripped away, I can transform it within my body. If those thirteen foreign Primordial Dao forms dare to come..."

"Then let them stay and become Heavenly Pillars," Embody decided in a few words, determining the fate of these foreign Nameless experts.

Meanwhile, Embody's action of weakening the upper limit of the [Wuji] Great Dao caused Li Fan to ponder deeply. Because, in a certain sense, this method seemed similar to his [True Illusion] ability of reducing spiritual essence.

"However, [True Illusion] involves existence and directly removes it, while Embody's innate divine ability merely transforms its nature and cannot directly erase it. But perhaps both are related to Mountains and Seas..."

"It is fortunate that the former Shouqiu Gong picked up and enlightened this spirit stone. With Embody's current moral principles, as long as he does not openly act against his beliefs, he will not cause trouble. Otherwise, even without using the Shouqiu Gong imprint, it would be extremely difficult to deal with him if he were to unleash this innate divine ability." Li Fan secretly marveled. The power of Mountains and Seas transcends the mortal world. All powers originating from the mortal world are no match for it. Only the transformation between True and False can contend with it.

"Perhaps Shouqiu Gong left behind his imprint, and also with a degree of monitoring. Otherwise, if he were to go mad and lose control, the destruction he would cause to the mortal world would be too great."

While Li Fan was contemplating, he had already decided that Embody was a friend, not an enemy. "Brother, rest assured. Since you trust me so much, I will never reveal your origins to anyone else," Li Fan vowed sincerely.

"Brother has such abilities, so I have no worries. However, it is not easy to directly release the True Immortals sealed within the Heavenly Pillars. I fear that the support may not be enough, and Dao Annihilation is imminent..." Li Fan explained with a troubled expression.

"I understand this logic, Brother. "Embody responded, stating he was not rigid. "Once there are enough foreign Heavenly Pillars to supplement, we can release them. I wonder, when will those foreign Nameless experts arrive?"

"Fifty short days, or a hundred long days." Embody nodded, "That's good. It's not too long. The grievances they suffered are not too great."

Li Fan agreed, "Heh heh, Brother is truly compassionate."

The billions of Dao strings that obscured the sky were retracted. Harmonious Prosperity and Chaos, who were still on high alert, looked at Li Biren and Embody standing together, as if they were close brothers, and were both astonished.

"Senior, what is the situation?" Chaos transmitted telepathically.

"It was a misunderstanding. This is [The Great Net], my senior brother." Li Biren's words greatly surprised the two Nameless True Immortals. They carefully examined the frail old man before them but could never connect him with the pair of large blue hands.

Embody, on the other hand, was too lazy to explain. He simply said, "Although you have repeatedly thwarted my plans, out of fellow disciple affection, I will not hold it against you." His words left Harmonious Prosperity and Chaos utterly bewildered, having no idea where this "fellow disciple" relationship originated. However, they dared not ask further.

Thus, a storm, or perhaps a farce, finally concluded. In the entire affair, although some True Immortals died, there were no casualties among the Nameless realm experts. They were merely temporarily sealed within the Heavenly Pillars and could be released at any time. As for the Immortal Hunters and mortals in the Star Sea... they were not within Embody's scope of consideration at all.

Li Fan felt he had a certain understanding of this "senior brother." His "fellow disciples" were also graded. Those who received the true inheritance from Shouqiu Gong were naturally the closest. Among the Immortals of the Immortal Realm, their importance was further divided by cultivation level. As for mortals in the lower realm, they were merely ants to do errands.

"I can only say that, as expected of a spirit stone born by the Mountains and Seas, although enlightened by Shouqiu Gong and awakened to sentience and morality, deep down, they are still cold-blooded and heartless," Li Fan thought inwardly.

But he showed no outward expression, addressing Embody as "Senior Brother" with great intimacy. Perhaps because he had never been truly addressed as such since his birth, Embody, feeling satisfied, became even more friendly towards Li Fan.

During their conversation, Li Fan also learned why a Nameless True Immortal like Embody would borrow the strength of mortals to maintain the Dao Net. "Mere mortals can actually contend with Brother?" Li Fan asked in disbelief, full of skepticism.

"If I were to fight with my life on the line, they naturally wouldn't be my match. However, even if they were defeated, they could still harm me. Therefore, I became interested in them." Embody's words, when mentioning the word [Jing Fen], caused Li Fan's heart to tremble, and a sense of foreboding enveloped him.

He subconsciously activated [Illusion is True]. Almost instantly, Li Fan felt a chilling sensation, as if a gaze had swept past Embody. However, after merely glancing, the attention was withdrawn. Embody seemed accustomed to it and continued speaking. He was completely unaware that Li Fan's outwardly calm heart was already in turmoil.

"Great Sage... Sage Lord."

"Mentioning it would be perceived."

"The fourth Sage Lord of the Immortal Realm, who is perceived whenever mentioned?"

"I was almost doomed by this old fellow!" Li Fan couldn't help but feel fear. The Sage Lord stood at the pinnacle of the Immortal Realm, even capable of altering Mountains and Seas to some extent. His power was unquestionable. Even with [True Revelation]'s protection, Li Fan was not entirely confident in escaping unscathed from such a powerful being. How could he not feel lingering fear?

Fortunately, through years of simulation, Li Fan had developed an extremely keen intuition. Acting on instinct, he timely activated the divine ability [Illusion is True], thus narrowly escaping disaster. Li Fan's [Illusion is True] this time simulated an ordinary immortal in the mortal world. Unlike previous instances where he transformed into targets with special properties, this time he hid his own special nature. If not for the fact that Li Fan had repeatedly practiced this during his previous enlightenments, he would not have reacted so quickly.

"Although [Illusion is True] cannot be maintained indefinitely, transforming into an ordinary True Immortal in the mortal world has minimal consumption and can almost be sustained perpetually. However, changing the effect of [Illusion is True] requires another twenty-four hours."

"I will need to be constantly vigilant when interacting with this old fellow in the future," Li Fan tried to calm himself and stop thinking about Jing Fen. He listened as Embody continued, "After I emerged from that experimental field, I naturally had to embody my master's Dao and bear Dao Annihilation. However, the surrounding star sea was desolate, and I didn't know where to find True Immortals. Coincidentally, the Master of the Sage Merchant told me they had a way..."

"Master of the Sage Merchant?" Li Fan's attention was drawn back.

"This mortal does have some ability. He can track the subtle connection between True Immortals and Mountains and Seas, and accurately locate hidden True Immortals in the vast, desolate, and dead star sea. While I can also do this, it would take more time. Having someone else do it is naturally better."

"Fortunately, my luck was good, and the first Nameless expert I encountered, [Grind], was relatively reasonable and willing to leave behind a projection to embody the Dao according to Master Gong's will."

"But as I said before, Dao Annihilation came faster than expected. There was simply not enough time," Embody said with some regret. "By the time [Grind] comprehends Master's divine techniques and creates a projection, perhaps this star sea would have long been swallowed by Dao Annihilation. How could my first battle after emerging from seclusion end so hastily? In a moment of urgency, I had no choice but to embody the Dao myself."

After Li Fan and Embody gradually became familiar with each other, Embody's narrative differed slightly from before. However, overall, it still aligned with Li Fan's judgment of Embody's character. Embody was originally a spirit stone from the side of the Mountains and Seas, an entity beyond the mortal world, naturally indifferent. However, he was enlightened by Shouqiu Gong and bound by rules. Therefore, his actions remained within the bounds of propriety.

"The effect was still good; it managed to resist the approaching Dao Annihilation Tribulation, though Grind inevitably had some complaints. But seeing that I myself entered the prison, he could not say much. As compensation, I even specially crafted the City of Ultimate Bliss for him. With a clone enjoying himself and venting outside, he is unique among the Immortals in the Dao Net." Embody said dismissively.

In his view, embodying Dao Annihilation to resist Dao Annihilation and fulfilling Shouqiu Gong's ideals was an immense honor.

"But not all True Immortals in the world are as reasonable as [Grind]. The vast majority are uncooperative. Out of consideration for our fellow disciple's feelings, I cannot directly attack them. Thus, I had to rely on the strength of these mortals in the Star Sea."

"I saved them from the Dao Annihilation Tribulation back then. Therefore, they are grateful to me and follow my every word. The Administration Council and Immortal Hunt also came into being as a result. It seems there are even some survivors from within the high wall..." Embody's tone was dismissive.

Li Fan could somewhat understand Embody's perspective. To him, these mortals were indeed not within his scope of consideration. Even though Li Fan had almost torn apart the Dao Net and killed countless Immortal Hunters, as long as he addressed Embody as "Senior Brother" a few more times, Embody could dismiss the matter. In short, the status of fellow disciples who inherited Shouqiu Gong's legacy was vastly different from that of mortal ants in Embody's heart.

"Even if mortals were wielding the weapons, with Brother overseeing, capturing True Immortals of the Star Sea should be easy. Why did I hear that the Immortal Hunt suffered repeated setbacks? They were even forced into a disadvantageous position at one point?"

Embody narrowed his eyes upon hearing this. Li Fan sensed a chilling killing intent emanating from him, along with a subtle, almost imperceptible greed. After a long pause, Embody finally admitted, "If they were all like Chaos and Harmonious Prosperity, there would be no trouble. The most crucial one is [Reverse]..."

"[Reverse]?" Li Fan immediately thought of the Nameless True Immortal from the True Immortal faction, rumored to have crafted the treasure, the Reverse Boat. He asked in surprise, "Does such a method of reversing time truly exist in the world?"

Embody's tone became somber, "Although there is no definitive proof, it is highly likely. Hmph, every time they can turn decay into magic and reverse the tide of battle. How can there be such a coincidence?"

"Although I tried everything, I could do nothing about this matter. Later, [Reverse]'s whereabouts became unknown. Only then did the True Immortals gradually become somewhat more compliant."

...

Li Fan fell into deep thought. "Reverse Boat, the second of the Three Avoidance Methods."

"If time could be reversed, what would happen when it encountered [True]." While thinking this in his heart, Li Fan said aloud, "[Reverse] disappeared. Perhaps he returned to the past by riding the Reverse Boat?"

"Perhaps. It's a pity I couldn't capture him. Otherwise, if I could return to the time when I was still a spirit stone by Master's side, Master would surely be pleasantly surprised." Such a statement coming from a gaunt old man was truly strange. However, it was enough to show how deeply Shouqiu Gong influenced Embody.

Li Fan was speechless, and both fell silent for a moment. Finally confirming the existence of a method to reverse time, Li Fan became fixated on it, hoping to gather more information from Embody. "I don't think such a heaven-defying divine ability exists in the world. How could Master, who is who he is, be unable to reverse time? It's hard to imagine that [Reverse] would be more powerful than Master."

After a period of silence, Li Fan shook his head and said.

"Regarding this point, I was also confused and sought advice from Master." Embody suddenly said.

"Oh? What did Master say?" Li Fan's heart skipped a beat. Not only because it concerned the reversal of time, but also because he discovered that Embody could communicate with Shouqiu Gong at any time.

"It is irrelevant to the final outcome."

"These four words, however, are something I still cannot comprehend." Embody sighed with regret.

"Irrelevant to the final outcome." Li Fan slowly repeated the words in his heart. It was clear that Shouqiu Gong's "final outcome" referred to the end of the mortal world, ultimately destined to be submerged by the Dao Annihilation Tribulation in a million years.

"Does this mean that the power to reverse time cannot solve such a catastrophe?" Li Fan found it hard to believe and was completely baffled. However, Shouqiu Gong's thoughts were beyond the current comprehension of Li Fan. From the perspective outside the mortal world, within the Mountains and Seas, the perspective was likely completely different from within the mortal world. Since Shouqiu Gong said so, there must be his reasoning. Li Fan could only comfort himself this way.

"Master's divine words are truly hard to fathom. Brother, do not worry. I do not understand either." Hearing Li Fan say this, Embody's mood instantly improved.

Li Fan continued to inquire, "Hearing Brother's words, it seems you can often receive teachings from Master? If you have such an opportunity next time, please don't forget to bring me along!"

"Although I obtained the [Shouqiu's Jottings] from Master, I have never had the chance to hear his words or see his person..." Li Fan's face was filled with envy.

Embody appeared somewhat pleased, yet also regretful, "It's not as easy as you imagine. Master has transcended and his movements are unpredictable. Moreover, the imprint exists within the Mountains and Seas. It is very normal to not receive a reply for several hundred years even after sending a message."

"That is truly a pity!" Li Fan sighed, but secretly felt relieved. "However, Junior Brother, rest assured, if I receive any news from Master next time, I will definitely bring you along!" Embody promised earnestly.

"Then thank you, Senior Brother!" Li Fan showed a happy expression.

...

The interaction between the two fellow disciples was indeed very pleasant. Although Embody's strength was unfathomable, after being enlightened by Shouqiu Gong, he was bound by rules. Li Fan catered to his preferences, and naturally, he could easily manipulate him. Gradually, Embody began to regard Li Fan as the most trustworthy person besides Shouqiu Gong.

Li Fan also benefited greatly from Embody. The most crucial of these were the complete Great Dao projections in Embody's memory. Although they were not the Great Daos themselves, they did not have a substantial impact on the advancement of Li Fan's Myriad Manifestations Dao Net. However, they directly unlocked the entire Great Dao bestiary that was previously shrouded in mist, allowing Li Fan to precisely hunt his targets in the future. Benefiting from their harmonious relationship, Embody was not stingy with these complete Great Dao memories. He often shared them with Li Fan. However, the complete Great Dao projections of the [Primordial] possibility were dozens of times more complex than the Great Daos Li Fan had previously glimpsed. It was not something that could be completely comprehended in a short time. Therefore, Li Fan almost always stayed by Embody's side.

As for his clone Li Biren, he was outside helping to repair the Dao Net. With the assistance of True Immortals like Chaos and Harmonious Prosperity, as well as the countless beings in the Primordial Immortal Realm, the Star Sea Dao Net was repaired quickly. In the Star Sea region, the actual controllers of the two largest forces were often engaged in profound discussions and pleasant conversations, bringing a rare period of peace and tranquility to the starry sky. Until thirty-three years later.

Harmonious Prosperity suddenly requested an audience with Li Fan. "A message from the Guangwu Star Sea?" Li Fan was somewhat surprised. He hadn't expected that after witnessing his divine ability to seize the Dao Saber Dao Sword with his bare hands, the Guangwu Star Sea would dare to come knocking again.

"What did they say?" Li Fan asked with great interest.

Harmonious Prosperity's expression was subtle. He glanced at Embody, who was still sitting silently beside Li Fan. "Brother and I are not blood brothers, but we are closer than brothers. We have no secrets between us. Speak freely!" Li Fan waved his hand. Harmonious Prosperity then recounted the events truthfully. "That [Star Peeker] first inquired about my recent situation. I did not reveal anything, merely pretending to have fled in panic and barely survived."

"Then [Star Peeker] actually proposed to continue cooperating."

"I resolutely refused. However, [Star Peeker] was relentless, seemingly..." Harmonious Prosperity glanced at Li Fan's expression and whispered, "It seems determined to capture Senior."

Before Li Fan could respond, Embody sneered. "You can agree to it for now and lure him here."

"I want to see what capability this [Star Peeker] truly possesses." Li Fan pondered, finding the situation peculiar. The Star Sea's Dao Net was a collaborative effort. Now, a similar creation appeared in the Primordial Immortal Realm, so how could they not be astonished and uncertain? Li Fan's displayed strength, capable of easily neutralizing the attack of the Dao Saber Dao Sword and even subduing this treasure with his bare hands, undoubtedly surpassed the realm of ordinary Nameless True Immortals. Yet, even so, the Star Sea faction represented by [Star Peeker] was determined to capture Li Fan.

Li Fan and the Guangwu Star Sea had no irreconcilable conflicts. "So, did they deduce the method of me collecting the Dao Saber Dao Sword?" Regarding [True Revelation], Li Fan had to become serious. Judging by the ability to casually produce treasures like the Dao Saber Dao Sword, the Guangwu Star Sea faction was likely not weak. There might even be Transcendent experts capable of traveling to other possibilities. After all, the Dao Saber Dao Sword originated from another possibility.

"Interesting." Although Li Fan could simply ignore [Star Peeker], the saying "One cannot sleep with a rival nearby" held true. Being constantly coveted by others felt unpleasant. Most importantly, Li Fan now had a powerful senior brother standing guard before him. "Let Embody test the strength of the Guangwu Star Sea first," Li Fan's eyes flashed with a cold light.

"Do as my senior brother says!" Li Fan commanded sternly.

Embody was very pleased with Li Fan's response. In his view, Li Fan's prompt agreement was much better than his previous hesitant responses. "Junior Brother, rest assured. As your elder brother always says."

"As long as I, your senior brother, am here, no one will be able to harm you," Embody solemnly promised.

Li Fan showed a grateful expression. At the same time, he instructed his clone, Li Biren, to prepare.

In the Primordial Immortal Realm. The influx of power from the Infinite Sea had already reached a balance. The continent within the high wall now differed little from the Immortal Realm in Li Fan's memory.

Chapter 1504: Mystery of the Finale

"In truth, ordinary mortals naturally cannot harm me. It is merely borrowing strength."

"However, being able to borrow the power of Great Sage Jing Fen is also a remarkable achievement." When the words "Great Sage Jing Fen" were spoken, just like when mentioning Duke Shouqiu, Cheng Dao's expression turned solemn and reverent.

Li Fan's heart skipped a beat, and an ominous premonition enveloped him.

Subconsciously, he cast the [Illusion is True] divine ability.

Mere moments later, Li Fan felt a chill run down his spine, as if a gaze had swept past Cheng Dao. However, it was only a fleeting glance, with no further attention paid.

This sense of being watched then dissipated.

Cheng Dao also seemed accustomed to it and continued speaking.

Completely oblivious, Li Fan, whose expression appeared calm, was already experiencing a tempest in his heart.

"Great Sage... Sage Lord."

"The Fourth Sage Lord of the Immortal Realm, who is perceived whenever mentioned?"

"I was almost harmed by this old fellow!"

Sage Lords stood at the apex of the Immortal Realm, even capable of influencing mountains and seas to a certain extent; their power was unquestionable. Even with the protection of [Return to Truth], Li Fan was not entirely confident of retreating unscathed from such a powerful being.

How could he not feel lingering fear?

Fortunately, through years of simulated reincarnations, Li Fan had cultivated an extremely keen spiritual sense. Acting on instinct, he had timely employed the divine ability [Illusion is True], thus narrowly escaping disaster.

Li Fan's [Illusion is True] this time simulated an ordinary immortal in the mortal world. Unlike previous instances where he transformed into targets with special properties, this time he concealed his own special nature. If not for the fact that Li Fan had repeatedly practiced this during his previous enlightenments, he would not have reacted so quickly.

"Although the [Illusion is True] divine ability cannot be maintained indefinitely. However, merely transforming into an ordinary True Immortal in the mortal world, with minimal consumption, can almost be sustained perpetually. But to alter the effect of [Illusion is True], another twenty-four hours are needed."

"In the future, when interacting with this old fellow, I must remain constantly vigilant," Li Fan tried to calm his emotions and stopped thinking about Great Sage Jing Fen.

Cheng Dao continued speaking: "After I emerged from that experimental field, I naturally had to embody my master's Dao and bear Dao Annihilation. But the surrounding star sea was barren, and I couldn't find True Immortals anywhere. Coincidentally, the Master of the Sage Merchant told me they had a way..."

"Master of the Sage Merchant?" Li Fan's attention was drawn back.

" this mortal indeed has some skills. He can track the subtle connection between True Immortals and the Mountains and Seas, precisely locating hidden True Immortals within the vast, desolate, and annihilated star sea. Though I can also do this, it would take more time. Having someone else do it is naturally better."

"I was fortunate to encounter the first Nameless expert, [Grind], who was relatively reasonable and willing to leave behind a projection to embody the Dao according to Master Gong's will."

"But as I mentioned earlier, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation came faster than expected. There was simply not enough time," Cheng Dao said with some regret.

"By the time [Grind] comprehended the profound techniques passed down by Master and differentiated a projection, this star sea would have likely been swallowed by Dao Annihilation. How could my first battle after emerging from seclusion end so hastily? In a moment of urgency, I had no choice but to embody the Dao myself." When Cheng Dao gradually became familiar with Li Fan, his words differed slightly from before.

However, overall, it still aligned with Li Fan's judgment of Cheng Dao's character. Cheng Dao was originally a spirit stone by the side of the Mountains and Seas. Being an entity from beyond the mortal world, he was naturally indifferent. However, he was enlightened by Duke Shouqiu and bound by rules. Thus, his actions still remained within the bounds of propriety.

"The effect was still quite good, managing to barely resist the approaching Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. Though Grind inevitably had some complaints. But seeing that I myself entered the prison, he could not say much. As compensation, I even specially crafted the City of Ultimate Bliss for him. With a clone enjoying himself and venting outside, he is unique among the Immortals in the Dao Net," Cheng Dao said dismissively.

In his view, being able to embody Dao Annihilation to resist Dao Annihilation and fulfill Duke Shouqiu's ideals was an immense honor.

"But not every True Immortal in the world is as reasonable as [Grind]. The vast majority are uncooperative. Out of consideration for our fellow disciple's feelings, I cannot directly attack them. Therefore, I had to rely on the strength of these mortals in the Star Sea."

"I saved them from the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation back then. Therefore, they are grateful to me and follow my every word. The Administrative Council and the Immortal Hunt also came into being as a result. It seems there are even some survivors from within the high wall..." Cheng Dao's tone was dismissive.

Li Fan could somewhat understand Cheng Dao's perspective. To him, these mortals were indeed not within his scope of consideration. Even though Li Fan had almost torn apart the Dao Net and killed countless Immortal Hunters, as long as he called Cheng Dao "Senior Brother" a few more times, Cheng Dao could dismiss the matter.

In short, the status of fellow disciples who received Duke Shouqiu's inheritance was vastly different from that of mortal ants in Cheng Dao's heart.

"Even if mortals were wielding the weapons, with Senior Brother overseeing, capturing True Immortals of the Star Sea should be effortless. Why did I hear that the Immortal Hunt suffered repeated setbacks? They were even forced into a disadvantageous position at one point?"

Cheng Dao narrowed his eyes upon hearing this. Li Fan sensed a chilling killing intent emanating from him, along with a subtle, almost imperceptible greed. After a long pause, Cheng Dao finally admitted, "If they were all like Chaos and Harmonious Prosperity, there would be no trouble. The most crucial one is [Reverse]..."

"[Reverse]?" Li Fan immediately thought of the Nameless True Immortal from the True Immortal faction, rumored to have crafted the treasure, the Reverse Boat. He asked in surprise, "Does such a method of reversing time truly exist in the world?"

Cheng Dao's tone became somber, "Although there is no definitive proof, it is highly likely. Hmph, every time they can turn decay into magic and reverse the tide of battle. How can there be such a coincidence?"

"Though I tried everything, I could do nothing about this matter. Later, [Reverse]'s whereabouts became unknown. Only then did the True Immortals gradually become somewhat more compliant."

...

Li Fan fell into deep thought.

"Reverse Boat, the second of the Three Avoidance Methods."

"If time could be reversed, what would happen when it encountered [True]?"

Thinking this in his heart, Li Fan said aloud, "[Reverse] disappeared. Perhaps he returned to the past by riding the Reverse Boat?"

"Perhaps. It's a pity I couldn't capture him. Otherwise, if I could return to the time when I was still a spirit stone by Master's side, Master would surely be greatly surprised." Such a statement coming from a gaunt old man was truly strange.

However, it was enough to show how deeply Duke Shouqiu influenced Cheng Dao.

Li Fan was speechless, and both fell silent for a moment. Finally confirming the existence of a method to reverse time, Li Fan became fixated on it, hoping to gather more information from Cheng Dao. "I don't think such a heaven-defying divine ability exists in the world. How could Master, who is who he is, be unable to reverse time? It's hard to imagine that [Reverse] would be more powerful than Master."

After a period of silence, Li Fan shook his head and said.

"Regarding this point, I was also confused and sought advice from Master," Cheng Dao suddenly said.

"Oh? What did Master say?" Li Fan's heart skipped a beat. Not only because it concerned the reversal of time, but also because he discovered that Cheng Dao could communicate with Duke Shouqiu at any time.

"It is irrelevant to the final outcome."

"These four words, however, are something I still cannot comprehend." Cheng Dao sighed with regret.

"Irrelevant to the final outcome." Li Fan slowly repeated the words in his heart. It was clear that Duke Shouqiu's "final outcome" referred to the end of the mortal world, ultimately destined to be submerged by the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation in a million years.

"Does this mean that the power to reverse time cannot solve such a catastrophe?" Li Fan found it hard to believe and was completely baffled. However, Duke Shouqiu's thoughts were beyond the current comprehension of Li Fan. From the perspective outside the mortal world, within the Mountains and Seas, the perspective was likely completely different from within the mortal world. Since Duke Shouqiu said so, there must be his reasoning. Li Fan could only comfort himself this way.

"Master's divine words are truly hard to fathom. Senior Brother, do not worry. I do not understand either." Hearing Li Fan say this, Cheng Dao's mood instantly improved.

Li Fan continued to inquire, "Hearing Senior Brother's words, it seems you can often receive teachings from Master? If you have such an opportunity next time, please don't forget to bring me along!"

"Although I obtained the [Shouqiu's Jottings] from Master, I have never had the chance to hear his words or see his person..." Li Fan's face was filled with envy.

Cheng Dao appeared somewhat pleased, yet also regretful, "It's not as easy as you imagine. Master has transcended and his movements are unpredictable. Moreover, the imprint exists within the Mountains and Seas. It is very normal that even after sending a message, there may be no reply for several hundred years."

"That is truly a pity!" Li Fan sighed, but secretly felt relieved.

"However, Junior Brother, rest assured, if I receive any news from Master next time, I will definitely bring you along!" Cheng Dao promised earnestly.

"Then thank you, Senior Brother!" Li Fan showed a happy expression.

...

The interaction between the two fellow disciples was indeed very pleasant. Although Cheng Dao's strength was unfathomable, after being enlightened by Duke Shouqiu, he was bound by rules. Li Fan catered to his preferences, and naturally, he could easily manipulate him. Gradually, Cheng Dao began to regard Li Fan as the most trustworthy person besides Duke Shouqiu.

Li Fan also benefited greatly from Cheng Dao. The most crucial of these were the complete Great Dao projections in Cheng Dao's memory. Although they were not the Great Daos themselves, they did not have a substantial impact on the advancement of Li Fan's Myriad Manifestations Dao Net. However, they directly unlocked the entire Great Dao bestiary that was previously shrouded in mist, allowing Li Fan to precisely hunt his targets in the future. Benefiting from their harmonious relationship, Cheng Dao was not stingy with these complete Great Dao memories. He often shared them with Li Fan. However, the complete Great Dao projections of the [Primordial] possibility were dozens of times more complex than the Great Daos Li Fan had previously glimpsed. It was not something that could be completely comprehended in a short time. Therefore, Li Fan almost always stayed by Cheng Dao's side.

As for his clone Li Biren, he was outside helping to repair the Dao Net. With the assistance of True Immortals like Chaos and Harmonious Prosperity, as well as the countless beings in the Primordial Immortal Realm, the Star Sea Dao Net was repaired quickly. In the Star Sea region, the actual controllers of the two largest forces were often engaged in profound discussions and pleasant conversations, bringing a rare period of peace and tranquility to the starry sky. Until thirty-three years later.

Harmonious Prosperity suddenly requested an audience with Li Fan. "A message from the Guangwu Star Sea?" Li Fan was somewhat surprised. He hadn't expected that after witnessing his divine ability to seize the Dao Saber Dao Sword with his bare hands, the Guangwu Star Sea would dare to come knocking again.

"What did they say?" Li Fan asked with great interest.

Harmonious Prosperity's expression was subtle. He glanced at Cheng Dao, who was still sitting silently beside Li Fan. "My brother and I are not blood brothers, but we are closer than brothers. We have no secrets between us. Say whatever you wish!" Li Fan waved his hand. Harmonious Prosperity then recounted the events truthfully. "That [Star Peeker] first inquired about my recent situation. I did not reveal anything, merely pretending to have fled in panic and barely survived."

"Then [Star Peeker] actually proposed to continue cooperating."

"I resolutely refused. However, [Star Peeker] was relentless, seemingly..." Harmonious Prosperity glanced at Li Fan's expression and whispered, "It seems determined to capture Senior."

Before Li Fan could respond, Cheng Dao sneered. "You can agree to it for now and lure him here."

"I want to see what capability this [Star Peeker] truly possesses." Li Fan pondered, finding the situation peculiar. The Star Sea's Dao Net was a collaborative effort. Now, a similar creation appeared in the Primordial Immortal Realm, so how could they not be astonished and uncertain? Li Fan's displayed strength, capable of easily neutralizing the attack of the Dao Saber Dao Sword and even subduing this treasure with his bare hands, undoubtedly surpassed the realm of ordinary Nameless True Immortals. Yet, even so, the Star Sea faction represented by [Star Peeker] was determined to capture Li Fan.

Li Fan and the Guangwu Star Sea had no irreconcilable conflicts. "So, did they deduce the method of me collecting the Dao Saber Dao Sword?"

Regarding [True Revelation], Li Fan had to become serious. Judging by the ability to casually produce treasures like the Dao Saber Dao Sword, the Guangwu Star Sea faction was likely not weak. There might even be Transcendent experts capable of traveling to other possibilities. After all, the Dao Saber Dao Sword originated from another possibility.

"Interesting."

Although Li Fan could simply ignore [Star Peeker], the saying "One cannot sleep with a rival nearby" held true. Being constantly coveted by others felt unpleasant. Most importantly, Li Fan now had a powerful senior brother standing guard before him.

"Let Cheng Dao, first test the strength of the Guangwu Star Sea," Li Fan's eyes flashed with a cold light.

"Do as my Senior Brother says!" Li Fan commanded sternly.

Cheng Dao was very pleased with Li Fan's response. In his view, Li Fan's prompt agreement was much better than his previous hesitant responses.

"Junior Brother, rest assured. As your elder brother always says."

"As long as I, your Senior Brother, am here, no one will be able to harm you," Cheng Dao solemnly promised.

Li Fan showed a grateful expression.

At the same time, he instructed his clone, Li Biren, to prepare.

In the Primordial Immortal Realm.

The influx of power from the Infinite Sea had already reached a balance.

The continent within the high wall now differed little from the Immortal Realm in Li Fan's memory.

Chapter 1505: Sea of Stars Mountain Sea

Among the Immortals of the Azure Star Sea, Divine Thoughts was known for his good temperament and popularity. His voice and appearance were still vivid in their minds, yet at this moment, Chaos and Shan Hua sensed the Dao aura belonging to Divine Thoughts from the blood-red circle in Li Fan's hand. The implication was self-evident. Their former companion had been transformed into food for an artifact.

These two Nameless realm powerhouses could not help but feel grief and fear. But seeing Li Fan's cold and emotionless gaze, they quickly sobered up from their sorrow. The deceased were gone; survival was the most important thing now!

Shan Hua naturally continued, "Divine Thoughts is gone, so for the time being, contact with the Guangwu Star Sea can only rely on me. In the past, when I returned to the Azure Star Sea, I did not go deep into the Dao Net, but contacted Chaos from afar to plan."

"Therefore, 'The Great Net' is currently unaware of the complete annihilation of our expeditionary True Immortals."

"Although a considerable time has passed without any reply, it will surely arouse his suspicion. However, he will at most assume that we are locked in a fierce battle or a stalemate. He will never believe that we have been so easily and comprehensively defeated. Otherwise, why would he have agreed to the expedition in the first place…"

Shan Hua analyzed methodically: "Under such circumstances, Chaos and I can send a signal for support to 'The Great Net.' Considering it from the overall strategic situation and the initial investment cost, 'The Great Net' is highly likely to come to our aid. And once he arrives, with Senior's methods, he can surely capture him with ease…"

Chaos added, "Although the strategy sounds exceedingly simple, the key lies in how to gain the trust of 'The Great Net.' Over the past period, Shan Hua and I have made ample preparations, constantly transmitting false battle reports to 'The Great Net.' 'The Great Net' seems to have detected nothing unusual and even proactively inquired if we needed support."

"Although 'The Great Net' is powerful, nearly half of its strength is embodied in the Dao Net. If we can lure him out of the Dao Net, capturing him will be twice as effective with half the effort," Shan Hua also chimed in.

...

After the two Nameless True Immortals briefly explained their plan, Li Fan looked at Chaos and smiled, praising, "It seems you have long harbored intentions of submission. Very good, very good."

Li Fan's fingers caressed the blood-red circle as he paced and approached one of the Heavenly Pillars standing in this space. "Your plan might barely work. Unfortunately, in my opinion, there is a fatal flaw."

His eyes shifted to the Heavenly Pillar, and his voice was ethereal. Chaos and Shan Hua's expressions became solemn. "We hope Great Venerable will enlighten us."

"Just as you are full of confidence in capturing me, your plan seems to assume that as long as 'The Great Net' is lured out, you can definitely defeat and suppress him."

"You overestimate your own strength while underestimating the opponent."

"Since his origins, background, and Dao path are unknown, how can you be so sure that as long as I act, I can definitely subdue him?"

"What if I inadvertently bring a wolf into the house and, through carelessness and underestimation, fall victim to defeat?"

"Or is this what you truly hope for? To feign surrender, but actually to enact a plan within a plan, just to turn the tables in a desperate situation?" Li Fan's voice grew colder.

Chaos and Shan Hua's expressions and bodies trembled violently. "Great Venerable, please do not misunderstand! How could we dare harbor such disloyal intentions?" Shan Hua quickly clarified. "Junior wholeheartedly considers your concerns, and the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth can bear witness to my sincerity." Chaos reiterated his loyalty.

In their hearts, they both lamented inwardly. This legendary Great Venerable seemed to have undergone a drastic change in temperament after experiencing the destruction of the Immortal Realm. He was suspicious, capricious, and cruel. Compared to the cruel Immortal Emperors of the past, he was even more so.

"Whether you truly intend to deceive me or not, and what your true thoughts are, I have no interest in knowing. It is not important."

"After all, whoever wins, you will follow. Whoever loses, you will follow."

"Since that is the case, I also have my own plans." Li Fan reached out his hand, seemingly touching the Wuji Heavenly Pillar, but in reality, the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net had already activated, engulfing the Heavenly Pillar and the stone statue of Grand Master contained within it. Although he had comprehended the Wuji Great Dao for a hundred years, he was certainly not as proficient as Grand Master Wuji himself.

"Since the enemy is there, let's just go and defeat them directly." Amidst a thunderous roar, the Wuji Heavenly Pillar was taken by Li Fan. It continuously shrank, finally transforming into a gray-white stone rod.

A figure flickered in the space ahead. It was Li Biren, summoned by Li Fan. "Take this!" Li Fan directly threw the Wuji Heavenly Rod towards his clone. Considering the possibility of the existence of the 'Sage Emperor Li Fan' from other possibilities, this time, the clone had to act on his behalf again.

Both cultivating the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net, Li Biren held the Wuji Heavenly Rod without any difficulty. Protected by the Wuji Great Dao, any Dao technique from the [Primordial] possibility could not approach Li Biren's body.

"Unless this 'Great Net' is also a visitor from another possibility, as long as this Wuji stone rod is in hand, the clone is in an invincible position."

"Protection is sufficient, but offense is still slightly lacking." Li Fan pondered, then spat out a pair of water-green saber and sword from his mouth. "Take this treasure as well."

"If you still cannot defeat him, then flee quickly. If you cannot even escape…"

"Then self-destruct immediately." These instructions were conveyed only telepathically. Shan Hua and Chaos, present at the scene, were unaware.

From their perspective, they only saw Li Fan generously distributing two supreme treasures without any reluctance. After a brief induction, their hearts were filled with both joy and shock. The joy stemmed from the fact that they had recognized the origins of these two supreme treasures. The pair of saber and sword originally belonged to Nameless [Star Peeker]. They had personally witnessed the power of this treasure before, otherwise, they would not have collaborated with him so easily and been persuaded by him. As for the gray stone rod, although its mysterious origins were unknown, its ability to ignore the senses of the two Immortals alone indicated that it was definitely an extraordinary treasure. With the assistance of these two treasures, 'The Great Net' was bound to become a prisoner.

The shock stemmed from how extraordinary the Dao Saber Dao Sword was, yet Li Fan, this Great Venerable, could subdue it in such a short time. More importantly, such a treasure was handed over so readily, as if it were nothing. If they were in Li Fan's position, they would definitely find a secluded and safe place to go into seclusion and comprehend it.

Chaos secretly mused, "That ancient scripture passed down by Sage Lord Tai Yi, he also regards it with indifference. Truly worthy of being someone who served Sage Lord for a long time; his vision is naturally far superior to us crude beings."

"You two can follow along. Whether you contribute or not is entirely up to yourselves," Li Fan instructed indifferently. Then, with a wave of his large sleeve, he sent Li Biren and the two Nameless beings out of the high wall.

"Although there is a ninety percent chance of success, we must also prepare for failure." Li Fan looked into the distance, thinking silently. The protection of 'Illusion is True' had already been bestowed upon him. As soon as there was any anomaly, he would immediately revert to 'True Revelation.' If 'The Great Net' could truly win against the combined might of the Wuji stone rod and the Dao Saber Dao Sword, then this person would be someone Li Fan, in his current state, could not contend with. Direct reversion would be the only correct choice.

...

In the dim starry sky, Li Biren placed the Wuji stone rod on his shoulder, just like his main body, swallowing the green saber and sword into his abdomen. Then, using his body as a path, he stirred up Shan Hua and Chaos and charged directly towards the Azure Star Sea's Dao Net.

As if they had rehearsed the attack route countless times, they were incredibly proficient, aiming directly for the core area of the Azure Star Sea's Administration Council. Using his body as a path, traversing the starry sky, covering millions of miles in an instant.

Before the two Nameless beings could react, Li Biren had already penetrated the Dao Net's coverage. Under normal circumstances, if there was any foreign object invading the Dao Net, it would instantly trigger a response from the entire Dao Net. Not only would they face the pressure of all the Daos within the Dao Net, but they would also be besieged by countless Immortal Hunters. Even for a Nameless True Immortal, being trapped so deeply within the net would result in either death or severe injury.

In their years of interaction with the Azure Star Sea, Shan Hua and Chaos had already recognized this as a fundamental truth. Therefore, in their previous battles with the Azure Star Sea, the True Immortal side had always used tactics such as attempting infiltration and ambushing the Dao Net's periphery. But now…

Li Biren's direct assault on the heart of the territory completely shattered their understanding. Wherever he passed, the Dao Net failed to react. The densely woven Dao strings seemed to crumble at the first blow, as if struck by a scorching flame, creating holes in the Dao Net! The Dao strings snapped one after another. The Dao Net was no longer a net!

This bizarre situation made Chaos and Shan Hua, the two Nameless beings, stare dumbfounded. Even in their wildest fantasies, they had never imagined such an easy dismantling of the Dao Net.

While they were still stunned, Li Biren had already reached the center of the Dao Net. The Immortal Hunter headquarters and the Azure Star Sea Administration Council were all located here. Looking at the Azure Star Sea personnel in utter chaos, as if waking from a dream, the two True Immortals looked at the gray stone rod in Li Biren's hand.

An unbelievable, yet the most fitting conclusion for the current situation, sprang into their minds. They had personally witnessed this stone rod transform from a Heavenly Pillar. They had been unable to ascertain the Dao path sealed within this Heavenly Pillar before, but now, as the stone rod displayed its might within the Dao Net, they could finally confirm it.

Thus, the two Nameless beings, who had lived for an unknown duration, trembled uncontrollably. "Wuji…"

"Great Venerable?" The reason they had mistaken Li Fan for the former Great Venerable Wuji, disciple of Sage Lord Tai Yi, was because Li Fan had previously displayed the Wuji power capable of nullifying all Daos. And now, as the gray stone rod displayed the same ability, they finally understood. The power of Wuji did not originate from the Hidden Emperor. Rather, it came from Wuji himself, who was sealed and suppressed by the Hidden Emperor!

"That is a disciple of a Sage Lord, an innate being, incredibly noble!"

"Even though the Immortal Realm is destroyed, the Sage Lord may not have perished. If they angered the Sage Lord…"

"Even Wuji Venerable ended up in such a state…"

In an instant, countless thoughts surged into the minds of the two Nameless beings. But ultimately, it transformed into a deep fear of Li Fan, the Hidden Emperor of unknown identity. And Chaos, in particular, became certain of his judgment.

"It seems he has truly embarked on the path of becoming a Sage."

"Only by being a Sage can one disregard the face of other Sage Lords."

The hearts of the two Immortals trembled violently. Meanwhile, Li Biren was already wreaking havoc in the depths of the Dao Net. After coldly stating, "Those who resist shall die," and the Azure Star Sea faction still continued to attack. Li Biren ruthlessly unleashed the Dao Saber Dao Sword. Billions of green lights fluttered like willow branches in the wind. Wherever they passed, no screams were heard. Beings vanished, leaving behind only emptiness. Only the flying green lights became slightly denser.

With the Wuji Heavenly Rod clearing the path and the Dao Saber Dao Sword eliminating the enemies, Li Biren plowed straight through, breaking open the densely packed Dao Net layer by layer. He did not search for the mysterious Nameless being 'The Great Net' within the Dao Net, but directly headed for the four pillars of the Dao Net. The cages that imprisoned the Nameless True Immortals.

As the most stable structures within the entire Dao Net, these solemn cages were like paper in the face of Wuji's power. They offered no defense whatsoever. Soon, Li Biren locked onto the location of one of the imprisoned Nameless True Immortals. The stone rod flickered, and with one blow, he shattered the cage. The imprisoned Nameless being had various colored Dao strings inserted into their body. They seemed to still be in a deep sleep. Li Biren waved his hand and removed all the Dao strings from their body. The imprisoned Nameless being then showed signs of slowly waking up.

"This one seems to be 'Lord of Wealth'?" Chaos, following behind Li Biren, seemed to recognize the Immortal's identity and exclaimed in surprise. Like Shouqiu Gong, they were both addressed as 'Gong.' But clearly, their strengths were incomparable. Perhaps it was merely because they were associated with the Dao of 'Wealth.'

Li Biren paid little attention and, before Lord of Wealth could fully awaken, the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net's power erupted, instantly enveloping him. Then, he was directly sent to the inside of the high wall, to the main body's location.

Seeing Li Biren's actions, Chaos seemed to want to speak but stopped short. However, Shan Hua shook his head slightly, causing him to suppress his words. With the loss of one of the Four Pillars, the already tattered Dao Net's suppression power was greatly reduced. Both Chaos and Shan Hua felt the pressure around them lessen significantly.

"Strange, even at this point, why hasn't 'The Great Net' appeared?"

"Be careful. 'The Great Net' is not someone who gives up easily. Based on my understanding of him, he must be gathering strength for a killing blow." Having completed the destruction of the Dao Net together with Li Biren, the two Nameless beings were now irrevocably tied to Li Fan, the Hidden Emperor. Their relationship with the Azure Star Sea had become one of mutual destruction, with no possibility of reconciliation. For the sake of their future, they had to remind him.

Li Biren seemed oblivious, continuing towards the next cage. This time, it was the Nameless True Immortal whose Dao was '[Rock Solid].' This Nameless being was in much better condition than Lord of Wealth. Despite being imprisoned for an unknown number of years, he appeared to be in high spirits. Seeing the sudden intruders, this '[Rock Solid]' Nameless being was somewhat taken aback. Just as he was about to say something, Li Biren's Myriad Manifestations Dao Net arrived.

Chapter 1506: Ink Kill's New Wonderful Use

"Life and death are as one; to merge with the Dao is to become true. Free and unfettered by the external world, my Dao Pill shall be formed."

Li Biren carefully mulled over the contents of the Dao Refining King’s Medicine Scripture, finally understanding the reason for his first failed attempt at alchemy.

"Too much of a specific objective. It doesn’t align with the essence of being unfettered..." Li Biren shook his head with a wry smile.

"Indeed, it was a bit too utilitarian."

"The so-called Dao Pills are merely embellishments. They are better to have, but if not, they have no practical impact."

For Li Fan, whether the Dao Pill could be successfully refined was not the main point. The crucial aspect was the entire process of refining the Dao Pill.

Having witnessed the grandeur of the true Great Dao at the Dao Observation Platform, Li Fan clearly realized that trying to comprehend the three thousand Great Daos of this world through his own efforts alone would be an exceedingly long and inefficient endeavor. He might not even fully comprehend them and weave a true Myriad Manifestations Dao Net by the time of the mortal world's end.

Therefore, he needed a shortcut. Besides directly absorbing the insights into the Great Dao from the Grand Master and those at the Dao Observation Platform, the Dao Refining King’s Medicine Scripture, passed down by Sun Piaomiao, was also an effective supreme method.

The Great Dao manifested in all things in the world, and through the process of 'Dao Refining,' all things could be slowly refined back into the state of 'Dao.' This was very similar to the function of the 'Primordial' technique. However, the Dao after tempering was not in the chaotic state of先天 (Xiantian) after the Primordial technique was applied. Instead, it was as if it had been filtered and organized, clear and distinct.

In simple terms, it was the difference between being able to 'see and understand.' Even if the Dao Pill failed to form, the process of condensing the Great Dao was sufficient for Li Biren to scrutinize these Dao principles in detail.

Seven days later, Li Biren began refining pills again. Although auspicious phenomena still occurred frequently, the beings of the Primordial Immortal Realm, having experienced the prior ordeal, were mostly no longer fearful. As for the five Heavenly Emperors and thirteen Heavenly Scars who benefited, they worked even harder.

Li Biren directed from afar. Amidst the leaping flames, the Dao Pill was initially formed.
