Compared to the previous defective product, this true Dao Pill, besides being enveloped in swirling purple qi, possessed a more peculiar trait: it seemed to have developed a nascent sentience. Facing Li Biren, who was about to consume it, the Dao Pill not only felt no fear but even exhibited a flicker of eagerness.

"A Dao Pill is, in essence, a condensation of countless Dao principles. It will not vanish simply because I consume it."

"Rather, it will henceforth integrate with my comprehension of the Great Dao..." Enlightenment surged within Li Biren's heart, but he paused the Dao Pill, which was already at his lips. His long-cultivated caution ultimately led him to abandon the plan of consuming the Dao Pill, even though it was merely a clone.

"I shall reward you with this." He casually tossed it out again. This immediately triggered a mad scramble among the Heavenly Emperors and Heavenly Scars. For these creations, a single Dao Pill was equivalent to tens of thousands of years of arduous cultivation, perhaps even more. This was because, within this Primordial Continent, Li Fan had rigidly defined the responsibilities and permissions of each being. Even a Heavenly Emperor could only observe Dao principles within a limited area. However, the Dao Pill bestowed by Li Fan could override these rule-based divisions.

"True power is like this."

"Breaking rules, ignoring rules, or even..."

"Creating rules." As more and more Dao Pills were refined, numerous insights accumulated in Li Fan's heart. Combined with what he had learned at the Dao Observation Platform, his progress could be described as a thousand miles in a day.

After the nineteenth Dao Pill, Li Biren stopped bestowing them upon the beings of the Primordial Immortal Realm. Instead, he began to collect and accumulate them. The convergence of Dao Pills was an incredibly potent temptation for any being, a thousand or ten thousand times more alluring than the 'Essence of the Heavens and Earth' that cultivators once encountered in the Xuanhuang Realm. Yet, Li Biren remained as calm as still water.

Familiarity breeds desire. Besides refining Dao Pills with ease, Li Biren also developed his own unique ideas. "Ink Slaughter, since it can appear in the form of the 'Essence of the Heavens and Earth,' it should logically be able to integrate into the Dao Pill." A thought arose in his mind. During the next refining process, Li Biren began to draw upon the power of the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul. However, Ink Slaughter itself possessed the ability to erode Dao principles to a certain extent, akin to Dao Annihilation. The integration of the Ink Slaughter's power actually caused this refining attempt to fail.

However, Li Biren saw hope for success. This was because the Dao Pill did not dissipate the moment the Ink Slaughter's power was integrated; it only disintegrated after a period. "This indicates that the ratio was incorrect. It needs to be adjusted."

After a full half-year of trials, Li Biren finally succeeded in refining the first 'Ink Slaughter Dao Pill.' Its exterior was still enveloped in sacred purple qi. In fact, the density of the purple qi was more than double that of a normal Dao Pill. Astonishingly, this Ink Slaughter Dao Pill surface naturally showed patterns resembling mountains and seas, lending it a divine aura. Li Biren stared at it for a long time, still unable to determine if this mountain and sea phenomenon was purely accidental.

Therefore, he refined another one. The result was the same. "This is somewhat interesting." Li Fan tossed this 'poisonous pill' out of the Dao Palace. After a long absence of Dao Pills, this exceptionally fine-looking one sparked a fierce competition among the beings of the Primordial Immortal Realm. The intensity of the struggle was even greater than all the previous occasions combined.

The last survivor, an Earth Spirit born since the initial creation of the Primordial Immortal Realm, fortunately obtained this Dao Pill. Filled with excitement, it consumed the Dao Pill. Amidst countless swirling purple qi, this Earth Spirit uncontrollably ascended, soaring towards Li Fan's Dao Palace, completely disappearing from the sight of all beings, eliciting countless gasps and envious murmurs.

Li Fan, observing the Earth Spirit before him, now completely transformed into 'purple qi' and seemingly devoid of its own consciousness, stroked his chin. "This is..."

"Dao transformation?" The Earth Spirit's life form had vanished, leaving only its form. However, there was no 'Dao of Earth Spirits' in the world. Thus, the scene before Li Fan was extremely peculiar. The Earth Spirit should have consumed and digested the Dao Pill; now, it was the reverse, with the Dao Pill consuming the Earth Spirit. Furthermore, Li Fan discovered that there was no Ink Slaughter power within this Dao-transformed Earth Spirit. During the process of Dao transformation, the already scarce Ink Slaughter power had been expended.

"So, this is another application of the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul's power?" A single experiment could not fully explain how this miraculous transformation occurred. Li Fan continued to refine fifteen more 'Ink Slaughter Dao Pills.' As more and more peculiar purple 'statues' appeared beside him, Li Fan gradually understood the reason. This time, the refining process was simplified. With a mere thought, the Ink Slaughter's power surged out, descending to capture the target. What was supposed to be near 'annihilation' for beings affected by Ink Slaughter, causing them to vanish without a trace, was now 'Dao transformation.' It presented the original form of the beings at the moment of their creation.

Chapter 1507: The Immortal from the Other Shore in the Coffin

"Ink Slaughter's near-Dao Annihilation ability, as it imitates the power of fusion between Mountains and Seas."

"And this current Dao transformation..."

Li Biren picked up one of the purple Dao-transformed statues before him and examined it carefully.

"Is merely the collision of Mountains and Seas. The process of fusion was prematurely halted."

"Mountains and Seas playing together..." Li Biren suddenly recalled a description from the legends of Mountains and Seas.

"And thus Dao is born. So that's how it is?"

Li Biren slowly swallowed all the purple light statues and experienced the Dao principles contained within these beings. After feeding the poisonous elixir to powerful beings and completing a transformation using their lives and intellect, Li Biren was convinced that these Dao-transformed statues no longer belonged to the category of [Dao Elixirs], and could therefore be consumed directly.

Although something extremely important seemed to have been lost during the Dao transformation process, the ability to greatly increase the efficiency of comprehending the Dao without risk was definitely worth it.

"Besides assisting in Dao comprehension, this poisonous elixir is inherently a formidable killing divine ability."

"Its essence is to use the methods of the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao to directly integrate the power represented by the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul with the enemy, striking a fatal blow at the foundational level of the Great Dao..."

"It's truly impossible to guard against!"

Besides being able to kill people invisibly like poison, the most important thing was that it could ignore the strength gap. As long as the opponent could not escape Dao Annihilation, or completely avoid the power of the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul, they would be affected by this poisonous elixir's methods.

It was merely a matter of the degree of "poisoning."

Li Biren began experimenting with the Nameless True Immortals sealed in the Great Desolate Immortal Realm.

Although he had promised to let them go, it did not prevent him from making use of them beforehand.

The formless Dao Elixir Fire surrounded the Heavenly Pillars.

The power of the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul infiltrated them silently.

The changes produced were different depending on the level of strength.

The most tragic was Situ Xing.

He was not the true body of a Nameless True Immortal to begin with, and under the Ink Slaughter's assault, he had almost no power to resist. The gray Heavenly Pillar slowly turned purple from top to bottom, revealing a strange blackness within.

Before this purple-black color could completely engulf the Heavenly Pillar, Li Fan promptly withdrew his divine ability, thus saving Situ Xing's life. However, only a wisp of consciousness remained, barely clinging to existence.

Li Fan held the Dao-transformed Heavenly Pillar and, with little effort, separated it from the normal part of the Heavenly Pillar, directly swallowing it into his abdomen.

Compared to his own slow comprehension, this direct devouring was indeed extremely efficient.

"This is truly a supreme wonder!" Li Biren praised inwardly.

However, not all Nameless True Immortals were as helpless as Situ Xing.

Especially Hungry Immortal.

Even in his sealed state, he could contend with the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul. Although destined to fail in the long run, being able to hold his own for a while already demonstrated his extraordinary nature.

Li Fan broke off a small purple Dao-transformed portion from Hungry Immortal's Heavenly Pillar and consumed it.

A moment later, he narrowed his eyes slightly: "As expected. Hungry Immortal's Dao originates from outside the [Primordial] possibility."

"Or rather, it is not entirely the Dao of [Primordial], but a fusion of a certain Great Dao with an external Dao."

In the complete Dao compendium Li Fan glimpsed in the Inheritor's Hall, he did not see the projection of Hungry Immortal's Dao. However, he saw something similar. It was likely one of the prototypes of the [Hungry] Dao.

Like the Dao Saber Dao Sword, Daos from outside the possibility greatly enhanced the filling of the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net, perhaps even opening up entirely new branches of Dao. The Myriad Manifestations Dao Net grew a blank area that was almost visible to the naked eye. Even though it was not fully filled yet, its complete scale could be estimated.

Facing this great tonic, Li Fan couldn't help but resist the urge to ignore the Inheritor's instructions and continue refining Hungry Immortal.

But thinking about it, he still held back.

"Refining Hungry Immortal can wait for the next life. She's always within the Immortal Ruins anyway."

"I still need to rely on the Inheritor in this life."

"No hurry."

However, the most surprising of the sealed Heavenly Pillars was the performance of the bone of [Primordial]. Under the assault of Ink Slaughter's purple-black power, it retreated step by step, not even as good as Situ Xing, whose main body had perished and only his clone survived.

It did not live up to the name of [Primordial] at all.

After some research, Li Fan understood the reason for this bizarre phenomenon.

"Therefore, what is here is not the complete bone of Primordial. It can even be said to be a very small part of [Primordial]."

"The vast majority of the rest is elsewhere."

Li Fan could even sense that some traces of Ink Slaughter power had followed the connection between [Primordial] entities and tracked it.

"Southern Immortal Heavenly Pillar." Li Fan thought of the true name of the bone of Primordial and shook his head slightly.

"I can only wish good luck to the beings under the protection of the Heavenly Pillar over there."

...

Li Fan did not go to extremes. Although the Heavenly Pillars were largely transformed by Dao, they still retained their shape. The Nameless True Immortals sealed within were also still alive. They had merely suffered severe damage and would need millions of years of nourishment to recover.

All the insights Li Fan gained were fed back to his main body, Li Fan.

However, he did not reveal them to the Inheritor, maintaining his guise as a diligent and inquisitive junior disciple.

...

After a full three years, Shan Hua brought news again.

"That Star Peeker is extremely cautious. It was only when I showed him the restored Dao Net and confirmed that Senior had not attacked them that he finally agreed to cooperate."

"We also noticed that recently, there have been attempts to approach and probe the periphery of the Star Sea near the border. Fortunately, our Dao Net was repaired quickly, otherwise, we might have revealed a flaw." Chaos stood by, exclaiming his luck.

"Even so, Star Peeker refused to reveal his entire plan, only telling us to 'follow orders and adapt to circumstances.' Hmph..." A fierce light flashed in Shan Hua's eyes.

"Be patient. Don't reveal any flaws," Li Fan said calmly, and Shan Hua immediately restrained himself.

"Just do as they instruct. My Senior Brother and I will wait in the Great Desolate Immortal Realm for your arrival." Li Fan looked at the Inheritor and smiled.

"Senior Brother, would you mind moving?"

The gaunt old man stretched his seemingly stiff body. "It's been a while since I've been outside, and I'm feeling restless. It wouldn't hurt to stay elsewhere for a while."

As he spoke, blue light surged around the Inheritor's body. The Inheritor's phantom clone replaced the main body, sitting at the deepest part of the Dao Net.

Li Fan carefully examined his surroundings and noticed that the Dao strings of the entire Dao Net had not shown any deviation despite the change of the main body and clone.

He couldn't help but marvel, "Senior Brother, your method of creating a phantom clone is almost indistinguishable from Master himself! I imagine transcendence is also within reach!"

The Inheritor, rising, stroked his beard and laughed, unable to conceal his pride. However, he remained humble, "You flatter me. I am still far from Master's level. This phantom clone can only substitute for the Inheritor for a hundred years at most. Any longer, and it won't suffice."

"With Senior Brother's talent, eternal inheritance would not take too long," Li Fan said with a smile.

Chaos and Shan Hua, accustomed to Li Fan's almost blind flattery, remained silent, their eyes focused on their noses and their hearts on their minds.

"Senior Brother, please." Li Fan led the Inheritor to stay in the Great Desolate Immortal Realm.

They would just wait for the Guangwu Star Sea's occupants to take the bait.

After another ten-plus days of progress, Shan Hua finally met with [Star Peeker] again.

It was still attached to the black cat.

"Fellow Daoist, aren't you being a bit too cautious? We lost so many companions, yet you're not like this," Shan Hua said with displeasure.

Star Peeker also complained, "Daoist Shan Hua, please don't mention it. I didn't want to. Last time, after losing my supreme treasure, I was almost flayed alive and sealed into a Heavenly Pillar. Fortunately, at the last moment, I recalled details of how that thief subdued the supreme treasure, which gave me a chance to atone for my mistakes."

"But this is also the last chance. If this matter still fails, you might never see me again."

Shan Hua seemed extremely sympathetic, stroking the cat's head. "You've really suffered, Daoist. If it's unbearable, just flee to our Star Sea. At least..."

"Heh heh." Star Peeker interrupted Shan Hua's words with a hint of embarrassment.

"Alright, let's get down to business. This operation wasn't entirely my idea. I'm just responsible for relaying messages and coordinating."

"Oh?" Shan Hua's hand, stroking the black cat, paused. "How should we cooperate?"

Star Peeker remained silent for a moment, seemingly listening to orders from the other side.

After a while, a voice slowly came through: "There is a coffin. Inside, a sleeping Nameless True Immortal is sealed. You just need to guide the coffin here, and then, by any means necessary, place it within the Great Desolate Immortal Realm."

Shan Hua wanted to ask for further details, but Star Peeker had already finished speaking and fallen silent.

"Just this?" Shan Hua sounded displeased.

"After going through so much trouble, you've only prepared this? What can this sleeping Nameless do? You know the strength of that Hidden Emperor. How can he be dealt with with just this?"

Star Peeker appeased him, "Daoist Shan Hua, please don't worry. I've risked my life, how could I be negligent? With this sleeping Nameless assisting, even if that Hidden Emperor has immense divine abilities, he won't be able to overturn the heavens!"

"This time, he will pay back everything, with interest."

Shan Hua pondered for a moment, then finally agreed.

He severed the connection with Star Peeker and, before heading to the agreed-upon location to find the sleeping Nameless in the coffin, relayed the detailed situation to Li Fan.

"It's fine. Just as he said, bring the coffin."

After hearing Li Fan's reply, Shan Hua breathed a sigh of relief.

He then went to the border of the Star Sea to search for the target.

Within the Great Desolate Immortal Realm.

Li Fan and the Inheritor sat facing each other, a wisp of green smoke burning in the center. The smoke spiraled upwards, formless and intangible.

"Senior Brother, do you have any clues about this sleeping Nameless in the coffin?"

"Perhaps, he is an Immortal from the Other Shore."

After a period of silence, the Inheritor spoke slowly, his tone somewhat grave.

Chapter 1508: I Am One With All Realms

"An Immortal from the Other Shore?" Li Fan's pupils contracted, and he couldn't help but lean closer.

"Is it that Other Shore?" he asked softly.

"Yes and no," the Inheritor seemed lost in memory, his expression somewhat dazed.

After a long while, he finally regained his senses and gently pointed to the wisp of green smoke before Li Fan.

As the green smoke swirled, various images appeared.

These were the Inheritor's memories from when he was a spirit stone by the side of Mountains and Seas.

"The legendary Other Shore is indeed a place longed for by all beings in the Immortal Realm. Even Master, after transcending, went to that place. However, the term 'Other Shore' does not solely refer to that sacred realm."

"Any possibility beyond the unknown can be called the Other Shore."

"In the ancient Immortal Realm, Immortal Coffins would occasionally appear during Dao Annihilation tribulations, crossing Mountains and Seas, floating freely. The Nameless within the coffins were mostly from their homelands that were destroyed by Dao Annihilation, and they themselves could not find a way to escape the possibility. To seek a sliver of hope for survival, they sealed themselves within coffins, drifting amid the Mountains and Seas, attempting to find another place to reside..."

Li Fan listened and couldn't help but think of the previous Hungry Immortal, whose Great Dao aura clearly came from outside the [Primordial] possibility.

"It seems she might be one of these Immortals from the coffins."

"They cannot traverse possibilities through their own strength, only drift with the Immortal Coffins. Their strength might not reach the level of transcendence, but the Immortal Coffins can withstand the great tide of Dao Annihilation, allowing them to survive long enough to reach another possibility. Such strength would be top-tier among the Nameless," Li Fan mused rapidly in his mind.

But a doubt arose again.

"What... what exactly are these Immortal Coffins? How can they protect those Nameless beings from Dao Annihilation? If one could collect enough Immortal Coffins, wouldn't they be able to build an unsinkable ship that perpetually floats on the great tide of Dao Annihilation?" Li Fan asked.

The Inheritor smiled wryly, "There is no 'forever.' It's merely delaying the inevitable. Those Immortal Coffins are, in reality, the final remaining condensations of Great Dao from a possibility."

"They still cannot prevent the erosion of Dao Annihilation, but due to a special method of compression and condensation, they can maximally slow down the speed of Dao Annihilation's erosion. The origin of this method is unknown, but it is universally used across all heavens. However, its effect is indeed remarkable, greatly increasing the drifting time for the Immortals within the coffins."

"I recall that Master once personally witnessed and salvaged an Immortal Coffin. It's a pity, however, that the Nameless within had long since decayed and perished. Master, pitying his fate, melted his remnants and the Immortal Coffin into a stubborn stone, similar to myself, and then cast it beyond the Mountains and Seas, hoping that one day it might regain its vitality..."

Li Fan stared at the stubborn stone manifested in the Inheritor's memory. For some reason, he felt a sense of familiarity.

But after searching his memories, he couldn't find the source of this familiarity.

It was only when the Inheritor waved his hand, interrupting the image, causing the stubborn stone to transform into countless points of light, that Li Fan suddenly awoke.

Each fragment evolved from this stubborn stone was like a pill!

"Medicine King Sect, Square Stone?"

The Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao was passed down by Sun Piaomiao. It originated from a giant square stone he meditated upon while refining elixirs.

Using any other method to identify it, this square stone was merely a pure, ordinary stone. Only when one inwardly determined it to be an elixir and consumed it would a faint voice of inheritance be heard.

This mode of discernment, where it was indistinguishable when combined but revealed its essence when separated, was something Li Fan had only encountered in Sun Piaomiao's inheritance. Now, he saw it again in the Inheritor's memory.

"Could it be that Sun Piaomiao was transformed from that stubborn stone?"

"Drifting through the Mountains and Seas for countless years, even his immortal body decayed. He certainly possessed the conditions to glimpse the secrets of Mountains and Seas."

"And..."

Li Fan recalled a statement made by Sun Piaomiao in Liu Ruchen's memory.

"Birth, aging, sickness, and death are eternal principles of the Great Dao, which even this starry sky cannot escape. How can you be an exception?"

Li Fan's thoughts solidified: "These words truly sound like they were spoken by someone who personally experienced the cycle of Dao's birth and death. Moreover, the method of condensing and folding true immortal inscriptions into pills to form immortal domains bears some similarity to the Immortal Coffins."

"If he were indeed a reincarnated Immortal from a coffin..."

The Inheritor seemed unaware of Li Fan's internal turmoil. After dispersing the image of the stubborn stone, he continued to speak about the Immortals from coffins.

"As you mentioned before, the Dao Saber Dao Sword treasure used by the Guangwu Star Sea came from another possibility. This indicates they possess the power to connect with other possibilities. Although they might not be able to complete the crossing, they should at least be capable of salvaging and capturing."

The Inheritor smiled, "Junior Brother, you've likely encountered a formidable enemy this time. Are you afraid?"

Li Fan also played along with a carefree smile, "With Senior Brother by my side, let alone a mere Immortal from a coffin, I'd dare to fight even a Transcendent expert!"

Highly satisfied with Li Fan's boldness, the Inheritor's smile faded, "Confidence is good. But Junior Brother, you must not be careless. After all, these Immortals from coffins survived the Dao Annihilation tribulation, so their strength must be considerable."

"Moreover, the Guangwu Star Sea released this Immortal Coffin specifically targeting your method of subduing the Dao Saber Dao Sword. It's likely not a randomly chosen Immortal Coffin..."

"Speaking of which, how did you manage to subdue that pair of saber and sword? Even I might have had difficulty." The Inheritor stared at Li Fan with a smile, suddenly asking.

Li Fan had long prepared an answer for this question.

Without any hesitation, he took out the Dao Saber Dao Sword and, in front of the Inheritor, activated his Myriad Manifestations Dao Net.

Li Fan had used this divine ability during his confrontation with the Inheritor, so the latter was not unfamiliar with it. But the next moment, the purple-black aura surging from the Dao Net caused the Inheritor's expression to change.

"This Dao Saber Dao Sword indeed originates from another possibility. Even the Supreme Dao cannot shake it in the slightest. However, it has always remained within the Mountains and Seas and has not transcended the mortal world. My Myriad Manifestations Dao Net's core, Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul, possesses power close to Dao Annihilation. Naturally, it can suppress it!" Li Fan said proudly.

As he spoke, the phantom of the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul, enveloped in purple-black energy, floated out of the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net, standing before the Inheritor.

The Inheritor, being a spirit stone nurtured by the side of Mountains and Seas, was naturally not unfamiliar with the aura of merging Mountains and Seas.

Upon seeing the phantom of the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul, he instinctively stood up, his expression showing nervousness.

"Senior Brother need not worry. This power is completely under my control," Li Fan retracted the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul and said indifferently.

"This... where did it come from?" The Inheritor's eyes flickered with confusion and uncertainty.

Li Fan saw this clearly and thus did not lie. "Senior Brother, we both hail from the [Broken Chessboard Dao Field]. Naturally, you should know the peculiarities of this experimental space."

Seeing the Inheritor nod slightly, Li Fan continued, "In my world, there exists a being called the Essence of Heaven and Earth. It is likely the embodiment of the laws of heaven and earth."

"Ink Slaughter is one of them. I stumbled upon Ink Slaughter's marvel and subsequently managed to tame it..."

Li Fan's tale was a mixture of truth and falsehood.

The Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul was perhaps one of Li Fan's most crucial secrets. Revealing it now, even the Inheritor couldn't help but be shaken.

The most brilliant aspect of this lie was that the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net's suppression strength for the Dao Saber Dao Sword, as witnessed by the Inheritor, was developed *after* subduing the saber and sword.

However, unless one was the owner of the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul, it would be impossible to know the truth. What the Inheritor saw now was the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net, empowered by the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul, easily suppressing the Dao Saber Dao Sword.

The Inheritor then marveled, "Junior Brother, you have excellent luck. If I'm not mistaken, this should be one of the targets the Immortal Realm was experimenting with."

"The power of merging Mountains and Seas."

"The starry sky where I gained sentience also had similar creations, specifically the spring that forms the rushing stream..."

"However, compared to your Ink Slaughter, Senior Brother, it is far inferior." Although envious, it was only envy. The Inheritor, having been enlightened by Shouqiu Gong, harbored no thoughts of seizing his junior brother's treasure.

"By the way, Senior Brother. Do you know why the Immortal Realm was suddenly abandoned? Even Master's inheritance was left behind? Based on my observations, perhaps finding a solution to Dao Annihilation was not far off." Li Fan appeared puzzled.

Li Fan's words did not reveal that he knew the original purpose of the experimental field was to capture the so-called "Treasure to Save the World."

He merely steered the conversation towards the topic of resisting the Dao Annihilation Tribulation.

The Inheritor remained silent for a moment.

Suddenly, he looked at Li Fan, his expression somewhat strange, "How do you know they didn't?"

"This Dao Field was built by the Immortal Realm with great effort and cost. It's impossible for it to be suddenly abandoned."

"It's empty now, perhaps because they achieved their goal."

"But the Immortal Realm was still destroyed, and the Dao Annihilation Tribulation still descended?" Li Fan was astonished.

The Inheritor sighed, "Junior Brother, you are too naive. Even Master, with his profound wisdom, did not cling to resisting Dao Annihilation and saving a realm. Otherwise, he wouldn't have left during the peak of the Dao Annihilation tribulation. Why should others?"

"From beginning to end, all the Immortals of the Immortal Realm, including the ruling Immortal Emperors, sought a way to ensure the survival of the majority of True Immortals."

"If the Immortal Realm is destroyed, a new one can be rebuilt on the Upper Mountain."

"Ultimately, the Other Shore is the place truly recognized by everyone as a solution to the calamity of merging Mountains and Seas."

"Everything else..."

"Is irrelevant to the grand scheme."

Li Fan was stunned by these words.

"Then the destruction of the Immortal Realm, and the True Immortals falling like ants..."

The Inheritor chuckled, "Those who died in the calamity of destruction were not within the scope of the 'majority.' Those who left are the true representatives of the 'Immortal Realm.'"

"The so-called three treasures of avoidance are merely the self-salvation of the abandoned and pitiful."

...

Li Fan vaguely felt that these words were incorrect.

"Then what about the Four Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm? Three of them perished, does that mean they are no longer considered part of the true Immortal Realm?"

The Inheritor sighed softly, "Lian Shan, Gui Hai, and Tai Yi, these three Sage Lords chose not to live. Look at Sage Jing Fen, he's still alive and well, isn't he? Does that mean Sage Jing Fen's strength surpasses the other three Sagely Lords?"

"Moreover, the 'demise' of these three Sage Lords might not be their actual demise."

"It's merely a matter of selective abandonment."

Perhaps it was because Li Fan had revealed the secret of his Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul earlier, gaining the other party's complete trust.

This time, the Inheritor explained exceptionally thoroughly.

Li Fan slowly calmed down from his shock and pondered the meaning behind the Inheritor's words.

"Senior Brother, do you mean that the three Sage Lords Lian Shan, Gui Hai, and Tai Yi are the only ones in all the worlds?"

"Perhaps not before. But since they established the Upper Mountain and opened the Infinite Spring, it has been so."

Chapter 1509: Dao Rong Shuo Shu Xian

"Are the Three Sage Lords now so powerful? The sole existence in all realms..." Li Fan was momentarily lost in thought.

"The Immortal Realm is boundless, and since ancient times, prodigies have emerged. However, only those four beings could be called 'Sages.' Even Master, with his extraordinary methods, was only respected as 'Duke' by the world, not as a 'Sage.' Junior Brother, how can you underestimate the Sages?" the Inheritor shook his head.

"It's not underestimation," Li Fan said with a wry smile. "It's just that my understanding of the Immortal Realm is based on vague records, and I cannot form a correct perception. If not for Senior Brother's guidance..."

"Being the sole existence in all realms, or the sole existence in Mountains and Seas, that must be the legendary realm of true transcendence, right? Sage Lord Lian Shan achieved his Dao by establishing the Upper Mountain, and Sage Lord Gui Hai achieved his Dao by opening the Infinite Spring. Then how did Sage Lord Tai Yi reach that level? Is there something in this world comparable to Mountains and Seas?" Li Fan directly changed the subject.

The Inheritor smiled, "Although my knowledge is vast, the secrets of the Sage Lords' path to enlightenment are beyond my understanding. If the Sage Lords themselves do not reveal such matters, who can know? However, speaking of which, Sage Lord Tai Yi's strength is indeed comparable to Sage Lords Lian Shan and Gui Hai. This is true because Sage Lord Lian Shan once admitted this in front of Immortal Emperor Lou Huang and a group of Nameless True Immortals. As for the last one to achieve enlightenment, Sage Jing Fen..."

"To put it disrespectfully, perhaps in the eyes of the three Sage Lords, Jing Fen is merely a powerful junior."

"The three Sage Lords are the Sage Lords of Mountains and Seas, while Jing Fen is merely the Sage Lord of our world."

"However, this is just a judgment based on the time when the Immortal Realm was destroyed. After so many years, no one can presume to know Sage Jing Fen's current strength. Perhaps he has already taken the final step towards transcendence, just like the other three Sage Lords?"

...

Afterward, Li Fan further inquired about some hidden secrets of the Immortal Realm from the Inheritor, and then skillfully guided the conversation back to the approaching enemies from the Guangwu Star Sea and the Immortal from the Other Shore in the coffin.

"Shan Hua has already found the Immortal Coffin according to Star Peeker's instructions."

"As Senior Brother predicted, the Immortal Coffin is indeed a condensation of Great Dao. Based on their current speed, it will take about five hours for the Immortal within the coffin to arrive in our Great Desolate Immortal Realm," Li Fan showed the image transmitted by Shan Hua to the Inheritor.

"Shall we move the battle to another location? If you and I engage in combat with that Immortal from the Other Shore, this continent might be affected," the Inheritor asked, glancing below.

"We can rebuild it after it's destroyed. If it can't even withstand this minor tribulation, then even if it's destroyed, it's not worth regretting. Moreover, although the beings in this realm are somewhat lacking in strength, they can still serve as temporary helpers," Li Fan politely declined.

The Inheritor praised sincerely, "Junior Brother's mindset truly has the air of an Immortal Realm Sage."

Li Fan chuckled and did not respond.

"However, with a formidable enemy approaching, we still need to make some preparations..."

The Inheritor pondered for a moment and then said, "If Junior Brother doesn't mind, I have a divine ability that I can pass on to you. Although I don't know which Dao the Nameless within the coffin has merged with, this divine ability should be sufficient for self-preservation, even if it can't defeat the enemy."

Li Fan was overjoyed: "Senior Brother, how can you say that? I could not ask for anything more!"

The Inheritor was not pretentious. He tapped Li Fan's forehead in mid-air.

Instantly, his body and soul felt as if they were back in the Infinite Sea, being cleansed by countless rapidly changing scenes.

Li Fan saw very clearly that the vast majority of these scenes depicted a solitary figure sitting on a mountain, gazing at the sea.

It was Shouqiu Gong!

Li Fan had encountered this scene countless times in [Shouqiu's Jottings].

However, the difference in the Inheritor's transmission was that this was an "overhead" view, looking up at Shouqiu Gong.

It was not Shouqiu Gong's own comprehension.

Shouqiu Gong not only sat on the mountain gazing at the sea but also protected a spirit stone beneath him, shielding it from the impacts of Mountains and Seas.

"[Mountain and Sea Unmoving Body]."

"When cultivating this divine ability, one can, like Shouqiu Gong, remain utterly still amidst the immense changes of Mountains and Seas. Besides defense, depending on one's comprehension of the phenomena of Mountains and Seas, one can also mimic the power of Mountains and Seas crashing and eroding. Of course, this does not mean one can truly imitate Mountains and Seas with this divine ability. Instead, it drags the opponent into the vast realm of Mountains and Seas perceived by oneself, making them feel as if they are facing Shouqiu gazing at the sea."

"If the opponent has the capability of Shouqiu Gong, or has obtained Shouqiu Gong's inheritance, they can naturally ignore this deterrent. But if it's an ordinary person..."

"Especially those who have truly experienced endless despair in Mountains and Seas, only to escape after countless years, only to face Mountains and Seas again. They would likely break down on the spot!"

Li Fan, while comprehending and learning the [Mountain and Sea Unmoving Body], elaborated on its profound mysteries.

He wasn't speaking to himself but to the Inheritor.

The Inheritor nodded repeatedly, very pleased with Li Fan's rapid comprehension.

"Senior Brother's technique is truly marvelous."

"It doesn't harm fellow disciples and is especially effective against True Immortals in the world. The more they fear the Dao Annihilation tribulation and shirk responsibility, the more they will be affected by this divine ability," Li Fan continued to praise.

At the same time, he demonstrated the [Mountain and Sea Unmoving Body].

Li Fan remained Li Fan.

But around him, it seemed as if Mountains and Seas were encircling him.

The Inheritor's eyes lit up, "Junior Brother, your comprehension of Mountains and Seas is quite profound!"

"It's all thanks to Master and Senior Brother's excellent teaching!"

...

In the following period, with the Inheritor's help, Li Fan consolidated his [Unmoving Body of Mountains and Seas] divine ability. Although he already had the protection of [Illusion is True], having more protective divine abilities never hurt. Perhaps in some future moment, it could save his life.

Therefore, Li Fan studied it very diligently. Whenever he had any doubts, he would consult the Inheritor.

The Inheritor not only did not find it troublesome but was rather pleased.

"He's here."

Li Fan suddenly retracted his dharma body and gazed at the horizon.

The mountain and sea lights that had been surrounding Li Fan instantly vanished. However, within the Great Desolate Immortal Realm, anomalies arose.

*Creak...*

A grating sound, like rotting metal rubbing against each other, echoed across the Great Desolate Continent. All beings who heard it felt an uncontrollable sense of vexation surge within their hearts.

Then, as the rubbing sound grew louder, this vexation gradually turned into an impulse.

Go to where the rubbing sound originated! Find the source of the sound!

Once this impulse arose, it became impossible to suppress.

Instantly, many figures on the continent lost control and shot towards the sky.

Li Fan's cold snort echoed throughout the Great Desolate Continent at this moment.

Under the deterrent power of the Creation Father God, many beings briefly regained clarity and forcibly suppressed their impulses, returning to the surface.

But some, disregarding everything, charged towards the sound.

It was as if the unpleasant rubbing sound was their eternal pursuit, its importance even surpassing their lives and Great Dao!

"A childish trick to bewitch the heart. This Immortal from the coffin, doesn't he have any other tricks?" Li Fan no longer intervened, letting the beings on the continent below rush to their deaths.

In his vision, the Immortal Coffin had indeed opened a corner of its lid.

But the gap was like an abyss, deep and bottomless, devouring everything that entered.

All beings that flew close to the Immortal Coffin were instantly swallowed by the unfathomable depths.

Within the Immortal Coffin, the sound grew louder.

And it began to be accompanied by different noises.

If the initial sound was that of the coffin lid slowly opening, then now it was as if an unknown, mysterious entity was scratching the inner walls of the coffin with its fingernails, seemingly struggling to climb out of the coffin!

The target of the Immortal Coffin was clearly Li Fan's Great Desolate Immortal Realm.

It continued to accelerate its approach.

The change in sound did not alter its bewitching and attractive effect. The beings in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, like moths to a flame, surged towards the Immortal Coffin.

With each one it devoured, its speed increased.

Li Fan's expression turned grave. The Immortal Coffin had already reached the sky of the Great Desolate Immortal Realm!

"Allow Senior Brother to be the first to greet him."

The Inheritor suddenly stood up, took a step, and in the next moment, appeared near the Immortal Coffin.

"How dare you make noise before my true self."

His seemingly frail body seemed to contain boundless energy. He reached out and slapped the Immortal Coffin fiercely.

With every move, a faint roaring sound of Mountains and Seas accompanied it, suppressing all the strange noises emanating from the Immortal Coffin.

In this instant, Li Fan seemed to see a spectacular scene of Mountains and Seas colliding, waves crashing against each other.

"Is this the Inheritor's true strength when he doesn't hold back?" Li Fan's pupils contracted.

Under the scouring of Mountains and Seas, the Immortal Coffin trembled violently.

Already dilapidated, it now faced the baptism of Mountains and Seas, reaching its limit.

It seemed on the verge of disintegration.

But the hope placed by the Guangwu Star Sea was never solely on an Immortal Coffin, but on the Immortal from the coffin within.

*Bang!*

A muffled, giant sound echoed from within the Immortal Coffin.

It was as if something was responding to the roaring sound of Mountains and Seas outside, violently pounding from the inside.

*Bang! Bang! Bang!*

The pounding grew more rapid.

Like thunder piercing the night sky, or a lighthouse dispelling the mist.

Even with the sound of Mountains and Seas swirling around, the pounding voice gradually became inaudible.

At its peak, the pounding abruptly ceased.

In that instant, the Immortal Coffin disintegrated inch by inch. A dark shadow emerged from it and shot straight towards the Inheritor near the Immortal Coffin.

"Senior Brother, be careful!" Li Fan exclaimed in alarm.

Before he could finish speaking, the dark shadow had already collided with the Inheritor.

The raindrops from the ensuing storm even reached Li Fan, who was watching from afar.

The Great Desolate Immortal Realm, comparable to the Immortal Realm, swayed like a lone boat on the surface of a stormy sea.

With gusts of wind, Li Fan sensed that the stable Dao principles of the Great Desolate Immortal Realm were being slowly disrupted.

Disregarding the Great Desolate Immortal Realm for the moment, hesummoned the Five Heavenly Emperors and Thirteen Heavenly Scars to maintain order.

Li Fan looked towards the direction of the Inheritor and the dark shadow.

The dark shadow, the Immortal from the coffin, had already revealed its true form.

It was not human.

But a giant rat!

Simply calling it a rat might not be accurate. Its swift pounces and claw swipes were astonishingly similar to human movements.

The fur on its body was even multicolored, as if adorned with brocade clothing.

It also wore a yellowish-brown straw hat on its head. However, the brim of the hat was bitten, leaving a small piece missing.

The expression on the rat's face was as vivid as a human's.

Greed, solemnity, urgency – all emotions were present.

"A異兽 (Exotic Beast) clan?"

Li Fan looked at the monstrous creature and couldn't help but think of Di San Mo's clan.

But he quickly dismissed this guess.

Not only did the Myriad Beasts Wheel show no reaction to this bizarre rat, but the Inheritor, currently locked in battle, also sent a telepathic reminder.

"Junior Brother, be careful, this is a [Gluttonous Rat Immortal]!"

Then, the Inheritor explained to Li Fan what a Gluttonous Rat Immortal was.

It was not a Nameless True Immortal who attained the Dao of [Gluttony], but a True Immortal that had mutated due to greedily and endlessly devouring the Great Dao.

Commonly, among the gathered Immortals of the Immortal Realm, Gluttonous Rat Immortals would not be born.

They generally only existed in possibilities where the apocalypse had arrived.

To maximize their chances of survival in the drifting Immortal Coffins, Immortals from coffins would often collect the remaining Great Dao to construct their Immortal Coffins.

And if they drifted in Mountains and Seas for too long, besides decaying and perishing, they would also be反噬 (counter-attacked) by the condensed Immortal Coffins of Great Dao.

The Nameless True Immortal realm was achieved by merging with the Dao.

Among the three thousand Great Daos, they were originally immiscible. Once one Dao was merged, no other Dao could be accommodated.

But in the special environment of drifting through Mountains and Seas within sealed Immortal Coffins, perhaps a miracle could occur – a Nameless True Immortal attaining multiple Daos.

The price, however...

Was the mutation of the Nameless True Immortal into various bizarre forms.

The Gluttonous Rat Immortal was the most typical example.

It still retained a certain level of sentience but was dominated by the instinctual desire to devour, wishing to consume everything useful around it.

"If Master encountered a fallen True Immortal from a coffin, he might help bury them. But these mutated True Immortals are simply killed without mercy!"

"Keeping them around is purely a menace!"

"When I suppress this fiend, I'll settle the score with the Guangwu Star Sea!" The Inheritor's voice carried a hint of anger.

Li Fan watched the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's form flicker, its claws striking and causing the surrounding Great Daos to tremble. A strange feeling suddenly arose in his heart.

"The Guangwu Star Sea came for my method of subduing the Dao Saber Dao Sword. They definitely wouldn't entrust the task to a gluttonous Rat Immortal without reason..."

Just then, Li Fan noticed a flash of brilliance in the rat's eyes.

He quickly sent a telepathic message: "Senior Brother, be careful! This is not a Gluttonous Rat Immortal in the ordinary sense!"

"Perhaps someone has possessed it, integrating themselves into it!"

The Inheritor heard this and his movements momentarily stiffened.

At this moment, a black light emerged from the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's front claws.

The light suddenly burst forth, enveloping the Inheritor.

The Gluttonous Rat Immortal itself retreated far away, like a human, stroking its whiskers with its front paws, a look of satisfaction on its face.

"This black light..."

Li Fan sensed an aura very similar to Ink Slaughter from it.

"It seems that not only the [Broken Chessboard] Dao Field is researching the power of merging Mountains and Seas," Li Fan mused thoughtfully.

Although this black light was terrifying, Li Fan did not worry about the Inheritor.

Having been by Shouqiu Gong's side and surviving by the side of Mountains and Seas for eons, how could he possibly perish so easily?

Chapter 1510: Immortal Emperor of a Billion Years

Li Fan's prediction was correct. Within the black light domain, which strongly resembled Ink Slaughter, absolute silence should have reigned. Yet, as the Gluttonous Rat Immortal stood smugly, a metallic grinding sound like waves crashing against mountains and seas suddenly pierced through the dark domain.

The sound resonated throughout the Primordial Immortal Realm, eliciting varied responses from different parts of the continent. The rustling of wind through mountains, the babbling of streams, the whistling of converging winds and clouds, the clear cries of newly born life, the rumbling of mountain ranges… These notes, representing life, motion, and change, resonated with the sound of mountains and seas from the sky. Like surging waves, they forcefully tore open the black domain.

"A petty trick, and you dare show off!" Cheng Dao roared, bursting forth from the black light. The moment he broke free, his form merged with the very fabric of this world, vanishing from sight.

Sensing that something was amiss, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal let out a strange laugh, yet it didn't panic. It shook its plump body, and from its brocade-like outer skin, thousands of small, differently colored hairs instantly detached. As these hairs fell, they transformed into towering, upright figures.

Suddenly, thousands of True Immortals stood in formation, surrounding the Rat Immortal like a protective shield.

"These figures are…"

"Nameless True Immortals?"

Li Fan observed clearly. Each hair shed from the Gluttonous Rat Immortal represented a Great Dao. At this moment, these Dao-transformed figures were fundamentally the same as Nameless True Immortals who had embodied their Dao! The Nameless True Immortal, who had greedily devoured Great Daos and thus become mutated, was now expelling the Great Daos he had already swallowed. Not only did he not weaken after losing some of his Great Daos, but his aura became even more erratic and unsettling. Li Fan also noticed that the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's appearance had subtly changed. Its claws transformed into palms, its hunched body straightened, and its facial expression became more human-like!

A great wind swept through the mountains and seas, roaring fiercely. It scattered all the Dao figures guarding the Rat Immortal. Witnessing this, Li Fan felt as if he were seeing countless possibilities, worlds, and lives consumed by the mountains and seas. Although Cheng Dao had contained his divine ability within a certain range, some residual winds, due to the fierce battle, broke free from their original position. Like invisible blades, they sliced through the Primordial Immortal Realm. Where the wind blades passed, all things perished. A massive rift, a chasm of void, appeared in its wake. Even with infinite immortal energy constantly replenishing it, it would take a considerable time to repair this scar. This demonstrated the destructive power at the heart of the battle.

Amidst the howling wind, figures danced like willow branches. Though they scattered, they remained indestructible, stubbornly maintaining their form in the winds of mountains and seas. It was at this moment that strange, continuous sounds emanated from the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's mouth. They were like the shrill, heart-wrenching cries of a rat, yet also like the impassioned recitations of a poet. More hairs fell from the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's body. True Immortals, countless as hemp, drifted outwards.

The Gluttonous Rat Immortal's body was now completely devoid of hair, making it even more human-like, though it still wore a rat's skin. The rapid chanting abruptly ceased, as if a knife had suddenly fallen, slicing through the skin. The Gluttonous Rat transformed into a human form. Unlike the hazy silhouettes of the surrounding True Immortal Dao forms, which lacked specific features, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal, though naked, was indistinguishable from a human.

"Two fellow Daoists…"

"Gluttonous Rat greets you~" A mixed voice, neither male nor female, emanating from the human-like Rat Immortal. It was a self-introduction, expecting no response from Li Fan or Cheng Dao. Before its words even finished, it extended its ten fingers remotely, controlling the surrounding True Immortal reflections that had completely fallen off. Like a puppeteer manipulating puppets from behind the scenes, with the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's assistance, the myriad True Immortal reflections gained faint human-like faces. They no longer attacked solely on instinct but truly fought like the reborn Nameless, unleashing their divine abilities and spells to their utmost.

Not only did they manifest the Dao principles of the Five Elements, Loneliness, and Silence, which existed within the [Primordial] possibility, but also Great Daos entirely unfamiliar to Li Fan. Before the Gluttonous Rat transformed into human form, the True Immortal Dao forms were like a leaderless army, fighting individually. But with the human-like Rat Immortal controlling them, their true strength was finally unleashed.

The pressure facing Cheng Dao instantly increased a hundredfold. Li Fan seemed to see a supreme figure commanding troops, annihilating powerful enemies with casual laughter.

"These Nameless beings once obeyed my commands and followed my directives in life."

"So, the true identity of this Gluttonous Rat Immortal is…"

"Something like a governing Immortal Emperor?" Li Fan's thoughts raced. Upon realizing the clue, he interjected with a probing question, "Your Majesty! Your subject has died unjustly!"

This ghostly voice pierced through the howling winds of the mountains and seas, traversing the formations of countless Nameless beings, and reached the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's ears. The Rat Immortal, who was enjoying the manipulation of the True Immortal Dao forms, suddenly froze. Although it quickly regained its composure, this subtle shift did not escape Li Fan's observation.

"Senior Brother, do not panic!"

"I will assist you!" With his suspicions confirmed, Li Fan let out a cold laugh, the Wuji Heavenly Rod leading the way, followed closely by himself, as he charged directly towards the Gluttonous Rat Immortal.

Sensing Li Fan's movement, the myriad True Immortal Dao forms moved to intercept. Most were blocked by the Wuji Heavenly Rod. Even the few that were not covered by the Primordial Wuji Great Dao’s scope could not penetrate the dual defenses of Li Fan's Myriad Manifestations Dao Net and the Mountain and Sea Unmoving Body. Bracing against the attacks of the True Immortal Dao forms, Li Fan pushed forward, aiming for the Gluttonous Rat Immortal. He intended to snatch the Immortal Emperor's head from amidst the enemy ranks!

Cheng Dao also understood Li Fan's intent and coordinated his efforts. Not only did the winds of mountains and seas become more turbulent, but above the army formation of True Immortal Dao forms, a massive figure seemingly loomed, looking down from above. Merely its gaze, as if watching over the mountains and seas, annihilated countless True Immortal Dao forms. Although the Gluttonous Rat Immortal had vomited out all the Great Daos it had devoured, increasing its combat power significantly, without a doubt, its true body was now at its most vulnerable.

Li Fan's movements were incredibly swift. In a flash, he had closed to within three feet of the Gluttonous Rat Immortal. This surprise attack was too fast; the Rat Immortal couldn't even retract its devoured Great Daos. Its body had only regenerated a thin layer of sparse fur when Li Fan's attack arrived. The Wuji Heavenly Rod struck first, followed by the saber and sword! Facing the combined assault of one rod, one saber, and one sword, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal showed no fear. It opened its mouth, revealing menacing fangs, and ferociously lunged towards the Wuji Heavenly Rod and the Dao Saber Dao Sword, as if intending to devour these deadly weapons directly! Truly befitting its gluttonous nature!

The Rat Immortal's reaction was entirely within Li Fan's expectations. With a loud laugh, the Wuji Heavenly Rod, Dao Saber, and Dao Sword vanished from sight. In their place appeared several cloudy purple pills. Even though it witnessed this instantaneous change, the Gluttonous Rat's inherent greed prevented it from retracting its fangs. It had once devoured Immortals in the court, it had once devoured entire worlds. What was there that it dared not devour!

As the myriad True Immortal reflections were rapidly recalled, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal finally reverted from its human form to its ferocious, beast-like appearance. After devouring the pills Li Fan had presented, it sought to locate Li Fan's figure. However, Li Fan had already retreated thousands of miles, returning to a safe position, waiting for the medicinal effect to take hold.

"Eating so many poison pills at once, it won't die from it!" However, the time it took for the Gluttonous Rat Immortal to succumb to the poison was far longer than Li Fan had anticipated. It seemed that after all, this tenacious character who had traversed Mountains and Seas in a coffin possessed some resistance to powers close to Dao Annihilation.

After a stalemate of half a day with Cheng Dao, anomalies finally began to appear on the Gluttonous Rat Immortal. Its originally colorful fur gradually turned purple and began to fall off uncontrollably. This was precisely the Dao transformation caused by the poison pills refined by Li Fan. At first, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal hadn't noticed, but when the purple hairs began to scatter everywhere, it finally realized in a panic.

It let out a piercing scream that ripped through the clouds. The Gluttonous Rat Immortal, disregarding its battle with Cheng Dao, frantically began collecting the falling hairs. From the Rat Immortal's cry, Li Fan not only heard fear but also a sense of urgency and reluctance. This was somewhat unexpected. But regardless of whatever past history existed between the Gluttonous Rat Immortal and its former subordinates, it did not hinder Li Fan's subsequent plan to strike while the iron was hot and seize its life.

With a wave of his sleeve, while snatching the Dao-transformed hairs from the Gluttonous Rat Immortal, Li Fan also connected with the medicinal power of the poison pills within its body, ready to tighten the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net at any moment. The more hairs that fell, the faster its strength declined. The weaker it became, the harder it would be to suppress the erupting poison pills. Once it showed signs of weakness, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's defeat was sealed.

Now that it was time to reap the rewards, Li Fan would not yield to Cheng Dao. "Life and death are as one; merging with the Dao is to become true. Free and unfettered by the external world, my Dao Pill shall be formed." Li Fan chanted softly in his heart, using the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net as a cauldron and the power of the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul as the alchemical fire, slowly refining this drifting Immortal from another possibility into a Dao Pill.

The Gluttonous Rat struggled desperately, but the net tightened relentlessly. Ultimately, it was in vain. At this moment, Cheng Dao also appeared, watching Li Fan refine the pill. After pondering for a moment, he did not intervene. The Gluttonous Rat Immortal, now devoid of its fur, had reverted to its human form. It no longer struggled, merely watching Li Fan and Cheng Dao from afar.

"The one who devours others is ultimately devoured."

"This saying is indeed true!"

"May you two Dao brothers not follow my footsteps!"

"Hahaha…" With a burst of mad laughter, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal was completely refined, becoming a crystal-clear, lustrous purplish-gold pill in Li Fan's palm. Without a doubt, this was the most beautiful and precious Dao Pill Li Fan had refined since mastering the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao.

"A pity, I cannot consume it directly." Li Fan looked at Cheng Dao, who had a solemn expression beside him, and a thought arose.

"Senior Brother, here." He said solemnly, intending to hand over the Dao Pill.

"Alas? There's no need for that." Cheng Dao was certainly taken aback by Li Fan's gesture, but he immediately shook his head and refused. It wasn’t that he saw through the pill’s mystery. Li Fan himself wasn’t certain if the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao left by Sun Piaomiao had any issues; it was merely Li Fan's inherent cautiousness. The reason Cheng Dao refused Li Fan’s kindness was entirely due to his adherence to the rules laid down by Duke Shouqiu: no matter how good a treasure was, it should not be snatched from a fellow disciple. The marvel of the current Dao Pill was not so profound as to make Cheng Dao break Duke Shouqiu’s rules.

"This victory in subduing this Rat Immortal is entirely thanks to Senior Brother's direct confrontation. If not for you drawing out the myriad True Immortal Dao forms, I absolutely could not have approached its true body so easily. To enjoy refining this Dao Pill, Senior Brother is truly deserving."

"Furthermore, after Senior Brother consumes this pill, you can share the other possibilities' Great Daos you comprehend with me. If I were to swallow it, I wouldn't have the ability to explain them to you in detail!" Li Fan's reasoning was sound. After a heartfelt speech, Cheng Dao finally could not refuse the offer. He half-heartedly swallowed the Gluttonous Rat Dao Pill.

"Senior Brother, how does it feel?" After a while, Li Fan asked tentatively.

"Alas."

"This Rat Immortal, and those myriad True Immortal reflections, are all just pitiable beings," Cheng Dao sighed deeply.

Li Fan: "What does Senior Brother mean?"

"It's the countless images I perceived from consuming the Dao Pill," Cheng Dao said, waving his hand lightly to present the scene before Li Fan. Initially, it was a magnificent Immortal Realm, peaceful, prosperous, and thriving. The Gluttonous Rat Immortal had already served as the governing Immortal Emperor for nearly two hundred million years. During its reign, all Immortals in the Immortal Realm submitted, and the realm was in a state of great prosperity. In fact, ever since the Gluttonous Rat Immortal took charge, even the Three Sages had ceased to inquire about the affairs of the Immortal Realm. The Immortals knew only of the Immortal Emperor, not the Three Sages. Decline followed prosperity, starting with the sudden arrival of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. Initially, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal was full of ambition, firmly believing it could lead the Immortals to conquer this mere Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. However, the Dao Annihilation would recede and then return, repeatedly. Although it could be suppressed for a short time, there seemed to be no end in sight. The Gluttonous Rat Immortal, while maintaining a calm facade, grew increasingly panicked and conceived the idea of secretly visiting the Three Sages to seek an answer. However, it was shocked to discover… the Three Sages had vanished. As if they had evaporated from this world, they could not be contacted at all. Although most Immortals in the Immortal Realm had forgotten the Three Sages, they still represented the Sages in the hearts of all Immortals. Already under the pressure of the tribulation and with people’s hearts in turmoil, if they learned that the Sages had disappeared, the Immortal Realm would descend into chaos long before being wiped out by the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. After much deliberation, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal decided to conceal this news. To prevent the disappearance of the Sages from being exposed, it even took it upon itself to impersonate the Three Sages. While the Gluttonous Rat Immortal, as an Immortal Emperor of millions of years, possessed supreme power and far surpassed the other Immortals, impersonating one Sage might not have been difficult. However, impersonating all three without revealing any flaws… was pushing its limits. Thus, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal desperately sought ways to enhance its power in a short time. In desperation, it thought of directly devouring True Immortals and stealing their comprehended Great Daos. The results were remarkable. Relying on its peerless cultivation, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal truly managed to integrate multiple different Dao paths into itself.

Chapter 1511: The Immortal Destiny is Finally Counted

The initial merging of two Daos was the most arduous.

The Gluttonous Rat Immortal originally cultivated the Great Dao of [Imperial Law]. The more subordinates who submitted and were loyal, the stronger the feedback he received.

The accumulation of two hundred million years allowed his Great Dao of [Imperial Law] to reach its theoretical extreme. Under heaven, none did not submit.

It was precisely by relying on the supreme Great Dao of [Imperial Law] that the Rat successfully merged and absorbed the second Great Dao alongside him, like a subordinate, with absolute crushing power.

But if one could merge, then two. If two, then three.

Under the guise of Immortal Emperor, he secretly summoned the Immortals and then devoured them one by one.

At first, the cautious Gluttonous Rat Immortal would choose True Immortals with ordinary strength and low renown to start with. But later, as the myriad Daos merged, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal became somewhat reckless.

However, it must be said that the Gluttonous Rat Immortal truly lived up to his title of [Eternal Immortal Emperor].

Even though the greed for Dao gradually engulfed his mind, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal did not forget his original intention. To embody three Sages with one person, and save the collapsing empire.

Under the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, the world on the verge of collapse, under his governance, actually continued for another hundred million years. It seemed he truly saw the hope of eternal existence.

But all stories must eventually reach their end.

After being delayed for hundreds of millions of years, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation seemed to have completely lost its patience for further stalemate. It mobilized its forces and concentrated its offensive.

One day, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal was horrified to discover that the pressure of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation facing the Immortal Realm had inexplicably doubled.

The hundred million years of stable peace had caused the Immortals to lose their sensitivity to the crisis. By the time they reacted and wished to use Immortals to mend the heavens, it was already too late.

The Gluttonous Rat Immortal could only watch helplessly as the terrifying tide of Dao Annihilation, with its unstoppable might, engulfed more than half of the Immortal Realm in an instant.

True Immortals perished, innumerable. The survivors were completely terrified, their courage to resist the calamity utterly extinguished.

As the actual ruler of the Immortal Realm, witnessing his territory collapse in such a short period, the sense of failure was undoubtedly extremely strong. However, at that moment, these so-called "emotions" were no longer important.

Survival was the only truly meaningful thing.

But the Gluttonous Rat Immortal, also known as the [Eternal Immortal Emperor], discovered in despair that under the impending catastrophe, they had no escape.

The Immortals gathered around him, begging for a way to survive.

But the Gluttonous Rat Immortal looked at the already tattered Immortal Realm, and he himself had fallen into despair.

However, after all, he was someone who had ruled the Immortal Realm for a full three hundred million years. The Gluttonous Rat Immortal would not give up so easily.

In desperation, a crazy idea emerged in his mind.

Gather the strength of all Immortals to directly reach the transcendent Other Shore.

In the possibility where the Gluttonous Rat Immortal resided, legends of the Other Shore and other possibilities also circulated. But they were extremely secret, the most confidential of the confidential. Even the Gluttonous Rat Immortal himself, when he was young, had only accidentally heard them from the Three Sages. Not to mention the birth of true transcendent experts.

With no one to emulate, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal could only explore on his own.

But the most crucial point was, he had very little time left.

Searching the remaining lands of the Immortal Realm, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal finally found a method that could barely traverse possibilities.

Immortal Coffin Crossing!

It was just unfortunate that among the surviving Immortals, he seemed to be the only one with sufficient strength to survive in the Immortal Coffin formed by the world, floating amidst the tide of Dao Annihilation.

Others, even if they could barely enter the Immortal Coffin, would likely not last long before completely perishing. Not to mention reaching the Other Shore directly.

The Gluttonous Rat Immortal could certainly escape alone. But as the dignified Eternal Immortal Emperor, would he just watch his subordinates die tragically?

The Gluttonous Rat Immortal was clearly not such a selfish person.

Relying on his rich experience in secretly devouring and merging the Daos of the Immortals over the years, at the last moment, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal actually devised a brilliant method. To use [Imperial Law] to control the Dao and maintain the balance of all Daos.

As long as he remained in a state of devouring or semi-devouring, the Immortals would not be truly absorbed by him. They would still possess their own independent Dao paths, cultivation bases, memories, emotions, and so on.

After hiding in the Immortal Coffin and successfully drifting to the Other Shore, he could then release the Immortals and thus successfully escape this calamity.

After experimentally absorbing more than ten True Immortals, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal found this method feasible. The only drawback was that he himself was both leading the devouring of Dao and desperately trying to maintain the clear demarcation of Daos.

This extremely contradictory practice would put him in ultimate torment.

And it would increase proportionally with the number of ingested Dao paths and the time spent maintaining the balance of all Daos.

There was a moment of hesitation in his heart, but amidst this hesitation, countless True Immortals perished.

The Gluttonous Rat Immortal immediately made up his mind.

The Immortal Realm was already in a precarious state, and the final tide of Dao Annihilation could erupt at any moment. There was simply no time to explain slowly to the surviving True Immortals.

Even if he explained, they might not believe him. Holding this belief, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal resolutely began to devour the Immortals on a large scale.

Facing the Immortal Emperor's sudden cannibalistic behavior, the Immortals were horrified and terrified.

But they were completely unable to resist.

They could only curse and beg in despair and fear.

Although the Eternal Immortal Emperor's actions were not hesitant in the slightest, the words and actions of the Immortals were deeply imprinted in his heart.

"Rat! You are the biggest rat in the Immortal Realm!"

"Your Majesty, spare my life!"

"Even if you devour me, I will become a vengeful spirit, waiting for the day of your demise!"

...

At first, he would still listen to those voices in his heart.

As the number of devoured Immortals increased, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal instinctively became more indifferent. Later, he simply ignored them completely.

In the instant before the Immortal Realm was completely destroyed and the tide of Dao Annihilation swallowed all things.

The Great Dao twisted and materialized, and an Immortal Coffin descended from the heavens.

The Gluttonous Rat Immortal, with the surviving True Immortals, hid inside.

Next came a period of extremely long years. So long that the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's memories became somewhat blurred.

Inside the coffin was absolute darkness. Outside the Immortal Coffin was the world-destroying tide of Dao Annihilation.

The Gluttonous Rat Emperor could clearly perceive the process of Dao Annihilation constantly eroding the Immortal Coffin.

He could only pray in his heart that before the Immortal Coffin was completely corroded, he would reach the Other Shore.

But perhaps his luck ran out after being the ruler of an Immortal Realm for three hundred million years. After an unknown amount of time, let alone the Other Shore, he didn't even encounter a safe place.

The Immortal Coffin drifted with the current, floating in the tide of Dao Annihilation.

It seemed like there was never any hope.

And the Gluttonous Rat Immortal had underestimated the difficulty of maintaining the merging of myriad Daos.

Perhaps it could be maintained in the normal Immortal Realm environment. But within the Immortal Coffin surrounded by the tide of Dao Annihilation, maintaining balance became increasingly difficult.

He did not want to devour the Immortals in his heart.

But he could only watch helplessly as his body merged with his former subordinates.

He himself seemed to have truly become the "Rat" cursed by millions of people.

The last glimmer of light in his heart gradually extinguished. The Eternal Immortal Emperor fell into endless darkness...

After another unknown number of years, when the Immortal Coffin had completely rotted and could no longer withstand the tide of Dao Annihilation.

With a great roar, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal, as if from another life, discovered that he had finally arrived in another starry sky.

This starry sky, although filled with the lingering decay of Dao Annihilation,

Was at least temporarily safe.

...

Li Fan and Cheng Dao, two fellow disciples, looked at the unfolding scene before them, speechless for a long time.

"If it were me, I wouldn't have done any better than this Eternal Immortal Emperor."

"He did his best, but the general trend was hard to reverse," Li Fan sighed.

Cheng Dao also commented, "His plight is pitiable, and his actions can be forgiven. If he hadn't been so aggressive, perhaps his life wouldn't have been forfeit."

Li Fan showed a look of shame, "I was reckless. I never expected this outwardly terrifying rat to have such a past."

Cheng Dao waved his hand, "Junior Brother, there's no need to blame yourself. Most Gluttonous Rat Immortals are not good people. Don't change your perception because of this anomaly, the Eternal Immortal Emperor."

"Senior Brother's teachings are correct."

Next, Cheng Dao fully explained the Dao paths he had comprehended from the Gluttonous Rat Dao Elixir to Li Fan, and even added his own insights into the Great Dao from time to time.

The comprehension of this spirit stone from the side of Mountains and Seas, disciple of Shouqiu, was truly extraordinary. Li Fan even suspected that even if he had swallowed the Dao Elixir himself, the effect would not have been better.

While listening to the scriptures and discussing the Dao, Li Fan also secretly observed Cheng Dao.

It seemed that after swallowing a Dao Elixir, the other party showed no abnormalities.

"However, we cannot draw conclusions so easily now. We still need to feed him a few more."

"Guangwu Star Sea, Hmph..."

Ninety-nine days later, Cheng Dao finished bestowing his teachings.

"Senior Brother, do you feel that the possibility where the Eternal Immortal Emperor resided seems much weaker in its Dao path than ours?" Li Fan asked with a frown after recalling everything, his tone somewhat uncertain.

"It's not your illusion. It is indeed so," Cheng Dao nodded.

"Why is that?"

Cheng Dao narrowed his eyes, fell silent for a moment, and then slowly said, "Perhaps, in that possibility, an unprecedented figure has already emerged."

"Hmm?"

"This is also my guess, and it has not been confirmed by Master."

Cheng Dao first stated a point, then continued, "Putting aside the Three Sages, in a certain possibility, there seems to be an upper limit to the number of powerful beings that can be born."

"It's not just a matter of quantity, but a combination of quantity and cultivation realm, all jointly determining it."

"Of course, when I say powerful beings, I mean transcendent experts who can jump out of their own possibilities."

Cheng Dao used his finger as a pen to draw a circle in front of Li Fan.

"It's like a water pool of a fixed size. Every time a powerful being is born, a certain area of this pool is marked out. Once the pool is completely occupied, any remaining individuals, even with heaven-defying talent, will be unable to reach the transcendent realm."

Li Fan stared intently at the constantly divided circle in front of him, showing a thoughtful expression. "Senior Brother, in the world where the Eternal Immortal Emperor resided, the Three Sages inexplicably disappeared. Could it be that this is because the potential there has been exhausted, and no more transcendent experts will be born?"

Cheng Dao looked at Li Fan with a half-smile, but did not answer.

Seeing this, Li Fan's heart already had an answer.

He continued to examine the small circle in front of him, and with a wave of his hand, he redrew the hundreds of divided areas.

"In that world, let alone powerful beings like Master, even transcendent realms are very few."

"If that's the case, how strong was the powerful being born before?"

"It almost exhausted the potential of an entire possibility?"

Li Fan temporarily used [Potential] to refer to the small circle in front of him.

"Could it be that their strength is even above Master's?" Li Fan couldn't help but gasp.

Cheng Dao, however, was very calm, "In the past, when Master resolved the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation and saved the Immortal Realm from dire straits, facing the admiration of the Immortal Emperors and all Immortals, Master remained very humble."

"He old man never considered himself a powerful being in the Mountains and Seas."

"In his own words, he was merely [Shouqiu Immortal Shengde]."

Upon hearing this, Li Fan immediately became solemn, nodding in agreement. "Master is not only a master due to his strength, but also for his breadth of mind and character. Even if, one day, Senior Brother's strength surpasses his, I believe Senior Brother will still respect him as Master."

"That is natural!" Cheng Dao did not deny it.

"The Mountains and Seas are truly filled with powerful individuals." Li Fan's gaze returned to the small circle in front of him, looking at the circle within a circle that almost occupied the entire area, and lost himself in thought.

"I truly wonder what the legendary Other Shore is like, with so many unimaginable powerhouses gathered together."

Cheng Dao smiled, "Junior Brother, do not worry. With the talent of us fellow disciples, reaching the Other Shore one day is a certainty."

Li Fan laughed heartily, "Then let me thank Senior Brother in advance for your auspicious words."

"Let's put the Other Shore aside for now. If you wish to see visitors from other possibilities, you can do so now," Cheng Dao suddenly spoke after a moment of silence.

"Senior Brother is referring to the Guangwu Star Sea?"

"Correct." Cheng Dao then displayed a completely new image in front of Li Fan.

A total of nine Heavenly Pillars, arranged in a circle.

In the center enclosed by the Heavenly Pillars was absolute darkness. Li Fan sensed a familiar aura of Dao Annihilation from it.

And outside the nine Heavenly Pillars, densely packed from sparse to dense. Were at least a hundred supporting Heavenly Pillars!

Although not every Heavenly Pillar might have sealed a Nameless True Immortal within.

Nevertheless, the grandeur of this pillar construction could still be felt.

Unlike Li Fan's approach of simply using Heavenly Pillars to support the collapsing heavens, these Heavenly Pillars were not of equal specification. They progressed from the inside out, from weak to strong.

It was as if a staircase had been formed.

The central nine Heavenly Pillars were the weakest.

Because they could attract Dao Annihilation to this place.

And the surrounding hundred densely packed Heavenly Pillars formed a solid defense, preventing this attracted Dao Annihilation from spreading.

Li Fan looked at the area enclosed by the nine Heavenly Pillars, like a "water reservoir".

He suddenly realized, "Is that how the Guangwu Star Sea salvages creations from other possibilities?"

"It should be. It is indeed quite ingenious."

"Besides being ingenious, the ability to construct these hundred Heavenly Pillars shows that the Guangwu Star Sea's strength is absolutely not to be underestimated. Before, I had underestimated them." Cheng Dao praised.

Chapter 1512: Fishing for the Annihilation of the Dao

Cheng Dao closed his eyes, remaining silent, while Li Fan's spirit was extremely tense.

He closely observed his surroundings. If anything was amiss, he would immediately activate [True Revelation].

Although Shouqiu Gong was humble and never considered himself a powerful being in the Mountains and Seas, Li Fan would not let himself be blinded by pride. If his disguise as a disciple of Shouqiu Gong and his deception were exposed, let alone Shouqiu Gong, Cheng Dao would likely never forgive him.
