The connection between the mortal world and the Mountains and Seas seemed extremely difficult. Cheng Dao closed his eyes for a full three days before finally completing the process and standing up.

"I have already sent a message, roughly explaining the situation to Master. I just don't know when he will have the time to see it," Cheng Dao said with some regret.

Communicating with the Mountains and Seas must have been a considerable burden for Cheng Dao. His already aged appearance now seemed even more frail and on the verge of decay and annihilation.

"Senior Brother, please rest," Li Fan said repeatedly.

Cheng Dao did not force himself and sat cross-legged in the void. It took him more than a month to recover.

Li Fan was somewhat surprised, "Is it really that difficult to contact Master?"

"Naturally," Cheng Dao said with a serious expression, "The space between Mountains and Seas is not a place ordinary mortal beings can tread. I am only able to barely maintain myself due to my special origins. Otherwise..."

"Let alone being able to withstand the pressure from Mountains and Seas, even if one could persist, one would face the aura of Dao Annihilation, which is countless times stronger than in the mortal world, at all times. It's like a mortal falling into water, their mind filled with suffocation and drowning. Perhaps they would go mad before being truly devoured by Dao Annihilation."

Cheng Dao sighed long and hard, "Since ancient times, the Mountains and Seas have not been a place that mortal beings can easily tread. If not for the meritorious deeds of Sage Lords Lianshan and Guihai in their creation, we would not even be able to gaze from afar."

Li Fan knew the terror of Mountains and Seas.

He had personally entered the Infinite Sea, and every drop of seawater seemed to possess the weight to completely crush his divine soul.

However, the difference was that Li Fan possessed the treasure of [Reality Rewriting]. Under the protection of [Illusion is True], the current Li Fan could now traverse Mountains and Seas without hindrance for a certain period.

"What does it feel like to wander in the Mountains and Seas?" Li Fan, pretending to have never seen it before and looking very yearning, asked Cheng Dao for advice.

Cheng Dao did not hide anything and elaborated on his feelings as his consciousness traveled through the Mountains and Seas.

Comparing Li Fan's own experiences, he felt even more deeply the power of [Reality Rewriting].

For someone like Cheng Dao, traveling in the Mountains and Seas was extremely difficult, walking on thin ice as if treading on eggs. With the slightest carelessness, there was a risk of perishing. Moreover, according to himself, this was under the premise of having the protection of Shouqiu Gong's imprint. Without Shouqiu Gong's guidance, with Cheng Dao's current strength, he could not travel far.

From their casual conversation, Li Fan also confirmed that Cheng Dao had not mentioned him to Shouqiu Gong during this communication. After all, every extra moment spent he faced immense pressure. He could only convey urgent matters.

Although Cheng Dao said this, Li Fan did not fully believe him and remained vigilant at all times, preventing Shouqiu Gong from suddenly appearing.

Since his Master had already been informed, Cheng Dao was unwilling to handle matters arbitrarily and could only wait for his Master's instructions. And based on previous experience, Shouqiu Gong's response time was erratic and had no fixed pattern.

However, the passage from the high wall to the outer starry sky was now completely sealed due to Dao Annihilation. Even if Li Fan and the others wanted to take revenge on the Guangwu Star Sea, they were helpless for the time being.

They could only wait patiently.

The Gluttonous Rat Immortal's merging of Daos had also provided considerable enlightenment to Cheng Dao. In Li Fan's perception, the Dao Net attached to the high wall not only became more solid but also sprouted many new Dao strings.

Some of these were even Dao principles that no longer existed in the original possibility. They were all derived from Cheng Dao's own enlightenment and evolution. Although they could not support Dao Annihilation, they served as auxiliary components to the Star Sea Dao Net, playing a supporting role.

Cheng Dao gradually immersed himself in his own contemplation, losing track of time.

Meanwhile, during this period, Li Fan was pondering the method of fishing for Dao Annihilation that the Guangwu Star Sea used.

The unknown existence hidden in Dao Annihilation had not yet left. Li Fan naturally would not court death by testing it within the high wall.

Li Fan's main body appeared to be meditating in the Primordial Immortal Realm.

In reality, his consciousness had entered the [Endless Cycle].

During this period of time when Li Fan was largely uninvolved, the time loop continued to play out within the Endless Cycle. The ending of the Hungry Immortal destroying the world had been repeated countless times.

The True Celestial Venerable, whose spiritual essence had been completely stripped away, now possessed no cultivation talent and had even gone mad.

Regardless of whether this outsider existed or not, the Endless Cycle still evolved according to the passage of time Li Fan had experienced before.

This time, Li Fan's consciousness entered it, not to toy with the True Celestial Venerable again, but to study the fishing technique of the Guangwu Star Sea using this time flow.

"First, I need to verify whether the Endless Cycle created by Reality Rewriting constitutes a complete possibility..."

As Li Fan thought this, his consciousness instantly spanned the Utmost Darkness Star Sea and arrived at the location of the high wall.

Familiar with the path, he entered the interior of the experimental field space.

As expected, he still saw the five projections left by Shouqiu Gong within.

"..."

Li Fan remained silent. After leaving the high wall, he explored the still intact Star Sea of Shuoxing.

The Dao Net, the Immortal Hunters, Cheng Dao.

All existed within this possibility.

Li Fan had not carefully considered the function of the Endless Cycle before. He had not thought much of this time flow created by Reality Rewriting. It wasn't until he came into contact with many Nameless beings after emerging from the high wall and understood the existence of the Three Sage Lords and even transcendent beings that Li Fan finally understood how incredible it truly was.

He also vaguely understood that his [Reality Rewriting] was qualitatively different from the time reversal.

"In reality, it is essentially the same as the [Primordial] possibility I experience every time I activate Reality Rewriting. It's just that a segment of time has been intercepted. And..."

Li Fan tried to enter the Infinite Sea within this Endless Cycle.

But as expected, he failed.

"The mortal world exists by relying on Mountains and Seas."

"And this Endless Cycle was created out of nothing by Reality Rewriting, only depending on Reality Rewriting. It cannot connect with Mountains and Seas. It is like a locked room. In a sense, it is absolutely safe for me."

"But inversely inferring..."

"Every time I activate Reality Rewriting in reality, I am resetting Mountains and Seas."

Previously, Li Fan had judged based on the lifespan of the mortal world in his Reality Rewriting panel, and concluded that the entire Mountains and Seas would be reset after activating Reality Rewriting.

But now, Li Fan had doubts again.

Because after truly seeing the power of Mountains and Seas and Reality Rewriting's performance when facing Mountains and Seas, Li Fan felt that Reality Rewriting might not be superior to Mountains and Seas. It was more likely on the same level.

This could be inferred from the fact that the duration of [Illusion is True] deceiving Mountains and Seas was very short.

"Of course, it is also possible that my body cannot withstand deceiving Mountains and Seas for a long time. Prolonged integration might bring unknown side effects. Reality Rewriting, to protect me, intentionally set this duration and cooldown time."

Li Fan shook his head slightly.

With his current strength, he was still too far from comprehending the true meaning of Mountains and Seas and Reality Rewriting.

Regardless, as long as it could be used by him, it was fine.

Within this Endless Cycle, Li Fan could be said to have no natural enemies. He did not need to worry about Mountains and Seas, and coupled with the experience gained in this life in the real world, it did not take him much effort to recreate the Primordial Immortal Realm within the high wall and erect numerous Heavenly Pillars.

"It can be said that this is a simulation within a simulation."

"Even the insights into the Great Dao that I absorb here are truly effective."

Li Fan slowly caressed the Dao principles flowing from the Hungry Immortal Heavenly Pillar, feeling it was incredibly miraculous.

Although the Hungry Immortal was temporarily sealed, the starting and ending points of this time flow had long been set. In a short period, she would return to the Immortal Ruins, remembering nothing.

Thinking of this, Li Fan ignored the Hungry Immortal for the time being.

He only looked at the Heavenly Pillars standing upright in the field.

"Because it is not truly connected to the Mountains and Infinite Sea above, the tide of Dao Annihilation here is also a simulation created by Reality Rewriting."

"But True dissolves into False, and False transforms into True. With Reality Rewriting's ability, False is almost indistinguishable from True. It is enough for me to experiment. If I can successfully build it within this Endless Cycle, I can replicate it in reality."

"Moreover, I can also freely adjust and control the flow of time here..."

The entire possibility of the Endless Cycle was equivalent to a playground built solely for Li Fan. The one-to-one replica of the real world eliminated his worries.

He began to diligently study the engineering of the Heavenly Pillar’s seawall and fishing for Dao Annihilation.

Even though it was just a fleeting glimpse in the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's memory, the principle was not complicated.

And for Li Fan, it was easy to reduce the Heavenly Pillars to varying heights using the methods of the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao.

It only took more than ten cycles of the Endless Cycle for Li Fan to successfully create this marvel for the first time.

With a flip of his mind, Li Fan temporarily withdrew the power of Shouqiu Gong's projection within the high wall.

As the supporting force suddenly disappeared, countless dark clouds began to appear in the sky near the central low Heavenly Pillars.

Sounds like mountains and seas roaring continuously, growing louder and louder.

Li Fan subconsciously flashed away from the area.

He looked solemnly at the dark abyss vortex in front of him. After observing for a long time, he could not discern the difference between this "false" Dao Annihilation and the real Dao Annihilation connected to Mountains and Seas.

"It seems my Dao of [True Illusion is False] still has a long way to go."

Li Fan calmed his mind and refocused his attention on the vortex of Dao Annihilation.

Since it was not connected to Mountains and Seas, no foreign objects would be attracted or washed ashore.

However, from the commotion caused by the descent of Dao Annihilation, Li Fan confirmed that this initial attempt had already succeeded.

The only thing he could not achieve at the moment was to restore the Heavenly Pillars, as the Guangwu Star Sea did when they successfully lured and trapped beings from Dao Annihilation.

The consequence was that once this project was initiated, it meant that the catastrophe of Dao Annihilation's destruction was not far away.

"Chipping away is simple. But to restore what was chipped away, and to have it fully restored in a short time..."

In Li Fan's mind, he recalled the bizarre scene of Nameless True Immortals' faces appearing in each Heavenly Pillar when the Guangwu Star Sea fished for the tide of Dao Annihilation.

"Without their cooperation, it probably wouldn't be possible."

Li Fan touched his chin and looked at the Hungry Immortal sealed within the Heavenly Pillar again.

In this Endless Cycle, the Hungry Immortal was almost identical to the one Li Fan knew from the original possibility. After witnessing Li Fan's heaven-defying methods and the tragic fate of his fellow Immortals who were even chopped off as Heavenly Pillars,

The Hungry Immortal wisely and decisively chose to cooperate.

"Since I can strip away all your Dao comprehension using the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao, you can naturally use the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao to reclaim what you have lost."

"Life and death are as one, merging with the Dao to attain true integration. Free from the external world, my Elixir shall be formed. This is the art of creating great elixirs in the world. I will teach it to you..."

Li Fan did not hesitate and passed on the entire supreme secret method.

Initially, the Hungry Immortal was somewhat fearful, but as her understanding of the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao deepened, her entire mind was gradually captivated.

The Hungry Immortal's comprehension could only be described as mediocre.

Li Fan was almost losing patience waiting for her to barely grasp this exquisite refining method.

However, Li Fan then realized that although the Hungry Immortal started slowly, in the actual application process, she was even more proficient than Li Fan.

After careful observation, Li Fan saw some clues: "This Dao of Hunger seems to be innately compatible with the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao. The Dao Elixirs I refine need to be consumed by others to be converted for absolute safety."

"But the Hungry Immortal has no such concerns and could swallow them directly without any scruples. Although she is imprisoned and has no need to worry about any hidden schemes of the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao, it also partly explains the uniqueness of the Dao of Hunger, this external Dao. After all, it is a Dao path that took root and reborn after arriving in another possibility..."

Thus, although Li Fan did not know how the Guangwu Star Sea achieved the conversion of Heavenly Pillar heights, Li Fan, through his own learning, reached the desired effect after some effort.

Furthermore, Li Fan modified the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao based on the feedback from the Hungry Immortal.

Unnecessary parts were removed.

The method only needed to cooperate with the change in the Heavenly Pillars.

...

The objective had been achieved. In total, it had only taken Li Fan more than twenty cycles within the Endless Cycle.

And in the real world, only a mere hour and a quarter had passed!

This was the terrifying power of Reality Rewriting.

Li Fan looked at the Hungry Immortal, who had gloriously mastered the technique and was happily admiring herself, and her expression of utter disbelief as the cycle restarted.

Li Fan couldn't help but think of a sentence that Shouqiu Gong had once said to Cheng Dao.

"Irrelevant to the final outcome."

"Just as the beginning and end of the Endless Cycle are predetermined. Perhaps everything in the mortal world is also already decided."

"No matter how much sentient beings struggle, the outcome will remain unchanged."

Li Fan pondered, lost in thought for a moment.

Chapter 1513: Reincarnation Creates the Immortal Embankment

"The entire mortal world, including Mountains and Seas, is merely a larger version of the [Endless Cycle]?"

"Just as the True Celestial Venerable, no matter how hard he tried, could not change the fate of the Profound Yellow Realm being engulfed by the Immortal Ruins. Mountains and Seas will ultimately be unable to escape the fate of merging."

"How can one truly change and transcend?"

...

When the time of the Endless Cycle restarted, Li Fan's consciousness had already left it. However, the doubts brought about by this attempt lingered in Li Fan's mind ever since.

They lingered for a long time, never to dissipate.

Even when he secretly experimented with the Heavenly Pillar Immortal Embankment in reality, these thoughts would often surface.

Facts proved that the Endless Cycle was almost identical to the [Primordial] possibility. Li Fan's experimental results within it could truly be replicated in reality without any modification.

When Cheng Dao witnessed the method of constructing the Immortal Embankment presented by Li Fan, he couldn't help but sigh, "Junior Brother, you are truly a heaven-sent genius. How could you replicate this project in such a short time? And you only relied on glimpses from memory, without actually visiting the location."

"Once the principle is understood, replication is not difficult. Senior Brother's newly born Dao strings after enlightenment are truly extraordinary. These are things that do not exist in our world." Li Fan pointed to the Dao Net surrounding the high wall and said with great humility.

While Li Fan was studying the Immortal Embankment, Cheng Dao had also truly integrated the original faint Dao strings into the Dao Net. Li Fan could faintly feel that with the addition of these new forces, the starry sky around the high wall and the Star Sea of Shuoxing had become much more stable.

It seemed that with the support of these originally non-existent Dao principles, the effect of one plus one being greater than two had been achieved.

Cheng Dao had also noticed this anomaly and told Li Fan an anecdote.

Once, during his communication with Shouqiu Gong, he had asked about possible methods to resist Dao Annihilation. Having inherited Shouqiu Gong's teachings, Cheng Dao also wished to emulate his Master's heroic deed of saving the world and turning the tide of disaster.

Shouqiu Gong did not mock his disciple's overestimation of his abilities but instead earnestly gave two suggestions.

First, to continue cultivating the art of [Phantom Dao Embodiment]. As long as one became sufficiently powerful, even if the fate of being devoured by Dao Annihilation could not ultimately be changed, one might be able to persist until the final moment of the merging of Mountains and Seas.

If the first method was to seek external assistance, then the second method was to help the possibility itself become stronger. A naturally solid foundation would then not require any Heavenly Pillars or phantoms.

However, the possibility where Cheng Dao resided was already terminally ill and riddled with holes. Reversing a late-stage terminal illness naturally required extraordinary measures.

To absorb the Great Dao from other possibilities to fill its own deficiencies.

"Harming the surplus to nourish the deficient!"

Shouqiu Gong also told Cheng Dao that such individuals did indeed exist in the Mountains and Seas, who traversed to other possibilities, extracted and refined the Great Dao, and then returned to their homeland to sustain the collapsing heavens.

"This corresponds to what Master said. It seems that in all matters, one must personally verify. No matter how much one envisions or muses, it is not as effective as trying it yourself," Cheng Dao stroked his beard and smiled, clearly satisfied with his own creation.

Li Fan and Cheng Dao then exchanged their insights.

Although Li Fan was in disguise, their interaction felt as genuine as that between biological brothers.

Time passed in this extremely harmonious atmosphere, and in the blink of an eye, fifty years had gone by.

Cheng Dao had still not received a message from Shouqiu Gong, but the thirteen Primordial Dao Forms that Li Fan had been waiting for had finally arrived.

One day, at the border of the high wall and the Star Sea of Shuoxing, subtle anomalies were detected.

Like the waves caused by a giant cruise ship riding the wind and waves, they continuously lapped against the shore. The area, already surrounded and encircled by annihilation, was supported only by the high wall's Dao Net.

At this moment, under this violent vibration, it felt like a solitary island in a massive tsunami, on the verge of collapse.

Li Fan and Cheng Dao both flashed out at the same time, looking in the direction of the anomaly.

It was very similar to the scene when Dao Annihilation was imminent outside the world.

However, besides the sound of mountains and seas roaring, there was also a dull sound like metal hammers constantly colliding and striking.

With each sound that occurred, it was as if a thread, from nothingness to existence, was being created.

With constant dull sounds, the ten thousand Dao threads overlapped and became thicker. It was like divine power parting the seas, forcefully carving a path out of Dao Annihilation.

Li Fan stared at the magnificent scene before him and suddenly recalled the scene of Hei Tian Yi breaking through the high wall and descending mightily.

"Senior Brother, have you ever seen someone traverse possibilities?"

Cheng Dao heard this, was slightly startled, and then thought of the alien Nameless beings Li Fan had mentioned before.

His expression immediately turned serious.

"It seems that Di San Mo and the others have concealed something."

"Such a commotion could not possibly be caused by merely thirteen Nameless True Immortals."

Li Fan also nodded in agreement, "That sound could briefly repel Dao Annihilation... Ordinary Nameless True Immortals would probably be shattered into dust by this sound."

"However, with Senior Brother here, there's no need to fear them."

Cheng Dao smiled and also said coldly, "The materials for mending the heavens naturally are the more the merrier, and the more they come, the better."

The anomaly at the border of the Star Sea of Shuoxing became increasingly magnificent until the thread in the void finally solidified from illusory to real. The dull sounds then abruptly ceased. A green pillar of light, moments later, flew out from this thread.

Behind the light pillar, Dao Annihilation once again swallowed the thread.

Unlike the great commotion during its creation, Dao Annihilation's consumption was so quiet, without a sound.

The light pillar seemed to have already locked onto the direction of the high wall. Although it was descending for the first time, it did not pause at all and headed straight towards them.

However, just as it was about to reach, it seemed to suddenly discover the layers of the Star Sea of Shuoxing's Dao Net attached to the outside, acting as a protective shield.

It then abruptly stopped.

The green light receded, revealing its true form.

It was a bizarre and strange thousand-handed fleshball.

A faint, eerie green light still shrouded the surface of the fleshball, obscuring its details.

However, Li Fan could vaguely see the characteristics of various strange beasts on this giant fleshball.

"Junior Brother, it seems that something major has happened to this exotic beast clan."

"Senior Brother is right, I can also see it. This giant fused body does not contain multiple consciousnesses..." Li Fan stared ahead, his heart stirred, and he attempted to activate the Myriad Beasts Wheel.

After activating the wheel, it did indeed have an effect. The countless tentacles on the giant fleshball swayed incessantly, as if waving in the wind.

It was also as if mocking Li Fan.

"Little boy, is the Myriad Beasts Wheel fun?"

As if a billion voices spoke at the same time. And each voice had a different emotion.

There was anger, mockery, greed at seeing delicious food, joy at surviving a disaster, and relief like finding a continent to survive on after drifting at sea for years.

Li Fan shook his head slightly, saying regretfully to Cheng Dao, "It seems I underestimated them after all."

"Ultimately, it is a complete possibility civilization. Even if they are exotic races, how can they be so easily manipulated? Even the same person will change drastically in different possibilities. Let alone an entire race," Cheng Dao comforted him.

"However, they have still come. It fulfills Master's saying, 'Irrelevant to the final outcome'."

After the encounter in the Endless Cycle, Li Fan had become increasingly fond of these four words. Besides the profound and unfathomable meaning of these four words themselves, Li Fan preferred the calmness implied by mastery over everything, contained within these four words.

"Hahaha, Junior Brother speaks well! 'Irrelevant to the final outcome'!"

"Arrogant exotic races, since you've come, you shall stay!"

Before Li Fan could make a move, Cheng Dao's figure had already disappeared from his original spot.

The hidden Dao Net outside the high wall instantly glowed with infinite brilliance. Then, it suddenly expanded, covering the entire surviving starry sky that was encircled by annihilation.

The giant thousand-handed fleshball was caught off guard and fell into the net.

Although it relied on the Azure Origin provided by Li Fan to traverse possibilities, the great commotion it caused upon arrival proved its strength. It was indeed not to be underestimated.

It was highly possible that it was a fusion of the entire exotic race, including the thirteen Primordial Dao Forms. Its strength naturally could not be underestimated.

Although it was now in the net, it was not panicked but instead overjoyed.

"Delicious!"

"You boy are so hospitable, I must thank you properly!"

"Hehehehehe!"

Billions of laughter emanated from the fleshball.

Countless images of ferocious exotic beasts successively lit up on the fleshball. Some had their eyes gouged out, some had their heads severed. In short, they were all incomplete and covered in blood. However, without exception, they all performed the action of "devouring" the surrounding Dao Net.

As if intending to devour the heavens and earth, a huge suction force instantly emanated from this monster.

This suction force was different from the devouring caused by the Hungry Immortal.

The Hungry Immortal's devouring was due to [Hunger], while this exotic fused body was simply devouring for the sake of devouring.

The Great Dao of Heaven and Earth, all things.

Were merely its nourishment!

In addition to devouring, the thousand-handed fleshball also revealed a crazy desire to accept and merge.

As if it wanted to turn Li Fan, and everything in this starry sky, into a part of itself.

The Dao Net of Shuoxing suffered a small-scale blank area due to this bite.

Even Li Fan hadn't expected that the speed at which this exotic fused body devoured and digested Dao principles could be so fast.

Not only did it devour, but it even transformed them into its own power in a very short time.

Li Fan clearly saw that due to this devouring, hundreds of tentacles had grown on the fleshball.

"Vermin!"

Cheng Dao roared. The light erupting from the tangible Dao Net became even brighter.

It stretched across the starry sky.

The exotic fused body's efficiency in devouring slowed down instantly.

At this moment, Cheng Dao's hands sliced through the void and descended above the thousand-handed fleshball.

Ignoring the beast's devouring, he grabbed and pressed it firmly.

No matter how the exotic beast images gnawed, it remained unshakable.

Cheng Dao's figure was even more stable than the Great Dao.

The exotic fused body could gnaw through the Great Dao, but it was powerless against the stubborn stones of the Mountains and Seas!

Instantly, due to the backlash, tens of thousands of tentacles disintegrated while screaming.

In the blurry flesh on the ground, their original forms seemed to be contained.

But before they could even struggle, countless dense, small tentacles surged from the surface of the exotic fused body, dragging this flesh back into its interior.

Before long, the giant fleshball grew new tentacles.

"Wind come!"

In the starry sky, a giant hand appeared by Cheng Dao, continuing to press down on the exotic fused body.

And the other hand beckoned towards the void where the thousand-handed fleshball had appeared.

Buzz buzz...

As if a prelude to a hurricane, the scene of continuous heavy pounding returned.

However, this time, it was not about parting the seas and carving paths in the void.

But waves of Dao Annihilation ripples were being attracted!

Li Fan, who was watching, saw his pupils contract. This move was something Cheng Dao had never used before. He had never even mentioned it during their usual discussions about Dao. Clearly, the exotic fused body's devouring had angered him.

"Those ripples... are not an illusion. They are genuine Dao Annihilation!"

"Although it's not in the form of a grand tide descending all at once, but in the form of gentle breezes?!"

Li Fan's eyes revealed surprise, and he quickly discerned the mystery of Cheng Dao's divine ability.

"The essence of Dao Annihilation is the merging of Mountains and Seas."

"Mountains and Seas connecting, the surging waves crashing against the shore is the merging of Mountains and Seas. But the howling wind between Mountains and Seas is also..."

Li Fan watched as the countless tentacles of the exotic fused body evaporated in these ripples stirred by Mountains and Seas. Not even flesh fragments were left behind.

It was as if he saw the scene of wind blowing from the Mountains and Seas, cleansing the mortal world.

"The tide has not yet arrived, but the wind has already come."

"Only those who guard the hills and observe the seas can be the first to know and perceive."

While Li Fan was gaining enlightenment, Cheng Dao's guidance also reached his ears.

It must be said that the exotic fused body was indeed ferocious.

Under the blowing of this great wind from Mountains and Seas, the entire Shuoxing Sea might not be able to withstand it for long, but it stubbornly persisted with its extremely powerful regenerative ability, remaining undefeated.

Even though ripples of wind had cleared away billions of surface tentacles, countless more quickly emerged from its interior.

These tentacles were its devoured kin. At this moment, they also served as its multiple layers of defense.

Although it knew it was no match for the powerful cultivator who unleashed the wind of Mountains and Seas, its path of retreat was cut off. With nowhere to retreat, in desperation, the exotic fused body's ferocity was further ignited.

Billions of piercing shrieks sounded from the surface of the fleshball.

Tentacles transformed back into their original exotic beast forms.

They flew away from the fused body and scattered in all directions.

But the giant fleshball itself split open from the center with a huge gap.

Hidden within the deep gap was an orange-yellow eyeball.

Under its gaze, even the ripples of Mountains and Seas momentarily stilled.

Although the wind of Mountains and Seas soon returned to normal, it bought precious time for the scattered tentacles to escape.

If Li Fan were not present.

Thousands of exotic beasts, shortly after flying out.

All inexplicably disappeared.

As if some unknown hunter had been waiting for a long time.

The exotic fused body even sensed that the parts that had disappeared were suffering the same fate as those cleansed by the ripples of Mountains and Seas.

Their connection with itself was completely severed.

"What the hell!"

Chapter 1514: The Great Wind Rises in the Mountains and Seas

Unlike Cheng Dao's magnificent display of summoning the great wind from Mountains and Seas to fight the enemy.

Li Fan hid in the shadows and captured all the fleeing beastly projections from the battlefield using the methods of the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao.

Even the slightest energy fluctuation was not caused, silently and tracelessly.

The exotic fused body only saw a dark abyss in front of it, ruthlessly devouring all the scattering parts of its body.

The great wind from Mountains and Seas grew stronger and stronger, and the countless tentacles on its body surface eventually became increasingly sparse.

With a roar of pain, the exotic fused body was slowly eradicated from the inside out.

It was impossible to win a frontal confrontation, and escape was also impossible. The exotic fused body was truly in a desperate situation.

The orange-yellow eyeball within the spherical body suddenly revealed a fierce glint.

Moments later, with a deafening roar, the incomplete giant fleshball suddenly exploded.

Countless flesh and blood flew in the starry sky, and a blood-red torrent of visceral bloody aura emerged, like a physical entity, colliding head-on with the great wind from Mountains and Seas.

Originally, even with the final struggle of this exotic fused body, it could not contend with the mighty power derived from Mountains and Seas.

"Hmm?"

However, Cheng Dao, upon discovering the countless overlapping shadows within this blood mist, exclaimed in surprise. He then deliberately weakened the power of the great wind from Mountains and Seas.

The original body of the exotic fused body, hidden amidst these billions of shadows, temporarily disappeared from this starry sky.

Cheng Dao did not rush to pursue, but looked solemnly at the countless blood shadows, like ghosts, in front of him. These were actually all human forms, released by the exotic fused body!

From their all being naked and acting like beasts, their tragic encounters could be vaguely discerned. They did not even possess normal, sound minds, but were treated like livestock.

"Although I knew that the place they came from was an exotic world dominated by thirteen Dao Forms, a hell for our human race, and I was mentally prepared."

"But witnessing such a scene with my own eyes now, it is difficult to suppress my righteous anger." Cheng Dao's calm voice echoed in the starry sky.

For a moment, it even overshadowed the roaring wind from Mountains and Seas.

Li Fan, who was already quite familiar with Cheng Dao, could hear the hidden anger beneath his Senior Brother's calm tone.

In fact, even he himself felt indignant after seeing the scene of billions of human blood shadows released by the exotic fused body.

"They must have been slaughtered and absorbed by the exotic races before fleeing here."

"But for them, death might be a form of liberation."

Li Fan could not imagine what fate awaited him if he, as a human, had traveled to such a possibility. Perhaps even with the divine ability of Reality Rewriting and Endless Cycles, he would not have been able to escape and alter his destiny.

"This creature deserves to die!"

"Do you think you can escape our sight just by hiding in the starry sky?"

"Do you know this is just an isolated island? Without the means to cross the ocean, since you've come, there's no escape!"

Li Fan, channeling his limited anger to the best of his ability, spoke with utmost conviction.

His voice, like thunder, echoed through the Star Sea of Shuoxing and the high wall for a long time.

Li Fan waved his large sleeve, temporarily collecting the billions of human blood shadows.

While discerning if the exotic fused body was hidden among them, he also took the opportunity to give salvation to these unjustly deceased vengeful souls.

This was not the kind of salvation that involved complete annihilation and dissipation of the soul.

Instead, after inspection, the blood shadows were transformed into streams of light and sent into the Primordial Immortal Realm within the high wall.

There, after decades of cosmic cycles, these vengeful souls would be reborn.

While it could not be guaranteed that all of them would be reborn as humans, even if they were spirits of mountains and seas in the Primordial Immortal Realm, it would be millions of times better than their fate as humans in the exotic possibility.

"Thank you, Junior Brother,"

Seeing Li Fan's benevolent act, Cheng Dao spoke, expressing his gratitude to the billions of human blood shadows in front of him. While Li Fan was skilled in many areas, Cheng Dao, who had followed Shouqiu Gong for many years and performed the deeds of Shouqiu Wanghai, possessed numerous great divine abilities and received immense blessings.

However, his abilities primarily involved macroscopic, transcendent forces of Mountains and Seas. He was not very familiar with the techniques for dealing with mortal beings in the mortal world. Li Fan's current ability of reincarnation and rebirth was something Cheng Dao himself would need to study carefully to achieve.

However, despite his anger, Cheng Dao would not waste his time searching for a path to salvation for these human blood shadows.

Therefore, it was best to have Li Fan, his Junior Brother, handle it.

Li Fan worked very efficiently. In just a short time, the selection was complete. Human blood shadows were reincarnated. The remnants of the exotic fused body were directly refined into Dao Elixirs.

Soon, the starry sky, which had been made chaotic by the self-detonation of the fused body, returned to its original state.

"Senior Brother, where do you think that vermin went?" Li Fan asked with a smile.

As he spoke, Li Fan's attention was still focused on recalling the technique of the great wind from Mountains and Seas that Cheng Dao had just used.

Having personally entered Mountains and Seas before, he could better appreciate the ingenuity of this move.

"That vermin cannot possibly cross the protection of Master's phantom."

"Nor is it within my Dao Net..."

Cheng Dao retracted his divine ability, scanned the starry sky, his eyes filled with undisguised killing intent.

After searching, he could not find any trace of the exotic fused body.

"It's quite good at hiding," Cheng Dao snorted coldly.

"I have an idea. Senior Brother, please follow me." Li Fan chuckled and led the way.

Cheng Dao followed closely behind. In a short while, they arrived at the border of the Star Sea of Shuoxing.

Due to the Guangwu Star Sea's scheme of luring enemies into the trap, a portion of the original Star Sea of Shuoxing sky had been engulfed by Dao Annihilation.

What was once the central region of the Star Sea had now become the border.

And the place Li Fan had come to was the exact location where Di San Mo had disappeared before crossing possibilities alone.

After explaining the situation to Cheng Dao, Li Fan added, "It's dragging its family and its dependents, fleeing in desperation, only to end up with the utter annihilation of its forces. In the end, it could only rely on the methods here to escape."

"However, wanting to escape from you and me..."

Li Fan looked ahead and said coldly, "Vermin! Why don't you come out!"

The starry sky was calm for a moment.

After a few breaths, a figure suddenly appeared.

Unlike the previous bizarre thousand-handed fleshball, what appeared before Li Fan and Cheng Dao was a Dao form filled with majestic and sacred aura.

Dragon's body, Qilin's horns, Xuanwu's tail, God's eyes, Vermillion Bird's feathers...

It was as if a fusion of many Dao forms, spanning across the starry sky. Although its size was far from its peak state, its ancient and primordial aura was undiminished.

The near-perfect form seemed to encapsulate the true meaning of the Great Dao.

Even Cheng Dao, who was accustomed to Mountains and Seas, was momentarily lost in thought upon witnessing the true form of this thirteen Dao Form fusion.

"Calling me 'vermin' again and again..."

"How ridiculously laughable?"

"In my eyes, you are the vermin!"

"Today's defeat is merely a matter of being outmatched. But the Mountains and Seas are infinite, how can you know that my race will not have experts who can easily suppress you?"

"Hahahaha! I await that day!"

The voice of the thirteen Dao Form fusion, like that of a decaying old man. With its last hiding place discovered and facing a dead end, its voice was extremely calm, merely laughing to vent its inner despair and unwillingness.

Cheng Dao shook his head slightly, too lazy to bother with the thirteen Dao Form fusion in front of him.

Just as he was about to make a move to seal it and turn it into a Heavenly Pillar.

Suddenly, a ethereal and murderous voice came from afar, traveling from the horizon.

"Unfortunately, that is no longer the case."

As the voice arrived, the figure appeared.

The newcomer was dressed in purple robes and had a jade-like face. A lock of red hair casually fell to his waist, and a red mole on his brow resembled a third eye.

The moment this figure suddenly appeared, Li Fan's entire body instinctively bristled, as if encountering an unparalleled ferocious beast, his body trembling with warning.

However, to Li Fan's relief, his spiritual sense did not give a warning.

Clearly, the overwhelming killing intent emanating from the purple-robed figure was not directed at him.

It was directed at the thirteen Dao Form fusion.

Three breaths after the purple-robed figure appeared.

Rumble, rumble, rumble...

The Star Sea of Shuoxing and the high wall starry sky violently trembled.

Like a lone boat in a stormy sea, it swayed precariously.

With gusts of wind, Li Fan sensed that the stable Dao principles of the Star Sea of Shuoxing were being slowly disrupted.

Disregarding the Star Sea of Shuoxing for the moment, he summoned the Five Heavenly Emperors and Thirteen Heavenly Scars to maintain order.

Li Fan looked in the direction of Cheng Dao and the dark shadow.

The dark shadow, the Immortal from the coffin, had already revealed its true form.

It was not human.

But a giant rat!

Simply calling it a rat might not be accurate. Its swift pounces and claw swipes were astonishingly similar to human movements.

The fur on its body was even multicolored, as if adorned with brocade clothing.

It also wore a yellowish-brown straw hat on its head. However, the brim of the hat was bitten, leaving a small piece missing.

The expression on the rat's face was as vivid as a human's.

Greed, solemnity, urgency – all emotions were present.

"An Exotic Beast clan?"

Li Fan looked at the monstrous creature and couldn't help but think of Di San Mo's clan.

But he quickly dismissed this guess.

Not only did the Myriad Beasts Wheel show no reaction to this bizarre rat, but Cheng Dao, currently locked in battle, also sent a telepathic reminder.

"Junior Brother, be careful, this is a [Gluttonous Rat Immortal]!"

Then, Cheng Dao explained to Li Fan what a Gluttonous Rat Immortal was.

It was not a Nameless True Immortal who attained the Dao of [Gluttony], but a True Immortal that had mutated due to greedily and endlessly devouring the Great Dao.

Commonly, among the gathered Immortals of the Immortal Realm, Gluttonous Rat Immortals would not be born.

They generally only existed in possibilities where the apocalypse had arrived.

To maximize their chances of survival in the drifting Immortal Coffins, Immortals from coffins would often collect the remaining Great Dao to construct their Immortal Coffins.

And if they drifted in Mountains and Seas for too long, besides decaying and perishing, they would also be counter-attacked by the condensed Immortal Coffins of Great Dao.

The Nameless True Immortal realm was achieved by merging with the Dao.

Among the three thousand Great Daos, they were originally immiscible. Once one Dao was merged, no other Dao could be accommodated.

But in the special environment of drifting through Mountains and Seas within sealed Immortal Coffins, perhaps a miracle could occur – a Nameless True Immortal attaining multiple Daos.

The price, however...

Was the mutation of the Nameless True Immortal into various bizarre forms.

The Gluttonous Rat Immortal was the most typical example.

It still retained a certain level of sentience but was dominated by the instinctual desire to devour, wishing to consume everything useful around it.

"If Master encountered a fallen True Immortal from a coffin, he might help bury them. But these mutated True Immortals are simply killed without mercy!"

"Keeping them around is purely a menace!"

"When I suppress this fiend, I'll settle the score with the Guangwu Star Sea!" Cheng Dao's voice carried a hint of anger.

Li Fan watched the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's form flicker, its claws striking and causing the surrounding Great Daos to tremble. A strange feeling suddenly arose in his heart.

"The Guangwu Star Sea came for my method of subduing the Dao Saber Dao Sword. They definitely wouldn't entrust the task to a gluttonous Rat Immortal without reason..."

Just then, Li Fan noticed a flash of brilliance in the rat's eyes.

He quickly sent a telepathic message: "Senior Brother, be careful! This is not a Gluttonous Rat Immortal in the ordinary sense!"

"Perhaps someone has possessed it, integrating themselves into it!"

Cheng Dao heard this and his movements momentarily stiffened.

At this moment, a black light emerged from the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's front claws.

The light suddenly burst forth, enveloping Cheng Dao.

The Gluttonous Rat Immortal itself retreated far away, like a human, stroking its whiskers with its front paws, a look of satisfaction on its face.

"This black light..."

Li Fan sensed an aura very similar to Ink Slaughter from it.

"It seems that not only the [Broken Chessboard] Dao Field is researching the power of merging Mountains and Seas," Li Fan mused thoughtfully.

Although this black light was terrifying, Li Fan did not worry about Cheng Dao.

Having been by Shouqiu Gong's side and surviving by the side of Mountains and Seas for eons, how could he possibly perish so easily?

Chapter 1515: The Purple Dao Outsider Arrives

Unlike Cheng Dao's grand display of summoning the great wind from Mountains and Seas to repel the enemy, Li Fan hid in the shadows, capturing all the fleeing beastly projections from the battlefield using the methods of the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao. Chapter 1516: The Projection Pearl of the Dao Chronicle

A path that arises from nothingness, born from annihilation. It seems to be not a physical entity but an extremely special form of energy, forcefully carving a route in the void.

With a single step, the figure in purple vanished, appearing at the end of the path in the next instant.

Li Fan and Cheng Dao exchanged glances and followed closely. If they were alone, venturing into the alien starry sky teeming with True Immortals, they might have been cautious. But now, with such a powerful expert forging the way, what was there to fear?

Stepping onto this path that reached the heavens, a peculiar sensation unlike any before washed over them. It was almost indescribable, but if forced to put it into words, it was 'safety'. Born into the mortal world, constantly under the threat of the Great Dao Annihilation Tribulation, Li Fan himself might not have been particularly concerned. However, this fact undoubtedly instilled a primal sense of crisis in their bodies and souls. Years of conditioning had made them like startled birds, perpetually anxious. Even though the Great Dao Annihilation Tribulation had not yet descended, and even with the support of the Nameless True Immortal Heavenly Pillars, the fear in their hearts remained. After all, let alone a few Heavenly Pillars, even the Immortal Realm had been annihilated by Dao Annihilation. Who could guarantee how long these Heavenly Pillars would last?

But now, within this path carved by the figure in purple, this long-standing sense of dread finally vanished. "Even if Dao Annihilation eventually arrives, with this path, I will be safe,” Li Fan thought inexplicably. This was a blind confidence, but it wasn't just Li Fan who felt it. Looking at Cheng Dao, he felt the same. As long as they remained in the mortal world, the inescapable sense of crisis would gradually be smoothed away. Li Fan felt an unprecedented calm descend upon his heart. Countless distracting thoughts slowly settled in the depths of his mind, leaving only the purest, clearest intention.

"An incredible divine ability!" Li Fan exclaimed inwardly. "It's a pity this path is not permanent. It was created by the figure in purple to forge the way. As he departs, it is destined to disappear soon. Such a powerful force that can repel Dao Annihilation..."

"Putting aside the fact that simply observing such divine power up close is a great fortune in itself. Even the environment created by this path is something that beings in the mortal world strive for a lifetime without achieving." "If I could stay here forever, my comprehension of True and False Transformation would surely reach a higher level very quickly." As the path reached its end, Li Fan felt a hint of reluctance. He even entertained the thought of repeating this entire sequence in his next reincarnation, experiencing this brief period of time again.

Li Fan had indeed seriously considered it. "From my current understanding, even more than ten continuous reincarnations would not accumulate as much insight into True and False Transformation as this brief moment within the path." "Thus, it is indeed not a loss..." Li Fan was immersed in the safety and beauty brought by the path. Cheng Dao felt the same. Facing the Mountains and Seas alone, one might maintain a steadfast will. But after suddenly finding a safe haven that could shield them from wind and rain, and staying inside for a short while, their sharpness was gradually eroded.

Cheng Dao's weathered and resolute face softened slightly. Perhaps sensing the thoughts of the two juniors, the figure in purple's voice drifted over, breaking their reverie. "You can observe it, but you cannot learn from it." "This is my Dao, not yours. In the end, you must still forge your own unique path to be qualified to traverse the Mountains and Seas."

Li Fan and Cheng Dao were shaken. The faint greed that had arisen in their hearts instantly vanished. "Thank you for your guidance, senior," the two, having regained their senses, quickly thanked the figure in purple. They had realized that the absolute sense of safety while within the path had, in a short time, made them dependent on it. Naturally, they had developed desires for greed and monopolization. However, due to the profound calmness of their minds, these distracting thoughts had only accumulated in their hearts without manifesting. Now that the figure in purple had exposed them, they surfaced from their hearts like pricked bubbles.

"The Mountains and Seas are boundless; only I can be the boat." "To traverse the Mountains and Seas, one cannot do without a firm Dao heart." "You two, although your strength and character are above average in the mortal world. However..." "You are still lacking somewhat." "This is truly troublesome..." The figure in purple finally shook his head and muttered, then disappeared from their sight.

Li Fan and Cheng Dao exchanged stunned glances. After descending from the path, they looked back. Both were drenched in a cold sweat. Cheng Dao lamented, "Junior Brother, I finally understand why Master chose to interact with us as little as possible." "Such protection is indeed not a good thing." Li Fan nodded slightly. "If we had stayed any longer, I'm afraid I would have been unwilling to leave."

Ultimately, the two managed to break free from the temptation of the path that led to the heavens, and followed the figure in purple. The figure in purple moved at an incredibly high speed, already out of sight. However, there was no need to worry about losing them. The colossal turbulence, like mountains collapsing and seas roaring, that the figure in purple caused wherever he went, was far too conspicuous.

Within the void engulfed by Dao Annihilation, a path had appeared out of thin air. How could the Guangwu Star Sea have failed to notice such a phenomenon? Their reaction was swift. Judging by the imposing aura emanating from afar, it was likely that the top fighting forces of the entire Guangwu Star Sea had gathered. But before the figure in purple, they were simply insufficient. An expert who could traverse possibilities was certainly not something the True Immortals of the Guangwu Star Sea could contend with.

Li Fan and Cheng Dao followed the path of the figure in purple, progressing forward and finally experiencing what it meant to be truly unstoppable. Scattered all around were purple talismans, remnants of True Immortals who had been suppressed and pulverized. Li Fan secretly experimented, collecting these talismans. He discovered that the figure in purple had not killed them, but had merely temporarily imprisoned them. Li Fan could faintly sense the extremely terrified thoughts of the True Immortals within these talismans. After a moment of contemplation, Li Fan and Cheng Dao decided not to act rashly for the time being and continued to move swiftly towards the location of the figure in purple.

The closer they got, the more sealed True Immortals they encountered. It seemed that something of great importance was located there, something they had to guard with their lives, even if it meant obstructing the enemy to their death. But their resistance was ultimately futile. The gap in strength was too immense. Even a desperate struggle would not serve any purpose beyond mere resistance. However, as a civilization that had survived the great tribulation and proliferated to this day, and could even fish in the Dao Annihilation, they certainly had their own foundations.

"Senior, do not push too far!" A roar erupted from ahead, followed by a violent surge of energy that was no longer inferior to the commotion caused by the figure in purple. When Li Fan and Cheng Dao arrived at the scene, they found that a large area of absolute vacuum had formed around them. What was once likely a gathering place of significant structures had been completely vaporized. The figure in purple watched with great interest a sphere of light in his hand. Images were constantly shifting within the sphere, as if countless figures were leaping about. And before the figure in purple stood a middle-aged man, his clothes tattered and his face etched with despair.

"Dao Chronicle Projection. This item, you are not capable of creating. Did you fish it up from Dao Annihilation?" the figure in purple asked plainly, gently squeezing the light sphere in his hand. It was infinitely compressed, finally condensing into a brilliant point of light. Then, the figure in purple tossed this point of light towards Cheng Dao. As if concerned that Cheng Dao might not be able to withstand the pressure of the light point, he also attached the protective power, similar to the path to the heavens, around it, allowing Cheng Dao to observe the details within the point of light without being affected.

Cheng Dao first thanked the figure in purple again, then looked towards the light point in his hand. A moment later... Li Fan sensed that his senior brother's body was trembling uncontrollably. Cold sweat beaded on his forehead, as if he were under immense strain. After a few breaths, Cheng Dao forcibly looked away. However, he still appeared weak and pale, as if his vitality had been drained. Li Fan was immediately astonished. After all, Cheng Dao's true form was a spirit stone nurtured by the side of the Mountains and Seas, accompanying Shou Qiu Gong, watching the Mountains and Seas. Even the scenery of the Mountains and Seas, he could face calmly. What was in this light sphere that could cause Cheng Dao such distress?

With a look of concern, Li Fan inquired. However, Cheng Dao seemed unable to fully recover from the aftereffects of observing the light sphere. He simply handed the light sphere, named Dao Chronicle Projection, to Li Fan, gesturing for him to see for himself, then closed his eyes to rest, no longer speaking. Li Fan's curiosity intensified. With his divine sense on high alert, Li Fan looked into the light sphere. The point of light exploded in his hand, instantly engulfing the surroundings, including Li Fan's entire consciousness.

Endless light and shadow unfolded like flowing water, evolving one after another. From absolute nothingness where the Great Dao did not exist, to chaotic void where Dao was born and grew, to the genesis of worlds and the manifestation of life, to life comprehending its own Dao and the birth of the Immortal Realm. Countless years of time flashed by rapidly. Until finally, all things and Great Daos withered, ushering in the end. From the beginning to the end, all that occurred and all beings born during this period were condensed into this single point of light. Furthermore, it was not merely a simple record of projection. In the light and shadow, all the Great Daos, divine abilities, and spell fluctuations that had ever appeared in this possibility throughout its countless years, were all replicated and integrated into the light sphere.

The explosion of the light sphere to target the enemy meant facing a combined attack of countless heroes from countless years within the river of time of a possibility! Such a terrifying scene almost made Li Fan's palm drop the light sphere. The words "Revert All" were almost on the tip of his tongue. A drop of cold sweat trickled down his forehead as Li Fan withdrew from the Dao Chronicle Projection, his palm feeling as if it held an immeasurable weight. Li Fan almost felt as if he couldn't hold onto the light sphere. "Fortunately, Senior's path-forging allowed us to enter, otherwise, faced with this Dao Chronicle Projection, just the two of us would likely have met our doom."

Li Fan and Cheng Dao, who had already opened his eyes, exchanged a look. Both saw the shock in each other's eyes. They had never imagined that the Guangwu Star Sea possessed such a treasure. The Dao Saber and Dao Sword of before, compared to this, were like fireflies against the bright moon. "Fishing in Dao Annihilation is indeed a means of survival. To survive in the Mountains and Seas, besides those True Immortals who took a desperate gamble in the apocalyptic era, there were also those powerful beings who failed in their transcendence and attempted to traverse the Mountains and Seas, only to be swallowed by them." "These beings might have had their consciousness erased by the Mountains and Seas, but their physical bodies and the treasures they carried might have survived. This Dao Chronicle Projection likely came from such a source."

The figure in purple first removed all the Heavenly Pillars that formed the embankment, gathering all the True Immortals within them. Then, with a forceful press of his hands towards the center, a new Heavenly Pillar enveloped in purple energy was born. The figure in purple placed the Heavenly Pillar there. With its presence, the rumbling of Dao Annihilation caused by the missing Heavenly Pillar finally ceased. Li Fan noticed that even during the brief interval when the Heavenly Pillar was being replaced, although there were phenomena of Dao Annihilation descending, the commotion was even less than that previously triggered within the Shuoxing Star Sea - High Wall. Clearly, the figure in purple was a factor. Just by standing there, he already acted as countless Heavenly Pillars, resisting Dao Annihilation to a certain extent.

The tattered middle-aged man from the Guangwu Star Sea, looking at the Heavenly Pillar of All Immortals before him, was lost in a daze. Ten thousand years of records, overthrown in an instant. It nearly shattered his will. Facing the question of the figure in purple, he did not reply. However, after a moment of silence, the middle-aged man slowly regained his senses and said hoarsely, "Senior is correct. It was indeed by chance that we acquired the remains of a powerful being." "This was originally our fortune, but who would have thought..."

The figure in purple interrupted the middle-aged man, "This is your fortune. The Dao Chronicle Projection may be nothing to speak of, but the remains of that powerful being might have already given rise to new transcendent experts. It is a pity that you took the wrong path." "Learning from the body, one could comprehend the Dao of past powerful beings. But what have you done?" The middle-aged man's expression was somewhat dazed. After a long while, he whispered, "Returning it to Dao Annihilation, using it as a boat. Firstly, to seek other safe havens. Secondly, to gather similar drifting treasures..."

The figure in purple snorted coldly, reprimanding mercilessly, "Fools!" The middle-aged man sighed, "It is not that we were unwilling to comprehend. It is that we could not." "The remains were like mountains before our eyes, yet we were like those within a mountain, unable to see their true form." "After trying for many years, we still found it so. We had no choice but to abandon it and seek a new use." The middle-aged man thought that such an explanation would elicit sympathy from the figure in purple. Yet, the figure in purple merely nodded and said coldly, "Even more foolish. There is no cure for this."

The figure in purple gently pointed at the Guangwu Star Sea man. The man opened his mouth, wanting to say something more. A moment later, he exploded like a bubble, turning into myriad purple wisps of light. These were then swallowed by the surrounding starry sky. A powerful being at least at the Nameless True Immortal realm, thus perished, casually wiped out by the figure in purple. Li Fan and Cheng Dao, witnessing this, couldn't help but inwardly tremble. "If not for Shou Qiu Gong's sake, this figure in purple would certainly not have been so accommodating."

The figure in purple seemed to have done something insignificant and quickly dismissed the matter of the middle-aged man. Striding to the center of the original Heavenly Pillar embankment, he stared ahead. His gaze seemed to pierce through Mountains and Seas and the mortal world.

Chapter 1517: Legacy Boat

Outside the mortal world, it seemed as though something was also confronting the gaze of the figure in purple.

After a brief silence, ripples erupted!

It was uncannily similar to the majestic waves of Mountains and Seas that had previously caused the collapse of the Star Sea of Shuoxing, but the commotion was tens of times greater!

It was as if the figure in purple's utterly indifferent expression had enraged the unknown entity within Dao Annihilation. It was determined to stir up fierce storms and engulf the mortal world where the figure in purple resided.

The Guangwu Star Sea trembled precariously.

Even the Purple Qi Heavenly Pillar, formed by the unity of all Immortals, could hardly withstand this catastrophe. Li Fan suspected that if the figure in purple were not standing there at this moment, the remaining remnants of the Guangwu Star Sea, and even the entire Primordial possibility struggling for survival, would collapse under this immense power.

"What is that over there? Could it be the so-called remains of a powerful being that the Guangwu Star Sea fished from Dao Annihilation?" Li Fan exchanged a glance with Cheng Dao, seeing the uncertainty in each other's eyes.

Yet, faced with such a world-shattering spectacle, the figure in purple regarded it as nothing. He didn't know what he had discovered, but a hint of a joyful smile appeared at the corner of his mouth.

"You two juniors, watch carefully,"

After saying this to Li Fan and Cheng Dao, the figure in purple vanished instantly.

In the next moment, the turmoil in the starry sea subsided!

It wasn't that the culprit causing the disturbance had been apprehended, but rather that at the same time, even greater waves surged upwards. It was as if an absolute king had emerged, drawing all the minor ripples in the starry sea towards himself.

Li Fan scanned his surroundings. The starry sky was silent, and he couldn't find the figure in purple. The place where the waves converged was, in fact, beyond the Primordial possibility!

A thin line, like a path to the heavens, suddenly appeared overhead.

Through this rift, Li Fan, in a daze, seemed to see a magnificent scene of endless Mountains and Seas connected together.

Looking from afar, it was entirely different from the experience of crossing the Immortal Ascension Terrace and sneaking into the Infinite Sea.

In the Infinite Sea, each drop of seawater represented the immense pressure accumulated over countless epochs of time, making it impossible for Li Fan to truly experience the scenery of the Infinite Sea in detail. Even after gaining the protection of [True Illusion is False] and freely roaming, Li Fan only glimpsed endless fragments within the sea, not the Mountains and Seas themselves.

However, at this moment, through the line created by the figure in purple, Li Fan finally got to see the majestic view of Mountains and Seas as perceived by a Transcendent expert.

Even a mere glimpse left Li Fan stunned and lost in thought.

Even after countless reincarnations, possessing the ultimate treasure of [Revert All], and having personally entered the Infinite Sea, Li Fan, faced with the boundless landscape of Mountains and Seas, could not suppress a sense of insignificance.

"Is this the Infinite Sea and the Upper Mountains that transcend the mortal world?" Li Fan murmured to himself.

There was no question of comprehending anything. Li Fan's entire consciousness was deeply shocked by this indescribably magnificent sight. There was no room left for other thoughts.

Compared to Li Fan, Cheng Dao, however, exhibited a phenomenon. His entire body emitted a crystalline white light, and behind him, the phantom of a stubborn stone vaguely appeared. Cheng Dao looked up at the sky, as if returning to his days of watching the sea by the Mountains and Seas.

From this spirit stone by the Mountains and Seas, all sorts of profound and mystical fluctuations surged forth, seemingly resonating with the Mountains and Seas beyond the firmament.

Thus, Li Fan was awakened from his shock by these fluctuations.

After carefully savoring them, Li Fan felt a pang of dissatisfaction: "We both glimpsed a corner of the Mountains and Seas, yet I can't comprehend anything, while Cheng Dao continuously gains insights into the Dao. The gap between us..."

At this moment, Li Fan's mind had cleared, but his mind remained blank after gazing at the Mountains and Seas. The gap between him and the Mountains and Seas was simply too vast. With the body of an ant, even if one saw the Mountains and Seas, it would be as if one saw nothing.

If it were a lower-level mortal Dao, he would not be so.

"It seems that with my current cultivation, traversing the mortal world is not a problem. However, to cross the Mountains and Seas, there is still a long way to go."

"Fortunately, my Senior Brother is not stingy. He doesn't intend to hoard his insights for himself," Li Fan mused inwardly, observing the enlightenment fluctuations emanating from Cheng Dao.

This spirit stone beside the Mountains and Seas was now like a mirror, reflecting the scenery of Mountains and Seas that Li Fan could not perceive, allowing Li Fan to gain enlightenment through it.

After the line tore open the firmament, revealing the true form of the Mountains and Seas, the immense commotion from Dao Annihilation vanished.

While Li Fan was gaining enlightenment, he also attempted to search for the whereabouts of the figure in purple amidst the Mountains and Seas.

However, given the boundless nature of the Mountains and Seas, even a powerful expert like the figure in purple would be like an ant. It was difficult to find any trace.

"Let us two juniors watch carefully..."

"Watching what?"

"Is it just the Mountains and Seas?"

Li Fan had a premonition that it was definitely not just that.

But due to his limitations, he couldn't see what the figure in purple was referring to.

It was Cheng Dao, however, who seemed to have discovered something, and the enlightenment fluctuations emanating from him became even more intense.

"Junior Brother, focus your will here!"

The deep bond that Li Fan had painstakingly cultivated with Cheng Dao over this period proved its worth at this critical juncture.

Ultimately, unable to bear the thought of his Junior Brother missing this opportunity, Cheng Dao, while immersed in his enlightenment, still called out a reminder.

Li Fan was overjoyed and followed Cheng Dao's guidance.

In an instant, his vision seemed to penetrate the line in the firmament, leaping out of the mortal world and arriving in the Mountains and Seas.

He could vaguely see the blurry figure of the figure in purple standing tall.

Before the figure in purple was a flat sphere, with countless fine lines extending from its front and back, converging in the center.

A power akin to the path connecting the heavens enveloped the figure in purple and the flat sphere. These fine lines seemed to attempt to break free from the sphere, but were firmly sealed by the figure in purple.

It was vaguely discernible that the flat sphere had once been human-shaped, but it had now decayed and decomposed into threads of Dao.

"Remains of a Transcendent expert crossing Mountains and Seas..."

Li Fan was not concerned with the battle between these two.

What he was interested in was what gradually appeared within the remains after they were suppressed and decomposed by the figure in purple.

Approximately in the position of the original head, various fleeting images slowly became visible.

To Li Fan's astonishment, the light shadows hidden within the brain of this expert's remains were actually the imagery of Mountains and Seas!

Even though the body had decayed and the soul had dissipated, this imagery of Mountains and Seas remained intact.

"Perhaps this is the fundamental reason why the remains could drift in the Mountains and Seas," Li Fan realized with a sudden understanding.

But what followed, a scene Li Fan glimpsed within this miniature depiction of Mountains and Seas, made Li Fan's heart tremble once more.

The Mountains and Seas within the remains of the expert's brain seemed no different from the Mountains and Seas Li Fan was currently witnessing.

However, upon closer inspection, a lone sail could be seen, traversing between the Mountains and Seas!

Even though the boundless and ancient essence of the Mountains and Seas seemed to be fading the lone sail, it did not completely swallow it.

Li Fan instantly understood: "It is not that the imagery of Mountains and Seas preserved the remains' immortality. It is this lone sail in the Mountains and Seas!"

"This is..."

"The transcendent Dao of the expert in life?!" Li Fan stared intently at the lone sail in the Mountains and Seas. For some reason, a sense of familiarity inexplicably arose in his heart.

At the same time, [Revert All], which had been dormant for a long time, finally transmitted faint waves of intent once more, further confirming Li Fan's judgment.

"Eternal Relic?!" Li Fan's heart pounded violently.

More accurately, that lone sail traversing the Mountains and Seas, compared to the various eternal relics Li Fan had encountered before, might have been the same in fundamental nature.

However, it was undoubtedly far more powerful than what Li Fan had previously absorbed. Even if it ultimately failed to cross the Mountains and Seas, its ability to protect the remains and ensure their survival for tens of millions of years amidst the great tide of merging Mountains and Seas was already extraordinary.

In comparison, the residual thoughts of figures like Tian Yang and Su Bai seemed insignificant.

"But the essence is the same."

"Not merely a simple projection of the Great Dao, but a resonance of one's own will. This is the fundamental reliance for crossing the Mountains and Seas..."

"The Mountains and Seas are boundless; only I can be the boat!"

The words of the figure in purple reappeared in Li Fan's mind, precisely and fittingly. It was like a lightning strike that cleared the fog, illuminating the answer.

"If Tian Yang were fortunate enough to reach the realm of transcendence, his method of traversing would be a boat formed by [Never Inferior to Others]. If it were Su Bai, it would be a difficult crossing through the path of [Compassionate True Love]."

"In simple terms, these cultivators whose residual thoughts can condense into [Eternal Relics] after death have, in reality, already taken half a step towards their own Dao, thus possessing the seeds of transcendent experts! This is not about cultivation realm, but seems to be related to one's own character and will."

"However, to achieve transcendence, one's own path and cultivation realm are both indispensable!"

"If one's cultivation is insufficient, and one cannot build a boat, one can only sigh at the vastness of the ocean. And if the boat is formed but one's own strength is insufficient, rashly entering the Mountains and Seas will only lead to death."

Li Fan's heart trembled.

Indeed, this was a great fortuitous encounter.

Through the remains of a powerful being, the figure in purple had, for Cheng Dao and Li Fan, almost illuminated the path to transcendence.

Perhaps if Li Fan had relied solely on himself, attempting and eventually comprehending this mystery through continuous reincarnations, he could have achieved it. But the figure in purple's guidance undoubtedly saved him several reincarnations' worth of time!

"The Dao of crossing Mountains and Seas. No wonder even [Revert All] transmitted desires of yearning every time it encountered them."

"Is [Revert All] absorbing these to simulate and deduce methods to counter Mountains and Seas?" A bold thought arose in Li Fan's mind.

Seemingly sensing the presence of the figure in purple nearby, [Revert All], after transmitting faint fluctuations, quickly fell silent again, offering no response to Li Fan's conjecture.

Outside the mortal world, the figure in purple had already extracted all the lines outside the lone sail of the Mountains and Seas. However, he did not absorb them himself but tossed them into the Mountains and Seas.

Without the support of the transcendent relic, these lines, like ice entering water, were swallowed by the Mountains and Seas without even causing a ripple.

The figure in purple, who had maintained an air of transcendence since his appearance, faced the lone sail in the Mountains and Seas with an unusually solemn expression, mixed with a sincere admiration.

The slightly yellowed lone sail, as if sensing the figure in purple's intentions, responded with waves of seven-colored mystical light.

The figure in purple displayed his transcendent Dao technique once more amidst the Mountains and Seas. A fine line instantly took shape, spanning across the Mountains and Seas, heading towards an unknown destination.

The lone sail, enveloped in seven-colored light, sailed along this path.

The figure in purple watched the lone sail depart. When it completely disappeared from view, he retracted his transcendent Dao technique.

Maintaining a path within the vastness of Mountains and Seas was clearly a significant burden for the figure in purple. His flowing robes fluttered as if blown by the wind. It was only when the blood-red mole on his brow, like a luminous pearl, emitted waves of red light that the figure in purple calmed down.

After escorting the lone sail, the figure in purple did not return from the Mountains and Seas.

Before the line connecting the heavens closed, he transmitted a message from afar: "My task is complete. I have extended the path to crossing for three days for you. Manage it yourselves."

Then, as abruptly as he had appeared, he vanished without a trace.

As for the countless purple talismans of True Immortals scattered in the Guangwu Star Sea, he paid them no mind.

He left behind only Li Fan and Cheng Dao, who had not yet recovered from their shock, standing silently in the starry sky.

After a long while.

As the line outside the firmament gradually faded and the scenery of the Mountains and Seas disappeared, Cheng Dao reluctantly withdrew his gaze.

With the cessation of his enlightenment fluctuations, Li Fan's method of cleverly reflecting the insights also became ineffective.

"Senior Brother, where do you think the final destination of that lone sail of the Mountains and Seas is..." Li Fan, recalling the events that had just transpired, asked softly, "Could it be the Other Shore?"

Cheng Dao's expression was serious, and he remained silent for a long time.

However, he finally nodded: "It should be."

"That lone sail seems to be the true intent of crossing Mountains and Seas condensed by the remains of an expert. I just don't know why that senior in purple expended so much effort to guide this lone sail to the Other Shore."

Li Fan simply sighed: "I never imagined that merely subduing the Dao Saber and Dao Sword so casually would lead to so many subsequent events."

"Junior Brother, do not blame yourself. This is fate. If not for your casual action, how could we two have gained such great fortune?"

The fortune Cheng Dao spoke of not only referred to the path to transcendence pointed out by the figure in purple but also to the Guangwu Star Sea, which had been swept clean by the figure in purple.

Cheng Dao surveyed the vast ruins: "That purple Heavenly Pillar is not to be trifled with. As for the other purple talismans of True Immortals, collecting them is fine."

"However, we must act quickly. The three days mentioned by Senior Purple Qi might not be the same concept as the three days we understand."

It had to be said that Cheng Dao's intuition was quite accurate.

After only one day had passed, the crossing path connecting the Star Sea of Shuoxing and the Guangwu Star Sea began to fade and disappear.

Fortunately, Li Fan and the others had finished their plundering and did not linger, returning to the Star Sea of Shuoxing in advance.

Looking at the disappearing path and the darkness of the starry sky where Dao Annihilation reappeared, they both felt as if they had dreamt.

"Fortunately, we have the protection of our Master, otherwise, our fate would likely be no better than these inscribed talismans of True Immortals," Cheng Dao said with a sigh.

Li Fan heartily agreed, nodding in silence.

Next, the two spread out their spoils from this expedition, arranging them in the starry sky.

The fused entity of the thirteen exotic Dao Forms, and the inscriptions of True Immortals from the Guangwu Star Sea. A total of three hundred and seventy-five pieces.

A supreme treasure, the Dao Chronicle Projection, one piece.

As for the other scattered immortal treasures, they were not worth mentioning.

"With so many materials in hand, our current starry sky should be safe for the time being," Li Fan said first.

His gaze, however, remained fixed on the Dao Chronicle Projection bead.

Since the departure of the figure in purple, this treasure, originally compressed to an extreme point of light, was now showing signs of expanding outwards again.

Chapter 1518: All Beings Return to the Dao

Li Fan's prediction was correct. Amidst the black light domain, which should have only contained absolute silence, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal, while smugly self-satisfied, heard the sound of crashing waves and colliding mountains and seas suddenly break through the black domain. The sound echoed throughout the Great Desolate Immortal Realm. It evoked different responses from various parts of the Immortal Realm. The rustling of wind through mountains, the gurgling of streams, the sharp sound of wind and clouds converging, the loud cries of newly born life, the rumbling of collapsing mountains... These notes, representing life, movement, and change, resonated with the sound of Mountains and Seas in the sky. Like surging waves, they forcefully tore open the black domain.

"A trivial skill, daring to show off before me!" Cheng Dao let out a furious roar and rushed out of the black light.
