The moment he broke free, his form merged with the surrounding world, disappearing from sight. Sensing something amiss, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal let out a strange laugh, but did not panic. It shook its plump body, and thousands of small, multicolored hairs instantly fell from its patterned outer skin. As these hairs detached, they transformed into standing figures. In an instant, thousands of True Immortals appeared, protecting the Gluttonous Rat in the center.

"These figures are..." "Nameless True Immortals?" Li Fan saw clearly that each hair shed from the Gluttonous Rat Immortal represented a Great Dao. These Dao-transformed figures were essentially the same as Nameless True Immortals who had merged with their Dao! The Nameless True Immortals, who had greedily devoured Great Dao and mutated, were now spitting out the Great Dao they had already swallowed. Despite losing some of their Great Dao, the Gluttonous Rat not only did not weaken but its aura became even more unpredictable and alarming. Li Fan also noticed that the Gluttonous Rat's appearance had subtly changed. Its claws transformed into palms, its hunched body straightened, and its facial expression became more human-like.

A great wind arose in Mountains and Seas. With a roaring sound. It dispersed all the Dao-transformed figures guarding the Gluttonous Rat. Witnessing this scene, Li Fan seemed to see countless possibilities, worlds, and beings that had sunk and vanished in Mountains and Seas. Although Cheng Dao had confined his divine ability to a certain range, some of the wind, due to the fierce battle, escaped its original trajectory. Like invisible blades, they slashed through the Great Desolate Immortal Realm. A massive void rift appeared in their wake. Even with the continuous replenishment of Infinite Immortal power, it would be difficult to repair this scar in a short time. This indicated the destructive power at the center of the battle had reached an unimaginable level. Amidst the howling wind, figures danced like willow branches in the breeze. Though scattered, they stubbornly maintained their forms in the wind of Mountains and Seas.

And at this moment, strange, continuous sounds came from the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's mouth. It was both a piercing shriek of a rat in agony and the impassioned chanting of a poet. More hairs fell from the Gluttonous Rat Immortal. True Immortals, like dense hemp, drifted out. The Gluttonous Rat was completely stripped of its fur, becoming even more human-like. However, it still wore a layer of rat skin. The rapid chanting abruptly ceased, as if a knife had suddenly fallen, slicing through the skin. The Gluttonous Rat transformed into a human. Unlike the blurry outlines of the surrounding True Immortal Dao shadows, which lacked any specific appearance, At this moment, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal, though naked, was indistinguishable from a human.

"Two Fellow Daoists..." "Gluttonous Rat pays his respects~" A mixed voice, neither male nor female, emanated from the human-shaped Gluttonous Rat. It was merely a self-introduction, not expecting any response from Li Fan and Cheng Dao. Before the words were even finished, it extended its ten fingers, remotely controlling the surrounding fallen True Immortal projections. Like a puppeteer controlling puppets from behind the scenes, With the enhancement of the Gluttonous Rat Immortal, the faces of the billions of True Immortal projections faintly took on human features. And they no longer attacked merely on instinct but truly fought like reincarnated Nameless beings, unleashing their divine abilities and techniques to their utmost. Not only did they possess the Dao principles of the Five Elements, Loneliness, and Silence present in the [Primordial] possibility, but there were also Great Daos completely unknown to Li Fan.

Before the Gluttonous Rat transformed, the True Immortal Dao shadows were like a leaderless horde, each fighting their own battle. But with the control of the human-shaped Gluttonous Rat, their true strength was finally unleashed. The pressure on the Inheritor increased a hundredfold instantly. Li Fan seemed to see a high and mighty figure commanding an army and destroying enemies with a smile. "These Nameless beings once took orders from him in life." "So, the true identity of this Gluttonous Rat Immortal is..." "An existence similar to a ruling Immortal Emperor?" Li Fan's thoughts raced. After sensing the clue, he blurted out a probing question: "Your Majesty! Your subject died unjustly!"

This ghostly voice pierced through the roaring wind of Mountains and Seas, transcending the formations of countless Nameless beings, and reached the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's ears. The Gluttonous Rat Immortal, who was enjoying the control of the True Immortal Dao shadows, suddenly froze. Even though it quickly recovered, this slight change did not escape Li Fan's observation. "Senior Brother, don't panic!" "I'll help you!" With his conjecture confirmed, Li Fan let out a cold laugh. The Wuji Heavenly Rod led the way, followed closely by himself, charging directly towards the Gluttonous Rat Immortal. Sensing Li Fan's actions, the myriad True Immortal Dao shadows moved to block him. Most were blocked by the Wuji Heavenly Rod. Even if a small portion fell outside the coverage of the Primordial Supreme Dao, they were still unable to penetrate the dual defenses of Li Fan's Myriad Manifestations Dao Net and the Unmoving Body of Mountains and Seas.

Enduring the attacks of the True Immortal Dao shadows, Li Fan charged straight towards the Gluttonous Rat Immortal. He aimed to take the Immortal Emperor's head amidst the myriad troops! The Inheritor also understood Li Fan's intention and cooperated. Not only did the wind of Mountains and Seas roar louder, but above the army formed by the True Immortal Dao shadows, a giant figure hovering and looking down vaguely appeared. Just the gaze of watching Mountains and Seas annihilated countless True Immortal projections. The Gluttonous Rat Immortal, having spat out all the Great Daos it had devoured, while its combat power increased significantly, was undoubtedly in its most vulnerable state at this moment. Li Fan's movements were extremely swift. In a flash, he had already reached within three feet of the Gluttonous Rat Immortal.

This surprise attack was too fast. The Gluttonous Rat could not even retract its devoured Great Dao. Only a sparse layer of fur was restored to its body before Li Fan's attack arrived. The Wuji Heavenly Rod struck first, followed by the saber and sword! With nowhere to dodge, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's eyes flashed fiercely. Facing the combined assault of a rod, a saber, and a sword, it showed no fear. It opened its mouth, revealing menacing fangs, and ferociously bit towards the Wuji Heavenly Rod and the Dao Saber Dao Sword. It seemed intent on devouring these three deadly weapons aimed at its life! Truly worthy of a Gluttonous Rat of immeasurable greed!

The Gluttonous Rat's reaction was within Li Fan's expectations. With a loud laugh, the Wuji Heavenly Rod and the Dao Saber Dao Sword vanished from thin air. Replaced by several pills swirling with purple energy. Even though it clearly saw the change in that instant, its greedy nature prevented the Gluttonous Rat from retracting its fangs. It had devoured Immortals in the court, it had devoured entire worlds. What was there that it dared not swallow! As the myriad True Immortal projections, which had been released, were quickly recalled, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal finally reverted from its human form to its fierce beast appearance. After consuming the elixirs delivered to it by Li Fan in large quantities, it tried to search for Li Fan's figure again. However, Li Fan had already fled thousands of miles away, returning to a safe position, waiting for the medicine to take effect.

"Eating so many poisonous elixirs at once, you won't die from it!" However, the time required for the Gluttonous Rat Immortal to be poisoned was much longer than Li Fan had anticipated. It seemed that after all, it was a formidable character who had traversed Mountains and Seas within a coffin, possessing some resistance even to power close to Dao Annihilation. After the Inheritor and the Gluttonous Rat Immortal stalemated for half a day, abnormalities began to appear on the Gluttonous Rat's body. The originally multicolored fur began to gradually turn purple. And uncontrollably, it began to shed from its body. This was the phenomenon of Dao transformation caused by the poisonous elixir refined by Li Fan.

Initially, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal did not notice it, until the purple fine hairs scattered all over the sky. It finally panicked in realization. It let out a piercing shriek that tore through the clouds. The Gluttonous Rat Immortal could no longer spare the time to fight the Inheritor. It hurriedly collected the shedding hairs from its body. From the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's cry, Li Fan not only heard fear but also anxiety and reluctance. This was somewhat unexpected. But regardless of the past events between the Gluttonous Rat Immortal and its former subjects, it did not prevent Li Fan from seizing the opportunity to strike while it was vulnerable.

With a wave of his large sleeve, while snatching the Dao-transformed hairs from the Gluttonous Rat Immortal, Li Fan also connected with the poisonous elixir's power within the Gluttonous Rat Immortal, ready to tighten the Myriad Manifestations Dao Net at any moment. The more hairs fell, the faster its strength declined. The weaker it became, the harder it was to suppress the erupting poisonous elixir. With the manifestation of its decline, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's defeat was sealed. Finally, it was time to harvest. Li Fan would not show courtesy to the Inheritor.

"Life and death are as one, merging with the Dao to attain true integration. Free from the external world, my Elixir shall be formed." Li Fan chanted softly in his heart. The Myriad Manifestations Dao Net served as the elixir furnace, and the power of the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul as the elixir fire. He slowly refined this drifting Immortal from the Other Shore, originating from another possibility, into a Dao Elixir. The Gluttonous Rat struggled desperately, but the net tightened relentlessly. Ultimately, it was all in vain. At this moment, the Inheritor also revealed himself. He looked at Li Fan refining the elixir, pondered for a moment, and did not intervene.

The Gluttonous Rat Immortal, having lost all its hairs, reverted to its human form. But it stopped struggling. It merely watched Li Fan and the Inheritor in the distance. "The devourer is ultimately devoured!" "These words are indeed true!" "Fellow Daoists, do not follow in my footsteps!" "Hahaha..." With a mad laugh, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal was completely refined. It became a crystal-clear, seven-colored purple energy-filled, perfectly round elixir in Li Fan's palm. Undoubtedly, this was the most beautiful and most precious Dao Elixir Li Fan had refined since mastering the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao.

"Alas, it's a pity I can't consume it directly." Li Fan looked at the solemn Inheritor beside him, a thought stirring in his mind. "Senior Brother, take this." He said very solemnly, offering the Dao Elixir. "Alas? This is unnecessary." The Inheritor was certainly surprised by Li Fan's action. However, he immediately shook his head and refused. It wasn't that he saw through the mystery of the Dao Elixir. After all, Li Fan himself was unsure if there were any issues with the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao left by Sun Piaomiao, but Li Fan's cautious nature led him to hesitate. The reason the Inheritor refused Li Fan's kind offer was entirely because he adhered to the rules set by Shou Qiu Gong. No matter how good a treasure it was, he should not snatch it from his fellow disciples. The miraculousness of the current Dao Elixir was not enough to make the Inheritor break Shou Qiu Gong's rules.

"This battle to suppress this Rat Elixir was entirely thanks to Senior Brother confronting it head-on." "If not for you distracting the billion True Immortal Dao shadows, I absolutely would not have been able to get close to its true form so easily. To enjoy refining this Dao Elixir, Senior Brother is truly worthy." "Besides, after Senior Brother consumes this elixir, you can also tell me about the other possibilities' Great Dao that you comprehend. If I were to consume it, I wouldn't have the ability to explain it clearly to Senior Brother!"

Li Fan's reasoning was indeed sound. After a heartfelt speech, the Inheritor finally could not refuse the kind offer. He half-pushed, half-accepted, and swallowed the Rat Dao Elixir. "Senior Brother, how does it feel?" Li Fan asked tentatively after a long while. "Alas." "This Gluttonous Rat, and those myriad True Immortal projections, are actually just a group of pitiful people," the Inheritor sighed, shaking his head. Li Fan: "What does Senior Brother mean?"

"It's what I perceived from the countless images seen after consuming the Dao Elixir," the Inheritor said, waving his hand to present the scene to Li Fan. Initially, it was a peaceful, prosperous, and magnificent Immortal Realm. The Gluttonous Rat Immortal had served as the ruling Immortal Emperor for nearly two hundred million years. During his reign, all the Immortals of the Immortal Realm submitted, and the scene was one of prosperity. In fact, since the Gluttonous Rat Immortal took the throne, even the Three Sage Lords had ceased to interfere in the affairs of the Immortal Realm. The Immortals only knew of the Immortal Emperor, not the Three Sage Lords. Prosperity turned to decline, starting from the sudden arrival of the Dao Annihilation tribulation. Initially, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal was full of ambition. He firmly believed that he could lead the Immortals to conquer this mere Dao Annihilation tribulation. However, the Dao Annihilation would subside and then resurge, repeating itself. Although it could be suppressed in the short term, there seemed to be no hope of completely resolving it. Maintaining a calm facade, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's heart gradually filled with panic. He conceived the idea of secretly visiting the Three Sage Lords to seek answers. However, he was shocked to discover... The Three Sage Lords had disappeared. As if they had vanished from this world into thin air, making them impossible to contact. Although most of the Immortals in the Immortal Realm had largely forgotten the Three Sage Lords, the Three Sage Lords of the Immortal Realm still represented the sages in the hearts of all Immortals. Already facing tribulation, with people's hearts in turmoil. If they were to learn that the sages had disappeared, The Immortal Realm would likely descend into chaos before even perishing under the Dao Annihilation tribulation. After much deliberation, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal decided to conceal this news. To prevent the disappearance of the sages from being exposed, he even impersonated the Three Sage Lords single-handedly. Although the Gluttonous Rat Immortal, as an Immortal Emperor of hundreds of millions of years, possessed supreme strength far beyond that of ordinary Immortals, perhaps impersonating one Sage might not have been difficult. But impersonating all three without revealing any flaws... Was stretching his capabilities too thin.

Thus, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal resorted to all sorts of methods to quickly increase his strength. In his desperation, he thought of directly devouring True Immortals and stealing their comprehended Great Dao. The effect was remarkable. With his unparalleled cultivation, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal truly managed to merge multiple different Dao paths into one body.

Chapter 1519: The Long Road to Immortality

The initial merging of two Daos was the most arduous. The Gluttonous Rat Immortal originally cultivated the Great Dao of [Imperial Law]. The more subordinates who submitted and were loyal, the stronger the feedback he received. The accumulation of two hundred million years allowed his Great Dao of [Imperial Law] to reach its theoretical extreme. Under heaven, none did not submit. It was precisely by relying on the supreme Great Dao of [Imperial Law] that the Rat successfully merged and absorbed the second Great Dao alongside him, like a subordinate, with absolute crushing power. But if one could merge, then two. If two, then three. Under the guise of Immortal Emperor, he secretly summoned the Immortals and then devoured them one by one. At first, the cautious Gluttonous Rat Immortal would choose True Immortals with ordinary strength and low renown to start with. But later, as the myriad Daos merged, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal became somewhat reckless.

However, it must be said that the Gluttonous Rat Immortal truly lived up to his title of [Eternal Immortal Emperor]. Even though the greed for Dao gradually engulfed his mind, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal did not forget his original intention. To embody three Sages with one person, and save the collapsing empire. Under the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, the world on the verge of collapse, under his governance, actually continued for another hundred million years. It seemed he truly saw the hope of eternal existence. But all stories must eventually reach their end. After being delayed for hundreds of millions of years, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation seemed to have completely lost its patience for further stalemate. It mobilized its forces and concentrated its offensive.

One day, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal was horrified to discover that the pressure of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation facing the Immortal Realm had inexplicably doubled. The hundred million years of stable peace had caused the Immortals to lose their sensitivity to the crisis. By the time they reacted and wished to use Immortals to mend the heavens, it was already too late. The Gluttonous Rat Immortal could only watch helplessly as the terrifying tide of Dao Annihilation, with its unstoppable might, engulfed more than half of the Immortal Realm in an instant. True Immortals perished, innumerable. The survivors were completely terrified, their courage to resist the calamity utterly extinguished.

As the actual ruler of the Immortal Realm, witnessing his territory collapse in such a short period, the sense of failure was undoubtedly extremely strong. However, at that moment, these so-called "emotions" were no longer important. Survival was the only truly meaningful thing. But the Gluttonous Rat Immortal, also known as the [Eternal Immortal Emperor], discovered in despair that under the impending catastrophe, they had no escape. The Immortals gathered around him, begging for a way to survive. But the Gluttonous Rat Immortal looked at the already tattered Immortal Realm, and he himself had fallen into despair.

However, after all, he was someone who had ruled the Immortal Realm for a full three hundred million years. The Gluttonous Rat Immortal would not give up so easily. In desperation, a crazy idea emerged in his mind. Gather the strength of all Immortals to directly reach the transcendent Other Shore. In the possibility where the Gluttonous Rat Immortal resided, legends of the Other Shore and other possibilities also circulated. But they were extremely secret, the most confidential of the confidential. Even the Gluttonous Rat Immortal himself, when he was young, had only accidentally heard them from the Three Sages. Not to mention the birth of true transcendent experts.

With no one to emulate, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal could only explore on his own. But the most crucial point was, he had very little time left. Searching the remaining lands of the Immortal Realm, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal finally found a method that could barely traverse possibilities. Immortal Coffin Crossing! It was just unfortunate that among the surviving Immortals, he seemed to be the only one with sufficient strength to survive in the Immortal Coffin formed by the world, floating amidst the tide of Dao Annihilation. Others, even if they could barely enter the Immortal Coffin, would likely not last long before completely perishing. Not to mention reaching the Other Shore directly.

The Gluttonous Rat Immortal could certainly escape alone. But as the dignified Eternal Immortal Emperor, would he just watch his subordinates die tragically? The Gluttonous Rat Immortal was clearly not such a selfish person. Relying on his rich experience in secretly devouring and merging the Daos of the Immortals over the years, at the last moment, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal actually devised a brilliant method. To use [Imperial Law] to control the Dao and maintain the balance of all Daos. As long as he remained in a state of devouring or semi-devouring, the Immortals would not be truly absorbed by him. They would still possess their own independent Dao paths, cultivation bases, memories, emotions, and so on. After hiding in the Immortal Coffin and successfully drifting to the Other Shore, he could then release the Immortals and thus successfully escape this calamity.

After experimentally absorbing more than ten True Immortals, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal found this method feasible. The only drawback was that he himself was both leading the devouring of Dao and desperately trying to maintain the clear demarcation of Daos. This extremely contradictory practice would put him in ultimate torment. And it would increase proportionally with the number of ingested Dao paths and the time spent maintaining the balance of all Daos. There was a moment of hesitation in his heart, but amidst this hesitation, countless True Immortals perished. The Gluttonous Rat Immortal immediately made up his mind. The Immortal Realm was already in a precarious state, and the final tide of Dao Annihilation could erupt at any moment. There was simply no time to explain slowly to the surviving True Immortals. Even if he explained, they might not believe him. Holding this belief, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal resolutely began to devour the Immortals on a large scale.

Facing the Immortal Emperor's sudden cannibalistic behavior, the Immortals were horrified and terrified. But they were completely unable to resist. They could only curse and beg in despair and fear. Although the Eternal Immortal Emperor's actions were not hesitant in the slightest, the words and actions of the Immortals were deeply imprinted in his heart. "Rat! You are the biggest rat in the Immortal Realm!" "Your Majesty, spare my life!" "Even if you devour me, I will become a vengeful spirit, waiting for the day of your demise!" ... At first, he would still listen to those voices in his heart. As the number of devoured Immortals increased, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal instinctively became more indifferent. Later, he simply ignored them completely.

In the instant before the Immortal Realm was completely destroyed and the tide of Dao Annihilation swallowed all things. The Great Dao twisted and materialized, and an Immortal Coffin descended from the heavens. The Gluttonous Rat Immortal, with the surviving True Immortals, hid inside. Next came a period of extremely long years. So long that the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's memories became somewhat blurred. Inside the coffin was absolute darkness. Outside the Immortal Coffin was the world-destroying tide of Dao Annihilation. The Gluttonous Rat Emperor could clearly perceive the process of Dao Annihilation constantly eroding the Immortal Coffin. He could only pray in his heart that before the Immortal Coffin was completely corroded, he would reach the Other Shore.

But perhaps his luck ran out after being the ruler of an Immortal Realm for three hundred million years. After an unknown amount of time, let alone the Other Shore, he didn't even encounter a safe place. The Immortal Coffin drifted with the current, floating in the tide of Dao Annihilation. It seemed like there was never any hope. And the Gluttonous Rat Immortal had underestimated the difficulty of maintaining the merging of myriad Daos. Perhaps it could be maintained in the normal Immortal Realm environment. But within the Immortal Coffin surrounded by the tide of Dao Annihilation, maintaining balance became increasingly difficult. He did not want to devour the Immortals in his heart. But he could only watch helplessly as his body merged with his former subordinates. He himself seemed to have truly become the "Rat" cursed by millions of people. The last glimmer of light in his heart gradually extinguished. The Eternal Immortal Emperor fell into endless darkness...

After another unknown number of years, when the Immortal Coffin had completely rotted and could no longer withstand the tide of Dao Annihilation. With a great roar, the Gluttonous Rat Immortal, as if from another life, discovered that he had finally arrived in another starry sky. This starry sky, although filled with the lingering decay of Dao Annihilation, Was at least temporarily safe. ... Li Fan and Cheng Dao, two fellow disciples, looked at the unfolding scene before them, speechless for a long time. "If it were me, I wouldn't have done any better than this Eternal Immortal Emperor." "He did his best, but the general trend was hard to reverse," Li Fan sighed.

Cheng Dao also commented, "His plight is pitiable, and his actions can be forgiven. If he hadn't been so aggressive, perhaps his life wouldn't have been forfeit." Li Fan showed a look of shame, "I was reckless. I never expected this outwardly terrifying rat to have such a past." Cheng Dao waved his hand, "Junior Brother, there's no need to blame yourself. Most Gluttonous Rat Immortals are not good people. Don't change your perception because of this anomaly, the Eternal Immortal Emperor." "Senior Brother's teachings are correct."

Next, Cheng Dao fully explained the Dao paths he had comprehended from the Gluttonous Rat Dao Elixir to Li Fan, and even added his own insights into the Great Dao from time to time. The comprehension of this spirit stone from the side of the Mountains and Seas, disciple of Shou Qiu, was truly extraordinary. Li Fan even suspected that even if he had swallowed the Dao Elixir himself, the effect would not have been better. While listening to the scriptures and discussing the Dao, Li Fan also secretly observed Cheng Dao. It seemed that after swallowing a Dao Elixir, the other party showed no abnormalities. "However, we cannot draw conclusions so easily now. We still need to feed him a few more." "Guangwu Star Sea, Hmph..."

Ninety-nine days later, Cheng Dao finished bestowing his teachings. "Senior Brother, do you feel that the possibility where the Eternal Immortal Emperor resided seems much weaker in its Dao path than ours?" Li Fan asked with a frown after recalling everything, his tone somewhat uncertain. "It's not your illusion. It is indeed so," Cheng Dao nodded. "Why is that?" Cheng Dao narrowed his eyes, fell silent for a moment, and then slowly said, "Perhaps, in that possibility, an unprecedented figure has already emerged." "Hmm?" "This is also my guess, and it has not been confirmed by Master." Cheng Dao first stated a point, then continued, "Putting aside the Three Sages, in a certain possibility, there seems to be an upper limit to the number of powerful beings that can be born." "It's not just a matter of quantity, but a combination of quantity and cultivation realm, all jointly determining it." "Of course, when I say powerful beings, I mean transcendent experts who can jump out of their own possibilities." Cheng Dao used his finger as a pen to draw a circle in front of Li Fan.

"It's like a water pool of a fixed size. Every time a powerful being is born, a certain area of this pool is marked out. Once the pool is completely occupied, any remaining individuals, even with heaven-defying talent, will be unable to reach the transcendent realm." Li Fan stared intently at the constantly divided circle in front of him, showing a thoughtful expression. "Senior Brother, in the world where the Eternal Immortal Emperor resided, the Three Sages inexplicably disappeared. Could it be that this is because the potential there has been exhausted, and no more transcendent experts will be born?" Cheng Dao looked at Li Fan with a half-smile, but did not answer.

Seeing this, Li Fan's heart already had an answer. He continued to examine the small circle in front of him, and with a wave of his hand, he redrew the hundreds of divided areas. "In that world, let alone powerful beings like Master, even transcendent realms are very few." "If that's the case, how strong was the powerful being born before?" "It almost exhausted the potential of an entire possibility?" Li Fan temporarily used [Potential] to refer to the small circle in front of him. "Could it be that their strength is even above Master's?" Li Fan couldn't help but gasp. Cheng Dao, however, was very calm, "In the past, when Master resolved the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation and saved the Immortal Realm from dire straits, facing the admiration of the Immortal Emperors and all Immortals, Master remained very humble." "He old man never considered himself a powerful being in the Mountains and Seas." "In his own words, he was merely [Shou Qiu Immortal Sheng De]."

Upon hearing this, Li Fan immediately became solemn, nodding in agreement. "Master is not only a master due to his strength, but also for his breadth of mind and character. Even if, one day, Senior Brother's strength surpasses his, I believe Senior Brother will still respect him as Master." "That is natural!" Cheng Dao did not deny it. "The Mountains and Seas are truly filled with powerful individuals." Li Fan's gaze returned to the small circle in front of him, looking at the circle within a circle that almost occupied the entire area, and lost himself in thought. "I truly wonder what the legendary Other Shore is like, with so many unimaginable powerhouses gathered together."

Cheng Dao smiled, "Junior Brother, do not worry. With the talent of us fellow disciples, reaching the Other Shore one day is a certainty." Li Fan laughed heartily, "Then let me thank Senior Brother in advance for your auspicious words." "Let's put the Other Shore aside for now. If you wish to see visitors from other possibilities, you can do so now," Cheng Dao suddenly spoke after a moment of silence. "Senior Brother is referring to the Guangwu Star Sea?" "Correct." Cheng Dao then displayed a completely new image in front of Li Fan. A total of nine Heavenly Pillars, arranged in a circle.

In the center enclosed by the Heavenly Pillars was absolute darkness. Li Fan sensed a familiar aura of Dao Annihilation from it. And outside the nine Heavenly Pillars, densely packed from sparse to dense. Were at least a hundred supporting Heavenly Pillars! Although not every Heavenly Pillar might have sealed a Nameless True Immortal within. Nevertheless, the grandeur of this pillar construction could still be felt. Unlike Li Fan's approach of simply using Heavenly Pillars to support the collapsing heavens, these Heavenly Pillars were not of equal specification. They progressed from the inside out, from weak to strong. It was as if a staircase had been formed. The central nine Heavenly Pillars were the weakest. Because they could attract Dao Annihilation to this place. And the surrounding hundred densely packed Heavenly Pillars formed a solid defense, preventing this attracted Dao Annihilation from spreading.

Li Fan looked at the area enclosed by the nine Heavenly Pillars, like a "water reservoir". He suddenly realized, "Is that how the Guangwu Star Sea salvages creations from other possibilities?" "It should be. It is indeed quite ingenious." "Besides being ingenious, the ability to construct these hundred Heavenly Pillars shows that the Guangwu Star Sea's strength is absolutely not to be underestimated. Before, I had underestimated them." Cheng Dao praised.

Chapter 1520: Obtaining the Fortune of Longevity

Cheng Dao closed his eyes, remaining silent, while Li Fan's spirit was extremely tense. He closely observed his surroundings. If anything was amiss, he would immediately activate [True Revelation]. Although Shou Qiu Gong was humble and never considered himself a powerful being in the Mountains and Seas, Li Fan would not let himself be blinded by pride. If his disguise as a disciple of Shou Qiu Gong and his deception were exposed, let alone Shou Qiu Gong, Cheng Dao would likely never forgive him. The connection between the mortal world and the Mountains and Seas seemed extremely difficult. Cheng Dao closed his eyes for a full three days before finally completing the process and standing up.

"I have already sent a message, roughly explaining the situation to Master. I just don't know when he will have the time to see it," Cheng Dao said with some regret. Communicating with the Mountains and Seas must have been a considerable burden for Cheng Dao. His already aged appearance now seemed even more frail and on the verge of decay and annihilation. "Senior Brother, please rest," Li Fan said repeatedly. Cheng Dao did not force himself and sat cross-legged in the void. It took him more than a month to recover.

Li Fan was somewhat surprised, "Is it really that difficult to contact Master?" "Naturally," Cheng Dao said with a serious expression, "The space between Mountains and Seas is not a place ordinary mortal beings can tread. I am only able to barely maintain myself due to my special origins. Otherwise..." "Let alone being able to withstand the pressure from Mountains and Seas, even if one could persist, one would face the aura of Dao Annihilation, which is countless times stronger than in the mortal world, at all times. It's like a mortal falling into water, their mind filled with suffocation and drowning. Perhaps they would go mad before being truly devoured by Dao Annihilation."

Cheng Dao sighed long and hard, "Since ancient times, the Mountains and Seas have not been a place that mortal beings can easily tread. If not for the meritorious deeds of Sage Lords Lian Shan and Gui Hai in their creation, we would not even be able to gaze from afar." Li Fan knew the terror of the Mountains and Seas. He had personally entered the Infinite Sea, and every drop of seawater seemed to possess the weight to completely crush his divine soul. However, the difference was that Li Fan possessed the treasure of [Reality Rewriting]. Under the protection of [Illusion is True], the current Li Fan could now traverse Mountains and Seas without hindrance for a certain period.

"What does it feel like to wander in the Mountains and Seas?" Li Fan, pretending to have never seen it before and looking very yearning, asked Cheng Dao for advice. Cheng Dao did not hide anything and elaborated on his feelings as his consciousness traveled through the Mountains and Seas. Comparing Li Fan's own experiences, he felt even more deeply the power of [Reality Rewriting]. For someone like Cheng Dao, traveling in the Mountains and Seas was extremely difficult, walking on thin ice as if treading on eggs. With the slightest carelessness, there was a risk of perishing. Moreover, according to himself, this was under the premise of having the protection of Shou Qiu Gong's imprint. Without Shou Qiu Gong's guidance, with Cheng Dao's current strength, he could not travel far.

From their casual conversation, Li Fan also confirmed that Cheng Dao had not mentioned him to Shou Qiu Gong during this communication. After all, every extra moment spent he faced immense pressure. He could only convey urgent matters. Although Cheng Dao said this, Li Fan did not fully believe him and remained vigilant at all times, preventing Shou Qiu Gong from suddenly appearing. Since his Master had already been informed, Cheng Dao was unwilling to handle matters arbitrarily and could only wait for his Master's instructions. And based on previous experience, Shou Qiu Gong's response time was erratic and had no fixed pattern.

However, the passage from the high wall to the outer starry sky was now completely sealed due to Dao Annihilation. Even if Li Fan and the others wanted to take revenge on the Guangwu Star Sea, they were helpless for the time being. They could only wait patiently. The Gluttonous Rat Immortal's merging of Daos had also provided considerable enlightenment to Cheng Dao. In Li Fan's perception, the Dao Net attached to the high wall not only became more solid but also sprouted many new Dao strings. Some of these were even Dao principles that no longer existed in the original possibility. They were all derived from Cheng Dao's own enlightenment and evolution. Although they could not support Dao Annihilation, they served as auxiliary components to the Star Sea Dao Net, playing a supporting role.

Cheng Dao gradually immersed himself in his own contemplation, losing track of time. Meanwhile, during this period, Li Fan was pondering the method of fishing for Dao Annihilation that the Guangwu Star Sea used. The unknown existence hidden in Dao Annihilation had not yet left. Li Fan naturally would not court death by testing it within the high wall. Li Fan's main body appeared to be meditating in the Primordial Immortal Realm. In reality, his consciousness had entered the [Endless Cycle]. During this period of time when Li Fan was largely uninvolved, the time loop continued to play out within the Endless Cycle. The ending of the Hungry Immortal destroying the world had been repeated countless times. The True Celestial Venerable, whose spiritual essence had been completely stripped away, now possessed no cultivation talent and had even gone mad. Regardless of whether this outsider existed or not, the Endless Cycle still evolved according to the passage of time Li Fan had experienced before.

This time, Li Fan's consciousness entered it, not to toy with the True Celestial Venerable again, but to study the fishing technique of the Guangwu Star Sea using this time flow. "First, I need to verify whether the Endless Cycle created by Reality Rewriting constitutes a complete possibility..." As Li Fan thought this, his consciousness instantly spanned the Utmost Darkness Star Sea and arrived at the location of the high wall. Familiar with the path, he entered the interior of the experimental field space. As expected, he still saw the five projections left by Shou Qiu Gong within. "..." Li Fan remained silent. After leaving the high wall, he explored the still intact Star Sea of Shuoxing. The Dao Net, the Immortal Hunters, Cheng Dao. All existed within this possibility.

Li Fan had not carefully considered the function of the Endless Cycle before. He had not thought much of this time flow created by Reality Rewriting. It wasn't until he came into contact with many Nameless beings after emerging from the high wall and understood the existence of the Three Sage Lords and even transcendent beings that Li Fan finally understood how incredible it truly was. He also vaguely understood that his [Reality Rewriting] was qualitatively different from the time reversal. "In reality, it is essentially the same as the [Primordial] possibility I experience every time I activate Reality Rewriting. It's just that a segment of time has been intercepted. And..." Li Fan tried to enter the Infinite Sea within this Endless Cycle. But as expected, he failed.

"The mortal world exists by relying on Mountains and Seas." "And this Endless Cycle was created out of nothing by Reality Rewriting, only depending on Reality Rewriting. It cannot connect with Mountains and Seas. It is like a locked room. In a sense, it is absolutely safe for me." "But inversely inferring..." "Every time I activate Reality Rewriting in reality, I am resetting Mountains and Seas." Previously, Li Fan had judged based on the lifespan of the mortal world in his Reality Rewriting panel, and concluded that the entire Mountains and Seas would be reset after activating Reality Rewriting. But now, Li Fan had doubts again. Because after truly seeing the power of Mountains and Seas and Reality Rewriting's performance when facing Mountains and Seas, Li Fan felt that Reality Rewriting might not be superior to Mountains and Seas. It was more likely on the same level. This could be inferred from the fact that the duration of [Illusion is True] deceiving Mountains and Seas was very short.

"Of course, it is also possible that my body cannot withstand deceiving Mountains and Seas for a long time. Prolonged integration might bring unknown side effects. Reality Rewriting, to protect me, intentionally set this duration and cooldown time." Li Fan shook his head slightly. With his current strength, he was still too far from comprehending the true meaning of Mountains and Seas and Reality Rewriting. Regardless, as long as it could be used by him, it was fine. Within this Endless Cycle, Li Fan could be said to have no natural enemies. He did not need to worry about Mountains and Seas, and coupled with the experience gained in this life in the real world, it did not take him much effort to recreate the Primordial Immortal Realm within the high wall and erect numerous Heavenly Pillars.

"It can be said that this is a simulation within a simulation." "Even the insights into the Great Dao that I absorb here are truly effective." Li Fan slowly caressed the Dao principles flowing from the Hungry Immortal Heavenly Pillar, feeling it was incredibly miraculous. Although the Hungry Immortal was temporarily sealed, the starting and ending points of this time flow had long been set. In a short period, she would return to the Immortal Ruins, remembering nothing. Thinking of this, Li Fan ignored the Hungry Immortal for the time being. He only looked at the Heavenly Pillars standing upright in the field.

"Because it is not truly connected to the Mountains and Infinite Sea above, the tide of Dao Annihilation here is also a simulation created by Reality Rewriting." "But True dissolves into False, and False transforms into True. With Reality Rewriting's ability, False is almost indistinguishable from True. It is enough for me to experiment. If I can successfully build it within this Endless Cycle, I can replicate it in reality." "Moreover, I can also freely adjust and control the flow of time here..." The entire possibility of the Endless Cycle was equivalent to a playground built solely for Li Fan. The one-to-one replica of the real world eliminated his worries. He began to diligently study the engineering of the Heavenly Pillar’s seawall and fishing for Dao Annihilation. Even though it was just a fleeting glimpse in the Gluttonous Rat Immortal's memory, the principle was not complicated. And for Li Fan, it was easy to reduce the Heavenly Pillars to varying heights using the methods of the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao. It only took more than ten cycles of the Endless Cycle for Li Fan to successfully create this marvel for the first time.

With a flip of his mind, Li Fan temporarily withdrew the power of Shou Qiu Gong's projection within the high wall. As the supporting force suddenly disappeared, countless dark clouds began to appear in the sky near the central low Heavenly Pillars. Sounds like mountains and seas roaring continuously, growing louder and louder. Li Fan subconsciously flashed away from the area. He looked solemnly at the dark abyss vortex in front of him. After observing for a long time, he could not discern the difference between this "false" Dao Annihilation and the real Dao Annihilation connected to Mountains and Seas. "It seems my Dao of [True Illusion is False] still has a long way to go."

Li Fan calmed his mind and refocused his attention on the vortex of Dao Annihilation. Since it was not connected to Mountains and Seas, no foreign objects would be attracted or washed ashore. However, from the commotion caused by the descent of Dao Annihilation, Li Fan confirmed that this initial attempt had already succeeded. The only thing he could not achieve at the moment was to restore the Heavenly Pillars, as the Guangwu Star Sea did when they successfully lured and trapped beings from Dao Annihilation. The consequence was that once this project was initiated, it meant that the catastrophe of Dao Annihilation's destruction was not far away. "Chipping away is simple. But to restore what was chipped away, and to have it fully restored in a short time..." In Li Fan's mind, he recalled the bizarre scene of Nameless True Immortals' faces appearing in each Heavenly Pillar when the Guangwu Star Sea fished for the tide of Dao Annihilation. "Without their cooperation, it probably wouldn't be possible."

Li Fan touched his chin and looked at the Hungry Immortal sealed within the Heavenly Pillar again. In this Endless Cycle, the Hungry Immortal was almost identical to the one Li Fan knew from the original possibility. After witnessing Li Fan's heaven-defying methods and the tragic fate of his fellow Immortals who were even chopped off as Heavenly Pillars, The Hungry Immortal wisely and decisively chose to cooperate. "Since I can strip away all your Dao comprehension using the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao, you can naturally use the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao to reclaim what you have lost." "Life and death are as one, merging with the Dao to attain true integration. Free from the external world, my Elixir shall be formed. This is the art of creating great elixirs in the world. I will teach it to you..." Li Fan did not hesitate and passed on the entire supreme secret method. Initially, the Hungry Immortal was somewhat fearful, but as her understanding of the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao deepened, her entire mind was gradually captivated. The Hungry Immortal's comprehension could only be described as mediocre. Li Fan was almost losing patience waiting for her to barely grasp this exquisite refining method.

However, Li Fan then realized that although the Hungry Immortal started slowly, in the actual application process, she was even more proficient than Li Fan. After careful observation, Li Fan saw some clues: "This Dao of Hunger seems to be innately compatible with the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao. The Dao Elixirs I refine need to be consumed by others to be converted for absolute safety." "But the Hungry Immortal has no such concerns and could swallow them directly without any scruples. Although she is imprisoned and has no need to worry about any hidden schemes of the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao, it also partly explains the uniqueness of the Dao of Hunger, this external Dao. After all, it is a Dao path that took root and reborn after arriving in another possibility..." Thus, although Li Fan did not know how the Guangwu Star Sea achieved the conversion of Heavenly Pillar heights, Li Fan, through his own learning, reached the desired effect after some effort. Furthermore, Li Fan modified the Alchemy King's Scripture of the Dao based on the feedback from the Hungry Immortal. Unnecessary parts were removed. The method only needed to cooperate with the change in the Heavenly Pillars.

The objective had been achieved. In total, it had only taken Li Fan more than twenty cycles within the Endless Cycle. And in the real world, only a mere hour and a quarter had passed! This was the terrifying power of Reality Rewriting. Li Fan looked at the Hungry Immortal, who had gloriously mastered the technique and was happily admiring herself, and her expression of utter disbelief as the cycle restarted. Li Fan couldn't help but think of a sentence that Shou Qiu Gong had once said to Cheng Dao. "Irrelevant to the final outcome." "Just as the beginning and end of the Endless Cycle are predetermined. Perhaps everything in the mortal world is also already decided." "No matter how much sentient beings struggle, the outcome will remain unchanged." Li Fan pondered, lost in thought for a moment.

Chapter 1521: The Body is One with the Mountains and Seas

Although the feeling of being watched from behind had disappeared, a chill still inexplicably ran down his spine from time to time.

“Mastering the Great Dao of the Mountains and Seas level doesn't have much to do with actual combat power. For example, even though I hold the supreme treasure [Revert All], before I fully comprehend the Transformation of True and False, my strength is not even as good as a Transcendent True Immortal.”

“Shou Qiu Gong holds the Dao of Longevity, but he hasn’t reached a level comparable to the Mountains and Seas. Judging from the attitude Shou Qiu Gong implicitly revealed in his words, their strengths should be roughly equivalent…” Li Fan pondered, looking at the Shuoxing Sea - High Wall Starry Sky, which was vastly different from a hundred years ago. He ultimately decided against taking risks.

“After further studying and experimenting with the Great Dao of Longevity in this life, I can then activate Revert All.” “I have gained too much in this life, and I am already vaguely touching upon the bottleneck. The specific path forward needs careful planning.” Relying on the benefits of Revert All, Li Fan had already reached the end of the Great Dao of Longevity. However, in the next life, Li Fan did not intend to inherit the cultivation base of this life. Anchoring to one year later, he didn’t know where Shou Qiu Gong was, or if he was within the Mountains and Seas world. If Shou Qiu Gong detected Li Fan, this sudden arrival on the path of Longevity, he might be in danger. Li Fan, whose Revert All was still on cooldown, would be like a turtle in a jar.

“The cultivation connection created by Revert All out of thin air is naturally undetectable by Nameless Immortals, Great Magi, and the like. But Shou Qiu Gong, who also masters the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, it’s hard to say.” “No need to take this risk.” “Anyway, the fundamental improvement in strength in this life is mostly reflected in the comprehension of the Great Dao. Even if I return to the Half-Immortal starting point, I can quickly recover my combat power.” Even though he had decided not to inherit his cultivation, Li Fan still wanted to comprehend the Great Dao of Longevity in the remaining time. He returned to the starting point of comprehending [Longevity], retraced his steps, and savored it carefully. This was because Li Fan was paving the way for the next life.

By activating Revert All and returning to one year later, if he chose not to inherit his cultivation, the connection between Li Fan and the Great Dao of Longevity would be severed. But Li Fan might be able to forge his own path of Longevity using the imprint left in this life. It wasn’t Shou Qiu Gong’s path of Mountains and Seas, and Li Fan had no intention of aiming for immediate transcendence. As long as he could touch upon some aspect of Longevity, it would be enough. “Shou Qiu Gong’s path of Longevity is sufficient to ignore the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. As for my path of Longevity, I only seek to cross the Mountains and Seas.” “Of course, this is just the first step I have taken. In the future, I might be able to integrate the Transformation of True and False.”

After learning about the mysterious connection between Mountains, Seas, Stars, Mountains and Seas, Longevity, and Revert All, Li Fan had once imagined what would happen if he possessed all these divine abilities. “Ascending to the True Immortal realm, endowed with the power of Mountains and Seas. Comprehending the Transformation of True and False, wielding the supreme power of Revert All. If, simultaneously, I also tread the path of Longevity...” In a certain sense, the current Li Fan was already a combination of the three. However, each of them was significantly lacking. He was still at the Half-Immortal realm, connecting to the Mountains and Seas solely through his clone. The Transformation of True and False was only superficially understood. The Great Dao of Longevity was merely a fleeting glimpse, lacking true understanding.

But even so, Li Fan could still clearly perceive certain indescribable changes occurring within himself. The most concrete example was the Dao Chronicle Projection Orb. Before comprehending the Great Dao of Longevity, even with the comprehension of countless beings in the vast starry sea, deciphering it was not difficult, but it definitely required some effort. But now… Upon seeing it, he understood it. It was as if he had seen this possibility’s countless divine abilities countless times before and practiced them countless times. Now, it was merely a return to the past, requiring only recollection, not revisiting. Furthermore, this process of his body actively integrating with the Great Daos was becoming increasingly rapid. To the point where later, he no longer needed the help of the starry sea beings to comprehend. The Dao Chronicle Projection Orb, like countless intertwined fine threads, Li Fan could see the trajectory of each thread and the specific situation with just a glance. Even unraveling it like a mirror reflecting reality was a common occurrence. What is talent? This is it. It had even begun to make Li Fan feel a little frightened. He wasn't overjoyed by these changes in his body, only feeling as if he were gradually being swallowed by the Mountains and Seas.

While Cheng Dao was not paying attention, Li Fan went to the edge of the Star Sea and drew in some Dao Annihilation energy to test. Although he hadn't truly entered it, standing near the tide of Dao Annihilation, the fatal sense of crisis that Li Fan had felt in the past had vanished. If in the past, standing at the edge of a ten-thousand-zhang abyss meant falling and being shattered into pieces with the slightest mistake, now it was like standing at the edge of an endless lake. Even if he accidentally fell in, he could paddle and barely return to shore. As long as he didn't court death by venturing into the center of the lake, his life would not be in danger. “Even, as time passes, my swimming skills are getting better and better.” “Even if I do nothing, as long as I live like this, one day, I will be able to cross the Mountains and Seas with my body as the boat.”

If an ordinary person received such a great fortune, they would have long rejoiced. But Li Fan felt only endless unease. The most bizarre thing was that Revert All seemed unaware of the changes occurring in Li Fan’s body. It even seemed to welcome these changes, remaining silent. It only once showed a slight difference, as if it wanted to speak but stopped. This made Li Fan feel even more uneasy. After carefully considering Revert All’s intentions, Li Fan realized that perhaps even Revert All hadn’t witnessed the myriad changes arising from the fusion of these three elements. Therefore, it was observing with curiosity.

As time passed, Li Fan’s feeling of being swallowed grew stronger. Illusions began to appear in his mind without reason. Li Fan was certain that these were definitely not from his own memories. They seemed to be various events that had occurred in the Mountains and Seas world. Externally, Li Fan's body began to assimilate with the surrounding world. The most obvious manifestation was that Cheng Dao, intentionally or unintentionally, began to forget Li Fan. Not long ago, he still frequently sought Li Fan to discuss insights into the Great Dao of Longevity. But gradually, he seemed to have forgotten that he even had such a junior brother. Whenever he instinctively intended to act, he would be bewildered for a moment, unable to recall what he was planning to do. Only when Li Fan appeared before him and was barely recognized would he recall.

Cheng Dao was like this, let alone other living beings. As the creator of the Primordial Immortal Realm, the Heavenly Emperors and Heavenly Scars in this world had all forgotten Li Fan. Even the connection between the Heavenly Realm of the Primordial Immortal Realm and Li Fan before had been severed. It was as if the Primordial Immortal Realm had been naturally conceived, having nothing to do with Li Fan. As the various imprints left by “Li Fan” in the mortal world slowly disappeared, he assimilated further into the Mountains and Seas world. Not limited to the Primordial possibility. Li Fan looked up at the sky. The originally dense sky seemed to have been shattered by countless fine cracks, as if someone had split it open. Through these cracks, he seemed to see the scene of the vast, continuous Mountains and Seas. And Li Fan, if he wished, could step out into the Mountains and Seas at any time! The opportunity for transcendence was right before his eyes.

Li Fan’s heart instinctively felt a tremor of longing. But the warnings from his spiritual sense made him hesitate to take that final step. “I can’t stay any longer.” At a moment of clarity, Li Fan thought so. The illusory feeling of being swallowed by the Mountains and Seas made Li Fan misjudge the passage of time. In his memory, it had only been a few days since he accepted Cheng Dao’s guidance and comprehended the Great Dao of Longevity. But before Li Fan finally decided to activate Revert All, he checked the situation in the Shuoxing Star Sea and was horrified to discover that ten years had passed in the world! Li Fan shook his head, trying to dispel the sense of dislocation caused by being swallowed by the Mountains and Seas. Calming himself, Li Fan mentally recited, “Revert All!”

In the mortal world, everything seemed to freeze. Li Fan waited for the darkness to swallow him. One breath, two breaths, three breaths… However, the familiar darkness did not descend. As if being doused with a basin of ice-cold water in winter, Li Fan mentally recited again, “Revert All!” “Revert All!” “Revert All!” ... But Revert All seemed to have malfunctioned. Or perhaps it had left him. There was not the slightest reaction. A great fear arose in Li Fan’s heart, even a thousand times greater than the fear of being swallowed by the Mountains and Seas. His face gradually became distorted, and Li Fan roared repeatedly. He was not just roaring in his heart but also shouting in reality. But it was as if he had been forgotten by the mortal world; nothing and no one responded to any of his actions.

In despair, a surge of ferocity arose in his heart. Li Fan used his divine abilities, attempting to destroy the Star Sea to vent his anger. But not only his spells, but even his divine sense and physical body, could no longer interact with reality. Disappearing from the mortal world, merging into the Mountains and Seas. Li Fan did not feel his body becoming transparent or fading. Instead, he was slowly disappearing from the world. The cracks in the sky grew more numerous. The next step seemed to be involuntarily being sucked into the Mountains and Seas. “Could this be my final end?” When nothing could change his destiny, Li Fan ironically became calm.

He vaguely felt that something was not quite right. However, he couldn't explain what was strange. It wasn't until half of his body had entered the rift, and Li Fan truly witnessed the magnificent scene of the Mountains and Seas outside the mortal world, that he suddenly awoke. Had Revert All truly left him? If he lost Revert All, how could the Great Dao of Longevity and the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas alone maintain this state of being swallowed by the Mountains and Seas? He would have likely detached himself long ago. Under the fusion of the three Daos, it was possible to integrate so naturally into the Mountains and Seas. Others, even if they transcended, even at the realm of the Three Sages, could not achieve this. Simple logical reasoning made Li Fan suddenly realize.

“I haven’t lost Revert All.” Like finding a life-saving straw, Li Fan’s previously calm, indifferent, and motionless eyes suddenly burst with a glimmer of hope. “From Revert All’s performance in the Infinite Sea before, and its主动 transmission of the Illusion is True method, it absolutely does not wish for me to be discovered by the Mountains and Seas right now.” “If the previous Three Dao fusion status was merely because Revert All was curious, then there’s no reason for it to remain indifferent now that I am about to be completely swallowed by the Mountains and Seas.” Li Fan’s thoughts raced faster and faster. The blurred sense of time also returned to normal amidst his contemplation. “So, it’s not that Revert All isn’t responding.” “It’s that...” “The connection between me and it has been severed.” “Or, it couldn’t hear my Revert All command.” Understanding dawned upon Li Fan’s heart. “As long as Revert All is still here, everything can be saved.” “If shouting yields no response, then kick down the door!”

Li Fan had completely entered the rift of the Mountains and Seas. The light from the Primordial possibility was disappearing as the rift closed. Upon entering the Mountains and Seas, Li Fan felt that the process of being swallowed had slowed down. But at the same time, countless images and shadows in his mind intensified like a rising storm. It seemed that in the next moment, these illusory images would transition from虚 to实, evolving from the Mountains and Seas. The Infinite Sea, the peaks of the Mountains, and the shores beyond the Mountains and Seas. It seemed that all of them perceived the anomaly at Li Fan's location. The Mountains and Seas roared and bellowed. Perhaps in the next moment, Li Fan would be exposed to all beings in the Mountains and Seas. But the more desperate the situation, the calmer Li Fan became. He quickly found the only way to save himself: self-destruction. The energy accumulated in his body through cultivation, as well as Li Fan’s divine soul will, were instantly ignited. Then, without reservation, he exploded outwards. The foundation of Immortality, the Great Dao of Longevity. All of it turned into fuel for infinite light at this moment.

Li Fan had never discovered that he contained such immense energy within his body. After being ignited instantly, it could even sever Dao Annihilation and fill mountains and seas! The first to be affected was the Primordial Possibility, whose rift had not yet fully closed. Like an infinite sun, the boundless radiance illuminated the originally dim starry sky. Shuoxing Sea, Primordial Immortal Realm. As well as the High Wall, the Dao Net. All of these melted away like ice and snow in the flame-like light. The entire Primordial Possibility had only a handful of people struggling to hold on. And starting from the Primordial Possibility, it was as if a raging forest fire had ignited. It spread rapidly at the speed of sight transfer. Wherever Li Fan looked, it was already engulfed by light. Towering infernos, blazing flames, obscured Li Fan's view from the outside.

In the midst of infinite light, Li Fan found a moment of respite. In a flash of insight, Li Fan observed that the surrounding possibilities being burned were not truly disappearing. Instead, they transformed into illusions and returned to the Mountains and Seas. Li Fan could even sense the images echoing in his mind. “What is the relationship between Mountains and Seas, and the mortal world?” “And beyond the Mountains and Seas...” Reaching the peak of power, he suddenly collapsed. Li Fan’s thoughts were interrupted, unable to ponder further. “Ultimately, I couldn’t awaken Revert All.” This was Li Fan’s last thought before losing consciousness.

Chapter 1522: Mortal Falls to the Mortal World

After losing consciousness, the concept of time ceased to exist.

Even if eons passed, or even longer. For the person involved, it was merely a difference between waking up and not.

Li Fan was awakened by the constantly flickering light symbols before his eyes.

As if urged for a long time, the light symbols flickered incessantly. Although the frequency of each flicker remained consistent, Li Fan instinctively perceived a sense of "urgency" from them.

This emotion even infected Li Fan, making him compelled to make a choice, even though his mind was still in a state of blankness.

Li Fan stared at the light symbols and after some effort, finally understood the meaning they conveyed.

[This simulation has ended]

[You may choose one of the following options to retain:

1. One item held by yourself during this simulation.

2. Your cultivation realm during this simulation.

3. The simulated memories of a person closely related to you during this simulation. This memory can be inherited by that person.

4. Forgo the above choices and accelerate the charging progress.]

...

"Simulation..."

"Retain..."

The familiar yet unfamiliar words seemed to awaken some past memories in Li Fan. But just as he was about to recall something, Li Fan's head suddenly felt a sharp pain.

Countless, innumerable images, as if finding an outlet, rushed forward. They drowned Li Fan in an instant.

His true memories vanished into the vast ocean, and Li Fan let out a scream, falling unconscious again.

"Don't worry, it's just wind evil entering the brain. Drink this bowl of charm water, and he will surely turn danger into safety and misfortune into peace. But to completely cure the symptoms, continuous consumption is needed. Shujuan, you must know that many people in the village are waiting for this charm water to save their lives. We had a good relationship when we were young. But providing you with one or two bowls for free is already doing our utmost. From now on, if you still want this charm water..."

"It depends on your sincerity."

"Xiaoyue... Lord Li Wu, please rest assured, even if I have to sell everything I own, I will save Fan'er."

...

While unconscious, Li Fan's ears were occasionally filled with two chattering female voices.

Then Li Fan felt a turbid liquid with a peculiar smell being forcibly poured into him.

It was as if it had been brewing in a ditch for over a decade. As the liquid entered his stomach, a nauseating, retching feeling surged to the top of his head.

"Ugh."

Li Fan suddenly turned over and began to vomit.

"Shujuan, look, I told you this charm water is miraculous! He needs to drink a few more bowls in time to recover completely..."

"Fan'er." A woman, disregarding the filth Li Fan had vomited, rushed forward with extreme joy to check on his condition.

Li Fan, who had just woken up, had a chaotic mind, unable to sort anything out. He only managed to grasp that the mystical, somewhat sharp voice wanted to force more of that turbid liquid down his throat. As if re-experiencing that extremely pungent smell, Li Fan felt an inexplicable anger surge within him.

"Hocus pocus!"

His voice was hoarse, cold, and cruel.

The two women in the room were startled.

The small hut fell silent. Li Fan instinctively reached out towards the witch with his hand, waving it in the air.

But as soon as he raised his hand, he felt a wave of weakness.

His stomach churned violently, and he couldn't help but vomit again.

"Shujuan, I think... your nephew's delusion is a bit serious. He needs to drink a few more bowls."

"Yes, yes, yes."

"How dare you!" Li Fan exclaimed, furious again.

But this body was indeed extremely weak.

Even with his best efforts to struggle, he was easily subdued by the two peasant women, forced to humiliatingly drink bowl after bowl of charm water.

...

A month later.

At the dinner table, Li Fan ate slowly and deliberately. The food was not particularly abundant: stir-fried vegetables, tofu, and a bowl of fish soup were all that was offered.

"Although we've sold more than half of the farmland, your body is slowly recovering, isn't it?"

"I asked Scholar Qian from the village. You were afflicted by many illnesses and invaded by wind evil, leading to various hallucinations. As long as you read more sage texts, righteous energy will naturally arise in your heart. The hallucinations will slowly disappear..."

Li Fan listened to the nag of the woman beside him, nodding occasionally in response.

At the same time, he was sorting through the myriad illusions in his mind.

After finishing his meal, Li Fan, as usual, went out for a walk and exercise. He ignored everyone who greeted him. After walking for a while, he finally arrived at a quiet, secluded place.

Only then did Li Fan carefully look at the rapidly flashing light symbols before him.

"Simulation, inheritance."

"What does this mean?"

During this period, whenever he looked at these constantly flashing words, Li Fan seemed to sense their urgency. Even on many quiet nights, lying in bed, he found it difficult to sleep.

He wanted to just choose something arbitrarily.

However, his naturally cautious nature ultimately prevented him from making a hasty decision.

Li Fan had a premonition.

No matter which option he chose, it was likely that none of them would lead to a good outcome.

Li Fan felt a slight headache, so he temporarily put it aside, refusing to think about it.

Instead, he continued to sort through the chaotic memories in his mind.

"Are these illusions real or fake?"

A month had passed, and Li Fan still couldn't figure this question out.

The images in his memory came from different people, different times, and even different worlds.

Bizarre and varied, in a kaleidoscope of forms.

There were firsthand experiences from a first-person perspective, and observations from a third-person point of view. There were even macroscopic aerial views from high above the sky.

It was truly difficult to discern reality from illusion.

"Perhaps... these are all real."

"These are all things I experienced in what was called 【simulation】." Li Fan closed his eyes, forcibly suppressing the endless phantom thoughts. He couldn't help but think this way.

"If these were all my memories, then no matter what, I couldn't be as weak as I am today."

"So, something must have gone wrong during the simulation."

"Cultivation..."

Li Fan couldn't help but stare again at the second option given in the character reminder.

During these days, Li Fan had also inquired indirectly and directly. Combining the countless phantom images in his mind, Li Fan was certain that only true cultivators could be associated with the words [cultivation].

"No matter what I experienced in the simulation, or what realm I reached in my cultivation. It would definitely be better than now. So, it seems there's no problem with choosing this option to inherit."

"Flying through the heavens, escaping the earth, immortal life."

Thinking of this, Li Fan instinctively felt a tremor in his heart, representing both instinctive longing and a premonition of inexplicable fear.

But after such a long time without making a decision, Li Fan would not change his mind so quickly.

He compared the option of inheriting cultivation with the other options one by one.

"If it's just an item, it seems unlikely to change my current predicament. Moreover, with my extremely weak body right now, I can barely hold a pair of chopsticks. Even if I obtained an immortal treasure, I probably wouldn't be able to use it." Li Fan shook his head secretly.

"Choosing a close person to inherit memories."

Li Fan pondered for a long time.

"The closest person... If that person inherits the memories from the simulation, upon seeing my current predicament, they should come forward to help."

When his attention focused on this option, dozens of different figures appeared in Li Fan's mind.

Li Fan scanned them one by one.

When he lingered on a white-haired old man, the feeling that arose in his heart was the most comfortable. As for the others...

"They don't seem to be kind people."

"Could it be that in my simulation, I was actually associated with these people?" Li Fan felt a bit incredulous.

He stared at the image of the old man for a long time. Li Fan then turned to look at the final option prompt: "Accelerate charging speed."

Based on his observations during this period, Li Fan roughly guessed that charging was the prerequisite for activating the simulation.

"In other words, I can initiate another simulation."

...

In reality, Li Fan slowly opened his eyes.

He had stayed in this quiet place outside the village for a long time. As evening approached, Li Fan hurried back.

For the next period, he maintained his disguise as usual.

His body recovered, and he studied day and night without stopping.

He was actually patiently waiting for the so-called charge to complete.

Finally, one day, he felt a mysterious sensation in his heart. The so-called simulation could be activated again.

Silently reciting the words in his mind, Li Fan once again fell into darkness.

When he woke up again, he looked around and was utterly astonished.

It was still the same familiar room.

It seemed like nothing had changed.

"Could it be that it was all just my hallucination?" Li Fan's mind trembled, and disappointment was beyond words.

But soon, he noticed subtle differences between the house he was in and the one he was familiar with.

"I've already used more than half of this ink."

"And..."

Li Fan's heart stirred, and he quickly flipped through the books and papers on the table.

"That's right. It seems I've returned to about a month ago?"

To verify his conjecture, Li Fan immediately ran out to find his aunt. As expected, she looked noticeably younger. Most of the white hair on her head was gone.

"So this is what they call simulation!"

After being extremely excited, Li Fan quickly calmed down. Apparently, this body had become accustomed to it.

"Returning to the past, having foreknowledge."

"Although the world is vast, I can go anywhere."

"However, I must be extremely careful. That thing that severely injured me in the simulation..."

An indescribable aura emanated from the young Li Fan's body.

Although his face was that of a young scholar, he possessed an unfathomable majesty.

Twenty years later.

"Congratulations to the Grand Tutor!"

In the Grand Tutor's mansion, Li Fan looked at the ministers of the Great Xuan dynasty, smiling as he raised his cup.

Facing the flattery of the court's key officials, his mind drifted elsewhere.

"What exactly is 'cultivation'?"

In twenty years, he had risen from a humble scholar to a Grand Tutor with immense power.

But he had never forgotten that he was merely in a simulation.

Nor had he forgotten his purpose.

To seek the truth behind his lost memories.

"These years, I have tirelessly sorted through them, and finally figured out some clues. However, without celestial spiritual energy, even with all my pre-arranged plans, I have absolutely no way to implement them!" Li Fan sighed in his heart.

After the wine flowed freely and the guests departed, Li Fan returned to his bedroom and quietly looked at himself in the mirror.

He stroked his dense beard and then removed his disguise.

"Compared to twenty years ago, there has been no change at all."

"Heh."

"Even this body."

Li Fan stretched and moved his body.

Twenty years had passed, and he not only felt no aging but also felt that as time accumulated, this body had become increasingly youthful and vibrant.

Keep in mind that he had not officially embarked on the path of cultivation.

"I am indeed not an ordinary person."

To conceal his secret of longevity, Li Fan had wives and concubines, but rarely slept with them. He used the excuse of being busy with state affairs. Even every few years, his bed partners would die of illness.

Initially, people in the court used this as a basis to spread various rumors.

However, after he personally killed the former emperor and supported the young prince to the throne, there were no longer any discussions in the world.

Li Fan became Grand Tutor not because he coveted power.

But to find a way to leave this world.

Although his body possessed the extraordinary ability of longevity, in other aspects, he was no different from an ordinary person. It was somewhat difficult to traverse the world and find the path of cultivation through his own efforts.

However, after becoming Grand Tutor, he established a secret organization specifically for seeking immortals. This would make things much more convenient in the future.

Another ten years later.

The young emperor gradually grew up and was unwilling to be controlled by Li Fan as a puppet.

He secretly nurtured loyal assassins and strategized with ministers.

He intended to kill Li Fan and reclaim his power.

The plan proceeded smoothly, and Li Fan, unknowingly, walked alone into the trap set by the emperor.

The young emperor looked at Li Fan, surrounded by dozens of assassins, and couldn't help but gloe, laughing heartily.

"Grand Tutor, back then, when you whipped me in the name of teaching me to read, did you ever imagine this day?"

However, in this desperate situation, Li Fan's expression remained unchanged from beginning to end.

"What about today?" He retorted with a smile.

"You're still talking tough at the brink of death." The young emperor sneered and waved his hand. The assassins then drew their sharp weapons and charged forward.

However, what happened next was far beyond his expectations.

As blades struck, they only produced the sound of metal clashing, unable to pierce even slightly.

And the seemingly frail Grand Tutor, with each punch he threw, sent the stout men he had personally selected flying, their flesh and blood exploding, instantly disintegrating.

The ambush that was meant to surround and kill turned into a bloody slaughterhouse.

When Li Fan, covered in blood, walked up to the young emperor.

The young emperor was already scared silly.

Li Fan frowned, looking at his blood-stained robes, "Without divine abilities or spells, relying only on mortal flesh and blood is indeed inconvenient."

"However, with such a strong scent of blood, I don't feel much discomfort."

"It seems that in my past simulations, what I experienced..."

"Grand Tutor, Grand Tutor, spare my life!" The young emperor wailed, and Li Fan simply snorted and stomped him to death with a single foot.

...

If one emperor died, there would be another.

In this world, only the Grand Tutor was eternal.

Time flowed by, and the Great Xuan dynasty changed hands several times. The world had grown accustomed to these frequent changes of dynasties.

On this day, it was the Grand Tutor's seventieth birthday.

Officials from all regions traveled thousands of miles to the capital to offer their congratulations.

All the worthies gathered at the Grand Tutor's mansion.

"Dao Xuanzi, do not push your luck too far!"

A furious roar suddenly echoed above the capital of Xuanjing.

Chapter 1523: Undying and Indestructible Body

After losing consciousness, the concept of time ceased to exist. Even if billions of years, or even longer, passed, for the person involved, it was merely a difference between waking up and before.

Li Fan was awakened by the flickering light symbols before his eyes. It was as if he had been urged for a long time, and the light symbols kept flashing. Although the frequency of each flash was consistent, Li Fan instinctively sensed an "urgency" from them. This emotion even infected Li Fan, making him have to make a choice even though his mind was still blank.

Li Fan stared at the light symbols for a long time before finally understanding the meaning they conveyed.

[Simulation ends] [You can choose one of the following options to keep: 1. An item held by yourself in this simulation. 2. Your cultivation realm in this simulation. 3. Simulated memories of a person closely related to you in this simulation. This memory can be passed on to that person. 4. Abandon the above options and speed up the charging progress.]

... “Simulation...” “Keep...”
