Familiar yet strange words seemed to awaken some past memories in Li Fan. But just as he was about to recall something, Li Fan’s head suddenly felt a sharp pain. Countless images rushed forward like a floodgate opening, engulfing Li Fan in an instant. His true memories were lost in the vast sea, and Li Fan let out a scream and fainted again.

“Don’t worry, it’s just ‘wind evil invading the head.’ Drink this bowl of talisman water, and he will surely turn danger into safety and recovery. But to completely cure the symptoms, continuous consumption is needed. Shu Juan, you know, how many people in the village are waiting for this talisman water to save their lives? When we were young, although our relationship was good, providing you with one or two bowls for free is already being generous. From now on, if you still want this talisman water...”

“It depends on your sincerity.”

“Xiao Yue… Lord Li Wu, don’t worry, I will definitely save Fan’er, even if it means selling everything.”

...

In his daze, two chattering female voices occasionally echoed in Li Fan’s ears. Then Li Fan felt someone forcibly pouring a turbid liquid with a unique smell into him. It was like something brewed in a sewer for more than ten years.

The liquid entered his stomach, and a nauseating feeling rushed straight to the top of his head.

“Ugh.”

Li Fan suddenly turned over and began to vomit.

“Shu Juan, see? I told you this talisman water is miraculous! We need to drink a few more bowls promptly to recover completely…”

“Fan’er.” A woman rushed forward, overjoyed, to check on Li Fan’s condition, disregarding the filth Li Fan had vomited.

Li Fan’s mind was in chaos, unable to sort anything out. He only managed to grasp the important point that the superstitious and sharp voice wanted to force more of that turbid liquid down his throat. As if feeling that extremely pungent smell again, Li Fan felt an inexplicable rage.

“Playing tricks!”

His voice was hoarse, cold, and cruel. The two women in the room were startled. The small room fell silent. Li Fan instinctively reached out towards the witch, flicking his hand in mid-air. But as soon as he raised his hand, he felt a wave of weakness. His stomach churned, and he couldn’t help but vomit again.

“Shu Juan, I think… your nephew’s delusion seems a bit serious. He needs to drink a few more bowls.”

“Yes, yes.”

“How dare you!” Li Fan was furious upon hearing this. But this body was indeed extremely weak. Even with all his efforts to struggle, he was easily subdued by the two peasant women, and could only humiliatingly drink bowl after bowl of talisman water.

...

A month later.

At the dinner table, Li Fan ate slowly. The food was not abundant: green vegetables, tofu, and a bowl of fish soup were all that was laid out.

“Although we had to sell more than half of our fields, your body is slowly getting better, isn’t it?”

“I asked Scholar Qian from the village. He said you were afflicted by illness and that wind evil invaded your body, causing all sorts of hallucinations. As long as you read more sacred texts, righteous energy will arise in your heart, and the hallucinations will gradually disappear...”

Li Fan nodded occasionally while listening to the nagging of the woman beside him. At the same time, he was sorting through the myriad illusions in his mind.

After dinner, Li Fan went out for his usual walk and exercise. He ignored everyone who greeted him. After walking for a while, he finally arrived at a quiet, deserted place. Li Fan then looked carefully at the rapidly flashing light symbols before him.

“Simulation, inheritance.”

“What does this mean?”

During this period, every time he looked at these continuously flashing lines, Li Fan seemed to feel their urgency. Even on several quiet nights, he lay in bed, unable to sleep. He wanted to just choose one and be done with it. However, his cautious nature ultimately prevented him from making a hasty decision. Li Fan had a premonition. No matter which option he chose, it was likely that the outcome would not be good.

Li Fan felt a slight headache and decided to put it aside for now and not think about it. Instead, he continued to sort through the chaotic memories in his mind.

“Are these illusions real or fake?”

After a month, Li Fan still couldn't figure this out. The images in his memory came from different people, different times, and even different worlds. They were bizarre and varied. There were first-person experiences, third-person observations, and even macroscopic views from above the sky. It was truly difficult to distinguish between reality and illusion.

“Perhaps… these are all real.”

“These are all things I experienced in the so-called ‘simulations’.”

Li Fan closed his eyes, forcefully suppressing the endless illusions and distracting thoughts. He couldn't help but think this.

“If these are all my memories, then no matter what, I could never be as frail as I am today.”

“Therefore, there must have been some accident during the simulation.”

“Cultivation…” Li Fan couldn’t help but stare at the second option given in the reminder again.

During these days, Li Fan had also inquired subtly. Combining this with the myriad illusions in his mind, Li Fan was certain that only true cultivators were related to the word ‘cultivation’.

“No matter what I experienced in the simulation, or what realm I reached, it must be better than now.”

“Thus, it seems there is no problem in choosing to inherit this option.”

“Flying through the heavens, escaping the earth, achieving immortality.”

Thinking of this, Li Fan instinctively felt a tremor in his heart, representing both instinctive yearning and a sense of unknown fear. But after not making a decision for so long, Li Fan wouldn't change his mind on a whim. He compared the option of inheriting cultivation with the other options.

“If it’s just an item, it seems unhelpful in changing the current predicament. Moreover, with my current extremely frail body, I can barely hold chopsticks. Even if I obtained an immortal treasure, I probably couldn’t use it,” Li Fan shook his head inwardly.

“Choose to inherit the simulated memories of a closely related person.” Li Fan pondered for a long time. “The most closely related person… If the other party inherits the simulated memories, seeing my current predicament, they should come forward to help.”

When his attention focused on this option, dozens of different figures appeared in Li Fan’s mind. Li Fan scanned them one by one. When his gaze lingered on an elderly figure with white hair, the feeling that arose in his heart was the most comfortable. As for the others…

“They don’t look like good people.”

“Could it be that in my simulation, I’ve associated with these people?” Li Fan felt a little incredulous. He stared at the old man’s image for a long time before turning his gaze to the last option: “Accelerate charging progress.”

Based on his understanding during this period, Li Fan roughly guessed that charging was a prerequisite for activating the simulation. “In other words, I can conduct another simulation.”

...

Li Fan slowly opened his eyes in reality. He had been in this quiet place outside the village for a long time. As dusk approached, Li Fan hurried back. For the next period, he maintained his disguise as usual, studying day and night while recovering his body. In reality, he was patiently waiting for the so-called charging to complete.

Finally, one day, he felt a mysterious sensation in his heart. The simulation could be activated again. With a mental command, Li Fan was once again enveloped in darkness.

When he awoke again, he looked around and was astonished. It was the familiar room. It seemed like nothing had changed.

“Could it be that all of this was just my delusion?” Li Fan’s heart trembled, filled with unspeakable disappointment. But soon, he noticed subtle differences between the house he was in and the one he knew.

“I clearly used more than half of this ink stone.”

“And…” Li Fan’s heart moved, and he quickly flipped through the books and papers on the table. “That’s right. It seems I’ve returned to more than a month ago?”

To verify his guess, Li Fan rushed out to find his aunt. Sure enough, she looked significantly younger. The white hair on her head had diminished considerably.

“So this is what ‘simulation’ means!”

After being extremely excited, Li Fan quickly calmed down. Obviously, this body was already accustomed to it.

“Returning to the past, possessing foreknowledge.”

“This world is vast, and I can go anywhere.”

“However, I must be extremely careful. That thing that caused me severe injuries in the simulation...” A sense of indescribable aura emanated from the youthful Li Fan. Although his face was that of a young scholar, he possessed an unfathomable imposing presence.

Twenty years later.

“Congratulations to the Grand Tutor!”

In the Grand Tutor’s mansion, Li Fan smiled and raised his cup, looking at the officials of the Great Xuan Dynasty. Amidst the congratulations from the court’s important officials, his mind drifted elsewhere.

“What exactly is this ‘cultivation’?”

In twenty years, he had risen from a humble scholar to become the Grand Tutor, wielding immense power. But he had never forgotten that he was merely within a simulation. Nor had he forgotten his goal: to uncover the truth behind his lost memories.

“Over the years, I have sorted through information day and night and finally figured out some clues. However, without ‘immortal spiritual energy,’ even with all my contingency plans, I have no way to implement them,” Li Fan sighed inwardly.

After the banquet, when the guests had dispersed, Li Fan returned to his bedroom and quietly looked at himself in the mirror. He touched his dense beard and then removed his disguise.

“Compared to twenty years ago, there has been no change at all.”

“Heh.”

“Even this body.” Li Fan stretched and moved his body. Twenty years had passed, and not only did he not feel aged, but he even felt that with the passage of time, his body was becoming younger and more vibrant. He hadn’t even officially started cultivating yet.

“I am indeed not an ordinary person.”

To conceal his secret of immortality, Li Fan had wives and concubines, but he rarely slept with them, always citing his heavy state affairs as an excuse. Even every few years, his bedside companions would die of illness. Originally, people in the court and the public had spread various rumors based on this. However, after he personally killed the former emperor and supported the young crown prince to the throne, all discussions ceased.

Li Fan became Grand Tutor not out of greed for power, but to find a way out of this world. Although his current body possessed the anomaly of longevity, in other aspects, he was no different from a mortal. It would be somewhat difficult to tread the path of cultivation solely on his own.

However, after becoming Grand Tutor, he established a secret organization dedicated to seeking immortal knowledge. This would greatly facilitate his future actions.

Ten years later.

The young emperor gradually grew up and was unwilling to be controlled by Li Fan as a puppet. He secretly nurtured elite assassins and courted ministers, intending to assassinate Li Fan and seize back power. The plan proceeded smoothly, and Li Fan, completely unaware, walked alone into the trap set by the emperor.

The young emperor looked at Li Fan, surrounded by dozens of elite assassins, and couldn't help but laugh triumphantly.

“Grand Tutor, Grand Tutor, back then you whipped me under the guise of teaching me! Who knew there would be a day like this?”

However, in this desperate situation, Li Fan’s expression remained unchanged from beginning to end.

“What about today? What about today?” he retorted with a smile.

“Facing imminent death and still being stubborn.” The young emperor sneered and waved his hand. The assassins then drew their weapons and rushed forward.

However, what happened next was far beyond his expectations. The blades and weapons struck, but only produced the sound of metal clashing. They couldn’t even pierce his skin. Yet, with each punch from the seemingly frail Grand Tutor, he sent the strong, stout men he had personally selected flying, their flesh and blood exploding. The trap that was meant to surround and kill Li Fan had turned into a bloody slaughterhouse.

When the blood-soaked Li Fan walked up to the young emperor, the young emperor was already scared stiff. Li Fan frowned slightly, looking at his blood-stained clothes, “Without divine abilities or magic, relying only on mortal flesh is inconvenient.”

“However, I don’t feel much discomfort from such heavy bloodshed.”

“It seems that in my past simulations...”

“Grand Tutor, Grand Tutor, spare my life!” The young emperor cried, but Li Fan merely snorted and stomped him to death.

...

One emperor died, and another would rise. In this world, only the Grand Tutor remained eternal. Time flowed, and the Great Xuan Dynasty changed hands several times. The world had grown accustomed to these frequent dynastic changes.

On this day, it was the Grand Tutor’s seventieth birthday. Officials from all regions traveled thousands of miles to the capital to offer their congratulations. The esteemed guests gathered at the Grand Tutor’s mansion.

“Dao Xuan Zi, do you think you can go too far trying to bully others?” A roar suddenly echoed above the capital of Xuan Jing.

Chapter 1524: All Beings' Fates Have Changed

Two figures streaked across the sky like shooting stars and stopped above the city of Xuan Jing. All the civil and military officials of the court turned pale, and many even cried out "Immortal Master," preparing to kneel on the spot. Only Li Fan remained unfazed, letting out a cold snort, “What are you panicking about!” Having imposed his authority over the court for decades, the Grand Tutor's absolute and irrefutable majesty had long been ingrained in the hearts of all officials, big and small. At his command, he managed to forcibly suppress the inherent fear of immortals in everyone, bringing about a temporary calm. However, as they looked up at the two immortal figures above, their faces still showed unconcealable fear.

In Xuan Jing City, mortals held their breath in terror. The dialogue between the two cultivators continued. “Kou Hong! Do you think you can escape just because you fled to this desolate land? Hand over the cultivation technique you obtained that day, or I will hunt you to the death!” “Ridiculous! It’s precisely because I lacked the method to form a core that I’ve been stuck at the Foundation Establishment stage for nearly a hundred years, and my lifespan is nearing its end, about to turn to dust. I obtained this core-forming technique, how could I possibly hand it over to others!” ... “This dialogue seems somewhat familiar.” “It seems this isn't the first time I've experienced this.” As Kou Hong and Dao Xuan Zi's thunderous dialogue continued, Li Fan’s mind suddenly felt a sharp pain. Then, myriad images rapidly surged forth.

“This is bad!” Recalling the subsequent turmoil caused by the battle between these two, which would turn the entire Xuan Jing city into ruins, Li Fan’s heart suddenly tightened. And the subsequent reality unfolded exactly as his memory depicted. “Kou Hong! What do you think you are doing!” “Just seeking a glimmer of hope for survival!” Following Kou Hong’s frenzied laughter, a colossal crimson dragon gradually descended. The scorching flames seemed capable of burning everything around them to ashes. Witnessing this scene, all the mortals in Xuan Jing city revealed expressions of fear and despair. Except for Li Fan.

His heart remained unmoved. Li Fan even felt a strange sensation as he sensed the crimson flames in the sky. “This…” “Is this the spiritual energy required for cultivation?” Li Fan attempted to sense it more comprehensively. The flow of time seemed to slow down immensely. Li Fan could clearly see the colossal flame seemingly frozen in mid-air, motionless. To Li Fan’s surprise, this so-called immortal spiritual energy was not that difficult to comprehend. In fact, it was somewhat rudimentary and… obedient. It seemed that with a mere thought, he could easily control it.

Thus, Li Fan attempted to draw the violent and scorching spiritual energy in the sky into his body. It was like water flowing into a stream, smooth and unimpeded. The immense energy that could burn Xuan Jing entered Li Fan’s body, as if a river flowing into the abyss, without causing even the slightest ripple. If Li Fan hadn’t felt the subtle changes in his body, he might have thought his attempt to draw spiritual energy into his body had failed. “The original attribute of the spiritual energy belonging to fire has also disappeared. Has it regained its original purity?” “Is this also a function of this body?”

... The sudden change in the field occurred so abruptly. Kou Hong’s ferocious expression was still on his face, but his killing move [Dao Technique: Fire Dragon Chant] inexplicably vanished. Kou Hong gradually became bewildered. “Are you cursing me?” Kou Hong immediately attributed this change to his sworn brother, asking with anger and disbelief. “...What?” Dao Xuan Zi was initially bewildered, not understanding Kou Hong’s line of reasoning. As the two were about to argue, a cold, stern, and supremely majestic voice suddenly sounded from below. “Impudent!” “Get down here!” Suddenly, a surge of immense force struck them, as if countless hands were dragging them downwards. Kou Hong and Dao Xuan Zi were caught off guard, losing their ability to float and crashing heavily onto the ground. Boom! They created two large pits on the bricks and stones of Xuan Jing city! Xuan Jing city instantly fell silent.

Who among the residents of the city didn't recognize the voice from above? They didn't have time to rejoice in their survival. At this moment, the entire Xuan Jing city was utterly shocked. In the Grand Tutor’s mansion, all the civil and military officials, regardless of rank, stared at Li Fan as if they had seen a ghost. However, one person reacted the fastest: “The Grand Tutor is wise and divine! Immortals bow their heads! With the Grand Tutor here, it is truly the fortune of our Great Xuan!” Saying this, he immediately bowed. The other officials, upon hearing this, quickly reacted. Regardless of their thoughts, they all echoed his sentiments and bowed in unison.

Li Fan ignored these people. He slowly walked towards the spot where the two cultivators had fallen. As he took his first step, there were still faint traces of spiritual energy remaining in Xuan Jing city. However, by the time Li Fan reached the somewhat disheveled Kou Hong and Dao Xuan Zi, all the spiritual energy had been completely absorbed by Li Fan. “Why is it only this much...” Li Fan felt a hint of dissatisfaction. Then he looked at these cultivators who had so abruptly intruded. At this moment, these two “Immortal Masters” were already surrounded by the Xuan Jing Guards. Although they had a natural fear of the legendary Immortal Masters, they still dutifully held their spears and pointed them at the intruders.

As Li Fan approached, without needing any instructions, a path was cleared for him. After trying all methods and being unable to escape the suppression of the immense force, Kou Hong and Dao Xuan Zi felt a sense of despair. “This desolate land is truly extremely dangerous…” A sense of regret welled up in their hearts. Just then, Li Fan arrived before them. Although he seemed to possess no spiritual energy fluctuations, his tangible imposing presence caused the two cultivators’ bodies to tremble uncontrollably. “Where did you two come from?” As he got closer, Li Fan could more clearly sense the spiritual energy contained within their bodies. However, he did not act rashly, suppressing the restless urge within him, and coldly asked, “Replying to Senior. We two came from the Profound Yellow Realm, from Mount Cong Yun… We accidentally entered this place and have offended you greatly. We hope you will forgive us.” Dao Xuan Zi said, sweating profusely, intermittently.

From the subsequent conversation, Li Fan gained a general understanding of the minor Great Xuan world and the Profound Yellow Realm. At the same time, with every sentence Dao Xuan spoke, corresponding images flashed in Li Fan’s mind. The Immortal-Sealing Grand Formation located in the Eastern Ruins, confining the minor mortal world, as well as the tomb of Yi Yin, a disciple of the Great Evolution Sect, containing the Dao Dissolving Stone and the Great Evolution Boat. Furthermore, the Stone Tablet of Halting in Qian Hong’s Tomb… What surprised Li Fan even more was that when he heard the word 【Cong Yun】, an image suddenly appeared before his eyes: a crimson figure stood tall in the sky, holding illusory flames, incinerating the vast sea.

“Could it be that I was severely injured and lost my memory because of such a calamity?” Li Fan carefully savored the emotions that arose in his heart when the image appeared. “Hmm… Incorrect.” “Was I really this strong before? I could disregard such a calamity?” Li Fan, upon discovering this, felt no joy at all. Instead, he became worried. The farther he had gone before losing his memory, the more difficult the crisis that caused his severe injuries would be to deal with. “I still need to proceed cautiously, step by step.”

... “Borrowing your two’s spiritual energy for a moment.” When the questioning was almost complete, Li Fan clasped his hands towards Kou Hong and Dao Xuan Zi. What happened next made the Kou Hong brothers’ faces turn ashen with terror. It was as if a hole had appeared in their bodies. All their spiritual energy flowed uncontrollably into this hole. In just a few breaths, the two were completely drained. Their spiritual energy was depleted, rendering them no different from mortals! But there was a strange point: according to common sense, ordinary cultivators would suffer backlash after losing all their spiritual energy, not to mention severe injuries. However, the two of them did not feel any pain or weakness at all. Instead, they felt unprecedented vitality, as if they had broken through several major realms!

The two were even shocked to discover that their Foundation Establishment Mystical Treasures, influenced by this vitality, began to crystallize inexplicably, showing signs of sublimation and transformation! “This… what is it?” The brothers were filled with shock and confusion. They simultaneously put away all their inner thoughts. Although the two of them were reckless, they were certainly not stupid. Judging by the abilities displayed by the elder before them, he was at least a Nascent Soul stage mighty being! “However, after the Nascent Soul stage, one forms their own internal Dantian. How could they lack spiritual energy?” “Could it be, before the great calamity…” Kou Hong and Dao Xuan Zi exchanged glances, thinking they had found the truth.

“If Senior has any requests, just command us. We would die without complaint!” Kou Hong said in a muffled voice. ... Li Fan merely waved his hand, and the Xuan Jing Guards swarmed forward, apprehending the two individuals who had lost all resistance and throwing them into the dungeons, transferring them under strict guard. Li Fan did not return to his mansion but stationed himself above the dungeon. The moment he absorbed all the spiritual energy from the two, Li Fan’s killing intent had flared in his heart. However, after faintly sensing that the two seemed to have other uses, he changed his mind. Li Fan sat in meditation, recalling the feeling he had just experienced.

“Eternal Remnant Will.” “Only I can be the boat… the method of traversing?” When these few fragmented words appeared in his mind one after another, myriad majestic figures suddenly flooded in. *Pfft!* Li Fan spat out a large mouthful of blood. His mind felt as if it had been repeatedly struck by a heavy hammer, spinning uncontrollably. It was not an illusion but a genuine severe injury to his brain. Besides the bright red blood, there were even some clotted white tissues spewing from his seven orifices. Instantly, Li Fan’s entire body was drenched in blood. Under normal circumstances, let alone mortals, even cultivators would die on the spot from such severe injuries. But Li Fan recovered instantly from his near-death state after forcibly severing the connection to his memories, without even feeling the slightest weakness. He wiped the blood from his face as if it were not his own. With a single thought, his blood transformed into wisps of green light and returned to his body. Not only did he recover completely, but Li Fan even felt that by venturing to the brink of life and death and mobilizing more of the life force contained within his body, he had become even stronger.

“The life force in this body is simply too formidable.” “But it’s ultimately a good thing.” Thinking of the Profound Yellow Realm outside the minor Great Xuan world, Li Fan vaguely had an idea. Half a day later. A body exactly identical to Li Fan’s appeared. It was not a clone technique. It was Li Fan, relying on his formidable life force, who had forcefully catalyzed the formation of another set of limbs, a torso, and even a head. Then he pieced them back together into a human. Strictly speaking, this body was only a part of Li Fan. After a brief period of adaptation, he adjusted to the perspective of two people existing simultaneously. Li Fan looked at his other self, and even though he was the creator of this masterpiece, he couldn’t help but feel a little incredulous. “...” “Let him go first to scout the way. If he encounters danger, he can sacrifice an arm to save himself.” Seven days later, Li Fan, along with Kou Hong and Dao Xuan Zi, flew out of Xuan Jing city. Heading straight for the Eastern Ruins.

He didn’t ask Kou Hong and Dao Xuan Zi how to fly. After achieving Qi Condensation, Li Fan's body naturally recalled it. Even with the two burdens, he didn’t feel the slightest strain. In a moment, they arrived outside the Ruins. “Senior, ahead lies the Immortal-Sealing Grand Formation that sealed the mortal world. It is fraught with danger. We two...” Kou Hong hadn’t finished speaking when Li Fan, after observing for a moment, frowned. Then he led them straight down. The hearts of the two brothers tightened. However, fortunately, their worst fears did not materialize. The restrictions within the Immortal-Sealing Grand Formation seemed to have all malfunctioned for some reason. Until they were about to break through, there was no movement. The two could only remain speechless.

Breaking through the darkness and reappearing in the light, the continuous Crimson Cloud mountain range appeared before the three. Kou Hong and Dao Xuan Zi greedily absorbed the spiritual energy in the heavens and earth. After finally recovering, they couldn’t help but sigh in relief. But when they looked at Li Fan, they found that inexplicably, he had not absorbed any spiritual energy around him the entire time. He had been looking up at the sky, seemingly contemplating something. The two dared not disturb him and quietly waited at his side. “How many years has it been since this place transformed from mountains into seas?” Li Fan asked after a long silence. The two were first startled, but Dao Xuan Zi reacted first, “About twenty years, Senior. How did you know?” Li Fan squinted and didn’t answer. He was merely sensing a crimson figure within his body. The moment they entered the Profound Yellow Realm, Li Fan had noticed the figure floating in the sky, identical to the perpetrator of burning mountains and boiling seas in his memory.

However, facing such a formidable being, Li Fan felt no fear. Instead, he felt a strange sensation. Thus, with just a thought, that crimson figure was “captured” and sealed within his body. From it, Li Fan sensed many principles related to “flame.” However, they seemed particularly rudimentary. Like a toddler babbling, somewhat childish and laughable. “It seems my original achievements were even greater than I had anticipated.” Li Fan slowly came to this realization. Recommend a book: Traveling through history, amending historical regrets, saving historical figures, and building a divine dynasty of destiny.

Chapter 1525: Life Swallowing Ruomu

Compelled by the situation, He Zheng Hao could only agree to Li Fan's request. “The Heaven Profound Mirror is a supreme treasure of the Immortal Alliance. Even though this esteemed Senior is powerful, he probably cannot harm the treasure, right?” Trembling, He Zheng Hao led Li Fan to a dark room at the deepest part of the Administration Hall. After activating the Crimson Cloud Prefecture’s Heaven Profound Branch Mirror, he couldn’t help but console himself. Amidst the flashing light, an ancient mirror floated into existence.

“It is indeed very familiar.” Mulling over the subtle feeling that surged in his heart again, Li Fan didn't hesitate. He took a step forward, his form shattering, and disappeared into the mirror. Only He Zheng Hao was left behind, wide-eyed and dumbfounded. Although Li Fan had entered the Heaven Profound Mirror, the Heaven Profound Mirror did not detect his intrusion. The functions that were originally locked by tiers of permissions were now all accessible to Li Fan, categorized and presented before him. He could even freely seize all items, resources, divine abilities, and cultivation techniques within the Heaven Profound Mirror. He could even utilize the Heaven Profound Mirror's computational power. And as long as it didn’t cause any major anomalies, the Heaven Profound Mirror wouldn’t detect it. If it weren’t for the many other memories in his mind that were clearly superior to the Heaven Profound Mirror, Li Fan would almost believe he was the Heaven Profound Mirror’s human host.

“I wonder if it’s a convenience provided by the previous simulations.” For the next three months, Li Fan resided within the Heaven Profound Mirror, perusing countless ancient texts and secret records. Although the mirror contained vast amounts of information, Li Fan felt a sense of vague familiarity every time he read through it. Often, after a cursory glance, insights would spontaneously emerge in his mind. Moreover, the more he pondered, the more fragmented memories transformed into clearer recollections. Li Fan’s reading speed also became increasingly rapid. By the end, he no longer needed to seek answers within the Heaven Profound Mirror.

“To seek longevity by defying the Heavenly Laws. This is clearly a flawed cultivation method, forever binding one to the Transcendent True Celestial Venerable. Perhaps I had a conflict with him in the past...” Li Fan did not rush to embark on the path of cultivation. Although he had read through everything in three months, even without cultivating, his body was continuously growing stronger. “The Heavenly Venerable’s method relies on external objects because the human body is inherently weak, and one needs external forces to change destiny against the heavens.” “But I already possess such powerful strength within my body. Therefore, I no longer need to practice the method of defying the Heavenly Laws.” Li Fan sat cross-legged within the Heaven Profound Mirror, meditating with his eyes closed. With each inhalation and exhalation, a stream of green light surged like a tide from his body but did not dissipate. It merely accumulated around Li Fan, illuminating his silhouette in a faint green glow.

When Li Fan opened his eyes again, outwardly, there were no significant changes, but a brilliant starry sky had formed in his Dantian. However, all the stars in this starry sky shone with a vibrant green light. “Strictly speaking, this is not cultivation, but ‘true cultivation,’ opening up my own potential.” “Although everyone speaks of the body’s hidden treasures, the mortal body’s hidden treasures are incomparable to the infinite life force contained within me. Perhaps even a single green dot within this sea of stars could be equivalent to the sum total of millions of living beings.” Li Fan carefully observed the phenomenon in his Dantian, lost in thought. Once one’s own power reaches a certain level, a mere gesture can distort and alter the Great Dao of heaven and earth.

Moreover, Li Fan instinctively sensed that his ability to subdue the Profound Yellow world seemed particularly outstanding. Just like the Crimson Flame, which he could summon with a mere thought, the Crimson Flame had also benefited greatly from the boundless life force within Li Fan. Its crimson color turned dazzling white, shedding its human form to become pure, dancing flames. “Transforming from human to flame, though it appears to be a regression, is actually an escape from the shackles of the Profound Yellow world. Although it is still one of the Heavenly Daos of the Profound Yellow world, a part of it already exists beyond this world.” “Crimson Flame is like this, and so am I.” Li Fan’s heart was filled with enlightenment.

“And all of this is due to this vitality.” Li Fan had indeed considered investigating the anomalies within his body, but the accumulation of just three months from the Heaven Profound Mirror was clearly insufficient to decipher the true mystery of his vitality. “Moreover, what I understand and see is only the part of the Heaven Profound Mirror that connects to the outside world. A portion of the Heaven Profound Mirror remains sealed. Only when one enters the Myriad Immortal Alliance headquarters, where the main body of the Heaven Profound Mirror is located, can one glimpse it.” Li Fan currently had no intention of venturing into danger.

Although the Profound Yellow world was not large, it concealed countless secrets. Perhaps he could start by exploring other areas to regain his knowledge and experience. Li Fan searched diligently through the endless illusions and found the most suitable destination for him at the moment. Suddenly, before another ancient mirror, his thoughts came to a halt. “Is this… the Boundless Mirror?” “Sun Luoyao, Sun Luyuan...” Information about the Sun family also emerged. “A direct descendant of the Mirror Master lineage. Approaching them will not be as easy as approaching He Zheng Hao. My current body, although strong, is not strong enough to withstand the attacks of multiple Harmonious Dao cultivators.” After some thought, Li Fan summoned He Zheng Hao.

At this moment, He Zheng Hao was both exhilarated and terrified. This was all due to the massive amount of resources mysteriously allocated through the Heaven Profound Mirror. Ten times the usual amount! He Zheng Hao swore that the Immortal Alliance headquarters would never be so generous! However, he was reluctant to return what he had gained. With wealth came confidence. Distributing a large amount of resources downwards made the subordinates believe it was due to He Zheng Hao’s connections at the Immortal Alliance headquarters, filling them with genuine awe and affection for him. Now, He Zheng Hao finally experienced the taste of truly being a ruler of a prefecture. However, this beautiful dream was about to shatter as Li Fan summoned him.

“How do you feel about allocating ten times the usual resources this time?” He Zheng Hao trembled, not daring to answer. Li Fan said calmly, “Don’t be nervous; it’s just a string of numbers. Let alone ten times, if you dare to ask for it, I can easily allocate a hundred times more for you.” He Zheng Hao trembled even more violently, saying he dared not. He knew that everything came at a price, and now it was time for the other party to collect his reward. “Senior, please give your command, and I will do my best,” He Zheng Hao said.

“The top ten in each prefecture’s political performance review can travel to the Immortal Alliance headquarters to receive rewards. Aim for this. The next assessment is in five years. Tell me whatever you need.” Li Fan said calmly. He Zheng Hao’s expression changed drastically upon hearing this. In this world, when would a thief openly boast about their crime? After gaining benefits, one should digest it secretly, not compete in performance reviews. The improvement in ranking required the support of a large amount of resources. To jump from the bottom ten to the top ten... This would not stand up to scrutiny! However, Li Fan’s eyes told He Zheng Hao that if he agreed, even if the truth was revealed later, he would only die five years from now. If he refused, today would be the day He Zheng Hao died.

With no other choice, He Zheng Hao gritted his teeth and agreed. Since he was already on the pirate ship, He Zheng Hao decided to go all out. With a wave of his hand, he submitted a list of resource demands several times higher than necessary. Who knew that Li Fan would agree without even batting an eye? In less than half a day, a mountain of resources began to appear in the Crimson Cloud Prefecture's Heaven Profound Branch Mirror. He Zheng Hao watched with both shock and fear. Besides the various resources needed to maintain governance, Li Fan even provided detailed information about the various major and minor caverns and nascent Heavenly Daos in Crimson Cloud Prefecture and the surrounding prefectures. With this information, it would be achievable to produce hundreds of Nascent Soul and Harmonious Dao cultivators within five years. He Zheng Hao wiped the cold sweat from his forehead, but he felt no excitement.

“Oh, and one more thing.” “Take me to Source Dao Prefecture and plant this anywhere underground,” Li Fan said, handing over a seedling. It looked like an ordinary sapling, but it was strange that He Zheng Hao felt no life force from it. He couldn't even sense its existence. Holding it in his hand, he felt nothing. If it weren’t for the occasional flashes of green light on it, He Zheng Hao would have completely forgotten about it. Li Fan’s instructions were not to be delayed. He Zheng Hao immediately headed for Source Dao Prefecture. In a short while, he entered Source Dao Prefecture. Finding a place where the earth veins converged, he planted the sapling. He then rushed back.

Through the part of Li Fan’s body that had separated, Li Fan’s mind also began to see images of Source Dao Prefecture. “This place seems to hold great danger.” “However, for me, it seems to be a great source of nourishment.” “But I must wait for the right opportunity to lay the groundwork first.” The sapling took root within the earth veins and began to grow without restraint. The growth process did not draw power from the earth veins; instead, it radiated its own life force outwards. This was even after Li Fan had tried his best to suppress the overabundance of vitality.

The Profound Yellow world, though seemingly vibrant, was actually gravely ill. At this moment, the life force brought by this sapling was like the refreshing fragrance of a potent elixir encountered by a dying person. It immediately attracted the attention of certain ‘sacred spirits’ within the Profound Yellow world. The first to notice was an ancient tree with withered yellow leaves and branches laden with cultivators! In just the time it took for an incense stick to burn after the sapling was planted, Li Fan sensed that his body in Source Dao Prefecture seemed to have been targeted by someone. Furthermore, the aura emanating from the other party felt strangely familiar.

“Hmm?” A hunched, frenzied figure flashed through his mind. Moments later, the figure’s owner appeared before the sapling. “This is… Ruo Mu?” Ruo Mu’s appearance triggered Li Fan’s lost memories. As Ruo Mu greedily reached out towards the sapling, a cold glint flashed in Li Fan’s eyes. “Since you want it so badly, I’ll fulfill your wish.” Li Fan was unsure if he, who had only cultivated from scratch for three months, was a match for this ancient tree of the Profound Yellow world. However, since the other party wanted to devour a part of his body, he had a way to deal with it.

A green light suddenly surged from Li Fan’s originally pitch-black eyes. Like a volcanic eruption, limitless life force emerged from the sapling underground in Source Dao Prefecture and flowed towards Ruo Mu. The aging Ruo Mu, sensing this surge of vitality, instinctively showed great joy and greedily absorbed it. But when it realized that no matter how much it absorbed, the life force from the sapling showed no signs of diminishing, and even seemed to be growing stronger. Its joy turned to fear.

The withered yellow leaves all turned vibrant green. Influenced by the external absorption of life force, countless new buds began to sprout from the body of the Suppressing Heaven Ruo Mu. However... the number of these new buds was simply too many! They densely sprouted from every part of Ruo Mu’s body, occupying every available space. In just half a day, the combined size of these new sprouts surpassed the original Ruo Mu! However, they showed no signs of stopping their growth. Even though Ruo Mu, in panic, had already fled the vicinity of the unknown sapling, immeasurable life force still surged from the green essence it had absorbed. Ruo Mu felt its body becoming heavier and heavier. Those new green branches were taking over its body!

But Ruo Mu was completely powerless. It couldn’t even find a way to resist. Strictly speaking, the new green branches were also part of Ruo Mu. It was just that they grew too fast, exceeding Ruo Mu’s control. Once they matured, they suppressed Ruo Mu itself. It was like the parts naturally eliminated during the body’s metabolism. Ruo Mu frantically felt that it was about to die! Not from exhaustion of life force. But from an overabundance of vitality. This way of death, which it had never imagined before, filled Ruo Mu with immense dread. It desperately tried to do something but found that it could do nothing against this incomprehensible vitality. “Where did that thing come from?” Ruo Mu’s heart was filled with confusion.

Just as the new branches were about to completely devour Ruo Mu, they suddenly stopped growing. Even so, Ruo Mu had already lost control of the ancient tree of the Profound Yellow world. It could only eke out an existence in a remote corner of the ancient tree. A blurry green figure appeared in this space as the situation stabilized. Knowing that this was the culprit that had taken over its body, Ruo Mu stared intently, but dared not make a sound. The visitor was, naturally, Li Fan. Taking over Ruo Mu was easier than he had imagined. This was also the first time Li Fan had unleashed the vitality within his body to its fullest without any restrictions. Its immense potential even surprised Li Fan, who had not fully recovered his memories. The Ruo Mu that controlled the Profound Yellow world’s life force was insignificant compared to the vast life force within his body. If he hadn't realized something was wrong later and stopped in time, Ruo Mu would probably no longer exist in this world. Li Fan glanced at his new body. Frowning, he shook off all the suspended cultivator fruits from the ground. Although they were asleep, they were still affected by the overflowing life force. Not only were their injuries from continuously generating Golden Cores healed, but their life potential was also further stimulated. In the future, forming Nascent Soul and Harmonious Dao would be as easy as drinking water, as long as there were sufficient resources.

Chapter 1526: The Reversing Boat Hidden in the Painting

“Heaven and earth possess the Ruo Mu, day and night consuming life and longevity.”

“Life and death have no cycles, only longevity remains…”

Li Fan slowly recited the lines that belonged to Ruo Mu, while perusing its memories. Ruo Mu itself, however, cowered in a corner, trembling, allowing Li Fan to probe its thoughts.

From the very beginning of the Profound Yellow Realm's creation until now was an incredibly long period of time. But Li Fan, observing from a bystander's perspective, only spent a little over ten breaths.

“This can also be called longevity…” Li Fan shook his head slightly.

Perhaps due to the prolonged state of near-death, Ruo Mu's memories were not particularly clear. There were even large gaps in some critical areas. However, it was enough for Li Fan to gain a general understanding of the Profound Yellow Realm's affairs.

In Ruo Mu's perspective, the Profound Yellow Realm could be roughly divided into three periods.

The first period, from the initial creation of the Profound Yellow Realm to the flourishing of immortal sects. At this time, the Profound Yellow Realm was still under the control of the Immortal Realm. Ruo Mu even retained memories of the True Immortals using it to balance the lifespans of all living beings in the world.

The second period, from the destruction of the Immortal Realm to the sudden demise of the Profound Heaven Sect. During this time, King Profound Heaven replaced the True Immortals as the helmsman of the Profound Yellow Realm. The various modifications made to Ruo Mu and the Profound Yellow Realm by him were still imprinted on Ruo Mu's body.

The third period was from the rule of the Ten Immortal Dao Sects to the present.

This was also the period when Ruo Mu had the most freedom. The Ten Immortal Dao Sects, and later the Myriad Immortal Alliance, and the Preaching Celestial Venerable. Although they claimed to also be able to control Ruo Mu and divide its longevity fruits, in reality, they were qualitatively different from the True Immortals and King Profound Heaven before them.

Their so-called control was merely the act of picking the fruit after it ripened. And if the Profound Yellow Realm's life force circulation became insufficient to bear fruit, they could do nothing.

As for the True Immortals and King Profound Heaven of the past, they could forcibly extract the life force of all living beings in the Profound Yellow Realm through Ruo Mu, condensing longevity fruits.

In simple terms, there was a world of difference between the true controllers and users of Ruo Mu.

This was also why the Myriad Immortal Alliance sat by and did nothing when Ruo Mu became ill and withered. Both the Heavenly Physician and the Preaching Celestial Venerable had tried to heal Ruo Mu. The reason for their failure was the unique creation restraint within Ruo Mu's body.

Created by the True Immortal, only the True Immortal could control it.

Moreover, Ruo Mu and the entire Profound Yellow Realm were not mere ordinary creations of a True Immortal.

However, at this moment, by obtaining absolute control over Ruo Mu through the immense life force within his own body, Li Fan, despite being in a mortal body, felt the restraint on Ruo Mu to be so familiar.

The theoretical chasm between Immortals and mortals did not stop him.

It was as if water flowing into a stream, solely relying on instinct, Li Fan completed the破解 and penetration within moments of sensing the restraint's existence.

The heavily guarded immortal restraint was like no defenses at all in front of the abundant green vitality controlled by Li Fan!

It was at this moment that Li Fan not only became [Ruo Mu] but also its master.

The ancient, towering tree that had regained its vitality was covered in extremely complex patterns at its core.

Although Li Fan seemed to be encountering them for the first time, after a moment of observation, he could quickly understand the meaning represented by these patterns.

What greatly concerned Li Fan were the modification imprints left by King Profound Heaven.

After careful consideration, Li Fan began to understand King Profound Heaven's intentions in modifying Ruo Mu back then.

“To convert a portion of the life force from Ruo Mu and use it independently.”

“Perhaps this is also one of the important reasons for the imbalance of life force circulation in the Profound Yellow Realm and Ruo Mu's rapid withering. But where did this transferred life force go?”

Li Fan frowned slightly, his perspective suddenly shrinking as he surveyed the surroundings of Ruo Mu.

Li Fan did not have much memory of King Profound Heaven that he could recall currently. However, whether it was his own intuitive impression or what he saw in Ruo Mu's memories, this King Profound Heaven was definitely among the strongest in the entire history of the Profound Yellow Realm.

Even though he had disappeared for many years, Li Fan still did not dare to be careless.

Ruo Mu permeated the Profound Yellow Realm.

Soon, Li Fan traced the separated life force to one of its branches.

A seemingly ordinary Taoist temple.

In the Taoist temple, there was an elderly man, a young Taoist boy, and a pool of ordinary pond water.

The old man had Nascent Soul cultivation, and the child did not seem to be human.

And finally…

“Hmm?”

After witnessing this scene, Li Fan instinctively felt a sense of crisis, but it was not from the old man and the child, but from the pond?

Images of countless exotic treasures shining like stars in the pond flashed in Li Fan's mind.

At the end of the images, a cat leaped up and devoured all the exotic treasures of the heavens.

“Fishing pond…”

“Cat?”

Li Fan involuntarily stopped his advance. Even though this current body was merely transformed from a branch of Ruo Mu that he was manipulating.

Without entering the Taoist temple, he merely observed from afar the destination of the life force being channeled from Ruo Mu.

Upon closer examination, Li Fan discovered that the life force was not directed towards the Taoist temple or the fishing pond, but rather into the nearby mountains and forests.

However, the two were very close, and the fishing pond was too conspicuous, which caused Li Fan's initial misjudgment.

Setting aside the fishing pond for the moment, Li Fan tracked the place where Ruo Mu's life force had been channeled.

Upon entering this underground space, he could not help but be surprised.

“This method of condensation…”

“Although a large amount of life force is gathered, there is no overflow. If I weren't Ruo Mu myself right now, even if I were standing on the ground, I wouldn't be able to detect the life force gathered below!”

“It is indeed worth my study.”

Li Fan's biggest problem right now was the uncontrollable overflow of life force. The life force contained within him was simply too immense. Even a fraction of a trillionth of his aura emanating outwards was undoubtedly a supreme treasure to any perceiver. This situation became more severe as Li Fan's potential life force erupted more strongly.

He had actually found a solution here, and could not help but observe it carefully.

It seemed that even with his lost memories, he only had a superficial understanding of the arrangement here. This truly surprised Li Fan.

This was the first time since he started his new round of simulations that he had encountered such a situation.

“Although I cannot understand why, I can at least ascertain the purpose of the life force.”

Li Fan scanned his surroundings.

Within this underground space, a village was buried. Besides some architectural items, there were no other living beings in the village. The guided Ruo Mu life force maintained the village's original form on one hand.

On the other hand, it was all concentrated in one room within the village.

“From the time King Profound Heaven made his modifications until now, the continuously drawn life force has accumulated to an incredibly vast amount. Although it is still far less than mine, it is far from the scale currently displayed.”

Li Fan's heart tightened, and after pondering for a moment, he finally slowly approached.

After standing outside the house for a while, he finally pushed the door open and entered.

According to the flow of life force, he passed through the small courtyard and arrived at the central room of the back house.

Li Fan's footsteps immediately halted.

Because through the door and windows, he vaguely saw a figure standing inside!

However, by observing through Ruo Mu's gathered life force, Li Fan finally confirmed that the figure did not seem to be a living being in the usual sense.

After a moment of hesitation, Li Fan decided to investigate.

Indeed, as he had guessed.

The so-called “figure” in the room was just a painting.

“Why does this painting need life force to nourish it?” Li Fan felt a trace of doubt in his heart.

The painting depicted several young children playing together in the mountains. Among these children, there was a boy and a girl holding hands. Li Fan felt a slight sense of familiarity the moment he saw them.

“This is King Profound Heaven. And…”

As if another switch was activated, the images flashing in Li Fan's mind told him that King Profound Heaven's companion should be his childhood sweetheart.

Li Fan pressed his temples, restoring his brain, which had temporarily exploded from the overwhelming influx of information. Then he continued to examine the painting before him.

Due to the massive influx of life force, the children in the painting seemed to have come to life.

Especially King Profound Heaven, his eyes looked forward, as if looking outside the painting!

In an instant, Li Fan almost had the illusion that the young King Profound Heaven had glanced at him!

But as he continued to study, Li Fan discovered that young King Profound Heaven was not the most special in this painting.

In an inconspicuous corner of the painting, outside a house in the village, lay a long-haired man in tattered clothes.

His face was hidden by his beard and hair, so his appearance could not be seen.

However, this man looked at the young children playing outside the village with a strange expression.

On the man's chest rested a palm-sized wooden boat.

Upon close inspection, one could faintly see the faces of the children outside the village through the window of the wooden boat!

“What does this mean?”

This painting seemed to possess a special magic, unconsciously captivating Li Fan's mind.

And no matter what he was pondering in his mind, his gaze would eventually fall upon that wooden boat.

The wooden boat seemed to have undergone the baptism of time and was already battered and broken, as if it would shatter completely at any moment.

However, perhaps due to the nourishment of infinite life force, it could still barely maintain its original form.

As Li Fan watched, he saw his own figure in the boat's window, as if in a trance. Just as he couldn't help but reach out to touch the wooden boat,

He met the gaze of his reflection.

Previously lost memories suddenly resurfaced, causing Li Fan to retract his hand as if electrocuted.

“King Profound Heaven, perhaps the person with the greatest 'luck' in the history of the Profound Yellow Realm. He was always able to turn danger into safety and fortune from misfortune. Even during the Great Tribulation of the destruction of the Immortal Realm, when countless Immortals perished, he was able to escape safely…”

Li Fan's gaze focused on the wooden boat in the painting: “Could this be the legendary [Contra-Flow Boat]?”

“Three Treasures of Seclusion…”

Li Fan forcibly summoned his life force to repair his severe injuries, desperately trying to recall more.

“However, this treasure was created after the destruction of the Immortal Realm, so how could it have been in King Profound Heaven's hands before the Great Tribulation descended?”

“Contra-flow… Could it be that he truly succeeded?”

Li Fan could not help but turn his gaze to the disheveled man holding the wooden boat.

Ultimately, his current body was not enough to support Li Fan in recovering all his memories.

Li Fan temporarily withdrew from his memories.

Looking at the painting before him, he showed a rare look of hesitation.

This painting had been nourished by Ruo Mu's life force for ten thousand years.

And now, Li Fan had become the new Ruo Mu. Theoretically, he could use the life force to take away the painting.

However, he would then have to face the unknown dangers hidden within the painting.

Li Fan did not act for the time being, pondering the matter of King Profound Heaven's disappearance.

“I seem to have investigated this matter before. King Profound Heaven should have finally disappeared within the fishing pond.”

“As for whether he disappeared voluntarily or passively…”

“Then this painting was intentionally left behind. Was it left for his childhood sweetheart? But in his communication, he did not mention this matter. Obviously, he did not want her to know.”

“If the Contra-Flow Boat is truly hidden within this painting, then why did King Profound Heaven abandon such a treasure that could change destiny against the heavens?”

……

These kinds of questions clearly could not be answered by mere thought.

In the minor Great Xuan world, in the Grand Tutor's mansion in Xuan Jing City, Li Fan's main body attempted it once, ensuring that he could return to the beginning of the simulation at any time. Feeling the immense life force within him, Li Fan's eyes flashed with a sharp light, and he made up his mind.

“Hesitating and shrinking back leads to no great achievements. It's just a simulation anyway. Even if I get seriously injured again, it's just losing my memory and being force-fed a few bowls of talisman water.”

“Rather than leaving this mystery as a potential disaster. It's better to understand its true nature now!”

“Since the life force is useful to it, then give it!”

……

In the Profound Yellow Realm, Li Fan also took action accordingly.

With the doubt disappearing from his eyes, he slowly exhaled a breath of longevity, directing it towards the painting before him.

This breath of longevity was condensed since he began cultivating in this life.

Compared to the life force he gave to Kou Hong, Dao Xuan Zi, and even the one used for possession of Ruo Mu, it was several magnitudes greater.

Even Li Fan himself turned pale after releasing this condensed energy.

However, the effect was immediate.

Li Fan stared intently at the changes ahead.

Faced with the suddenly descending life force, the painting did not refuse it. No matter how much life force it was, it accepted it all.

Strands of green appeared within the painting.

As life force poured in, the scene in the painting also underwent corresponding changes.

On the ground, green grass and flowers flourished. In the sky, colorful auspicious clouds descended in abundance.

And the wooden boat, which was originally close to decay and damage, was renewed at a visible speed.

The changes in the wooden boat attracted the attention of the sloppy man who controlled it.

His beard and hair flew, revealing his hidden true face.

The man suddenly looked up, looking outside the painting.

His eyes met Li Fan's.

Then Li Fan felt a dizzying sensation, and his consciousness was instantly drawn into the painting!

Before he could struggle, he felt a hand press on his shoulder.

“The Great Dao of Longevity?”

The sloppy man opposite him asked with great surprise.

Seeing Li Fan's eyes meet his reflection, Li Fan's mind was filled with a sense of familiarity.

Chapter 1527: Hidden Emperor Builds Immortal Boat

Instantly finding himself under someone else's control, Li Fan was alarmed but did not show it verbally.

He also asked, "The Contra-Flow Boat?"

His eyes were fixed on the sloppy man's shoulder, and the wooden boat, which looked renewed, was on it.

The sloppy man chuckled and released Li Fan.

"As expected of a disciple of Shou Qiu Gong, your knowledge is indeed extraordinary." He did not hide anything at all and openly admitted the identity of the treasure in his hand.

"Shou Qiu Gong..." Li Fan muttered the name, which was both familiar and strange, in his heart. Numerous images flashed through his mind. At the same time, Li Fan sensed the anomaly in his own body.

After entering this painting, when he recalled the past, he inexplicably did not feel the previous headache. It seemed he could freely browse through past memories.

But a subtle intuition told Li Fan that if he did so, the outcome would certainly not be good.

The strong sense of contradiction made Li Fan instinctively feel the strangeness of this place.

Seeing Li Fan's silence, the sloppy man was not annoyed. Instead, he changed the subject: "Since you are a disciple of Shou Qiu, you should not covet my Contra-Flow Boat. Little brother, why have you come here?"

"I thought I would never see anyone else in this life," the sloppy man said with some emotion.

Li Fan noticed that although he had transferred a large amount of life force into the painting, it seemed to have been completely absorbed by the Contra-Flow Boat. As for the sloppy man, the owner of the Contra-Flow Boat, he did not receive even a sliver. He remained in the same condition as before.

Although his appearance was that of a middle-aged man, he exuded an indescribable aura of death.

Li Fan, who nurtured abundant life force within his body, was naturally extremely sensitive to life force.

During this period of silence, he finally confirmed that the sloppy man before him was not a real being, but merely a projection or something similar.

However, Li Fan did not let his guard down because of this.

After all, the power displayed by the sloppy man just now was truly terrifying. Such a projection alone possessed such oppressive power. It was hard to imagine what realm the sloppy man was in during his prime.

"The Great Dao of Longevity, disciple of Shou Qiu."

"Could this be the source of the] infinite life force within me?" Li Fan vaguely recalled more.

Since the other party did not show any particularly obvious hostility, Li Fan decided to press his luck and probe further.

He said in a deep voice, "Senior, aren't you being too generalized? How can a disciple of Shou Qiu not covet a treasure like the Contra-Flow Boat? Reversing time, what a miraculous opportunity! It is perhaps no less than the Great Dao of Longevity."

The sloppy man looked at Li Fan with some surprise upon hearing this.

Then, as if realizing something, he let out a relieved laugh. He then directly threw the wooden boat in his arms towards Li Fan.

"Shou Qiu Gong must be trapped in the [Eternal Silence Void], which is why he only passed down his teachings and not his disciples. Take a look at this Contra-Flow Boat. See if it is as miraculous as you imagine."

Since the other party dared to throw it, Li Fan dared to catch it.

Holding the supreme treasure, the Contra-Flow Boat, Li Fan began to examine it carefully.

As if sensing the endless life force within Li Fan, the treasure boat became even more greedy, attempting to snatch it like a black hole. Li Fan did not completely block the transmission of life force, but consciously continued to channel thin streams of life force. At the same time, using this strand of life force, he sensed the internal condition of the Contra-Flow Boat.

He had always been curious why this treasure, said to be able to reverse time, needed life force to sustain itself, just like living beings.

Although the wooden boat was only palm-sized, it felt as heavy as a mountain. Li Fan used all his strength to barely hold onto it. His divine sense followed the flowing life force into the treasure boat's interior.

He discovered that the condition inside the Contra-Flow Boat was even worse than its exterior.

Shocking cracks spread throughout every corner of the treasure boat, like terrifying scars. Through these cracks, Li Fan vaguely saw countless scenes that did not belong to this time and space.

Li Fan vaguely understood that this was not his hallucination. These scenes were definitely not mere illusions. If one accidentally fell into these cracks, they might indeed get lost in the turbulent flow of time.

Avoiding these extremely dangerous cracks, Li Fan's divine sense attempted to lock onto the direction of the life force within the entire Contra-Flow Boat.

Affected by the pervasive spatial cracks, his perception of life force also became chaotic. After considerable effort, he finally figured it out.

“Contra-flow, contra-flow.”

Li Fan crouched down and gently touched the deck of the treasure boat with his hand, musing, “Although it appears to be an object, it is actually a living being. To flow upstream, it also requires the expenditure of one's own lifespan. Moreover, under the erosion of the power of time, it consumes hundreds or even thousands of times more. Furthermore, besides life force, it seems to consume something else…”

Li Fan narrowed his eyes.

From his perspective, this Contra-Flow Boat was like an elder on the verge of death. Although it tried its best to absorb external life force to maintain its survival, it could at best only keep itself barely alive. And it was hard to say how long such a life-sustaining state could last.

If Li Fan had not come here today and contributed a large amount of life force, this world-shattering immortal treasure might have silently disappeared along with this painting one day.

“How could this be?”

Li Fan could not help but feel a sense of disappointment.

He thought he had found news of a treasure that could reverse time, but unexpectedly, this treasure was in a severely depleted and almost destroyed state.

After checking several times and confirming this fact, Li Fan withdrew his consciousness from the Contra-Flow Boat.

“How is it? Even if I gave you this treasure boat, would you dare to take it? You would probably drown in the river of time before you could even reach your target time node…” the sloppy man said with a half-smile.

He didn't expect Li Fan to not play by the usual rules and directly replied, "Yes, of course I want it."

"Even a damaged Contra-Flow Boat represents a chance for a desperate escape. Even if the probability of success is infinitesimally small, when one is truly cornered, it is the only glimmer of hope." Li Fan said with a solemn expression.

The sloppy man was stunned for a moment, and the smile on his lips slowly disappeared.

After a long silence, he finally said in a melancholic tone, "What you said is not wrong."

"If Xuan Yuanhong had possessed this kind of awareness back then, he wouldn't have left the Contra-Flow Boat here."

Li Fan heard the familiar name and immediately followed up, "Xuan Yuanhong… is he the King Profound Heaven of the Profound Yellow Realm? Did he achieve his past accomplishments thanks to this Contra-Flow Boat?"

The sloppy man's eyes revealed a look of reminiscence, and he shook his head slightly, saying, "In my opinion, Xuan Yuanhong's achievements were a combination of three parts luck and three parts his own effort and disposition. As for the remaining four parts, the Contra-Flow Boat only accounted for half. As for the other half..."

"The Mountains and Seas Fishing Ground deserves the credit," the sloppy man's gaze drifted outside the painting.

"Mountains and Seas Fishing Ground?" Li Fan was first stunned, then realized that the other party was referring to the fishing pond.

"However, why is it named after Mountains and Seas?"

In a trance, the scene of boundless oceans and continuous mountains suddenly reappeared in Li Fan's mind, along with endless light and heat. The scene of countless possibilities melting in the scorching light.

It seemed that he was one step closer to fully recovering his memories.

Just at this critical moment, the sloppy man clapped his hand on Li Fan's shoulder again.

He pulled Li Fan back from the fantasy of his memories to reality.

Li Fan then realized his dangerous situation in reality.

Whether it was the clone in the Profound Yellow Realm or the main body in the minor Great Xuan world.

His head had already exploded into a pool of blood.

Even a large part of his body was gradually evaporating from top to bottom due to the shock caused by the phenomenon of mountains and seas. Even the "Great Dao of Longevity" within his body could not stop this trend of disappearance. If the sloppy man had not woken him up in time, Li Fan would have likely become like an illusion, ceasing to exist.

"Your condition… seems a bit off?" the sloppy man looked at Li Fan with some surprise and uncertainty.

Li Fan cupped his hands and said, "Senior, you indeed have discerning eyes. To be honest, I seem to have made a mistake during my cultivation, and most of my past memories have vanished. I can barely recall anything, and my body suffers severe backlash. I have re-cultivated from a mortal all the way to this point, relying entirely on instinct and the assistance of the Great Dao of Longevity within me."

"As for what Senior mentioned about Shou Qiu Gong..."

"I do have some impression. I also remember some vague images," Li Fan said, projecting a solitary figure of Shou Qiu guarding the sea onto the sloppy man.

Upon seeing Shou Qiu Gong, the sloppy man's expression immediately became solemn, showing respect.

Then, he carefully observed Li Fan again before slowly saying, "The Great Dao of Longevity within you is indeed presided over by Shou Qiu Gong. Since Shou Qiu Gong is present, there is no falsehood."

"However, I only had the good fortune to hear Shou Qiu Gong explain some things about the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas back then. I don't know the specifics, so I can't help you much."

"But don't worry too much. With the protection of the Great Dao of Longevity, even if this world is annihilated, you will remain safe." The sloppy man's tone carried a hint of envy.

Li Fan nodded upon hearing this, "Thank you for your guidance, Senior. By the way, what is your name, Senior?"

The sloppy man waved his hand and said, "A dead person, their name and surname are like passing clouds, why mention them again?"

Li Fan replied, "One day, when I recover my memories and return to Master's side, I will certainly explain today's events to Master. Although Senior has perished, there is still this trace of a phantom surviving. With Master's divine abilities, perhaps he can even bring about reincarnation."

The sloppy man seemed to have given up hope at first.

However, after a moment, as if thinking of something, he changed his mind.

"I was the Heaven Emperor of the Immortal Realm."

"I governed for a thousand years, undisturbed, and then retired. When the Dao Annihilation descended and intensified, I secretly sought a method of salvation. This Broken Chessboard Dao Field was built under my leadership." The sloppy man spoke calmly.

Immortal Emperor in seclusion, Broken Chessboard Dao Field, Tribulation of Dao Annihilation...

With each keyword, corresponding passages of memory were triggered in Li Fan's mind.

It took a long time before Li Fan could barely recover from the severe injury.

Li Fan's gaze towards the sloppy man changed.

"Senior, you were once an Immortal Emperor of the Immortal Realm, you must have reached the peak of perfection. Why did you end up in this state?" Although Li Fan's words were somewhat harsh, he spoke directly and with full of doubts.

"Is it because of this item?" Li Fan pointed at the Contra-Flow Boat.

The Heaven Emperor nodded, "This is one reason. But the main reason is that my cultivation was insufficient, and I failed at the last moment."

He sighed, seemingly lost in past memories.

After a while, he continued, "Have you noticed the life force within this treasure boat? You have also entered this treasure boat with your divine sense. Did you notice it?"

"I did perceive it. This treasure, though like an object, is actually a spirit."

"That's because this Contra-Flow Boat was made from my own body," the Heaven Emperor chuckled.

Li Fan's eyes widened in shock.

He looked at the sloppy man before him, certain that he was not joking.

"But the world's legends say that the Contra-Flow Boat was created by a so-called 'Anti-Immortal'..."

"Oh? Anti-Immortal? I haven't heard of that. But there might not be only one Contra-Flow Boat in the world. As long as one understands the Dao of Contra-Flow, one can create a new one, even if they haven't heard of it," the Heaven Emperor said calmly.

"Understanding the Dao of Contra-Flow?" Li Fan seemed to have thought of something.

"King Profound Heaven?"

The Heaven Emperor remained noncommittal, "I am merely a lonely wandering spirit, how could I know everything about the outside world? However, if there is anyone in this world who could recreate the Contra-Flow Boat, I think Xuan Yuanhong is the most likely candidate. After all, when we parted ways, his understanding of the Dao of Contra-Flow had already reached a considerable level."

Li Fan remained silent.

"Some things can only be understood by experiencing them oneself. For example, perhaps most things in the world can be changed by reversing time. But it is precisely those tiny portions that cannot be changed that ultimately determine the final outcome of the river of time."

"If you don't have the power to change the entire ocean, even reversing time is merely a futile struggle." The Heaven Emperor spoke calmly.

Li Fan felt a sense of familiarity listening to his words.

It seemed he himself had had similar thoughts before.

"Irrelevant to the final outcome."

The four words involuntarily surged into his mind, corresponding to the scene described by the Heaven Emperor.

"Although I was once an Immortal Emperor, how many Immortal Emperors have there been in the Immortal Realm?"

"How many people could transcend like Shou Qiu Gong?"

"You, as a disciple of Shou Qiu, have obtained the Great Dao of Longevity. You already have the foundation for transcendence. You are far stronger than ordinary Immortal Emperors."

Although Li Fan had been praised by the Heaven Emperor like this all along, he felt no honor, but rather unease.

It was as if he did not particularly approve of the identity of a disciple of Shou Qiu.

"Strange."

"Could it be..."

Li Fan suppressed this strange thought in his heart and followed the Heaven Emperor's words, asking, "A figure like Master should possess the power to change the entire ocean, as you described?"

"There is only a slight possibility. In the Eternal Silence Void, even Shou Qiu Gong would find it difficult to move forward."

Chapter 1528: Sparks Save the Mortal World

"Eternal Silence Void?" This was the second time Li Fan had heard this term from the Heaven Emperor.

Although he had lost most of his memories, in Li Fan's impression, Shou Qiu Gong was still an extremely powerful figure rarely seen in the world. And such a figure would also find it difficult to move forward?

"What kind of place is this so-called Eternal Silence Void?" Li Fan could not help but ask.

"What place?" The Heaven Emperor's expression was somewhat strange.

He gestured to their surroundings, "This place, that place, everywhere you have seen... can actually be called the Eternal Silence Void. Even if it is not now, it is destined to fall into it eventually. This is the fate of all beings in the Mountains and Seas."

The Heaven Emperor's words made Li Fan even more confused.

However, this former Immortal Emperor, who had perished and only had a phantom remnant, seemed intent on speaking in riddles and continued to talk about seemingly irrelevant matters: "Back then, I transformed myself into the Contra-Flow Boat and traveled upstream in the river of time again and again. Initially, with my strength, which was almost enough to transcend, I could only barely return to three thousand years ago..."

"Three thousand years seem long, but it is merely a fleeting moment. With foreknowledge, I made many arrangements in advance for the arrival of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, but it was all in vain."

"I could save some True Immortals, but not the Immortal Realm."

"So I tried again and again. Attempting to return to a more distant past to gain more preparation time. As my understanding of the Dao of Contra-Flow deepened, the upper limit of time I could backtrack also increased. From three thousand years, five thousand years, then ten thousand years, fifty thousand years!"

Although the Heaven Emperor's tone was calm, the content of his words already revealed the demeanor of a peerless expert.

"Even though the Contra-Flow Boat was filled with cracks, I still held onto hope. Until..."

"That day, I finally saw the end of the river of time."

Infinite reminiscence surged into the Heaven Emperor's eyes.

"The end of the river of time? How is that possible?" Li Fan was shaken by the news. His eyes were filled with disbelief. Suddenly, some images flashed in his mind, causing a slight sting. After a moment, Li Fan finally began to understand.

The Heaven Emperor continued, "Just like a great river formed out of nothing, I, who am traveling upstream, no matter how hard I struggle in the river water, cannot take another step forward!"

"The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation?" Li Fan slowly uttered four words.

The Heaven Emperor nodded, "That's right! The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, this terrifying disaster, not only devours our world at the present time point but also erases the traces of our existence throughout history. It reduces everything in the mortal world to complete nothingness!"

"Seventy-four thousand, eight hundred and seventy-six years. This is the upper limit of the river of time that I saw while traveling upstream. However, I haven't embarked on a journey again for a long time. In the years I've spent in the painting, this number has probably decreased significantly..." the Heaven Emperor sighed.

Even just by listening, Li Fan deeply felt the irresistible pressure. What could be more despairing than fate that could not be changed even by reversing time? He felt as if he had followed the Heaven Emperor of the past and personally experienced the terrifying scene of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, step by step, descending from the upper reaches of the river of time.

Suddenly, a flash of inspiration struck Li Fan, and he seemed to understand, "So, the Eternal Silence Void you mentioned refers to..."

The Heaven Emperor nodded, "That's right. The Eternal Silence Void refers to those places that have already been swallowed by the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation."

Although he received the explanation, greater doubts arose in his heart.

"Senior, since you said that the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation has swallowed everything of the past, then how did my Master, Shou Qiu Gong, and others 'travel' to those places that should not exist? Traveling through the void of time, even Master would face mortal peril. Why would they risk their lives like this?"

Facing Li Fan's many questions, the Heaven Emperor did not choose to conceal anything and answered them all.

With a wave of his large sleeve, a vivid, flowing river of time appeared between the two.

The Heaven Emperor used his finger as a sword and lightly drew a line. The brilliant image of the river of time directly erased a small segment from the front, leaving only the latter half, continuing to flow through time and space in a strange scene.

"Have you ever wondered why the river of time was completely swallowed, yet we, who are in the downstream, still exist?"

"Without the foundation of the past, can we exist independently? Just like if I went back to your mortal phase and killed you directly, would you still be standing before me now?"

Li Fan narrowed his eyes. He had indeed considered this question and subconsciously felt it was impossible. But the fact that the entire mortal world still existed led Li Fan to have to believe this inference.

It seemed that the disappearance of the upper reaches of the river of time did not directly affect the downstream. Only when the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation truly reached the "present" would the entire space-time disappear completely.
