The Heaven Emperor looked deeply at Li Fan, "In the past, I, including the many experts of the Immortal Realm, and even the Three Sage Lords, all thought this way. Until later..."

"We realized we were terribly wrong!"

The Heaven Emperor did not explain in detail how the Immortal Realm's celestial executioners discovered their cognitive errors, but directly stated with unshakeable certainty the conclusion.

He waved his hand again, and the horizontal image of the river of time suddenly became vertical.

The image suddenly shrunk countless times, and the upper part of the river where it disappeared was revealed.

"The river of time still has its foundation. The fact that we are still alive in the world today is the best proof. Its being swallowed by the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation is merely an illusion."

Li Fan looked at the miraculous scene displayed by the Heaven Emperor before him.

A continuous, sky-reaching river, emitting a faint blue light, was being stained by unknown darkness.

It had become intermittent.

"The invasion of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation does not proceed in order from ancient to present. Instead, it happens synchronously in every part of the river. Some historical segments have completely disappeared without warning. While some places have temporarily survived."

"We are within such a surviving node!"

The Heaven Emperor's eyes looked towards the distant past of the river of time, "The same question remains. The reason we can exist is precisely because, in that seemingly completely swallowed darkness, there are still people struggling tenaciously!"

"Should they ever completely fall..."

"We will also cease to exist."

"We won't even be aware of how we disappeared, as if we never should have existed in this world. At that time, no matter how powerful one is, even Shou Qiu Gong, who wields the Great Dao of Longevity, will not be able to escape destruction." The Heaven Emperor sighed deeply.

"!" Li Fan's mind trembled.

With a rapid turn of his thoughts, he finally understood the reason why Shou Qiu Gong had gone to the Eternal Silence Void.

It was rescue.

And self-preservation.

"Once this was understood, the goals of all the powerful beings in the mortal world became unified. While maintaining their own existence, they crossed the desolate time and space, going to the previous surviving node to provide assistance. This cycle continued, eventually..."

"Returning to the distant past where the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation could be completely resolved."

"It's a pity that my lifespan has reached its limit. I have the will, but not the strength. Traveling upstream is my limit. Crossing the desolate time and space is far beyond my ability." The Heaven Emperor sighed again, his expression somewhat dejected.

The truth revealed by the Heaven Emperor far exceeded Li Fan's expectations.

It seemed that in his past memories, there was no such acknowledgment.

His brain, in extreme shock, was unable to accept and process it for a while.

After a long period of silence, Li Fan suddenly realized something and quickly asked, "Could it be that our sudden awakening and knowledge of the current state of the river of time was because..."

Li Fan pointed to the section above himself in the intermittent river of time before him.

"Did someone come from the future, traversing the desolate time and space to aid us?" Li Fan's voice trembled slightly.

The Heaven Emperor nodded solemnly.

Li Fan gazed at the scene before him, seemingly seeing the efforts of all powerful beings uniting to save the devoured river of time.

His heart was stirred, and he was unable to calm down for a long time.

After a brief moment of excitement, he stared at the scene before him, and many more questions arose in his mind.

How exactly could one traverse the desolate time and space?

And how could one be sure that returning to the most ancient past would also find a solution to the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation? What if countless people worked together, endured hardships, and ultimately found that everything was irreversible...

What should they do then?

……

After pondering for a long time, Li Fan could not help but express the doubts in his heart.

The Heaven Emperor's expression was solemn, "If we don't try, then all that awaits us is annihilation. By trying, perhaps we can find a glimmer of hope."

"We can only hope that those powerful beings in the ancient past can hold on until the reinforcements arrive."

The Heaven Emperor raised his hand and pointed to the sky outside.

"Know that those who can go to the Other Shore are all earth-shattering powerful beings. And those qualified to traverse the desolate time and space and enter the Eternal Silence Void are even rarer than one in a billion. Such individuals, even without any hope, will still fight with all their might. How could they be deterred by the possibility of this crisis?" The Heaven Emperor's expression and tone were unusually solemn.

"Although you have received the inheritance of Shou Qiu and transcendence is almost certain, if you still have this mindset, you may not be qualified to progress further on a larger stage."

"The Great Dao of Longevity can only protect you in living a long and free life in this realm."

Li Fan looked at the section of the river of time pointed to by the Heaven Emperor, with an expression of being taught.

"Who among us cultivators, upon hearing of this plan, would not be filled with righteous indignation and willing to sacrifice themselves? I am filled with regret that due to my own fate and fortune, I cannot participate."

"However, you still have a great opportunity!"

"Stumbling into this place might also be destined." The Heaven Emperor said, gradually murmuring to himself. His expression seemed to have thought of something incredibly exciting, and his illusory body, originally shrouded in death, slowly emitted a special aura.

"Lingering alive here is no longer meaningful. So, today, I will impart to you all my insights into the Dao of Contra-Flow!"

"If one day, you can go to the Eternal Silence Void in my stead and provide assistance, then my sacrifice today will not have been in vain!"

The Heaven Emperor seemed to suddenly achieve enlightenment.

His entire body emitted a bright light.

His figure gradually floated into the Contra-Flow Boat, and in a flash, merged with the boat itself.

The Contra-Flow Boat suddenly floated up, and then in a flash, shot towards Li Fan. Li Fan, who had been deeply moved by the Heaven Emperor's heroic words just moments ago, felt immense gratitude.

However, at this moment, the Contra-Flow Boat flew towards him uncontrollably, and he instinctively wanted to dodge.

But Li Fan was no match for the Heaven Emperor.

Even though the Heaven Emperor was just a phantom remnant.

Therefore, he could only watch as the Contra-Flow Boat flew into his own body.

Boom!

The river of time displayed before him by the Heaven Emperor seemed to have crashed into Li Fan's mind all at once.

Everything the Heaven Emperor experienced while traveling upstream in the river of time was replayed in Li Fan's mind.

It was the same as being engulfed by his own lost memories.

However, the Heaven Emperor had clearly considered Li Fan's "fragile" tolerance.

Under the constant barrage of fleeting images, the irrelevant details slowly faded away.

Only certain critical matters and the Heaven Emperor's insights into the Dao of Contra-Flow remained, as if precipitated.

The Heaven Emperor's inheritance seemed to have resonated with Li Fan's lost memories.

The scenes he had experienced in the past were stimulated and could no longer be suppressed, erupting from the depths of his mind.

"Is it real?!"

Among the many scenes, Li Fan grasped the most crucial matter.

He finally remembered the name of the supreme treasure he possessed, and its various miraculous uses.

"What's going on? How did Revert All become like this?"

"The functions of Endless Cycle and many others are gone, and even the anchors I set have all disappeared!"

Although he had recalled some lost memories, Li Fan's mind did not calm down.

Instead, it became even more turbulent.

Coupled with the Heaven Emperor's inheritance, the situation worsened.

In the Profound Yellow Realm, in the secret chamber of the Grand Tutor's mansion, Li Fan's main body had already exploded into a pool of flesh and blood from the immense pressure. The aura of longevity continuously flowed from the remaining corpse, trying to repair the injuries.

However, the turmoil suddenly triggered in Li Fan's mind this time had already exceeded his capacity to bear.

Even the Great Dao of Longevity he upheld seemed unable to save him.

"Revert All! Revert All! Revert All!"

Seeing that it was futile and helpless, Li Fan could only cry out in his heart.

But a familiar scene occurred again.

Revert All seemed not to have heard him and did not respond at all.

Li Fan called out several more times, unwilling to give up.

The result remained the same.

In a state of shock and anger, looking at his body being gradually swallowed, Li Fan inevitably felt despair.

But, in a daze, Li Fan recalled the Heaven Emperor's words just now.

"Such a person, even without any hope, will still struggle with all their might!"

The panic gradually subsided, and Li Fan's eyes were filled only with unwavering determination.

In an instant, he had found his path to survival.

Contra-Flow Boat!

Chapter 1529: Cross-Temporal Anchor

Although the upper half of his body had become a pool of flesh and blood, Li Fan could still "feel" that the Contra-Flow Wooden Boat gifted by the Heaven Emperor still quietly existed within his "mind."

At this moment, as Li Fan's desire for contra-flow intensified, the Contra-Flow Boat began to emit a crystalline, warm white light. A wisp of green also seemed to accompany the white light.

The scene in the real world began to dissolve and distort, like a painting splashed with water.

An almost unbearable pain also appeared in Li Fan's mind. It was as if billions of chains were simultaneously piercing his skull. Then, with high-speed rotation, these billions of chains churned within Li Fan's mind.

“Aaaaaah!”

Even without a head, Li Fan's remaining flesh and blood began to convulse and tremble from this indescribable pain.

Although the Heaven Emperor imparted all his insights into the Dao of Contra-Flow, he had never mentioned that the side effects of activating the Contra-Flow Boat were so terrifying.

Li Fan vaguely recalled that in his past simulations, he had also endured various painful torments, but none of them were even one-thousandth of what he was suffering now.

The pain synchronized with his flesh and blood, divine soul, and will, and memories.

It seemed to have spread to Li Fan's true core.

Faint sounds of wind and rain could be heard gradually from all around, and countless "water droplets" struck him head-on.

Each drop was like the sharpest blade in the world, cutting Li Fan.

Li Fan felt even more pain.

However, the invisible, immense power from his memories had already completely crushed his remaining body. With flesh and blood gone, Li Fan, who wanted to survive, had no retreat.

Amidst boundless pain, he managed to maintain a sliver of clarity and continued to maintain the power of the Contra-Flow Boat from dissipating.

The sound of wind and rain grew louder.

The water droplets hitting him were no longer isolated, but connected into lines.

The Contra-Flow Boat let out loud rumbling sounds amidst constant collisions. It seemed on the verge of disintegration.

Fortunately, at the critical moment, the hidden green lights erupted, quickly repairing the damage to the boat.

After enduring for nine breaths.

The lines of water droplets finally converged into a river.

In an instant, Li Fan fell into it. All the pain he felt disappeared at this moment.

He seemed to detach himself from the entire world.

His perspective rose from the minor Great Xuan world and the Profound Yellow Realm. After a moment of stillness, it began to rewind.

Li Fan saw the scene of himself entering the sealed village below the Mountains and Seas Fishing Ground, saw the scene of himself suppressing and subduing the Profound Yellow Ruo Mu. He saw himself as the Grand Tutor, dominating the world. He saw himself regaining his memories and being forced to drink disgusting talisman water…

The river of time flowed turbidly, and the Contra-Flow Boat traveled upstream precariously.

It seemed that with the slightest carelessness, it was in danger of capsizing.

However, precisely because of his experiences in past years, these existences were like anchors, allowing Li Fan to "borrow strength" every time he traveled upstream for a period, stabilizing his figure in the river.

But when Li Fan returned to the anchor point of one year ago, and wanted to travel further upstream, things changed.

The moment he passed this important temporal node, the scouring of the river of time instantly became thousands of times more violent.

It was as if he had entered a more muddy and turbulent area from a clear, rushing river channel. Li Fan could no longer see any scenes from the river of time.

The surroundings were filled with swirling lines formed by the fusion of millions of colors, obscuring the perception of Li Fan, the upstream traveler.

The terrifying power that suddenly erupted in the river almost directly destroyed the unprepared Contra-Flow Boat. The white light on the boat was too weak compared to the surging river, even less than a single drop of water in the river. However, it desperately maintained the white light, preventing the boat from being crushed on the spot.

Li Fan knew the consequences of failing to travel upstream.

It was not as simple as returning to reality.

He would completely disappear from history, leaving no trace of his existence in the world.

Li Fan desperately tried to reverse his fate.

But a single person was too small compared to the vast river of time. Even with the understanding of the Dao of Contra-Flow, being in the river at this moment, he could only obey fate.

It seemed like a desperate situation.

However, Li Fan still did not give up on surviving and continued to operate the Contra-Flow Boat, adhering to the Dao of Contra-Flow.

While struggling, Li Fan also had many unanswered questions in his heart.

According to the Heaven Emperor's inheritance, the contra-flow journey should not have been so difficult. At the very least, when backtracking within a thousand years, even a damaged and almost disintegrating Contra-Flow Boat should have been able to handle the waves in the river.

But now, Li Fan had only traveled upstream for about fifty years, and the waves in the river had already reached a scale comparable to traveling ten thousand years back!

Remembering the Heaven Emperor's experience, the further one traveled back in time, the greater the pressure would be, increasing exponentially.

And now, Li Fan had just started, but he had encountered such great resistance...

It was hard to imagine how great the waves would be when he traveled back ten thousand or thirty thousand years!

“How could this be!”

Li Fan was extremely puzzled in his heart.

Suddenly, he recalled the images of his own experiences that he had glimpsed in the river before.

When these images were present, the river's behavior was within the normal range. But after the images disappeared, the river of waves surged, wanting to choose him and devour him!

“Perhaps, it's because I never truly experienced this period of time. Without the anchor as support, the resistance has increased a millionfold?” Li Fan's inspiration struck, and this thought arose in his heart.

However, even knowing the reason for the sudden surge of the river, Li Fan was now in a predicament.

The river of time was murky, making it impossible to distinguish directions. The immense scouring force was constantly "cutting" Li Fan.

It made it impossible for him to find a safe temporal node to "land."

Amidst the waves, the light of the Contra-Flow Boat grew dimmer and dimmer, seeming on the verge of collapse.

It seemed like it would be destroyed in the next moment.

Just at this critical juncture, a boundless and infinite green light suddenly erupted out of nowhere.

Like a wave-suppressing pearl, it temporarily suppressed the storm in the river.

This green light seemed to originate from Li Fan's body, but in the endless river of time, countless dots of green light simultaneously flashed from ancient times to the present.

They were like beacons, illuminating the path forward for Li Fan.

Although their effect seemed slightly inferior to his own anchor, they were undoubtedly Li Fan's lifelines.

The Contra-Flow Boat followed the direction of the green light and moved forward.

One hundred years, three hundred years, five hundred years…

Until one thousand years, five thousand years…

Li Fan's green light was already beginning to be depleted.

The green beacons in the river grew dim again, gradually disappearing into the surging history.

However, Li Fan still could not find a safe landing point outside the illumination of the green light.

“If I were to forcibly leave the river of time and return to reality right now, there might be two outcomes.”

“One is unfortunate death, being crushed into dust by the scouring of time, becoming a speck of dust in history.”

“The second is to luckily succeed in landing…”

“Let’s wait a bit longer.”

Although Li Fan's experience in traveling upstream was mostly derived from the Heaven Emperor's inheritance, their encounters in the river of time were vastly different.

Li Fan had endured more turbulent waves, but in contrast, he did not feel much of the erosion and stripping sensation of the river of time that the Heaven Emperor had so feared.

Keep in mind that the Heaven Emperor's first attempt at traveling upstream, which lasted only three thousand years, made him feel like he was about to completely dissolve into the river of time and had to return to reality.

But now, Li Fan's first attempt had already traced back several thousand years. Moreover, Li Fan did not feel much pressure from this so-called stripping.

If it weren't for the protection and guidance of the Great Dao of Longevity, and the waves in the river being too fierce, making it difficult to navigate upstream.

Li Fan even felt that he could continue to backtrack like this.

Although the pressure of erosion was small, the further back in time Li Fan went, the greater the pressure he endured.

When time was traced back to about eight thousand years ago,

The waves in the river of time had completely lost the conditions for navigation.

Li Fan was swept into it, unable to even discern the direction of time.

He carefully observed every detail in the river of time, striving to find a glimmer of hope at the last moment.

However, he was ultimately not a lucky person.

Bang!

The Contra-Flow Boat began to disintegrate. Without the protection of the treasure boat, Li Fan, directly exposed to the river of time, faced pressures that were thousands of times greater.

Li Fan finally understood what the Heaven Emperor meant by the sensation of melting.

With each scouring of the river, Li Fan lost a part of himself.

Cultivation, divine abilities, enlightenment experiences...

These were like external objects, gradually shedding away with the scouring of the river.

Only the core within continued to struggle.

When the true core was damaged, Li Fan instinctively felt an extreme fatal threat. He knew he couldn't delay any longer. Even crashing "land" prematurely was better than dying in the river of time.

Manipulating the dilapidated Contra-Flow Boat, Li Fan gradually broke free from the insights of the Dao of Contra-Flow.

The scene of the river of time slowly receded from his vision. Instead, it was replaced by a torrential downpour.

In an instant, Li Fan almost lost his direction.

In the transitional zone between the river of time and reality, he was caught in a dilemma of advancing or retreating.

Advancing rashly might lead him to plunge back into the river of time. Staying here, still within the range of the river of time's scouring, with the core continuously being eroded, was also a dead end.

Just as Li Fan was hesitating, he suddenly saw a familiar ray of light amidst the pouring rain before him.

This perhaps represented that in the time node eight thousand years later, he had once had contact with this ray of light.

Although it did not exist in the past timeline, through this contact, a cross-temporal anchor point was formed.

Li Fan knew how difficult it was to find something related to himself amidst the pouring rain eight thousand years ago.

Seizing the opportunity, Li Fan did not hesitate. He immediately controlled the dilapidated Contra-Flow Boat and flew towards the fleeting ray of light.

With the anchor point as his guide, before the Contra-Flow Boat completely disintegrated, Li Fan finally traversed the wind and rain of the river of time.

And arrived in the real world.

The Profound Yellow Realm.

8,643 years before the initial anchor point!

"That beam of light... is it from the Medicine King Sect?! How dare they run away?"

"Quick, go inform the Elder!"

"Wait! Although the Medicine King Sect is not a large sect, its assets are quite substantial. They wouldn't possibly pack all their treasures when fleeing in such a hurry..."

"Let's go. Don't let others get there first!"

"Wait, what is that? Is it another beam of light?"

"Could it be that the Medicine King Sect had a disagreement and decided not to run anymore?"

"Let's go and see!"

……

When Li Fan woke up from his昏厥, he was already surrounded.

“Hmm?”

In a daze, Li Fan had not yet fully recovered. He only noticed the cultivators around him, while counting their spoils, occasionally glancing at him.

“You’re finally awake, kid.”

“Quickly tell us what happened to the Medicine King Sect. Confess honestly, and we might spare your life. Otherwise…”

“Stop talking nonsense with him, just search his soul directly!”

“You idiot, these two beams of light are so conspicuous. We can’t hide them. How will we explain to the Elder when he asks!”

These people were whispering among themselves, completely ignoring Li Fan, who was tightly bound.

Li Fan ignored them for now and first checked his current condition.

Although his body had almost completely disappeared in the river of time, as soon as he returned to reality, the Great Dao of Longevity within him re-evolved into a new body.

However, to Li Fan's regret, after this voyage, the Great Dao of Longevity seemed to have suffered great damage.

And this damage seemed irreversible.

At least, for now, it could not be restored.

“After all, it’s not truly mine, but a gift from Shou Qiu Gong,” Li Fan said with a self-deprecating smile.

“Hmm?”

“Shou Qiu Gong?”

A moment later, Li Fan reacted.

He had traveled eight thousand years upstream in the river of time.

Although his cultivation and divine abilities, as well as the Great Dao of Longevity, had been completely scoured and tempered, in return, his lost memories had all been recovered.

The events of these two lives played out one after another before Li Fan, causing him to sigh softly.

“Due to a momentary greed, it led to infinite variables.”

“The consequences of the fusion of the three Daos – Mountains and Seas, Longevity, and Revert All – were indeed beyond my current capacity to bear.”

“Fortunately, my luck is not bad. Even when I lost my memories, I found great opportunities.”

“The Dao of Contra-Flow…”

Li Fan lowered his head, recalling everything he had experienced in the river of time, a peculiar light appearing in his eyes.

“Revert All.” After thinking, Li Fan first called out in his heart.

The repeated failure of Revert All caused Li Fan a sense of extreme unease.

There was still no response.

However, after careful sensing, Li Fan finally confirmed that Revert All was still within him.

It was just that for some reason, it seemed to be in a dormant state.

Simulator genre. "You were born into this world as the son of the Flame Emperor."

"You met a competitive girl of the Ji surname at Zhuolu and easily defeated her."

"You promoted agriculture, forged weapons, broke superstitions, and were slandered by the gods of all heavens as Chiyou."

"You sacrificed your father and made a final charge towards destiny."

Chapter 1530: Simplified Illusion

Li Fan couldn't help but guess if it was to help him get rid of the influence of the fusion of the three Daos that Revert All fell into dormancy. For him, Revert All had accompanied him throughout his rebirth and cultivation. Having lost its trump card suddenly, Li Fan felt extremely uncomfortable. Fortunately, the decades he experienced during his amnesia could be considered a buffer. It was as if it told Li Fan that even without Revert All, he could forge a path to immortality on his own. "However, compared to Revert All, which can be activated with a single thought to undo everything, the Contra-Flow Boat is far inferior. Without a life-saving trump card, I have to be more cautious. Otherwise, if I die this time, it will be for real." A shadow flickered in Li Fan's eyes.

He gave up on bothering the dormant Revert All and shifted his attention to the Contra-Flow Boat. Although weak, as his only means of survival for now, it still needed close attention. The Contra-Flow Boat, which was already at the brink of collapse after traveling upstream for eight thousand years, could only be described as tragic. After Li Fan's forced landing, only a bare deck and a few remaining pillars were left. If it weren't for the faint aura of the Dao of Contra-Flow still emanating from the deck, Li Fan might have thought the Contra-Flow Boat was completely destroyed.

"Although Heaven Emperor Tai said that as long as one understands the Dao of Contra-Flow, anyone can build a Contra-Flow Boat. But in the entire primordial possibility, over countless years, only two Contra-Flow Boats seem to have been created. Clearly, it's not as simple as Heaven Emperor Tai said. At least..." Li Fan sensed the wooden board of the Contra-Flow Boat and observed it for a long time, but ultimately found no way to repair it.

Let alone creating a new one.

Revert All, the Great Dao of Longevity, and the Contra-Flow Boat were all on strike at the moment. Li Fan's current situation could definitely not be described as pleasant.

Therefore, the main goal for this life became clear.

First and foremost, to find a way to help Revert All awaken as soon as possible. Secondly, to repair the Contra-Flow Boat and accumulate the power of the Great Dao of Longevity.

Whether it was any of these, for the current Li Fan, it was beyond his reach.

Now, there were several problems facing Li Fan.

First, Revert All had fallen into a dormant state, so were his self-comprehended [Transformation of True and False] and the divine ability [Illusion is True] still useful?

Second, with the help of the Heaven Emperor, he had returned to eight thousand years ago. So, at this time node, in the sealed village beneath the Mountains and Seas Fishing Ground, was there another Heaven Emperor? If so, could he sense what had happened to Li Fan eight thousand years later? If not...

Third, after his strength was fully restored and his condition was optimal, what should he do next? Should he return to the safe temporal domain of the anchor point of one year ago, or continue to drift into the past until he found true safety?

……

Even for Li Fan, these questions were quite tricky for a while.

He could only tackle them one by one.

Facing the surrounding disciples who were suspected to be from the Ten Immortal Dao Sects and were trying to capture him, Li Fan first tested the Transformation of True and False. His current body had no cultivation. However, with the empowerment of the residual Great Dao of Longevity, it was enough to withstand the strength equivalent to his Nascent Soul stage in the past.

"When the true becomes false, and the false becomes true~"

Li Fan chanted in his heart.

However, nothing happened, as if nothing had changed.

But Li Fan did not feel afraid because of this. Instead, he breathed a sigh of relief.

In fact, the moment he cast [Illusion is True], Li Fan did feel the unique fluctuations of the Transformation of True and False. In fact, it proved that even without Revert All, he could still achieve the transformation of true and false himself. After all, this was a path he had comprehended himself. As long as there was a Dao of True and False between Mountains, Seas, and the mortal world, he could still cast it freely.

The reason there was no change in him was simply because the temporal environment eight thousand years ago was significantly different from that of eight years ago.

Nearly ten thousand years of time, the birth and death of Daos, coupled with the shaping influence of the external Dao Annihilation Tribulation, could completely be regarded as two different worlds.

Therefore, although Li Fan's [Illusion is True] divine ability had been successfully cast, his attempt to manifest his imagined cultivation within his body had failed.

As the saying goes, a hair's breadth deviation can lead to a thousand-mile error. The subtle differences and drastic environmental changes caused the failure of Li Fan's [Illusion is True] divine ability. To put it simply, the effectiveness of the Transformation of True and False relied on a thorough understanding of the Great Dao of the world. The current situation was that the Great Dao had changed, and Li Fan needed to re-establish his understanding.

However, this was not a major problem. Although eight thousand years had passed, it was still the same possibility and the same world. As long as Li Fan was given some time to re-establish his understanding of the Great Dao environment, he would be able to use the Transformation of True and False smoothly again.

"It's a pity, though, that the divine ability [Illusion is True] seems to have disappeared from me along with Revert All's dormancy." After sensing carefully for a long time, Li Fan finally confirmed this and sighed softly.

However, he was not particularly surprised. Having experienced the gain and loss of the Great Dao of Longevity, Li Fan understood that his own connection was fundamentally different from what others had bestowed upon him.

But even if it was lost, Li Fan had not completely given up on [Illusion is True], arguably the strongest life-saving divine ability in the Mountains and Seas. Being able to transform and hide his identity in the face of the Infinite Sea, once one had tasted its sweetness, how could Li Fan be willing to give it up?

"The so-called [Illusion is True] is merely a very advanced application of the Transformation of True and False. Relying on my comprehension of the Transformation of True and False..." Li Fan carefully savored the feeling of being protected by [Illusion is True] back then.

It was fortunate that he had constantly maintained it, leaving him with enough profound experience. This allowed Li Fan to recall it more easily now.

"Even if I cannot replicate the true [Illusion is True], it is not difficult to achieve a weakened version."

Li Fan's gaze swept over the disciples with unfriendly expressions around him. After a moment, a change quietly occurred.

"You brat have been holding back for so long, and you haven't done anything. I think you..." Originally, one of the cultivators had already become impatient and was about to slap Li Fan on the head. He was cursing and his eyes showed fierce intent.

But as Li Fan cast his [Illusion is True] divine ability, his unfriendly expression slowly disappeared.

The people around him were the same.

It was as if they had forgotten Li Fan's identity as a "Medicine King Sect disciple who fell from the sky," and only regarded him as "one of their own."

The cultivator who had slapped Li Fan on the head earlier, after a moment of daze, looked around blankly. After a while, he seemed to come to his senses and exclaimed, slapping his thigh, "It's bad! Where did that kid go?"

The others also seemed to awaken from a dream, each exclaiming in shock, "How is that possible? Under everyone's watchful eyes, he actually escaped?"

"I didn't sense any spiritual energy fluctuations from that person at all. How did he escape?"

Everyone was in disbelief. They searched the surroundings with their divine senses but found no suspicious traces.

Just then, Li Fan spoke, "Do you smell a faint medicinal fragrance lingering in the air? I heard that the disciples of the Medicine King Sect are best at using medicine. They can heal or kill. It seems we have fallen into a trap!"

Li Fan's tone was full of regret and self-blame.

"Indeed!"

The other cultivators sniffed the air and also seemed to realize something. They all regretted it.

They did not notice the anomaly of Li Fan, who should not have existed.

Having temporarily escaped mortal danger, Li Fan breathed a slight sigh of relief.

For now, this was the best he could do.

Restoring his strength would depend on his observation of this past era. He could only proceed slowly.

"Although I have lost my past enlightenment experiences due to the scouring of the river of time, as long as I see the Dao again, I should be able to re-comprehend it quickly."

"Others need to create their Dao from scratch, but I only need to retrace my steps."

Li Fan looked up at the Profound Yellow sky at this moment. A sense of both familiarity and strangeness welled up in his heart.

However, he was still surrounded by enemies. Li Fan's [Illusion is True] had not yet been able to completely alter the perceptions of others. Therefore, he did not show anything special, but followed the path of enlightenment and accumulated strength.

Just as the group of cultivators was at a loss because they had lost their target. A beam of light flew from the distant horizon, rapidly approaching.

"It's bad, Elder Song is here."

The cultivators' expressions changed.

"Brothers, we must keep our story consistent. Let's insist that we never saw another beam of light." Soon, the group reached a consensus through divine sense communication.

Li Fan looked up at the approaching figure.

He could clearly see that Elder Song, whom these cultivators feared so much, only appeared to be at the Nascent Soul cultivation stage.

However, his flight speed was not slow, and he soon landed before them.

When asked about the departure of the Medicine King Sect and the other beam of light moving in the opposite direction.

The group replied according to their agreed-upon story.

Elder Song scanned the crowd, his gaze lingering on Li Fan the longest, a hint of doubt flashing in his eyes. However, he soon dismissed it. He didn't say much.

"The departure of the Medicine King Sect was within the expectations of the Masters of the Ten Sects. Hmph, a bunch of ignorant fools, let them go." Elder Song's tone was dismissive, his verdict final.

"Although they have left, the foundations of their sect still remain. Although our Evergreen Valley is the closest, it is still difficult to swallow everything the Medicine King Sect left behind alone. We can only take the most essential areas. Quickly return to the sect with me and prepare to deal with the upcoming disputes."

"This world is about to become turbulent," Elder Song sighed.

Everyone took their orders. They exchanged glances, and a hint of relief from escaping disaster flashed in their eyes. Li Fan also blended in and returned to this so-called Evergreen Valley.

Relying on the ability of [Illusion is True], he felt like he was returning home no matter where he went. After inquiring, he quickly understood the situation.

Evergreen Valley was a subordinate sect of the Supreme Sect, one of the Ten Immortal Dao Sects. Although it was called subordinate, it only held the title. They enjoyed few benefits, but the annual tribute could not be missed. If the Ten Sects needed conscription, they had to respond without delay. It could be said that they were no different from slaves to the Ten Sects.

However, the Ten Immortal Dao Sects were powerful, and even if the disciples of Evergreen Valley were dissatisfied, they could do nothing. They could only endure in silence.

Evergreen Valley was adjacent to the Medicine King Sect. The Medicine King Sect saved countless lives with its medical practices, while Evergreen Valley accumulated considerable wealth by taking advantage of the convenience provided by the Medicine King Sect.

As a small sect, with a sect leader at the God Transformation stage and three Elders at the Nascent Soul stage, their strength was quite good within a radius of ten thousand miles.

Not long ago, it seemed that the Ten Immortal Dao Sects had sensed the Medicine King Sect's intention to flee, and thus issued an order to monitor them. If there were any abnormalities, they were to report them immediately.

This was why the disciples of Evergreen Valley discovered Li Fan, who had descended from the sky.

……

"Elder Song, I have something important to report." Just as Evergreen Valley was shrouded in tension as they prepared to fight over the territory left behind by the Medicine King Sect. Li Fan secretly found Elder Song.

"Oh? What is it?" Elder Song recognized Li Fan and a glint flashed in his eyes. "You are the disciple who guarded the mountain that day? What was your name again."

"Replying to Elder, my name is Li Ping. I just joined recently." Li Fan spoke without hesitation. With the enhancement of [Illusion is True], this Elder, who was only at the Nascent Soul stage, could not see through him.

"What do you have to report?"

"That day, in reality, a beam of light from the Medicine King Sect returned to the Profound Yellow Realm and landed in our central area. Although we captured it, the thief accidentally escaped… " Li Fan put on a frightened expression.

Elder Song's eyes narrowed instantly.

"Those few people actually colluded to deceive the Elder and threatened me. Although I agreed at the time, after thinking it over when I returned, I still felt uneasy."

"You are quite conscientious." Elder Song suddenly stood up and walked out.

After only half a day, he returned.

However, he now had a faint scent of blood on him.

"Although you acted deceitfully, you were able to repent in time and even made a contribution by exposing them."

"You deserve a reward!"

"What do you want?" Elder Song asked indifferently.

"This humble servant dares not ask for anything. I will accept whatever Elder bestows." Li Fan replied.

Elder Song's face showed a smile, and after pondering for a moment, he rewarded Li Fan with a defensive magical artifact. With the conflicts about to arise, having this artifact to protect him would definitely increase his chances of survival.

"Elder Song is indeed a good person." Li Fan played with the dragon-patterned fire shield in his hand and smiled.

Of course, he didn't care about this magical artifact reward. The reason he went to Elder Song again was simply to test the effectiveness of his [Illusion is True]. Initially, Elder Song had instinctively felt suspicious. But now, he was completely deceived and regarded Li Fan as a disciple of Evergreen Valley.

"It will still take some time to deceive a cultivator at the God Transformation stage."

"The more I comprehend the Dao of this time node, the faster this time will be."

The surrounding spiritual energy seemed to be drawn towards him, swirling around him.

But Li Fan deliberately did not absorb it.

He just looked up at the sky.

Frowning, a hint of doubt flickered in his eyes.

Although it was the same Dao, when he comprehended it, he felt a sense of powerlessness.

It was not that his previous comprehension memories had become invalid.

But the Dao laws of the Profound Yellow Realm were instinctively refusing to be comprehended by him.

"Hmph, the Heavenly Dao of the Profound Yellow."

A sharp light emerged from Li Fan's eyes.
